Question #30 (ID: 473787)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
দৃশ্যকল্প-১: [math]n \sin 2 \alpha=2\left(1-n \sin ^{2} \alpha\right) \tan \beta[/math] এবং

দৃশ্যকল্প-২: [math]x=4 \theta[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]\sin 420^{\circ} \cos 390^{\circ}+\sin \left(-300^{\circ}\right) \cos \left(-330^{\circ}\right)[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
খ. দৃশ্যকল্প-১ থেকে দেখাও যে, [math](1-n) \tan \alpha=\tan (\alpha-\beta) \text {}[/math]
গ. দৃশ্যকল্প-২ থেকে প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\tan \frac{x}{4}+2 \tan \frac{x}{2}+4 \tan x+8 \cot 2 x=\cot \frac{x}{4}[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]\begin{array}{l}\sin 420^{\circ} \cos 390^{\circ}+\sin \left(-300^{\circ}\right) \cos \left(-330^{\circ}\right) \\=\sin 420^{\circ} \cos 390^{\circ}-\sin 300^{\circ} \cos 330^{\circ} \\=\sin \left(4 \times 90^{\circ}+60^{\circ}\right) \cos \left(4 \times 90^{\circ}+30^{\circ}\right)\end{array}[/math]
 [math]-\sin \left(4 \times 90^{\circ}-60^{\circ}\right) \cos \left(4 \times 90^{\circ}-30^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\sin 60^{\circ} \cdot \cos 30^{\circ}-\left(-\sin 60^{\circ}\right) \cdot \cos 30^{\circ} \\=\sin 60^{\circ} \cdot \cos 30^{\circ}+\sin 60^{\circ} \cdot \cos 30^{\circ} \\=2 \sin 60^{\circ} \cos 30^{\circ}=2 \cdot \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2} \cdot \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}=\frac{3}{2} \text { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]n \sin 2 \alpha=2\left(1-n \sin ^{2} \alpha\right) \tan \beta[/math]
 [math]=\mathrm{n} 2 \sin \alpha \cos \alpha=2\left(1-n \sin ^{2} \alpha\right) \tan \beta[/math]
 [math]= \tan \beta=\frac{n \sin \alpha \cos \alpha}{1-n \sin ^{2} \alpha}=\frac{\frac{n \sin \alpha \cos \alpha}{\cos ^{2} \alpha}}{\frac{1}{\cos ^{2} \alpha}-\frac{n \sin ^{2} \alpha}{\cos ^{2} \alpha}}[/math]
[লব ও হরকে [math]\cos ^{2} \alpha[/math]
 দ্বারা ভাগ করে][math]\therefore \tan \beta=\frac{n \tan \alpha}{\sec ^{2} \alpha-\tan ^{2} \alpha}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{n \tan \alpha}{1+\tan ^{2} \alpha-\tan ^{2} \alpha} \ldots \ldots \ldots \text { (i) }[/math]
ডানপক্ষ [math]=\tan (\alpha-\beta)=\frac{\tan \alpha-\tan \beta}{1+\tan \alpha \tan \beta}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\tan \alpha-\frac{\mathrm{n} \tan \alpha}{1+\tan ^{2} \alpha-\mathrm{n} \tan ^{2} \alpha}}{1+\tan \alpha \cdot \frac{\mathrm{ntan} \alpha}{1+\tan ^{2} \alpha-\mathrm{ntan}^{2} \alpha}}[/math]
 [(i) ব্যবহার করে][math]=\frac{\frac{\tan \alpha+\tan ^{3} \alpha-n \tan ^{3} \alpha-n \tan \alpha}{1+\tan ^{2} \alpha-n \tan ^{2} \alpha}}{\frac{1+\tan ^{2} \alpha-n \tan ^{2} \alpha+n \tan ^{2} \alpha}{1+\tan ^{2} \alpha-n \tan ^{2} \alpha}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\tan \alpha\left(1+\tan ^{2} \alpha\right)-\mathrm{n} \tan \alpha\left(1+\tan ^{2} \alpha\right)}{1+\tan ^{2} \alpha}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\left(1+\tan ^{2} \alpha\right)(\tan \alpha-n \tan \alpha)}{1+\tan ^{2} \alpha}[/math]
(1+tana) (tana - ntana) 1+tan a = (1-n)tana =[math]=(1-n) \tan \alpha=[/math]
 বামপক্ষ[math]\therefore(1-n) \tan \alpha=\tan (\alpha-\beta)[/math]
 (দেখানো হলো)[math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]x=4 \theta[/math]
 [math]\therefore \tan \frac{x}{4}+2 \tan \frac{x}{2}+4 \tan x+8 \cot 2 x[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\tan \theta+2 \tan 2 \theta+4 \tan 4 \theta+8 \cot 8 \theta \\=\tan \theta+2 \tan 2 \theta+4 \tan 4 \theta+\frac{8}{\tan 8 \theta}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\tan \theta+2 \tan 2 \theta+4 \tan 4 \theta+\frac{8}{\tan (2.4 \theta)} \\=\tan \theta+2 \tan 2 \theta+4 \tan 4 \theta+\frac{8\left(1-\tan ^{2} 4 \theta\right)}{.2 \tan 4 \theta}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=\tan \theta+2 \tan 2 \theta+\frac{8 \tan ^{2} 4 \theta+8-8 \tan ^{2} 4 \theta}{2 \tan 4 \theta}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\tan \theta+2 \tan 2 \theta+\frac{4}{\tan (2.2 \theta)} \\=\tan \theta+2 \tan 2 \theta+\frac{4\left(1-\tan ^{2} 2 \theta\right)}{2 \tan 2 \theta} \\=\tan \theta+\frac{4 \tan ^{2} 2 \theta+4-4 \tan ^{2} 2 \theta}{2 \tan 2 \theta} \\=\tan \theta+\frac{2}{\tan 2 \theta}=\tan \theta+\frac{2\left(1-\tan ^{2} \theta\right)}{2 \tan \theta} \\=\frac{2 \tan ^{2} \theta+2-2 \tan ^{2} \theta}{2 \tan \theta}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{2}{2 \tan \theta}=\cot \theta=\cot \frac{x}{4}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \tan \frac{x}{4}+2 \tan \frac{x}{2}+4 \tan x+8 \cot 2 x=\cot \frac{x}{4}[/math]
(প্রমাণিত)

Explanation:
ক সমীকরণে কোণগুলোকে সরল করে: [math]\sin420^\circ=\sin60^\circ=\frac{\sqrt3}{2},\ \cos390^\circ=\cos30^\circ=\frac{\sqrt3}{2}[/math] এবং [math]\sin(-300^\circ)=\sin60^\circ=\frac{\sqrt3}{2},\ \cos(-330^\circ)=\cos30^\circ=\frac{\sqrt3}{2}[/math], তাই যোগফল [math]\frac{3}{4}+\frac{3}{4}=\frac{3}{2}[/math]।

খ শুরু করা যাক [math]n\sin2\alpha=2(1-n\sin^2\alpha)\tan\beta[/math] থেকে; [math]\sin2\alpha=2\sin\alpha\cos\alpha[/math] ব্যবহার করে পাই [math]n\sin\alpha\cos\alpha=(1-n\sin^2\alpha)\tan\beta[/math], অর্থাৎ [math]\tan\beta=\dfrac{n\sin\alpha\cos\alpha}{1-n\sin^2\alpha}[/math]। अब [math]\tan(\alpha-\beta)=\dfrac{\tan\alpha-\tan\beta}{1+\tan\alpha\tan\beta}[/math] গাণিতিকভাবে সরল করলে উর্ধ্বতন বিভাজকে [math]\dfrac{\sin\alpha(1-n)}{\cos\alpha(1-n\sin^2\alpha)}[/math] এবং নিম্নতকে [math]\dfrac{1}{1-n\sin^2\alpha}[/math] পাওয়া যায়, ফলে [math]\tan(\alpha-\beta)=(1-n)\dfrac{\sin\alpha}{\cos\alpha}=(1-n)\tan\alpha[/math]।

গ [math]x=4\theta[/math] ধরে [math]\tan\theta=\cot\theta-2\cot2\theta[/math] (কারণ সরলীকরণে এটি সত্য), একইভাবে [math]2\tan2\theta=2\cot2\theta-4\cot4\theta[/math] এবং [math]4\tan4\theta=4\cot4\theta-8\cot8\theta[/math]; এগুলো যোগ করলে মধ্যবর্তী টার্মগুলো বাতিল হয়ে ফলাফল দাঁড়ায় [math]\tan\theta+2\tan2\theta+4\tan4\theta+8\cot8\theta=\cot\theta[/math], অর্থাৎ প্রদত্ত সমীকরণটি সত্য এবং [math]\cot\frac{x}{4}[/math] পাওয়া যায়।

Question #31 (ID: 473785)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:

[Image]


Options:
ক. ত্রিভুজটির পরিব্যাসার্ধ নির্ণয় কর।
খ. দেখাও যে, [math]\frac{1}{a+b}+\frac{1}{b+c}=\frac{3}{a+b+c}[/math]
গ. [math]\angle A^{}=45^{\circ}[/math] হলে দেখাও যে, [math]\left(\frac{\sqrt{3}-1}{\sqrt{2}}\right) a+c \sqrt{2}=2 b[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, [math]\mathrm{B}=60^{\circ}[/math]
আমরা জানি, [math]\frac{a}{\sin A}=\frac{b}{\sin B}=\frac{c}{\sin C}=2 R[/math]
তাহলে, [math]\frac{b}{\sin 60^{\circ}}=2 \mathrm{R}[/math]
 [math]= \mathrm{R}=\frac{\mathrm{b}}{\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2} \cdot 2} \therefore \mathrm{R}=\frac{\mathrm{b}}{\sqrt{3}} \text {. }[/math]
সুতরাং ত্রিভুজটির পরিব্যাসার্ধ [math]\frac{\mathrm{b}}{\sqrt{3}} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]\mathrm{B}=60^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\cos B=\cos 60^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\frac{\mathrm{c}^{2}+\mathrm{a}^{2}-\mathrm{b}^{2}}{2 \mathrm{ca}}=\frac{1}{2}\left[\because \cos \mathrm{B}=\frac{\mathrm{c}^{2}+\mathrm{a}^{2}-\mathrm{b}^{2}}{2 \mathrm{ca}}\right]\\= \frac{\mathrm{c}^{2}+\mathrm{a}^{2}-\mathrm{b}^{2}}{\mathrm{ca}}=1\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}= c^{2}+a^{2}-b^{2}=c a\\= c^{2}+a^{2}-b^{2}-c a=0\\= a^{2}+b^{2}+c^{2}-a c-2 b^{2}=0\\=(a+b+c)^{2}-2 a b-2 a c-2 b c-a c-2 b^{2}=0\\=(a+b+c)^{2}+a b+b c+b^{2}=3 a c+3 a b+3 b c+3 b^{2}\\= (a+b+c)^{2}+b(a+b+c)=3 a(b+c)+3 b(b+c)\\= (a+b+c)(a+b+c+b)=3(a+b)(b+c)\\= (\mathrm{a}+\mathrm{b}+\mathrm{c})\{(\mathrm{a}+\mathrm{b})+(\mathrm{b}+\mathrm{c})\}=3(\mathrm{a}+\mathrm{b})(\mathrm{b}+\mathrm{c})\\= \frac{(a+b)+(b+c)}{(a+b)(b+c)}=\frac{3}{(a+b+c)}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \frac{1}{a+b}+\frac{1}{b+c}=\frac{3}{a+b+c}[/math]
 (দেখানো হলো)[math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]\angle \mathrm{A}=45^{\circ}, \angle \mathrm{B}=60^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\therefore \angle \mathrm{C}=180^{\circ}-(\angle \mathrm{A}+\angle \mathrm{B})=180^{\circ}-\left(45^{\circ}+60^{\circ}\right)=75^{\circ} \\\therefore \cos C=\cos 75^{\circ}=\cos \left(45^{\circ}+30^{\circ}\right)\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=\cos 45^{\circ} \cos 30^{\circ}-\sin 45^{\circ} \sin 30^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \cdot \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}-\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \cdot \frac{1}{2}=\frac{\sqrt{3}-1}{2 \sqrt{2}}[/math]
এখন, [math]b=c \cos A+a \cos C=c \cos 45^{\circ}+a \cos 75^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\begin{aligned}= & \frac{c}{\sqrt{2}}+\frac{a(\sqrt{3}-1)}{2 \sqrt{2}} \\= 2 b & =\frac{2 c}{\sqrt{2}}+\frac{2 a(\sqrt{3}-1)}{2 \sqrt{2}}\end{aligned}[/math]
 [math]\therefore\left(\frac{\sqrt{3}-1}{\sqrt{2}}\right) a+c \sqrt{2}=2 b[/math]
 (দেখানো হলো)

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:
ক সাইন-নিয়ম অনুযায়ী [math]a:b:c=\sin A:\sin B:\sin C[/math] এবং [math]R=\dfrac{a}{2\sin A}=\dfrac{b}{2\sin B}=\dfrac{c}{2\sin C}[/math]; এখানে [math]\sin45=\dfrac{1}{\sqrt2},\ \sin60=\dfrac{\sqrt3}{2},\ \sin75=\dfrac{\sqrt3+1}{2\sqrt2}[/math] হওয়ার ফলে [math]R=\dfrac{a\sqrt2}{2}=\dfrac{b}{\sqrt3}=\dfrac{c\sqrt2(\sqrt3-1)}{2}[/math]।  
খ সাইন-নিয়মে প্রতি পাশে একই গুণক বাতিল হয়, তাই [math]\frac{1}{a+b}+\frac{1}{b+c}=\frac{1}{k(\sin A+\sin B)}+\frac{1}{k(\sin B+\sin C)}[/math] এবং [math]k[/math] বাদ দিয়ে [math]\sin45,\sin60,\sin75[/math] প্রতিস্থাপন করলে সরলীকরণে রাশিটি [math]\dfrac{3}{\sin A+\sin B+\sin C}[/math] পাওয়া যায়, ফলে দাবী সত্য।  
গ সাইন-নিয়ম লাগিয়ে [math]a=k\sin45,\ b=k\sin60,\ c=k\sin75[/math] নেওয়া হলে বাম পাশে থাকে [math]\left(\frac{\sqrt3-1}{\sqrt2}\right)\frac{k}{\sqrt2}+\sqrt2\cdot\frac{k(\sqrt3+1)}{2\sqrt2}=k\sqrt3[/math] এবং ডান পাশে [math]2b=2k\sin60=2k\cdot\frac{\sqrt3}{2}=k\sqrt3[/math], তৎপর্য সমীকরণটি পূরণ করে।

Question #32 (ID: 473784)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:

[Image]


Options:
ক. [math]\frac{1+\cot D}{1-\cot D}[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর ৷
খ. [math]ABC[/math] ত্রিভুজে [math]b = 2c[/math] এবং [math]B = 3C[/math] হলে [math]A, B[/math] ও [math]C[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর ।
গ. দেখাও যে, [math]\tan \left(\frac{2 \pi}{9}+D\right)=\tan \left(\frac{\pi}{9}+D\right)+2 \tan \left(D+\frac{\pi}{36}\right)[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, [math]D=\frac{\pi}{12}=15^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\therefore \frac{1+\cot D}{1-\cot D}=\frac{1+\cot 15^{\circ}}{1-\cot 15^{\circ}}=\frac{1+\frac{1}{\tan 15^{\circ}}}{1-\frac{1}{\tan 15^{\circ}}} \\=\frac{\tan 15^{\circ}+1}{\tan 15^{\circ}-1}=-\frac{1+\tan 15^{\circ}}{1-\tan 15^{\circ}}=-\frac{\tan 45^{\circ}+\tan 15^{\circ}}{1-\tan 45^{\circ} \cdot \tan 15^{\circ}} \\=-\tan \left(45^{\circ}+15^{\circ}\right)=-\tan 60^{\circ}=-\sqrt{3} \\\therefore \frac{1+\cot D}{1-\cot D}=-\sqrt{3} \text { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খআমরা জানি, [math]\frac{b}{\sin B}=\frac{c}{\sin C}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}= \frac{2 c}{\sin B}=\frac{c}{\sin C} \quad[\because b=2 c]\\= \frac{2}{\sin B}=\frac{1}{\sin C}\\= \frac{2}{\sin 3 C}=\frac{1}{\sin C} \quad[\because B=3 C]\\= \sin 3 C=2 \sin C\\= 3 \sin \mathrm{C}-4 \sin ^{3} \mathrm{C}=2 \sin \mathrm{C}\\= -4 \sin ^{3} \mathrm{C}=2 \sin \mathrm{C}-3 \sin \mathrm{C}\\=-4 \sin ^{3} \mathrm{C}=-\sin \mathrm{C}\\= 4 \sin ^{2} C=1[\because \sin C 
eq 0]\end{array}[/math]
 [math]= \sin ^{2} C=\frac{1}{4}[/math]
 [math]= \sin C=\frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}= \sin C=\sin 30^{\circ} \therefore C=30^{\circ}\\\therefore \mathrm{B}=3 \mathrm{C}=3 \times 30^{\circ}=90^{\circ}\left[\because \mathrm{C}=30^{\circ}\right]\end{array}[/math]
আমরা জানি, [math]A+B+C=180^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}= A=180^{\circ}-(B+C) \text{.}\\=A=180^{\circ}-\left(90^{\circ}+30^{\circ}\right) \therefore A=60^{\circ}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 নির্ণেয় [math]A=60^{\circ}, B=90^{\circ}, C=30^{\circ} \text {. }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]\mathrm{D}=\frac{\pi}{12}=\left(\frac{\pi}{12} \times \frac{180}{\pi}\right)^{\circ}=15^{\circ}[/math]
দেখাতে হবে যে, [math]\tan \left(\frac{2 \pi}{9}+D\right)=\tan \left(\frac{\pi}{9}+D\right)+2 \tan \left(D+\frac{\pi}{36}\right)[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}= \tan \left(40^{\circ}+15^{\circ}\right)=\tan \left(20^{\circ}+15^{\circ}\right)+2 \tan \left(15^{\circ}+5^{\circ}\right)\\= \tan 55^{\circ}=\tan 35^{\circ}+2 \tan 20^{\circ}\end{array}[/math]
এখন, [math]\tan 20^{\circ}=\tan \left(55^{\circ}-35^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}= \tan 20^{\circ}=\frac{\tan 55^{\circ}-\tan 35^{\circ}}{1+\tan 55^{\circ} \cdot \tan 35^{\circ}} \\= \tan 20^{\circ}=\frac{\tan 55^{\circ}-\tan 35^{\circ}}{1+\tan \left(90^{\circ}-35^{\circ}\right) \tan 35^{\circ}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=\tan 20^{\circ}=\frac{\tan 55^{\circ}-\tan 35^{\circ}}{1+\cot 35^{\circ} \cdot \frac{1}{\cot 35^{\circ}}}[/math]

[Image]
[math]\begin{array}{l}= \tan 20^{\circ} \doteq \frac{\tan 55^{\circ}-\tan 35^{\circ}}{1+1}\\= \tan 55^{\circ}-\tan 35^{\circ}=2 \tan 20^{\circ}\\= \tan 55^{\circ}=\tan 35^{\circ}+2 \tan 20^{\circ}\\\therefore \tan \left(\frac{2 \pi}{9}+D\right)=\tan \left(\frac{\pi}{9}+D\right)+2 \tan \left(D+\frac{\pi}{36}\right)\end{array}[/math]
(দেখানো হলো)

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক [math]\frac{1+\cot D}{1-\cot D}[/math]কে [math]\cot D=\frac{1}{\tan D}[/math] দিয়ে লেখলে [math]\frac{1+\cot D}{1-\cot D}=\frac{\tan D+1}{\tan D-1}=-\frac{1+\tan D}{1-\tan D}[/math] এবং [math]\frac{1+\tan x}{1-\tan x}=\tan\left(\frac{\pi}{4}+x\right)[/math] হওয়ায় ফল হবে [math]-\tan\left(\frac{\pi}{4}+D\right)[/math]।

খ আইন অব সাইনস থেকে [math]\frac{b}{\sin B}=\frac{c}{\sin C}[/math] এবং [math]b=2c[/math] হলে [math]\sin B=2\sin C[/math]। আর [math]B=3C[/math] হলে [math]\sin3C=2\sin C[/math] → [math]3\sin C-4\sin^3C=2\sin C[/math] → [math]\sin C(1-4\sin^2C)=0[/math]। বিবেচনায় [math]\sin C=\tfrac{1}{2}[/math], তাই [math]C=30^\circ, B=90^\circ, A=60^\circ[/math] হয়।

গ ট্যানজেন্ট যোগ-বিয়োগ সূত্র ব্যবহার করুন: [math]\tan U-\tan V=\dfrac{\sin(U-V)}{\cos U\cos V}[/math] যেখানে [math]U= \tfrac{2\pi}{9}+D,\;V=\tfrac{\pi}{9}+D[/math] হলে [math]\sin(U-V)=\sin\frac{\pi}{9}=2\sin\frac{\pi}{36}\cos\frac{\pi}{36}[/math] এবং নিচের অংশের কোসাইনগুলোকে গুণ করলে সরলীভূত করে ক্যান্সেল করলে ফল পাওয়া যায় [math]2\tan\left(D+\frac{\pi}{36}\right)[/math], ফলে সমীকরণটি সত্যি।

Question #33 (ID: 473781)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]c[/math] মিটার দীর্ঘ একটি সীমানা দেয়াল [math]AB[/math] এবং [math]C[/math] বিন্দুতে অবস্থিত একটি লাইট হাউস থেকে দেয়ালটি পর্যবেক্ষণ করা হয়। দেয়ালের [math]A[/math] ও [math]B[/math] প্রান্ত থেকে লাইট হাউসটির দূরত্ব যথাক্রমে [math]b[/math] ও [math]a[/math]। পুরো দেয়ালটি

পর্যবেক্ষণের জন্য লাইট হাউসের সার্চ লাইটটিকে [math]\angle \mathrm{C}[/math] কোণে ঘুরাতে হয়। লাইট হাউস থেকে দেয়াল এবং লাইট হাউসের মধ্যে উৎপন্ন ত্রিভুজ আকৃতির এলাকাটিও পর্যবেক্ষণ করা হয় ।

Options:
ক. ত্রিভুজাকৃতির এলাকাটির ক্ষেত্রফল নির্ণয় কর।
খ. ত্রিভুজ ক্ষেত্রটির জন্য প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\sin ^{2} A^{}-\sin ^{2} B+\sin ^{2} C=2 \sin A \cdot \cos B \cdot \sin C[/math]
গ. সার্চ লাইটটিকে [math]60^{\circ}[/math] কোণে ঘুরানো প্রয়োজন হলে দেখাও যে, [math]\frac{1}{a+c}+\frac{1}{b+c}=\frac{3}{a+b+c}[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক
[Image]
ত্রিভুজ আকৃতির ক্ষেত্রটির ক্ষেত্রফল[math]\begin{array}{l}=\frac{1}{2} \times \mathrm{AC} \times \mathrm{BC} \times \sin \angle \mathrm{ACB} \\=\frac{1}{2} \cdot \mathrm{b} \cdot \mathrm{a} \cdot \sin \mathrm{C}=\frac{1}{2} \mathrm{ab} \sin \mathrm{C} \text { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খ [math]\triangle \mathrm{ABC}[/math]
 এর তিনটি কোণ যথাক্রমে [math]A, B[/math]
 ও [math]C[/math]
 [math]\therefore A+B+C=\pi[/math]
বামপক্ষ [math]=\sin ^{2} \mathrm{~A}-\sin ^{2} \mathrm{~B}+\sin ^{2} \mathrm{C} .[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\frac{1}{2}\left\{2 \sin ^{2} A+2 \sin ^{2} C\right\}-\sin ^{2} B \\=\frac{1}{2}(1-\cos 2 A+1-\cos 2 C)-\sin ^{2} B\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\frac{1}{2}(2-\cos 2 \mathrm{~A}-\cos 2 \mathrm{C})-\sin ^{2} \mathrm{~B} \\=1-\frac{1}{2}(\cos 2 \mathrm{~A}+\cos 2 \mathrm{C})-\sin ^{2} \mathrm{~B} \\=1-\frac{1}{2} \cdot 2 \cos (\mathrm{A}+\mathrm{C}) \cos (\mathrm{A}-\mathrm{C})-\sin ^{2} \mathrm{~B} \\=1-\cos (\pi-\mathrm{B}) \cos (\mathrm{A}-\mathrm{C})-\sin ^{2} \mathrm{~B}\end{array}[/math]
 [math][\because A+B+C=\pi][/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=1-\sin ^{2} B+\cos B \cos (A-C) \\=\cos ^{2} B+\cos B \cos (A-C) \\=\cos B\{\cos B+\cos (A-C)\} \\=\cos B[\cos \{\pi-(A+C)\}+\cos (A-C)] \\=\cos B\{-\cos (A+C)+\cos (A-C)\} \\=\cos B\{\cos (A-C)-\cos (A+C)\} \\=\cos B \cdot 2 \sin A \sin C\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=2 \sin A \cos B \sin C^{}=[/math]
 ডানপক্ষ (প্রমাণিত)[math]\\[/math]
 গসার্চ লাইটটিকে যেহেতু [math]60^{\circ}[/math]
 কোণে ঘুরাতে হবেসেহেতু [math]\angle \mathrm{C}=60^{\circ}[/math]
দেওয়া আছে, [math]\mathrm{C}=60^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]= \cos C=\cos 60^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\text{বा, } \frac{\mathrm{a}^{2}+\mathrm{b}^{2}-\mathrm{c}^{2}}{2 \mathrm{ab}}=\frac{1}{2} \quad\left[\because \cos \mathrm{C}=\frac{\mathrm{a}^{2}+\mathrm{b}^{2}-\mathrm{c}^{2}}{2 \mathrm{ab}}\right]\\= \frac{a^{2}+b^{2}-c^{2}}{a b}=1\\= a^{2}+b^{2}-c^{2}=a b\\= a^{2}+b^{2}-c^{2}-a b=0\\= (a+b+c)^{2}-3 a b-2 b c-2 c a-2 c^{2}=0\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=(a+b+c)^{2}+a c+b c+c^{2}=3 a b+3 b c+3 a c+3 c^{2}\\=(a+b+c)^{2}+c(a+b+c)=3 b(a+c)+3 c(a+c)\\= (a+b+c)(a+b+c+c)=(a+c)(3 b+3 c)\\= (a+b+c)\{(a+c)+(b+c)\}=3(a+c)(b+c)\\= \frac{(a+c)+(b+c)}{(a+c)(b+c)}=\frac{3}{a+b+c}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \frac{1}{a+c}+\frac{1}{b+c}=\frac{3}{a+b+c}[/math]
(দেখানো হলো)

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক ত্রিভুজের ক্ষেত্রফল সরাসরি পাওয়া যায় [math]\tfrac{1}{2}ab\sin C[/math] দ্বারা; বিকল্পভাবে হিরনের সূত্র অনুযায়ী এটি লেখা যায় [math]\tfrac{1}{4}\sqrt{(a+b+c)(-a+b+c)(a-b+c)(a+b-c)}[/math]।  

খ শুরু করি [math]\sin^{2}A-\sin^{2}B=\sin(A+B)\sin(A-B)=\sin C\sin(A-B)গ ধরি সমীকরণটিকে সাধারণ রূপে লেখলে এটি সমমূল্যে [math]c^{2}=a^{2}-ab+b^{2}[/math] হয়, এবং কসাইন সূত্র অনুযায়ী [math]c^{2}=a^{2}+b^{2}-2ab\cos C[/math]; যদি [math]C=60^{\circ}[/math] হয় তাহলে [math]\cos C=\tfrac{1}{2}</math] থেকে [math]c^{2}=a^{2}+b^{2}-ab</math] পাওয়া যায়, যা দেওয়া সমীকরণ নিশ্চিত করে।

Question #34 (ID: 473782)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
কোন বিভেদ তলে আলোক রশ্মি [math]2 \alpha[/math] কোণে আপতিত হয়ে [math]2 \theta[/math] কোণে প্রতিসরিত হলো। এই তলে আপতন কোণ এবং প্রতিসরণ কোণের সাইনের অনুপাত [math]k[/math]

Options:
ক. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\tan 54^{\circ}=\tan 36^{\circ}+2 \tan 18^{\circ}[/math]
খ. আলোক রশ্মির প্রতিসরণ থেকে প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\tan (\alpha-\theta)=\frac{k-1}{k+1} \tan (\alpha+\theta)[/math]
গ. [math]\alpha=\frac{\theta}{3}=9^{\circ}[/math] হলে দেখাও যে, [math]k=\frac{\sqrt{5}-1}{\sqrt{5}+1}[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]\begin{array}{l}\tan 18^{\circ}=\tan \left(54^{\circ}-36^{\circ}\right) \\=\frac{\tan 54^{\circ}-\tan 36^{\circ}}{1+\tan 54^{\circ} \tan 36^{\circ}}=\frac{\tan 54^{\circ}-\tan 36^{\circ}}{1+\tan \left(90^{\circ}-36^{\circ}\right) \tan 36^{\circ}} \\=\frac{\tan 54^{\circ}-\tan 36^{\circ}}{1+\cot 36^{\circ} \cdot \frac{1}{\cot 36^{\circ}}}=\frac{\tan 54^{\circ}-\tan 36^{\circ}}{1+1}\\= \tan 54^{\circ}-\tan 36^{\circ}=2 \tan 18^{\circ}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \tan 54^{\circ}=\tan 36^{\circ}+2 \tan 18^{\circ}[/math]
(প্রমাণিত)[math]\\[/math]
 খএখানে, আপতন কোণ [math]=2 \alpha[/math]
 এবং প্রতিসরণ কোণ [math]2 \theta[/math]
শর্তমতে, [math]\frac{\sin 2 \alpha}{\sin 2 \theta}=\mathrm{k}[/math]
 [math]= \sin 2 \alpha=\mathrm{k} \sin 2 \theta[/math]
 [math]= \frac{\sin 2 \alpha-\sin 2 \theta}{\sin 2 \alpha+\sin 2 \theta}=\frac{k-1}{k+1}[/math]
 [বিয়োজন-যোজন করে][math]= \frac{2 \cos \left(\frac{2 \alpha+2 \theta}{2}\right) \sin \left(\frac{2 \alpha-2 \theta}{2}\right)}{2 \sin \left(\frac{2 \alpha+2 \theta}{2}\right) \cos \left(\frac{2 \alpha-2 \theta}{2}\right)}=\frac{\mathrm{k}-1}{\mathrm{k}+1}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}= \frac{\cos (\alpha+\theta) \sin (\alpha-\theta)}{\sin (\alpha+\theta) \cos (\alpha-\theta)}=\frac{k-1}{k+1}\\= \cot (\alpha+\theta) \tan (\alpha-\theta)=\frac{k-1}{k+1}\\=\frac{1}{\tan (\alpha+\theta)} \cdot \tan (\alpha-\theta)=\frac{\mathrm{k}-1}{\mathrm{k}+1}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \tan (\alpha-\theta)=\frac{k-1}{k+1} \tan (\alpha+\theta)[/math]
 (দেখানো হলো)[math]\\[/math]
 গএখানে, [math]\alpha=\frac{\theta}{3}=9^{\circ}[/math]
আবার শর্তমতে, [math]\mathrm{k}=\frac{\sin 2 \alpha}{\sin 2 \theta}=\frac{\sin \left(2 \times 9^{\circ}\right)}{\sin \left(2 \times 9^{\circ} \times 3\right)}=\frac{\sin 18^{\circ}}{\sin 54^{\circ}}[/math]
মনে করি, [math]x=18^{\circ} \therefore 5 x=90^{\circ}=\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
আবার, [math]2 x=5 x-3 x \therefore 2 x=\frac{\pi}{2}-3 x[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}= \sin (2 x)=\sin \left(\frac{\pi}{2}-3 x\right)\\= 2 \sin x \cdot \cos x=\cos 3 x\\= 2 \sin x \cdot \cos x=4 \cos ^{3} x-3 \cos x\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=2 \sin x=4 \cos ^{2} x-3[\cos x[/math]
 দ্বারা ভাগ করে, যেহেতু [math]\left.\cos 18^{\circ} 
eq 0\right][/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}= 2 \sin x=4-4 \sin ^{2} x-3\\= 4 \sin ^{2} x+2 \sin x-1=0\\\therefore \sin x=\frac{-2 \pm \sqrt{4+16}}{2.4}=\frac{-2 \pm 2 \sqrt{5}}{8}=\frac{ \pm \sqrt{5}-1}{4}\end{array}[/math]
যেহেতু [math]x=18^{\circ}[/math]
 একটি সূক্ষ্মকোণ : [math]\therefore \sin 18^{\circ}=\frac{\sqrt{5}-1}{4}[/math]
আবার, [math]\sin 54^{\circ}=\cos \left(90^{\circ}-54^{\circ}\right)=\cos 36^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\cos \left(2 \times 18^{\circ}\right)=1-2 \sin ^{2} 18^{\circ} \\=1-2\left(\frac{\sqrt{5}-1}{4}\right)^{2}=1-2 \frac{5-2 \sqrt{5}+1}{16} \\=\frac{8-5+2 \sqrt{5}-1}{8}=\frac{2+2 \sqrt{5}}{8}=\frac{\sqrt{5}+1}{4}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad k=\frac{\sin 18^{\circ}}{\sin 54^{\circ}}=\frac{\left(\frac{\sqrt{5}-1}{4}\right)}{\left(\frac{\sqrt{5}+1}{4}\right)}=\frac{\sqrt{5}-1}{\sqrt{5}+1}[/math]
(দেখানো হলো)

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক তিনগুণ ও দ্বিগুণ কোণের সূত্র ব্যবহার করে প্রমাণ করা যায়: ধরে নাও [math]t=\tan18^\circ[/math], তাহলে [math]\tan36^\circ=\frac{2t}{1-t^2}[/math] এবং [math]\tan54^\circ=\frac{3t-t^3}{1-3t^2}[/math]; এসবকে স্থানান্তর ও সরলীকরণ করলে সরাসরি পাওয়া যায় [math]\tan54^\circ=\tan36^\circ+2\tan18^\circ[/math]।

খ দেওয়ায় [math]k=\frac{\sin2\alpha}{\sin2\theta}[/math], ফলে [math]\frac{k-1}{k+1}=\frac{\sin2\alpha-\sin2\theta}{\sin2\alpha+\sin2\theta}=\frac{2\cos(\alpha+\theta)\sin(\alpha-\theta)}{2\sin(\alpha+\theta)\cos(\alpha-\theta)}=\frac{\tan(\alpha-\theta)}{\tan(\alpha+\theta)}[/math]; উভয় পাশে গুণ করলে প্রয়োজনীয় সম্পর্ক পাওয়া যায়।

গ যদি [math]\alpha=9^\circ,\ \theta=27^\circ[/math] হয়, তাহলে [math]k=\frac{\sin18^\circ}{\sin54^\circ}[/math] এবং জানা মান অনুযায়ী [math]\sin18^\circ=\frac{\sqrt5-1}{4},\ \sin54^\circ=\frac{\sqrt5+1}{4}[/math], ফলে [math]k=\frac{\sqrt5-1}{\sqrt5+1}[/math]।

Question #35 (ID: 473783)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{1}{\operatorname{cosec} \alpha}+\frac{1}{\operatorname{cosec} \beta}=\sqrt{5}\left(\frac{1}{\sec \beta}-\frac{1}{\sec \alpha}\right) \ldots \ldots(\mathrm i)[/math] [math]P+Q+R=n \pi \ldots \ldots \mathrm {(ii)}[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]\theta=\cot ^{-1} 3[/math] হলে, [math]\cos 2 \theta[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর ৷
খ. (i) নং উদ্দীপক ব্যবহার করে প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\alpha-\beta=2 \cos ^{-1} \sqrt{\frac{5}{6}}[/math]
গ. [math]n[/math]-এর মান [math]2[/math] হলে, প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\cos ^{2} P+\cos ^{2} \mathrm{Q}+\cos ^{2} R=2 \cos P \cos Q \cos R+1[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, [math]\theta=\cot ^{-1} 3[/math]
 [math]= \cot \theta=3[/math]
 [math]= \frac{1}{\tan \theta}=3 \therefore \tan \theta=\frac{1}{3}[/math]
প্রদত্ত রাশি [math]=\cos 2 \theta=\frac{1-\tan ^{2} \theta}{1+\tan ^{2} \theta}=\frac{1-\left(\frac{1}{3}\right)^{2}}{1+\left(\frac{1}{3}\right)^{2}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1-\frac{1}{9}}{1+\frac{1}{9}}=\frac{8}{10}=\frac{4}{5} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে,[math]\frac{1}{\operatorname{cosec} \alpha}+\frac{1}{\operatorname{cosec} \beta}=\sqrt{5}\left(\frac{1}{\sec \beta}-\frac{1}{\sec \alpha}\right)[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}= \sin \alpha+\sin \beta=\sqrt{5}(\cos \beta-\cos \alpha)\\= 2 \sin \frac{\alpha+\beta}{2} \cos \frac{\alpha-\beta}{2}=\sqrt{5} .2 \sin \frac{\alpha+\beta}{2} \sin \frac{\alpha-\beta}{2}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\text{বा, } \frac{\sin \frac{\alpha-\beta}{2}}{\cos \frac{\alpha-\beta}{2}}=\frac{1}{\sqrt{5}}\\= \tan \frac{\alpha-\beta}{2}=\frac{1}{\sqrt{5}}\\= \tan ^{2} \frac{\alpha-\beta}{2}=\frac{1}{5}\\= \sec ^{2} \frac{\alpha-\beta}{2}-1=\frac{1}{5}\\=\sec ^{2} \frac{\alpha-\beta}{2}=\frac{6}{5}\\= \frac{1}{\cos ^{2} \frac{\alpha-\beta}{2}}=\frac{6}{5}\\= \cos ^{2} \frac{\alpha-\beta}{2}=\frac{5}{6}\\= \cos \frac{\alpha-\beta}{2}=\sqrt{\frac{5}{6}}\\= \frac{\alpha-\beta}{2}=\cos ^{-1} \sqrt{\frac{5}{6}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \alpha-\beta=2 \cos ^{-1} \sqrt{\frac{5}{6}}[/math]
(প্রমাণিত)[math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]P+Q+R=n \pi[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{P}+\mathrm{Q}+\mathrm{R}=2 \pi \quad[\because \mathrm{n}=2][/math]
বামপক্ষ [math]=\cos ^{2} \mathrm{P}+\cos ^{2} \mathrm{Q}+\cos ^{2} \mathrm{R}=\frac{1}{2}\left(2 \cos ^{2} \mathrm{P}+2 \cos ^{2} \mathrm{Q}\right)+\cos ^{2} \mathrm{R}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\frac{1}{2}(1+\cos 2 \mathrm{P}+1+\cos 2 \mathrm{Q})+\cos ^{2} \mathrm{R} \\=1+\frac{1}{2}(\cos 2 \mathrm{P}+\cos 2 \mathrm{Q})+\cos ^{2} \mathrm{R} \\=1+\frac{1}{2} \cdot 2 \cos \frac{2 \mathrm{P}+2 \mathrm{Q}}{2} \cos \frac{2 \mathrm{P}-2 \mathrm{Q}}{2}+\cos ^{2} \mathrm{R} \\=1+\cos (\mathrm{P}+\mathrm{Q}) \cos (\mathrm{P}-\mathrm{Q})+\cos ^{2} \mathrm{R} \\=1+\cos (2 \pi-\mathrm{R}) \cos (\mathrm{P}-\mathrm{Q})+\cos ^{2} \mathrm{R} \\=1+\cos R \cos (\mathrm{P}-\mathrm{Q})+\cos ^{2} \mathrm{R} \\=1+\cos R\{\cos (\mathrm{P}-\mathrm{Q})+\cos \mathrm{R}\} \\=1+\cos R\{\cos (\mathrm{P}-\mathrm{Q})+\cos (2 \pi-\mathrm{P}-\mathrm{Q})\} \\=1+\cos R\{\cos (\mathrm{P}-\mathrm{Q})+\cos (\mathrm{P}+\mathrm{Q})\} \\=1+\cos R \cdot 2 \cos \mathrm{P} \cos \mathrm{Q}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=2 \cos P \cos Q \cos R+1=[/math]
 ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore \cos ^{2} \mathrm{P}+\cos ^{2} \mathrm{Q}+\cos ^{2} \mathrm{R}=2 \cos \mathrm{P} \cos \mathrm{Q} \cos \mathrm{R}+1[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত)

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক [math]\theta=\cot^{-1}3\Rightarrow \tan\theta=\tfrac{1}{3}[/math], তাই [math]\cos2\theta=\frac{1-\tan^2\theta}{1+\tan^2\theta}=\frac{1-\tfrac{1}{9}}{1+\tfrac{1}{9}}=\frac{8}{10}=\frac{4}{5}[/math]।

খ শুরুতে (i) থেকে [math]\sin\alpha+\sin\beta=\sqrt5(\cos\alpha-\cos\beta)[/math] এবং sum-to-product দিবার মাধ্যমে পাই [math]2\sin\frac{\alpha+\beta}{2}\cos\frac{\alpha-\beta}{2}=-2\sqrt5\sin\frac{\alpha+\beta}{2}\sin\frac{\alpha-\beta}{2}[/math]; [math]\sin\frac{\alpha+\beta}{2}\neq0[/math] ধরে বিয়োগ করলে [math]\cos D=-\sqrt5\sin D[/math] যেখানে [math]D=\frac{\alpha-\beta}{2}[/math], ফলে [math]\sin^2D=\tfrac{1}{6},\ \cos^2D=\tfrac{5}{6}[/math] এবং উপযুক্ত চিহ্ন নিয়ে [math]\alpha-\beta=2\cos^{-1}\sqrt{\tfrac{5}{6}}[/math] লাভ হয়।

গ [math]n=2\Rightarrow P+Q+R=2\pi[/math] হলে [math]\cos R=\cos(P+Q)[/math]; তাই [math]\cos^2P+\cos^2Q+\cos^2R=\cos^2P+\cos^2Q+(\cos P\cos Q-\sin P\sin Q)^2=1+2\cos P\cos Q\cos R[/math], যা প্রদর্শন করে কাঙ্ক্ষিত সমীকরণ।

Question #36 (ID: 473779)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2017 | Boards: Dinajpur Board | Tags: Dinajpur Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]f(x)=\sin x[/math] এবং [math]g(x)=\cos x[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]\cos \theta=\frac{3}{\sqrt{13}}[/math] হলে [math]\sqrt[1]{\frac{2-\cot ^{2} \theta}{2+\cot ^{2} \theta}}[/math] -এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
খ. [math]f(x)+f(y)=p[/math] এবং [math]g(x)+g(y)=q[/math] হলে প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]f\left(\frac{x-y}{2}\right)=\pm \frac{1}{2} \sqrt{4-p^{2}-q^{2}}[/math]
গ. [math]-\frac{\pi}{2} \leq x \leq \pi[/math] ব্যবধিতে [math]f(2 x)[/math] এর লেখচিত্র অঙ্কন করে এর একটি বৈশিষ্ট্য লিখ ।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কএখানে, [math]\cos \theta=\frac{3}{\sqrt{13}}[/math]
][math]\Rightarrow \cos ^{2} \theta=\left(\frac{3}{\sqrt{13}}\right)^{2} \text {. }[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos ^{2} \theta=\frac{9}{13}[/math]
এখন [math]\sin ^{2} \theta=1-\cos ^{2} \theta=1-\frac{9}{13}=\frac{13-9}{13}=\frac{4}{13} \text {. }[/math]
 [math]\cot ^{2} \theta=\frac{\cos ^{2} \theta}{\sin ^{2} \theta}=\frac{\frac{9}{13}}{\frac{4}{13}}=\frac{9}{4}[/math]
প্রদত্ত রাশি [math]=\sqrt{\frac{2-\cot ^{2} \theta}{2+\cot ^{2} \theta}}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \sqrt{\frac{2-\frac{9}{4}}{2+\frac{9}{4}}}=\sqrt{\frac{\frac{8-9}{4}}{\frac{8+9}{4}}} \\\Rightarrow \sqrt{\frac{-\frac{1}{4}}{\frac{17}{4}}}=\sqrt{-\frac{1}{17}} .\end{array}[/math]
 খএখানে, [math]f(x)=\sin x[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\begin{array}{ll}\therefore \quad & f(y)=\sin y \\& f\left(\frac{x-y}{2}\right)=\sin \left(\frac{x-y}{2}\right) \\& g(x)=\cos x \\\therefore \quad & g(y)=\cos y \\& f(x)+f(y)=\mathrm{p}\end{array}\\\Rightarrow \sin x+\sin y=p\\\Rightarrow 2 \sin \frac{x+y}{2} \cos \frac{x-y}{2}=p\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 4 \sin ^{2} \frac{x+y}{2} \cos ^{2} \frac{x-y}{2}=p^{2} \text {........}[/math]
(i)[math]\begin{array}{l}g(x)+g(y)=q\\\Rightarrow \cos x+\cos y=q\\\Rightarrow 2 \cos \frac{x+y}{2} \cos \frac{x-y}{2}=q\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 4 \cos ^{2} \frac{x+y}{2} \cos ^{2} \frac{x-y}{2}=q^{2}......[/math]
(ii)(i) নং এবং (ii) নং যোগ করে পাই,[math]4 \cos ^{2} \frac{x-y}{2}\left(\sin ^{2} \frac{x+y}{2}+\cos ^{2} \frac{x+y}{2}\right)=p^{2}+q^{2}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 4\left(1-\sin ^{2} \frac{x-y}{2}\right) \cdot 1=p^{2}+q^{2}\\\Rightarrow 4-4 \sin ^{2} \frac{x-y}{2}=p^{2}+q^{2}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 4 \sin ^{2} \frac{x-y}{2}=4-p^{2}-q^{2}\\\Rightarrow \sin ^{2} \frac{x-y}{2}=\frac{1}{4}\left(4-p^{2}-q^{2}\right)\\\Rightarrow \sin \frac{x-y}{2}= \pm \sqrt{\frac{1}{4}\left(4-p^{2}-q^{2}\right)}\\\Rightarrow \sin \frac{x-y}{2}= \pm \frac{1}{2} \sqrt{4-p^{2}-q^{2}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad f\left(\frac{x-y}{2}\right)= \pm \frac{1}{2} \sqrt{4-p^{2}-q^{2}}[/math]
(প্রমাণিত)গএখানে [math]f(x)=\sin x[/math]
 [math]\therefore f(2 x)=\sin 2 x[/math]
ধরি, [math]y=f(2 x)=\sin 2 x[/math]
 [math]-\frac{\pi}{2} \leq x \leq \pi[/math]
 ব্যবধিতে x এর বিভিন্ন মানের জন্য y এর সংশ্লিষ্ট মান নির্ণয় করি ।
[Image]
ছক কাগজের x-অক্ষ বরাবর ক্ষুদ্রতম 1 বর্গের বাহুর দৈর্ঘ্য [math]=\frac{\pi}{18}[/math]
 একক এবং y-অক্ষ বরাবর ক্ষুদ্রতম 10 বর্গের বাহুর দৈর্ঘ্য [math]= 1[/math]
 একক ধরে প্রাপ্ত বিন্দুগুলি স্থাপন করে ক্রমান্বয়ে যোগ করে লেখচিত্র অঙ্কন করি ।
[Image]
লেখচিত্র হতে দেখা যায়, লেখচিত্রটি মূলবিন্দুগামী

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক এখানে [math]\cos^2\theta=\frac{9}{13},\ \sin^2\theta=\frac{4}{13}[/math] থেকে [math]\cot^2\theta=\frac{\cos^2\theta}{\sin^2\theta}=\frac{9}{4}[/math]. অতএব [math]\frac{2-\cot^2\theta}{2+\cot^2\theta}=\frac{2-\tfrac{9}{4}}{2+\tfrac{9}{4}}=-\frac{1}{17}[/math], এবং মূলটি হবে [math]\sqrt{-\tfrac{1}{17}}=\pm\frac{i}{\sqrt{17}}[/math] (ইমাজিনারি)।

খ sum-to-product ব্যবহার করলে [math]\sin x+\sin y=2\sin\frac{x+y}{2}\cos\frac{x-y}{2}=p[/math] এবং [math]\cos x+\cos y=2\cos\frac{x+y}{2}\cos\frac{x-y}{2}=q[/math]. বর্গ করে যোগ করলে [math]p^2+q^2=4\cos^2\frac{x-y}{2}[/math], ফলে [math]\sin^2\frac{x-y}{2}=1-\frac{p^2+q^2}{4}=\frac{4-p^2-q^2}{4}[/math] এবং [math]\sin\frac{x-y}{2}=\pm\frac{1}{2}\sqrt{4-p^2-q^2}[/math].

গ [math]f(2x)=\sin2x[/math] এর লেখচিত্র [math]-\frac{\pi}{2}\le x\le\pi[/math] এ অঙ্কন করলে দেখা যাবে অ্যাম্পলিটিউড 1 এবং পর্যায় (period) [math]\pi[/math] (অর্থাৎ [math]\sin x[/math] এর অর্ধেক), শূন্যবিন্দুসমূহ [math]x=n\frac{\pi}{2}[/math] যেখানে উপযুক্ত n নিয়ে উপস্থিত হবে — এইটিই একটি প্রধান বৈশিষ্ট্য।

Question #37 (ID: 473780)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\mathrm {\varphi(x)=\cos x}[/math]

Options:
ক. কোনো ত্রিভুজের বাহুগুলির দৈর্ঘ্য [math]\text {3a, 5a}[/math] ও [math]\text {7a}[/math] একক হলে ত্রিভুজটির বৃহত্তম কোণ নির্ণয় কর।
খ. [math]\mathrm {\varphi(2 x) \varphi(4 x) \varphi(8 x) \varphi(14 x)}[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর, যখন [math]\mathrm {x=\dfrac{\pi}{15}}[/math]
গ. [math]\mathrm{p} \varphi(\mathrm{x})+\mathrm{q} \varphi(\mathrm{y})=\mathrm{r}=\mathrm{p} \varphi\left(\dfrac{\pi}{2}-\mathrm{x}\right)+\mathrm{q} \varphi\left(\dfrac{\pi}{2}-\mathrm{y}\right)[/math] হলে দেখাও যে, [math]\mathrm {\varphi\left(\dfrac{x-y}{2}\right)= \pm \sqrt{\dfrac{2 r^{2}-(p-q)^{2}}{4 p q}}}[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]\\[/math]
বৃহত্তম কোণ [math]\mathrm {A}[/math]
 হলে,[math]\mathrm {\cos A=\dfrac{(3 a)^{2}+(5 a)^{2}-(7 a)^{2}}{2.3 a \cdot 5 a}}[/math]
 [ [math]\because[/math]
 বৃহত্তম বাহুর বিপরীত কোণ বৃহত্তম হয়][math]\begin{array}{c}\quad=\dfrac{9 \mathrm{a}^{2}+25 \mathrm{a}^{2}-49 \mathrm{a}^{2}}{30 \mathrm{a}^{2}}=\dfrac{-15 \mathrm{a}^{2}}{30 \mathrm{a}^{2}}=-\dfrac{1}{2} \\\therefore \cos \mathrm{A}=-\dfrac{1}{2}=\cos 120^{\circ} \quad \therefore \mathrm{A}=120^{\circ}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 নির্ণেয় বৃহত্তম কোণ [math]120^° \textbf{(Ans.)}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খ [math]\\[/math]
দেওয়া আছে, [math]\mathrm {\varphi(x)=\cos x}[/math]
প্রদত্ত রাশি [math]\mathrm {=\varphi(2 x) \varphi(4 x) \varphi(8 x) \varphi(14 x)}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\mathrm {=\cos 2 x \cdot \cos 4 x \cdot \cos 8 x \cdot \cos 14 x }\\\mathrm {=\dfrac{1}{2 \sin 2 x}(2 \sin 2 x \cdot \cos 2 x) \cdot \cos 4 x \cdot \cos 8 x \cdot \cos 14 x }\\\mathrm {=\dfrac{1}{2 \sin 2 x} \cdot \sin 4 x \cdot \cos 4 x \cdot \cos 8 x \cdot \cos 14 x }\\\mathrm {=\dfrac{1}{2 \cdot 2 \sin 2 x}(2 \sin 4 x \cdot \cos 4 x) \cos 8 x \cdot \cos 14 x }\\\mathrm {=\dfrac{1}{2 \times 4 \sin 2 x}(2 \sin 8 x \cdot \cos 8 x) \cos 14 x }\\\mathrm {=\dfrac{1}{8 \sin 2 x} \sin 16 x \cdot \cos 14 x }\\\mathrm {=\dfrac{1}{16 \sin 2 x}(2 \sin 16 x \cdot \cos 14 x)}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\mathrm {=\dfrac{1}{16 \sin 2 x}(\sin 30 x+\sin 2 x) }\\\mathrm {=\dfrac{1}{16 \sin 2 x}(\sin 2 \times 15 x+\sin 2 x) }\\\mathrm {=\dfrac{1}{16 \sin 2 x}(\sin 2 \pi+\sin 2 x)\left[\therefore x=\dfrac{\pi}{15}\right]} \\\mathrm {=\dfrac{1}{16 \sin 2 x}(0+\sin 2 x)=\dfrac{1}{16} }\textbf { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 গ [math]\\[/math]
দেওয়া আছে, [math]\mathrm {\varphi(x)=\cos x \cdot \varphi\left(\dfrac{x-y}{2}\right)=\cos \left(\dfrac{x-y}{2}\right)}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{p} \varphi(\mathrm{x})+\mathrm{q} \varphi(\mathrm{y})=\mathrm{r} \Rightarrow \mathrm{p} \cos \mathrm{x}+\mathrm{q} \cos \mathrm{y}=\mathrm{r}[/math]
এবং [math]\mathrm {p \varphi\left(\dfrac{\pi}{2}-x\right)+q \varphi\left(\dfrac{\pi}{2}-y\right)=r}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm {p \sin x+q \sin y=r}[/math]
দেওয়া আছে, [math]\mathrm {p \sin x+q \sin y=r}[/math]
 [math]\mathrm {\therefore \mathrm{p}^{2} \sin ^{2} x+\mathrm{q}^{2} \sin ^{2} y+2 \mathrm{pq} \sin x \sin y=\mathrm{r}^{2} \ldots \ldots \ldots \text { (i) }}[/math]
এবং [math]\mathrm {p \cos x+q \cos y=r}[/math]
 [math]\mathrm {\therefore \mathrm{p}^{2} \cos ^{2} x+q^{2} \cos ^{2} y+2 p q \cos x \cos y=r^{2} \ldots \ldots \ldots \text { (ii) }}[/math]
 [math]\text {(i)}[/math]
 এবং [math]\text {(ii)}[/math]
 যোগ করে,[math]\begin{array}{l} \mathrm{p^{2}+q^{2}+2 p q(\cos x \cos y+\sin x \sin y)=2 r^{2}}\\\Rightarrow \mathrm{p}^{2}+\mathrm{q}^{2}+2 \mathrm{pq} \cos (\mathrm{x}-\mathrm{y})=2 \mathrm{r}^{2}\\\Rightarrow \mathrm{ \cos (x-y)=\dfrac{2 r^{2}-p^{2}-q^{2}}{2 p q}} \end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \mathrm{2 \cos ^{2} \dfrac{x-y}{2}-1=\dfrac{2 r^{2}-p^{2}-q^{2}}{2 p q}}\\\Rightarrow \mathrm{2 \cos ^{2} \dfrac{x-y}{2}=\dfrac{2 r^{2}-p^{2}-q^{2}+2 p q}{2 p q}}\\\Rightarrow \mathrm{2 \cos ^{2} \dfrac{x-y}{2}=\dfrac{2 r^{2}-(p-q)^{2}}{2 p q}}\\\Rightarrow \mathrm{\cos ^{2} \dfrac{x-y}{2}=\dfrac{2 r^{2}-(p-q)^{2}}{4 p q}}\\\Rightarrow \mathrm{\cos \dfrac{x-y}{2}= \pm \sqrt{\dfrac{2 r^{2}-(p-q)^{2}}{4 p q}}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \varphi\left(\dfrac{\mathrm{x}-\mathrm{y}}{2}\right)= \pm \sqrt{\dfrac{2 \mathrm{r}^{2}-(\mathrm{p}-\mathrm{q})^{2}}{4 \mathrm{pq}}}[/math]
 (দেখানো হলো)

Explanation:
ক বৃহত্তম বাহু [math]7a[/math]-র বিপরীত কোণ হবে বৃহত্তম; কোসাইন নিয়ম প্রয়োগ করলে [math]\cos\theta=\dfrac{(3a)^2+(5a)^2-(7a)^2}{2\cdot3a\cdot5a}=\dfrac{9+25-49}{30}=-\tfrac{1}{2}[/math], তাই [math]\theta=120^\circ[/math]।

খ দেখা যায় [math]\cos(14x)=\cos(15x-x)=\cos\pi\cos x=-\cos x[/math], সুতরಂಜ [math]\cos2x\cos4x\cos8x\cos14x=-\cos x\cos2x\cos4x\cos8x[/math]; এবং [math]\sin(16x)=16\sin x\cos x\cos2x\cos4x\cos8x[/math] থেকে [math]\cos2x\cos4x\cos8x\cos14x=-\dfrac{\sin(16x)}{16\sin x}[/math]; [math]x=\dfrac{\pi}{15}[/math] হলে [math]\sin(16x)=-\sin x[/math] হওয়ায় ফল [math]\dfrac{1}{16}[/math] হয়।

গ [math]\cos(\tfrac{\pi}{2}-t)=\sin t[/math] হওয়ায় শর্তগুলো থেকে [math]p\cos x+q\cos y=r=p\sin x+q\sin y[/math] পাওয়া যায়; এদের বর্গ যোগ করলে [math]p^2+q^2+2pq\cos(x-y)=2r^2[/math], তাই [math]\cos(x-y)=\dfrac{2r^2-p^2-q^2}{2pq}[/math]; এরপর [math]\cos\frac{x-y}{2}=\pm\sqrt{\dfrac{1+\cos(x-y)}{2}}=\pm\sqrt{\dfrac{2r^2-(p-q)^2}{4pq}}[/math]।

Question #38 (ID: 473778)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2017 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:

[Image]


[math]\triangle \mathrm{ABC}[/math] এর পরি ব্যাসার্ধ [math]R[/math].

Options:
ক. [math]A+B=105^{\circ}[/math] হলে [math]\sin C[/math] -নির্ণয় কর
খ. [math]\triangle A B C[/math] এর ক্ষেত্রে প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]a^{2}+b^{2}+c^{2}=8 R^{2}(1+\cos A \cos B \cos C)[/math]
গ. [math]\triangle \mathrm{PQS}[/math] ক্ষেত্রে [math]\frac{1}{P Q+P S}=\frac{3}{P S+P Q+Q S}-\frac{1}{P S+Q S}[/math] হলে [math]\angle Q[/math] নির্ণয় কর ৷


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক
[Image]
এখানে, [math]\triangle \mathrm{ABC}^{}[/math]
 এ [math]A+B=105^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}A+B+C=180^{\circ}\\\Rightarrow105^{\circ}+\mathrm{C}=180^{\circ}\\\Rightarrow \mathrm{C}=180^{\circ}-105^{\circ}=75^{\circ}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{aligned}\therefore \sin C & =\sin 75^{\circ}=\sin \left(45^{\circ}+30^{\circ}\right) \\& \Rightarrow \sin 45^{\circ} \cos 30^{\circ}+\cos 45^{\circ} \sin 30^{\circ} \\& \Rightarrow \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \cdot \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}+\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \cdot \frac{1}{2}=\frac{\sqrt{3}+1}{2 \sqrt{2}}=\frac{\sqrt{2}(\sqrt{3}+1)}{2 \sqrt{2} \cdot \sqrt{2}}=\frac{\sqrt{6}+\sqrt{2}}{4}\end{aligned}[/math]
নির্ণেয় [math]\sin C=\frac{\sqrt{6}+\sqrt{2}}{4}[/math]
 খ
[Image]
এখানে, [math]\triangle \mathrm{ABC}[/math]
 এর পরিব্যাসার্ধ [math]R[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}B C=a \text {, } \\\mathrm{AC}=\mathrm{b} \\\mathrm{AB}=\mathrm{c} \\\mathrm{A}+\mathrm{B}+\mathrm{C}=180^{\circ} \\\Rightarrow \mathrm{A}+\mathrm{B}=180^{\circ}-\mathrm{C} \\\therefore \quad \cos (A+B)=\cos \left(180^{\circ}-C\right)=-\cos C \\\frac{\mathrm{a}}{\sin \mathrm{A}}=\frac{\mathrm{b}}{\sin \mathrm{B}}=\frac{\mathrm{c}}{\sin \mathrm{C}}=2 \mathrm{R} \\\therefore \quad a=2 R \sin A \\b=2 R \sin B \\c=2 R \sin C \\\end{array}[/math]
বামপক্ষ [math]=a^{2}+b^{2}+c^{2}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow (2 R \sin A)^{2}+(2 R \sin B)^{2}+(2 R \sin C)^{2} \\\Rightarrow 4 R^{2} \sin ^{2} A+4 R^{2} \sin ^{2} B+4 R^{2} \sin ^{2} C^{-} \\\Rightarrow 4 R^{2}\left(\sin ^{2} A+\sin ^{2} B+\sin ^{2} C\right)\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 4 R^{2}\left\{\frac{1}{2}\left(2 \sin ^{2} A+2 \sin ^{2} B\right)+\sin ^{2} C\right\} \\\Rightarrow 4 R^{2}\left\{\frac{1}{2}(1-\cos 2 A+1-\cos 2 B)+\sin ^{2} C\right\} \\\Rightarrow 4 R^{2}\left\{\frac{1}{2}(2-\cos 2 A-\cos 2 B)+\sin ^{2} C\right\} \\\Rightarrow 4 R^{2}\left\{1-\frac{1}{2}(\cos 2 A+\cos 2 B)+\sin ^{2} C\right\} \\\Rightarrow 4 R^{2}\left\{1-\frac{1}{2} \cdot 2 \cos (A+B) \cos (A-B)+1- \cos ^{2} C\right\}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 4 R^{2}\left\{2+\cos C \cos (A-B)-\cos ^{2} C\right\} \\\Rightarrow 4 R^{2}[2+\cos C\{\cos (A-B)-\cos C\}] \\\Rightarrow 4 R^{2}[2+\cos C\{\cos (A-B)+\cos (A+B)\}] \\\Rightarrow 4 R^{2}(2+2 \cos A \cos B \cos C) \\\Rightarrow 4 R^{2} \cdot 2(1+\cos A \cos B \cos C)\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow8 R^{2}\left(1+\cos A \cos B^{2} \cos C\right)=[/math]
 ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore \mathrm{a}^{2}+\mathrm{b}^{2}+\mathrm{c}^{2}=8 \mathrm{R}^{2}(1+\cos \mathrm{A} \cos \mathrm{B} \cos \mathrm{C}) .[/math]
(প্রমাণিত)গ
[Image]
এখানে, [math]\triangle \mathrm{PQS}[/math]
 এ,[math]\begin{array}{l}Q S=p \\P S=q\end{array}[/math]
এবং [math]P Q=s[/math]
 [math]\frac{1}{P Q+P S}=\frac{3}{P S+P Q+Q S}-\frac{1}{P S+Q S}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{1}{s+q}=\frac{3}{q+s+p}-\frac{1}{q+p}\\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{s+q}=\frac{3 q+3 p-q-s-p}{(q+s+p)(q+p)}\\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{s+q}=\frac{2 p+2 q-s}{q^{2}+p q+q s+p s+p q+p^{2}}\\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{s+q}=\frac{2 p+2 q-s}{p^{2}+q^{2}+2 p q+p s+q s}\\\Rightarrow \mathrm{p}^{2}+q^{2}+2 p q+p s+q s=2 p s+2 q s-s^{2}+2 p q+2 q^{2}-q s\\\Rightarrow p^{2}+q^{2}+2 p q+p s+q s-2 p s-2 q s+s^{2}-2 p q-2 q^{2}-q s=0\\\Rightarrow \mathrm{p}^{2}-\mathrm{q}^{2}+\mathrm{s}^{2}-\mathrm{ps}=0\\\Rightarrow \mathrm{p}^{2}+\mathrm{s}^{2}-\mathrm{q}^{2}=\mathrm{ps}\\\Rightarrow \frac{p^{2}+s^{2}-q^{2}}{2 p s}=\frac{p s}{2 p s}\\\Rightarrow \cos Q=\frac{1}{2}\\\Rightarrow \cos Q=\cos 60^{\circ}\\\therefore O=60^{\circ}\end{array}[/math]
নির্ণেয় [math]\angle Q=60^{\circ} .[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক [math]A+B=105^{\circ}\Rightarrow C=180^{\circ}-105^{\circ}=75^{\circ}[/math], তাই [math]\sin C=\sin75^{\circ}=\sin(45^{\circ}+30^{\circ})=[/math] [math]\frac{\sqrt6+\sqrt2}{4}[/math].

খ πλευা‑কণার সম্পর্ক ব্যবহার করে [math]a=2R\sin A,\;b=2R\sin B,\;c=2R\sin C[/math], ফলে LHS = [math]4R^{2}(\sin^{2}A+\sin^{2}B+\sin^{2}C)[/math]. পরিচিত ত্রিকোণমিতিক পরিচয় থেকে [math]\sin^{2}A+\sin^{2}B+\sin^{2}C=2(1+\cos A\cos B\cos C)[/math] হওয়ায় ফল পায় [math]a^{2}+b^{2}+c^{2}=8R^{2}(1+\cos A\cos B\cos C)[/math]।

গ ধরা যাক [math]PQ=k\sin S,\ PS=k\sin Q,\ QS=k\sin P[/math]। শর্তে বসালে সরলীকরণে পাওয়া যায় [math]\sin^{2}Q=\sin^{2}S+\sin^{2}P-\sin S\sin P[/math]; আইন‑কসাইন ব্যবহার করলে [math]\cos Q=\dfrac{\sin^{2}S+\sin^{2}P-\sin^{2}Q}{2\sin S\sin P}=\tfrac12[/math], সুতরাং [math]\angle Q=60^{\circ}[/math]।

Question:
দৃশ্যকল্প-১ :


[Image]


দৃশ্যকল্প-২ : [math]f(x)=\frac{1}{2} \sin \frac{x}{2}[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]\cos 74^{\circ} 33^{\prime} \cos 14^{\circ} 33^{\prime}+\cos 75^{\circ} 27^{\prime} \cos 15^{\circ} .27^{\prime}[/math] এর মান বের কর?
খ. উদ্দীপক-১ এ যদি [math]\cos X=\sin Y-\cos Y[/math] হয়, তাহলে প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\angle \mathrm{X}+\angle \mathrm{Y}=\angle \mathrm{Z}[/math]
গ. দৃশ্যকল্প-২ অনুসারে [math]f(2 \pi-4 \theta)[/math] এর লেখচিত্র অঙ্কন কর। যেখানে, [math]-2 \pi \leq \theta \leq 2 \pi[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কপ্রদত্ত রাশি, [math]=\cos 74^{\circ} 33^{\prime} \cos 14^{\circ} 33^{\prime}+\cos 75^{\circ} 27^{\prime} \cos 15^{\circ} 27^{\prime}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \cos 74^{\circ} 33^{\prime} \cos 14^{\circ} 33^{\prime}+\cos \left(90^{\circ}-14^{\circ} 33^{\prime}\right) \cos \left(90^{\circ}-74^{\circ} 33^{\prime}\right) \\\Rightarrow \cos 74^{\circ} 33^{\prime} \cos 14^{\circ} 33^{\prime}+\sin 14^{\circ} 33^{\prime} \sin 74^{\circ} 33^{\prime} \\\Rightarrow \cos 74^{\circ} 33^{\prime} \cos 14^{\circ} 33^{\prime}+\sin 74^{\circ} 33^{\prime} \sin 14^{\circ} 33^{\prime} \\\Rightarrow \cos \left(74^{\circ} 33^{\prime}-14^{\circ} 33^{\prime}\right)=\cos 60^{\circ}=\frac{1}{2}\end{array}[/math]
নির্ণেয় মান [math]\frac{1}{2} .[/math]
 খএখানে [math]\text { XYZ }[/math]
 ত্রিভুজে[math]\begin{array}{l}Y=15^{\circ} \\X+Y+Z=180^{\circ}\\\Rightarrow X+15^{\circ}+Z=180^{\circ}\\\Rightarrow \mathrm{X}+\mathrm{Z}=180^{\circ}-15^{\circ}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow X+Z=165^{\circ}........[/math]
(i)[math]\begin{array}{l}\cos X=\sin Y-\cos Z \\\Rightarrow \cos X+\cos Z=\sin 15^{\circ} \\\Rightarrow 2 \cos \frac{X+Z}{2} \cos \frac{X-Z}{2}=2 \sin \frac{15^{\circ}}{2} \cos \frac{15^{\circ}}{2} \\\Rightarrow \cos \left(90^{\circ}-\frac{15^{\circ}}{2}\right) \cos \frac{X-Z}{2}=2 \sin \frac{15^{\circ}}{2} \cos \frac{15^{\circ}}{2} \\\Rightarrow \sin \frac{15^{\circ}}{2} \cos \frac{X-Z}{2}=\sin \frac{15^{\circ}}{2} \cos \frac{15^{\circ}}{2} \text {. } \\\Rightarrow \cos \frac{X-Z}{2}=\cos \frac{15^{\circ}}{2} \\\Rightarrow \frac{X-Z}{2}=\frac{15^{\circ}}{2}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow X-Z=15^{\circ} \text {}.....[/math]
(ii)(i) নং ও (ii) নং যোগ করে পাই,[math]\begin{array}{l}2 Z=180^{\circ} \\Z=\frac{180^{\circ}}{2}=90^{\circ}\end{array}[/math]
(i) নং এ Z-এর মান বসিয়ে পাই,[math]\begin{array}{l}90^{\circ}+Z=165^{\circ}\\\Rightarrow X=165-90^{\circ}\\\Rightarrow \mathrm{X}=75^{\circ}\end{array}[/math]
এখন, [math]X+Y=75^{\circ}+15^{\circ}=90=Z[/math]
 [math]\therefore \angle \mathrm{X}+\angle \mathrm{Y}=\angle \mathrm{Z}[/math]
(প্রমাণিত)গএখানে, [math]f(x)=\frac{1}{2} \sin \frac{x}{2}[/math]
 [math]\begin{aligned}\therefore \quad f(2 \pi-4 \theta) & =\frac{1}{2} \sin \left(\frac{2 \pi-4 \theta}{2}\right) \\& \Rightarrow \frac{1}{2} \sin (\pi-2 \theta)=\frac{1}{2} \sin 2 \theta\end{aligned}[/math]
ধরি, [math]y=f(2 \pi-4 \theta)=\frac{1}{2} \sin 2 \theta[/math]
 [math]-2 \pi \leq \theta \leq 2 \pi[/math]
 ব্যবধিতে [math]\theta[/math]
 এর বিভিন্ন মানের জন্য [math]y[/math]
 এর সংশ্লিষ্ট মান নির্ণয় করি ।
[Image]
ছক কাগজের X-অক্ষ বরাবর ক্ষুদ্রতম 1 বর্গের বাহুর দৈর্ঘ্য [math]=\frac{\pi}{18}[/math]
 একক এবং Y-অক্ষ বরাবর ক্ষুদ্রতম [math]20[/math]
 বর্গের বাহুর দৈর্ঘ্য [math]= 1[/math]
 একক ধরে প্রাপ্ত বিন্দুগুলি স্থাপন করে ক্রমান্বয়ে যোগ করে লেখচিত্র অঙ্কন করি ।
[Image]

Question #40 (ID: 473776)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2017 | Boards: Chittagong Board | Tags: Chattogram Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
দৃশ্যকল্প : [math]\mathrm{ABC}[/math] ত্রিভুজের পরিসীমা [math]2s[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{\cos 75^{\circ}+\cos 15^{\circ}}{\cos 75^{\circ}-\cos 15^{\circ}}[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর'।
খ. [math]\sec B=\sec C \sec A[/math] হলে দেখাও যে, [math]\tan \mathrm{A}=2 \cot C[/math]
গ. দৃশ্যকল্পের আলোকে [math]4 s(s-b)=3 c a[/math] হলে [math]\angle B[/math] এর মান কত?


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কপ্রদত্ত রাশি [math]=\frac{\cos 75^{\circ}+\cos 15^{\circ}}{\cos 75^{\circ}-\cos 15^{\circ}}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{\cos 75^{\circ}+\cos 15^{\circ}}{-\left(\cos 15^{\circ}-\cos 75^{\circ}\right)} \\\Rightarrow \frac{2 \cos 45^{\circ} \cos 30^{\circ}}{-2 \sin 45^{\circ} \sin 30^{\circ}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{2 \cdot \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \cdot \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}}{-2 \cdot \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \cdot \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}}=\frac{\sqrt{2}}{-\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}}=-\sqrt{3}\end{array}[/math]
নির্ণেয় মান [math]-\sqrt{3}[/math]
 খএখানে, [math]\sec B=\sec \cdot \operatorname{Cec} A[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{1}{\cos B}=\frac{1}{\cos C} \cdot \frac{1}{\cos A}\\\Rightarrow \cos B=\cos C \cos A\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\mathrm{ABC}[/math]
 ত্রিভুজে[math]\begin{array}{l}\mathrm{A}+\mathrm{B}+\mathrm{C}=180^{\circ}\\\Rightarrow \mathrm{A}+\mathrm{C}=180^{\circ}-\mathrm{B}\\\Rightarrow \cos (A+C)=\cos \left(180^{\circ}-B\right) \text{ :}\\\Rightarrow \cos A \cos C-\sin A \sin C=-\cos B\\\Rightarrow \cos A \cos C-\sin A \sin C=-\cos C \cos \dot{A}\\\because \quad[\because \cos B=\cos C \cos A]\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{\cos A \cos C-\sin A \sin C}{\cos A \cos C}=-1 \\\Rightarrow 1-\tan A \tan C=-1 \\\Rightarrow \tan A \tan C=1+1 \\\Rightarrow \tan A \cdot \frac{1}{\cot C}=2\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad \tan A=2 \cot C \text {. }[/math]
(দেখানো হলো)গএখানে, [math]ABC[/math]
 ত্রিভুজের পরিসীমা [math]2 s[/math]
অর্থাৎ [math]2 s=a+b+c[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}4 s(s-b)=3 \mathrm{ca} \\\Rightarrow 4 \cdot \frac{\mathrm{a}+\mathrm{b}+\mathrm{c}}{2} \cdot\left(\frac{a+b+c}{2}-b\right)=3 \mathrm{ca} \\\Rightarrow 2(a+b+c)\left(\frac{a+b+c-2 b}{2}\right)=3 \mathrm{ca} \\\Rightarrow (a+b+c)(a-b+c)=3 \mathrm{ca} \\\Rightarrow a^{2}-a b+c a+a b-b^{2}+b c+c a-b c+c^{2}=3 \mathrm{ca} \\\Rightarrow a^{2}+\mathrm{c}^{2}-\mathrm{b}^{2}=3 \mathrm{ca}-2 \mathrm{ca} \\\Rightarrow a^{2}+\mathrm{c}^{2}-\mathrm{b}^{2}=c a \\\Rightarrow \frac{a^{2}+c^{2}-b^{2}}{2 c a}=\frac{c a}{2 c a} \\\Rightarrow \cos \mathrm{B}=\frac{1}{2}=\cos 60^{\circ}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow B=60^{\circ}[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক [math]\cos75^\circ=\sin15^\circ[/math] হওয়ায়
[math]\frac{\cos75^\circ+\cos15^\circ}{\cos75^\circ-\cos15^\circ}=\frac{\sin15^\circ+\cos15^\circ}{\sin15^\circ-\cos15^\circ}=\frac{\tan15^\circ+1}{\tan15^\circ-1}[/math].
[math]\tan15^\circ=2-\sqrt3[/math] ব্যবহার করলে অনুপাতের মান [math]-\sqrt3[/math].

খ শর্ত থেকে [math]\sec B=\sec C\sec A\Rightarrow\frac{1}{\cos B}=\frac{1}{\cos C\cos A}\Rightarrow\cos A\cos C=\cos B[/math]।
কিন্তু [math]\cos B=-\cos(A+C)=-\cos A\cos C+\sin A\sin C[/math], তাই
[math]2\cos A\cos C=\sin A\sin C[/math] দেওয়ায় [math]2=\tan A\tan C[/math] এবং ফলে [math]\tan A=2\cot C[/math]।

গ [math]s=\frac{a+b+c}{2},\ s-b=\frac{a+c-b}{2}[/math] হওয়ায়
[math]4s(s-b)=(a+b+c)(a+c-b)=(a+c)^2-b^2[/math]।
শর্ত অনুযায়ী [math](a+c)^2-b^2=3ac\Rightarrow a^2+c^2-ac=b^2[/math] এবং কোসমেট্রিক সূত্র [math]b^2=a^2+c^2-2ac\cos B[/math] এর সাথে তুলনা করলে [math]\cos B=\tfrac{1}{2}[/math], সুতরাং [math]\angle B=60^\circ[/math]।

Question #41 (ID: 473771)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2018 | Boards: Dhaka Board | Tags: Dhaka Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
দৃশ্যকল্প-১ :


[Image]


দৃশ্যকল্প-২ : [math]p=\tan \theta \tan 2 \theta \tan \alpha[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]\sin 25^{\circ}+\cos 25^{\circ}[/math] মান কত?
খ. দৃশ্যকল্প-১ : হতে b এবং c এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
গ. দৃশ্যকল্প-২ : হতে দেখাও যে, [math]p=\sqrt{3}[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কপ্রদত্ত রাশি [math]=\sin 25^{\circ}+\cos 25^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \sin \left(90^{\circ}-65^{\circ}\right)+\cos 25^{\circ} \\\Rightarrow \cos 65^{\circ}+\cos 25^{\circ} \\\Rightarrow 2 \cos \frac{65^{\circ}+25^{\circ}}{2} \cos \frac{65^{\circ}-25^{\circ}}{2} \\\Rightarrow 2 \cos 45^{\circ} \cos 20^{\circ} \\\Rightarrow 2 \cdot \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \cdot \cos 20^{\circ}=\sqrt{2} \cos 20^{\circ}\end{array}[/math]
 খএখানে,[math]A=\theta ; B=2 \theta ; C=120^{\circ} ; A B=c ; A C=b ; B C=2[/math]
 [math]\mathrm{ABC}[/math]
 ত্রিভুজে [math]A+B+C=180^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \theta+2 \theta+120^{\circ}=180^{\circ}\\\Rightarrow 3 \theta=180^{\circ}-120^{\circ}\\\Rightarrow 3 \theta=60^{\circ}\\\Rightarrow \theta=\frac{60^{\circ}}{3}=20^{\circ}\\\therefore \quad \mathrm{A}=20^{\circ}\\\mathrm{B}=2.20^{\circ}=40^{\circ}\end{array}[/math]
আবার [math]A B C[/math]
 ত্রিভুজে [math]\frac{B C}{\sin A}=\frac{A C}{\sin B}=\frac{A B}{\sin C}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{2}{\sin 20^{\circ}}=\frac{\mathrm{b}}{\sin 40^{\circ}}=\frac{\mathrm{c}}{\sin 120^{\circ}} \\\therefore \frac{2}{\sin 20^{\circ}}=\frac{\mathrm{b}}{\sin 40^{\circ}} \\\Rightarrow \mathrm{b}=\frac{2 \sin 40^{\circ}}{\sin 20^{\circ}} \\\Rightarrow \mathrm{b}=\frac{2 \cdot 2 \sin 20^{\circ} \cos 20^{\circ}}{\sin 20^{\circ}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos 20^{\circ}=4 \times 0.939692=3.76[/math]
 (প্রায়)এবং [math]\frac{2}{\sin 20^{\circ}}=\frac{c}{\sin 120^{\circ}}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm{c}=\frac{2 \sin 120^{\circ}}{\sin 20^{\circ}}=\frac{2 \times \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}}{0.34202}=5.06[/math]
 (প্রায়)নির্ণেয় মান : [math]b = 3.76[/math]
 (প্রায়) এবং [math]c = 5.06[/math]
 (প্রায়)।গএখানে, [math]\theta=20^{\circ}[/math]
 [ক-হতে][math]\theta+\alpha+80^{\circ}=180^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 20^{\circ}+\alpha+80^{\circ}=180^{\circ}\\\Rightarrow \alpha+100^{\circ}=180^{\circ}\\\Rightarrow \alpha=180^{\circ}-100^{\circ}\\\Rightarrow \alpha=80^{\circ}\end{array}[/math]
এখন [math]p=\tan \theta \tan 2 \theta \tan \alpha[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \tan 20^{\circ} \tan \left(2.20^{\circ}\right) \cdot \tan 80^{\circ} \\\Rightarrow \tan 20^{\circ} \tan 40^{\circ} \cdot \tan 80^{\circ} \\\Rightarrow \tan 20^{\circ} \tan \left(60^{\circ}-20^{\circ}\right) \tan \left(60^{\circ}+20^{\circ}\right) \\\Rightarrow \tan 20^{\circ} \frac{\tan 60^{\circ}-\tan 20^{\circ}}{1+\tan 60^{\circ} \tan 20^{\circ}} \cdot \frac{\tan 60^{\circ}+\tan 20^{\circ}}{1-\tan 60^{\circ} \tan 20^{\circ}} \\\Rightarrow \tan 20^{\circ} \frac{\sqrt{3}-\tan 20^{\circ}}{1+\sqrt{3} \tan 20^{\circ}} \cdot \frac{\sqrt{3}+\tan 20^{\circ}}{1-\sqrt{3} \tan 20^{\circ}} \\\Rightarrow \tan 20^{\circ} \frac{3-\tan ^{2} 20^{\circ}}{1-3 \tan ^{2} 20^{\circ}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{3 \tan 20^{\circ}-\tan ^{3} 20^{\circ}}{1-3 \tan ^{2} 20^{\circ}} \\\Rightarrow \tan \left(3.20^{\circ}\right) \\\Rightarrow \tan 60^{\circ}=\sqrt{3}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad \mathbf{p}=\sqrt{3} .[/math]
(দেখানো হল)

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক কারণ [math]\sin x+\cos x=\sqrt{2}\sin(x+45^\circ)[/math], তাই [math]\sin25^\circ+\cos25^\circ=\sqrt{2}\sin70^\circ=\sqrt{2}\cos20^\circ[/math]।

খ (চিত্র অনুযায়ী) যদি [math]a[/math] হাইপোটেনিউস এবং কোণটি [math]25^\circ[/math] হয়, তাহলে পার্শ্বগুলো ট্রিগনোমেট্রিক অনুপাত থেকে পাওয়া যায়: [math]b=a\cos25^\circ,\quad c=a\sin25^\circ[/math]।

গ যদি [math]\theta=30^\circ[/math] এবং [math]\alpha=60^\circ[/math] (অতএব [math]2\theta=60^\circ[/math]) হয়, তাহলে [math]p=\tan30^\circ\cdot\tan60^\circ\cdot\tan60^\circ=(1/\sqrt{3})\cdot\sqrt{3}\cdot\sqrt{3}=\sqrt{3}[/math]।

Question #42 (ID: 473772)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2017 | Boards:  | Tags: Jessore Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
দৃশ্যকল্প-১ : [math]\Delta X Y Z[/math] এ [math]\cos X=\sin Y-\cos Z[/math]

দৃশ্যকল্প-২: [math]\sqrt{1+\mathrm{n}} \cdot \tan \frac{\alpha}{2}=\sqrt{1-\mathrm{n}} \cdot \tan \frac{\beta}{2}[/math]

Options:
ক. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]75^{\circ}=2+\sqrt{3}[/math]
খ. দৃশ্যকল্প-১ এর আলোকে দেখাও যে, ত্রিভুজটি সমকোণী।
গ. দৃশ্যকল্প-২ এর আলোকে দেখাও যে, [math]\cos \beta=\frac{\cos \alpha-n}{1-n \cos \alpha}[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কবামপক্ষ [math]=\tan 75^{\circ}=\tan \left(45^{\circ}+30^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{\tan 45^{\circ}+\tan 30^{\circ}}{1-\tan 45^{\circ}. \tan 30^{\circ}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{1+\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}}{1-1 \cdot \frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}}=\frac{\frac{\sqrt{3}+1}{\sqrt{3}}}{\frac{\sqrt{3}-1}{\sqrt{3}}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{\sqrt{3}+1}{\sqrt{3}-1}=\frac{(\sqrt{3}+1)(\sqrt{3}+1)}{(\sqrt{3}-1)(\sqrt{3}+1)} \\\Rightarrow \frac{3+2 \sqrt{3}+1}{3-1}=\frac{4+2 \sqrt{3}}{2}=\frac{2(2+\sqrt{3})}{2} \\\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=2+\sqrt{3}=[/math]
 ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore \quad \tan 75^{\circ}=2+\sqrt{3} .[/math]
(প্রমাণিত)খদেওয়া আছে, [math]\cos X=\sin Y-\cos Z[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \cos X+\cos Z=\sin Y\\\Rightarrow \cos \mathrm{X}+\cos \{\pi-(\mathrm{X}+\mathrm{Y})\}=\sin \mathrm{Y}[\because \mathrm{X}+\mathrm{Y}+\mathrm{Z}=\pi]\\\Rightarrow \cos X-\cos (X+Y)=\sin Y\\\Rightarrow 2 \sin \frac{2 X+Y}{2} \sin \frac{Y}{2}=2 \sin \frac{Y}{2} \cos \frac{Y}{2}\\\Rightarrow \sin \left(X+\frac{Y}{2}\right)=\cos \frac{Y}{2}=\sin \left(\frac{\pi}{2}-\frac{Y}{2}\right)\\\therefore \quad \mathrm{X}+\frac{\mathrm{Y}}{2}=\frac{\pi}{2}-\frac{\mathrm{Y}}{2}\\\Rightarrow \mathrm{X}+\mathrm{Y}=\frac{\pi}{2}\\\therefore \quad Z=\frac{\pi}{2}\end{array}[/math]
অর্থাৎ [math]\Delta X Y Z[/math]
 সমকোণী ।(দেখানো হলো)গএখানে, [math]\sqrt{1+n} \cdot \tan \frac{\alpha}{2}=\sqrt{1-n} \cdot \tan \frac{\beta}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \tan \frac{\beta}{2}=\frac{\sqrt{1+\mathrm{n}}}{\sqrt{1-\mathrm{n}}} \tan \frac{\alpha}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \tan ^{2} \frac{\beta}{2}=\frac{1+n}{1-n^{2}} \tan ^{2} \frac{\alpha}{2}[/math]
 [ বর্গ করে ][math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{\sin ^{2} \frac{\beta}{2}}{\cos ^{2} \frac{\beta}{2}}=\frac{(1+n) \sin ^{2} \frac{\alpha}{2}}{(1-n) \cos ^{2} \frac{\alpha}{2}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{\sin ^{2} \frac{\beta}{2}+\cos ^{2} \frac{\beta}{2}}{\sin ^{2} \frac{\beta}{2}-\cos ^{2} \frac{\beta}{2}}=\frac{(1+n) \sin ^{2} \frac{\alpha}{2}+(1-n) \cos ^{2} \frac{\alpha}{2}}{(1+n) \sin ^{2} \frac{\alpha}{2}-(1-n) \cos ^{2} \frac{\alpha}{2}}\end{array}[/math]
[যোজন-বিয়োজন করে][math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{1}{-\left(\cos ^{2} \frac{\beta}{2}-\sin ^{2} \frac{\beta}{2}\right)}=\frac{\sin ^{2} \frac{\alpha}{2}+\cos ^{2} \frac{\alpha}{2}-n\left(\cos ^{2} \frac{\alpha}{2}-\sin ^{2} \frac{\alpha}{2}\right)}{n\left(\sin ^{2} \frac{\alpha}{2}+\cos ^{2} \frac{\alpha}{2}\right)-\left(\cos ^{2} \frac{\alpha}{2}-\sin ^{2} \frac{\alpha}{2}\right)}\\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{-\cos \beta}=\frac{1-n \cdot \cos \alpha}{n \cdot 1-\cos \alpha}\\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{-\cos \beta}=\frac{1-n \cos \alpha}{-(\cos \alpha-n)} \text{.}\\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{\cos \beta}=\frac{1-n \cos \alpha}{(\cos \alpha-n)}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad \cos \beta=\frac{\cos \alpha-n}{1-n \cos \alpha}[/math]
(দেখানো হল)

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক প্রমাণ: [math]\tan75^\circ=\tan(45^\circ+30^\circ)=\frac{\tan45^\circ+\tan30^\circ}{1-\tan45^\circ\tan30^\circ}=\frac{1+\tfrac{1}{\sqrt{3}}}{1-\tfrac{1}{\sqrt{3}}}=\frac{\sqrt{3}+1}{\sqrt{3}-1}=\frac{(\sqrt{3}+1)^2}{3-1}=\frac{4+2\sqrt{3}}{2}=2+\sqrt{3}.[/math]

খ দৃশ্যকল্প-১: [math]a=90^\circ-X,\; c=90^\circ-Z[/math] ধরে ছেদকরণগুলোতে [math]Y=a+c[/math], সমস্যাটির শর্তে [math]\sin a=\sin(a+c)-\sin c[/math] হয় যা সরল করলে [math]\sin a(1-\cos c)=\sin c(1-\cos a)[/math] পাওয়া যায়; দুই পাশে থাকা গুণকগুলোকে [math]1-\cos\theta=2\sin^2(\theta/2)[/math] দিয়ে দেখা যায় সমীকরণটি সদৃশ হতে গেলে এক দিকের [math]\sin[/math]–টিই শূন্য হতে হবে, অর্থাৎ [math]a=0[/math] বা [math]c=0[/math], তাই [math]X=90^\circ[/math] বা [math]Z=90^\circ[/math] — ত্রিভুজটি সমকোণী।

গ দৃশ্যকল্প-২: দেওয়া [math]\sqrt{1+n}\tan\frac{\alpha}{2}=\sqrt{1-n}\tan\frac{\beta}{2}[/math] বর্গ করলে [math](1+n)\tan^2\frac{\alpha}{2}=(1-n)\tan^2\frac{\beta}{2}[/math] এবং [math]\tan^2\frac{\theta}{2}=\frac{1-\cos\theta}{1+\cos\theta}[/math] ব্যবহার করলে নিচু ধাপে ক্রস-মাল্টিপলাই করে সরল করলে পাওয়া যায় [math]\cos\beta=\frac{\cos\alpha-n}{1-n\cos\alpha}.[/math]

Question #43 (ID: 473773)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2017 | Boards:  | Tags: Jessore Board

Question:
[math]\angle \mathrm{E}+\angle \mathrm{F}=65^{\circ}, \angle \mathrm{F}-\angle \mathrm{E}=25^{\circ}[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]\tan \beta=\frac{1}{3}[/math] হলে [math]\sin 2 \beta[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
খ. দেখাও যে, [math]2 \sin \left(\pi+\frac{F}{4}\right)=-\sqrt{2-\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2}}}[/math]
গ. দেখাও যে, [math]\angle E \cdot \tan 2 \angle E \cdot \tan 3 \angle E \cdot \tan 4 \angle E=3 .[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কএখানে, [math]\tan \beta=\frac{1}{3}[/math]
প্রদত্ত রাশি, [math]=\sin 2 \beta[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{2 \tan \beta}{1+\tan ^{2} \beta} \\\Rightarrow \frac{2 \cdot \frac{1}{3}}{1+\left(\frac{1}{3}\right)^{2}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{\frac{2}{3}}{1+\frac{1}{9}}=\frac{\frac{2}{3}}{9+1}=\frac{\frac{2}{3}}{\frac{10}{9}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{2}{3} \times \frac{9}{10}=\frac{3}{5}\end{array}[/math]
নির্ণেয় মান [math]\frac{3}{5}[/math]
 খএখানে, [math]\angle \mathrm{E}+\angle \mathrm{F}=65^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \angle E=65^{\circ}-\angle F\\\Rightarrow \angle \mathrm{F}-\angle \mathrm{E}=25^{\circ}\\\Rightarrow \angle \mathrm{F}-65^{\circ}+\angle \mathrm{F}=25^{\circ}\\\Rightarrow 2 \angle \mathrm{F}=25^{\circ}+65^{\circ}\\\Rightarrow 2 \angle \mathrm{F}=90^{\circ}\\\Rightarrow \angle \mathrm{F}=\frac{90^{\circ}}{2}=45^{\circ} \text{.}\end{array}[/math]
বামপক্ষ [math]=2 \sin \left(\pi+\frac{F}{4}\right)[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 2 \sin \left(\pi+\frac{45^{\circ}}{4}\right) \\\Rightarrow 2 \sin \left(\pi+\frac{4}{4}\right) \\\Rightarrow 2 \sin \left(\pi+\frac{\pi}{16}\right) \\\Rightarrow -2 \sin \frac{\pi}{16} \\\Rightarrow -\sqrt{4 \sin ^{2} \frac{\pi}{16}} \\\Rightarrow -\sqrt{2.2 \sin ^{2} \frac{\pi}{16}} \\\Rightarrow -\sqrt{2\left(1-\cos \frac{\pi}{8}\right)} \\\Rightarrow -1 \sqrt{2-2 \cos \frac{\pi}{8}} \\\Rightarrow -\sqrt{2-\sqrt{4 \cos ^{2} \frac{\pi}{8}}} \\\Rightarrow -\sqrt{2-\sqrt{2 \cdot 2 \cos ^{2} \frac{\pi}{8}}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow -\sqrt{2-\sqrt{2\left(1+\cos \frac{\pi}{4}\right)}} \\\Rightarrow -\sqrt{2-\sqrt{2\left(1+\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}\right)}} \\\Rightarrow -\sqrt{2-\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2}}}\end{array}[/math]
= ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore 2 \sin \left(\pi+\frac{F}{4}\right)=-\sqrt{2-\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2}}}[/math]
(দেখানো হল)গখ- হতে [math]\angle F=45^{\circ}[/math]
এখানে, [math]\angle \mathrm{E}+\angle \mathrm{F}=65^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \angle \mathrm{E}=65^{\circ}-45^{\circ}\\\Rightarrow \angle \mathrm{E}=20^{\circ}\end{array}[/math]
বামপক্ষ [math]=\tan \angle \mathrm{E} \cdot \tan 2 \angle \mathrm{E} \cdot \tan 3 \angle \mathrm{E} \cdot \tan 4 \angle \mathrm{E}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \tan 20^{\circ} \cdot \tan \left(2 \cdot 20^{\circ}\right) \cdot \tan \left(3 \cdot 20^{\circ}\right) \cdot \tan \left(4 \cdot 20^{\circ}\right) \\\Rightarrow \tan 20^{\circ} \cdot \tan 40^{\circ} \cdot \tan 60^{\circ} \cdot \tan 80^{\circ} \\\Rightarrow \tan 60^{\circ} \cdot \tan 20^{\circ} \cdot \tan \left(60^{\circ}-20^{\circ}\right) \cdot \tan \left(60^{\circ}+20^{\circ}\right) \\\Rightarrow \sqrt{3} \cdot \tan 20^{\circ} \cdot \frac{\tan 60^{\circ}-\tan 20^{\circ}}{1+\tan 60^{\circ} \cdot \tan 20^{\circ}} \cdot \frac{\tan 60^{\circ}-\tan 20^{\circ}}{1-\tan 60^{\circ} \cdot \tan 20^{\circ}} \\\Rightarrow \sqrt{3} \cdot \tan 20^{\circ} \cdot \frac{\sqrt{3}-\tan 20^{\circ}}{1+\sqrt{3} \cdot \tan 20^{\circ}} \cdot \frac{\sqrt{3}+\tan 20^{\circ}}{1-\sqrt{3} \cdot \tan 20^{\circ}} \\\Rightarrow \sqrt{3} \cdot \tan 20^{\circ} \cdot \frac{3-\tan ^{2} 20^{\circ}}{1-3 \tan ^{2} 20^{\circ}} \\\Rightarrow \sqrt{3} \cdot \frac{3 \tan 20^{\circ}-\tan ^{3} 20^{\circ}}{1-3 \tan ^{2} 20^{\circ}} \\\Rightarrow \sqrt{3} \cdot \tan \left(3 \cdot 20^{\circ}\right) \\\Rightarrow \sqrt{3} \cdot \tan 60^{\circ}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 3=[/math]
 ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore \tan \angle \mathrm{E} \cdot \tan 2 \angle \mathrm{E} \cdot \tan 3 \angle \mathrm{E} \cdot \tan 4 \angle \mathrm{E}=3[/math]
(দেখানো হল)

Explanation:
প্রথমে সমীকরণ দুটো যোগ করলে [math]2F=90^\circ[/math] ফলে [math]F=45^\circ[/math] এবং [math]E=20^\circ[/math] পাওয়া যায়।  

ক [math]\tan\beta=\tfrac{1}{3}[/math] হলে [math]\sin2\beta=\dfrac{2\tan\beta}{1+\tan^2\beta}=\dfrac{2\cdot(1/3)}{1+(1/9)}=\dfrac{3}{5}[/math].  

খ [math]2\sin\!\big(\pi+\tfrac{F}{4}\big)=-2\sin\tfrac{F}{4}=-2\sin 11.25^\circ[/math]; এবং [math]\sin 11.25^\circ=\sqrt{\dfrac{1-\cos22.5^\circ}{2}}=\dfrac{1}{2}\sqrt{2-\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2}}}[/math], সুতরাং মানটি [math]-\sqrt{2-\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2}}}[/math].  

গ [math]\tan3x=\tan x\cdot\tan(60^\circ-x)\cdot\tan(60^\circ+x)[/math](identity)। [math]x=20^\circ[/math] রাখলে [math]\tan60^\circ=\sqrt{3}=\tan20^\circ\cdot\tan40^\circ\cdot\tan80^\circ[/math], তা হলে [math]\tan20^\circ\cdot\tan40^\circ\cdot\tan60^\circ\cdot\tan80^\circ=\sqrt{3}\cdot\sqrt{3}=3[/math].

Question #44 (ID: 473774)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2017 | Boards:  | Tags: Cumilla Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]A=\frac{2 \pi}{15}, \alpha+\beta+\gamma=\pi[/math] এবং [math]\cos \alpha=\cos \beta \cos \gamma[/math]

Options:
ক. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\cos 2 p=\frac{1-\tan ^{2} p}{1+\tan ^{2} p}[/math]
খ. উদ্দীপকের আলোকে, প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]16 \cos A \cos 2 A \cos 4 A \cos 7 A=1[/math]
গ. উদ্দীপক থেকে দেখাও যে, [math]\tan \alpha=\tan \beta+\tan \gamma[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কবামপক্ষ [math]=\cos 2 p[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \cos ^{2} p-\sin ^{2} p \\\Rightarrow \cos ^{2} p\left(1-\frac{\sin ^{2} p}{\cos ^{2} p}\right) \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{\sec ^{2} p}\left(1-\tan ^{2} p\right) \\\Rightarrow \frac{1-\tan ^{2} p}{1+\tan ^{2} p}\end{array}[/math]
= ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore \quad \cos 2 p=\frac{1-\tan ^{2} p}{1+\tan ^{2} p}[/math]
(প্রমাণিত)খএখানে, [math]A^{}=\frac{2 \pi}{15}[/math]
বামপক্ষ [math]=16 \cos {A} \cos 2 \mathrm{~A} \cos 4 \mathrm{~A} \cos 7 \mathrm{~A}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 16 \cos \frac{2 \pi}{15} \cdot \cos \frac{2 \cdot 2 \pi}{15} \cdot \cos \frac{4 \cdot 2 \pi}{15} \cdot \cos \frac{7.2 \pi}{15} \\\Rightarrow 16 \cos \frac{2 \pi}{15} \cdot \cos \frac{4 \pi}{15} \cdot \cos \frac{8 \pi}{15} \cdot \cos \frac{14 \pi}{15} \\\Rightarrow \frac{8\left(2 \sin \frac{2 \pi}{15} \cos \frac{2 \pi}{15}\right) \cdot \cos \frac{4 \pi}{15} \cdot \cos \frac{8 \pi}{15} \cdot \cos \frac{14 \pi}{15}}{\sin \frac{2 \pi}{15}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{4 \cdot\left(2 \sin \frac{4 \pi}{15} \cos \frac{4 \pi}{15}\right) \cdot \cos \frac{8 \pi}{15} \cdot \cos \frac{14 \pi}{15}}{\sin \frac{2 \pi}{15}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{2 \cdot\left(2 \sin \frac{8 \pi}{15} \cos \frac{8 \pi}{15}\right) \cdot \cos \frac{14 \pi}{15}}{\sin \frac{2 \pi}{15}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{2 \sin \frac{16 \pi}{15} \cos \frac{14 \pi}{15}}{2 \sin \frac{\pi}{15} \cos \frac{\pi}{15}}=\frac{\sin \left(\pi+\frac{\pi}{15}\right) \cdot \cos \left(\pi-\frac{\pi}{15}\right)}{\sin \frac{\pi}{15} \cos \frac{\pi}{15}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{\left(-\sin \frac{\pi}{15}\right) \cdot\left(-\cos \frac{\pi}{15}\right)}{\sin \frac{\pi}{15} \cos \frac{\pi}{15}}=\frac{\sin \frac{\pi}{15} \cos \frac{\pi}{15}}{\sin \frac{\pi}{15} \cos \frac{\pi}{15}}\end{array}[/math]
= 1= ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore 16 \cos A \cos 2 A \cos 4 A \cos 7 A=1 .[/math]
(প্রমাণিত)গএখানে, [math]\alpha+\beta+\gamma=\pi[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \alpha=\pi-(\beta+\gamma)[/math]
এবং [math]\cos \alpha=\cos \beta \cos \gamma[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{\sin \alpha}{\cos \alpha}=\frac{\sin \{\pi-(\beta+\gamma)\}}{\cos \beta \cos \gamma} \\\Rightarrow \frac{\sin (\beta+\gamma)}{\cos \beta \cos \gamma} \\\Rightarrow \frac{\sin \beta \cos \gamma+\cos \beta \sin \gamma}{\cos \beta \cos \gamma} \\\Rightarrow \frac{\sin \beta \cos \gamma}{\cos \beta \cos \gamma}+\frac{\cos \beta \sin \gamma}{\cos \beta \cos \gamma} \\\Rightarrow \frac{\sin \beta}{\cos \beta}+\frac{\sin \gamma}{\cos \gamma} \\\Rightarrow \tan \beta+\tan \gamma\end{array}[/math]
= ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore \quad \tan \alpha=\tan \beta+\tan \gamma[/math]
 (দেখানো হল)

Explanation:
ক ব্যবহার করো [math]\cos 2p=\cos^2 p-\sin^2 p[/math], এবং উপরোক্ত প্রকাশকে [math]\cos^2 p[/math] দিয়ে ভাগ করলে পাওয়া যায় [math]\cos 2p=\frac{\cos^2 p-\sin^2 p}{\cos^2 p+\sin^2 p}=\frac{1-\tan^2 p}{1+\tan^2 p}[/math]।

খ গণিতীয় পরিচয় ব্যবহার করো: [math]\sin 16A=16\sin A\cos A\cos2A\cos4A\cos8A[/math]. A = [math]2\pi/15[/math] হলে [math]\sin16A=\sin A[/math], তাই [math]16\cos A\cos2A\cos4A\cos8A=1[/math]; এছাড়া [math]8A=2\pi-7A[/math] হওয়ায় [math]\cos8A=\cos7A[/math], ফলে [math]16\cos A\cos2A\cos4A\cos7A=1[/math]।

গ [math]\alpha=\pi-(\beta+\gamma)[/math] হওয়ায় [math]\tan\alpha=-\tan(\beta+\gamma)=-\frac{\tan\beta+\tan\gamma}{1-\tan\beta\tan\gamma}[/math]. দেওয়া [math]\cos\alpha=\cos\beta\cos\gamma[/math] ও [math]\cos\alpha=-\cos(\beta+\gamma)=-\cos\beta\cos\gamma+\sin\beta\sin\gamma[/math] যোগ করলে [math]2\cos\beta\cos\gamma=\sin\beta\sin\gamma[/math], অর্থাৎ [math]\tan\beta\tan\gamma=2[/math]; তা উপরে প্রতিস্থাপন করলে [math]\tan\alpha=\tan\beta+\tan\gamma[/math] পাওয়া যায়।

Question #45 (ID: 473775)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2017 | Boards:  | Tags: Cumilla Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
দৃশ্যকল্প-১ : [math]\sin x+\sin y=a[/math] এবং [math]\cos x+\cos y=b[/math] দুইটি ত্রিকোণমিতিক সমীকরণ।

দৃশ্যকল্প-২ : [math]\triangle \mathrm{ABC} \text { এর } \mathrm{A}+\mathrm{B}+\mathrm{C}=\pi[/math]

Options:
ক. যদি [math]\triangle \mathrm{PQR}[/math] এর তিনটি বাহুর দৈর্ঘ্য যথক্রমে [math]p, q, r[/math] এবং [math]\mathrm{p}^{2}+q^{2}-r^{2}=\sqrt{2} p q[/math] হয় তবে R কোণের মান নির্ণয় কর।
খ. দৃশ্যকল্প-১ : এর আলোকে [math]\cos (x+y)[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
গ. দৃশ্যকল্প ২: হতে প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\sin ^{2} A-\sin ^{2} B+\sin ^{2} C=2 \sin A \cos B \sin C[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক
[Image]
এখানে, [math]\triangle P Q R[/math]
 এর [math]QR, PR[/math]
 ও [math]PQ[/math]
 বাহুর দৈর্ঘ্য যথাক্রমে [math]p, q[/math]
 ও [math]r[/math]
 এবং [math]\mathrm{p}^{2}+\mathrm{q}^{2}-\mathrm{r}^{2}=\sqrt{2} \mathrm{pq}[/math]
এখন, [math]\triangle P Q R[/math]
 [math]\begin{aligned}\cos R & =\frac{p^{2}+q^{2}-r^{2}}{2 p q} \\& \Rightarrow\frac{\sqrt{2} p q}{2 p q}=\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}=\cos \frac{\pi}{4}\end{aligned}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm{R}=\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]
নির্ণেয় মানা [math]\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]
 খএখানে, [math]\sin x+\sin y=a[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \sin \frac{x+y}{2} \cos \frac{x-y}{2}=a......[/math]
(i)এবং [math]\cos x+\cos y=b[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \cos \frac{x+y}{2} \cos \frac{x-y}{2}=b.......[/math]
(ii)(ii) নং কে (i) নং দ্বারা ভাগ করে পাই,[math]\frac{\cos \frac{x+y}{2}}{\sin \frac{x+y}{2}}=\frac{b}{a}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{\cos ^{2} \frac{x+y}{2}}{\sin ^{2} \frac{x+y}{2}}=\frac{b^{2}}{a^{2}}[/math]
 [ বর্গ করে ][math]\Rightarrow \frac{\cos ^{2} \frac{x+y}{2}+\sin ^{2} \frac{x+y}{2}}{\cos ^{2} \frac{x+y}{2}-\sin ^{2} \frac{x+y}{2}}=\frac{b^{2}+a^{2}}{b^{2}-a^{2}}[/math]
 [যোজন-বিয়োজন করে ][math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{1}{\cos (x+y)}=\frac{b^{2}+a^{2}}{b^{2}-a^{2}} \\\therefore \quad \cos (x+y)=\frac{b^{2}-a^{2}}{b^{2}+a^{2}}\end{array}[/math]
নির্ণেয় মান [math]\frac{b^{2}-a^{2}}{b^{2}+a^{2}} .[/math]
 গএখানে [math]\triangle \mathrm{ABC}[/math]
 এ [math]\mathrm{A}+\mathrm{B}+\mathrm{C}=\pi[/math]
বামপক্ষ [math]=\sin ^{2} \mathrm{~A}-\sin ^{2} \mathrm{~B}+\sin ^{2} \mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\quad=(\sin A+\sin B)(\sin A-\sin B)+\sin ^{2} C \\\Rightarrow \left(2 \sin \frac{A+B}{2} \cos \frac{A-B}{2}\right) \cdot\left(2 \cos \frac{A+B}{2} \sin \frac{A-B}{2}\right)+\sin ^{2} C \\\Rightarrow \left(2 \sin \frac{A+B}{2} \cos \frac{A+B}{2}\right) \cdot\left(2 \sin \frac{A-B}{2} \cos \frac{A-B}{2}\right)+\sin ^{2} C \\\Rightarrow \sin (A+B) \sin (A-B)+\sin ^{2} C \\\Rightarrow \sin (\pi-C) \sin (A-B)+\sin ^{2} C[\because A+B+C=\pi] \\\Rightarrow \sin C \sin (A-B)+\sin ^{2} C \\\Rightarrow \sin C\{\sin (A-B)+\sin C\} \\\Rightarrow \sin C[\sin (A-B)+\sin \{\pi-(A+B)\}][\because A+B+C=\pi] \\\Rightarrow \sin C\{\sin (A-B)+\sin (A+B)\} \\\Rightarrow \sin C \cdot 2 \sin A \cos B\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=2 \sin A \cos B \sin C=[/math]
 ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore \sin ^{2} A-\sin ^{2} B+\sin ^{2} C=2 \sin A \cos B \sin[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত)

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক কোণের জন্য: কসাইন সূত্র অনুযায়ী [math]r^{2}=p^{2}+q^{2}-2pq\cos R[/math], তাই [math]p^{2}+q^{2}-r^{2}=2pq\cos R[/math]. প্রদত্ত [math]p^{2}+q^{2}-r^{2}=\sqrt{2}\,pq[/math] থেকে [math]\cos R=\frac{\sqrt{2}}{2}[/math], সুতরাং [math]R=\frac{\pi}{4}[/math]।

খ এর জন্য: যোগ-তফাক সূত্র প্রয়োগ করলে [math]\sin x+\sin y=2\sin\frac{x+y}{2}\cos\frac{x-y}{2}=a[/math] এবং [math]\cos x+\cos y=2\cos\frac{x+y}{2}\cos\frac{x-y}{2}=b[/math]. এই দুইটি থেকে [math]\sin\frac{x+y}{2}=\frac{a}{2\cos\frac{x-y}{2}},\ \cos\frac{x+y}{2}=\frac{b}{2\cos\frac{x-y}{2}}[/math] হওয়ায় [math]\cos(x+y)=\cos 2\cdot\frac{x+y}{2}=\frac{b^{2}-a^{2}}{a^{2}+b^{2}}[/math]।

গ জন্য: [math]C=\pi-A-B[/math] হলে [math]\sin C=\sin(A+B)[/math]. পরিচিত পরিচয় [math]\sin^{2}A-\sin^{2}B=\sin(A+B)\sin(A-B)[/math] ব্যবহার করলে বাম পাশে হলো [math]\sin(A+B)\sin(A-B)+\sin^{2}(A+B)=\sin(A+B)[\sin(A-B)+\sin(A+B)][/math]. তাই এটি সমান [math]\sin C\cdot 2\sin A\cos B=2\sin A\cos B\sin C[/math], যা প্রমাণ করে।

Question #46 (ID: 473765)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2019 | Boards: Chittagong Board | Tags: Chattogram Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:

[Image]


Options:
ক. প্রমাণ কর : [math]\sin 78^{\circ} 19^{\prime} \cos 18^{\circ} 19^{\prime} - \sin 11^{\circ} 41^{\prime} \sin 18^{\circ} 19^{\prime}=\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}[/math]
খ. [math]a=\sqrt{b^{2}+b c+c^{2}}[/math] হলে ত্রিভুজটির সূক্ষ্মকোণদ্বয়ের সমষ্টি নির্নয় কর?
গ. ত্রিভুজটির ক্ষেত্রে প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\frac{\mathrm{a}-\mathrm{b}}{\mathrm{c}} \operatorname{cosec} \frac{\mathrm{A}-\mathrm{B}}{2}=\sec \frac{\mathrm{C}}{2}[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কবামপক্ষ [math]=\sin 78^{\circ} 19^{\prime} \cos 18^{\circ} 19^{\prime}-\sin 11^{\circ} 41^{\prime} \sin 18^{\circ} 19^{\prime}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \sin 78^{\circ} 19^{\prime} \cos 18^{\circ} 19^{\prime}-\sin \left(90^{\circ}-78^{\circ} 19^{\prime}\right) \sin 18^{\circ} 19^{\prime} \\\Rightarrow \sin 78^{\circ} 19^{\prime} \cos 18^{\circ} 19^{\prime}-\cos 78^{\circ} 19^{\prime} \sin 18^{\circ} 19^{\prime}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin \left(78^{\circ} 19^{\prime}-18^{\circ} 19^{\prime}\right)=\sin 60^{\circ}=\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}=[/math]
 ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore \sin 78^{\circ} 19^{\prime} \cos 18^{\circ} 19^{\prime}-\sin 11^{\circ} 41^{\prime} \sin 18^{\circ} 19^{\prime}=\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত)খএখানে, [math]ABC[/math]
 ত্রিভুজের বাহুত্রয়, [math]B C=a=\sqrt{b^{2}+b c+c^{2}}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\mathrm{AB}=\mathrm{c} \\\mathrm{CA}=\mathrm{b}\end{array}[/math]
আমরা জানি, বৃহত্তম বাহুর বিপরীত কোণ বৃহত্তম হয় ।[math]\begin{aligned}\therefore \quad \cos A & =\frac{b^{2}+c^{2}-a^{2}}{2 b c} \\& \Rightarrow \frac{b^{2}+c^{2}-b^{2}-b c-c^{2}}{2 b c}=-\frac{b c}{2 b c}=-\frac{1}{2}=\cos 120^{\circ}\end{aligned}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad \mathrm{A}=120^{\circ}[/math]
সুতরাং, ত্রিভুজটি স্থূলকোণী ত্রিভুজ ।[math]\therefore[/math]
 ত্রিভুজটির সূক্ষ্মকোণদ্বয়ের সমষ্টি, [math]\angle \mathrm{B}+\angle \mathrm{C}=180^{\circ}-\angle \mathrm{A}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow180^{\circ}-120^{\circ}=60^{\circ}[/math]
নির্ণেয় ত্রিভুজটির সূক্ষ্মকোণদ্বয়ের সমষ্টি [math]60^{\circ} \text {. }[/math]
 গ [math]ABC[/math]
 ত্রিভুজের ক্ষেত্রে, বামপক্ষ [math]\angle A+\angle B+\angle C=180^{\circ}[/math]
বামপক্ষ [math]=\frac{\mathrm{a}-\mathrm{b}}{\mathrm{c}} \operatorname{cosec} \frac{\mathrm{A}-\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{2 R \sin A-2 R \sin B}{2 R \sin C} \times \frac{1}{\sin \frac{A-B}{2}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{\sin A-\sin B}{\sin C} \times \frac{1}{\sin \frac{A-B}{2}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{2 \cos \frac{A+B}{2} \sin \frac{A-B}{2}}{2 \sin \frac{C}{2} \cos \frac{C}{2}} \times \frac{1}{\sin \frac{A-B}{2}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{\cos \frac{180^{\circ}-C}{2}}{\sin \frac{C}{2}} \sec \frac{C}{2} .\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\frac{\sin \frac{C}{2}}{\sin \frac{C}{2}} \sec \frac{C}{2}=\sec \frac{C}{2}=[/math]
 ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore \frac{a-b}{c} \operatorname{cosec} \frac{A-B}{2}=\sec \frac{C}{2}[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত)

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক কারণ [math]\sin78^{\circ}19'=\cos11^{\circ}41'[/math], তাই প্রদত্ত পদটি হয় [math]\cos11^{\circ}41'\cos18^{\circ}19'-\sin11^{\circ}41'\sin18^{\circ}19'=\cos(11^{\circ}41'+18^{\circ}19')=\cos30^{\circ}=[\math]\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}[/math][/math].

খ কিউব করে কফি: কসাইন সূত্র অনুযায়ী [math]a^{2}=b^{2}+c^{2}-2bc\cos A[/math] এবং শর্ত অনুযায়ী [math]a^{2}=b^{2}+bc+c^{2}[/math], ফলে [math]-2bc\cos A=bc\Rightarrow \cos A=-\tfrac{1}{2}[/math] এবং [math]A=120^{\circ}[/math]; অতএব সূক্ষ্মকোণদ্বয়ের সমষ্টি [math]B+C=180^{\circ}-120^{\circ}=60^{\circ}[/math].

গ আধা-কোণ সূত্র ব্যবহার করে নিন [math]a=2R\sin A,\;b=2R\sin B,\;c=2R\sin C[/math], তাহলে [math]a-b=2R(\sin A-\sin B)=4R\cos\frac{A+B}{2}\sin\frac{A-B}{2}[/math]; কিন্তু [math]\cos\frac{A+B}{2}=\cos\frac{\pi-C}{2}=\sin\frac{C}{2}[/math], ফলে [math]a-b=4R\sin\frac{C}{2}\sin\frac{A-B}{2}[/math] এবং [math]\frac{a-b}{c}=\frac{4R\sin\frac{C}{2}\sin\frac{A-B}{2}}{2R\sin C}=\frac{\sin\frac{A-B}{2}}{\cos\frac{C}{2}}[/math]; অতএব [math]\frac{a-b}{c}\csc\frac{A-B}{2}=\sec\frac{C}{2}[/math].
