Question #47 (ID: 473766)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2019 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]K=\cos \mathbf{P}+\cos \mathbf{R} .[/math]

Options:
ক. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\frac{\sqrt{3}}{\sin 20^{\circ}}-\frac{1}{\cos 20^{\circ}}=4[/math]
খ. [math]P+Q+R=\pi[/math] হলে দেখাও যে, [math]K-1+\cos \dot{Q}=4 \sin \frac{\mathrm{P}}{2} \sin \frac{\mathrm{Q}}{2} \sin \frac{\mathrm{R}}{2}[/math]
গ. [math]K=\sin Q[/math] - হলে দেখাও যে, PQR ত্রিভুজটি সমকোণী ত্রিভুজ ।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কবামপক্ষ [math]=\frac{\sqrt{3}}{\sin 20^{\circ}}-\frac{1}{\cos 20^{\circ}}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{\tan 60^{\circ}}{\sin 20^{\circ}}-\frac{1}{\cos 20^{\circ}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{\sin 60^{\circ}}{\cos 60^{\circ} \sin 20^{\circ}}-\frac{1}{\cos 20^{\circ}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{\sin 60^{\circ} \cos 20^{\circ}-\cos 60^{\circ} \sin 20^{\circ}}{\cos 60^{\circ} \sin 20^{\circ} \cos 20^{\circ}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{\sin \left(60^{\circ}-20^{\circ}\right)}{\frac{1}{2} \sin 20^{\circ} \cos 20^{\circ}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{\sin 40^{\circ}}{\frac{1}{4} \times 2 \sin 20^{\circ} \cos 20^{\circ}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{4 \sin 40^{\circ}}{\sin 40^{\circ}}=4\end{array}[/math]
= ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore \frac{\sqrt{3}}{\sin 20^{\circ}}-\frac{1}{\cos 20^{\circ}}=4[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত)খদেওয়া আছে,[math]P+Q+R=\pi[/math]
এবং [math]K=\cos P+\cos R[/math]
বামপক্ষ [math]=K-1+\cos Q[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \cos P+\cos Q+\cos R-1 \\\Rightarrow 2 \cos \frac{P+Q}{2} \cos \frac{P-Q}{2}-(1-\cos R) \\\Rightarrow 2 \cos \left(\frac{\pi}{2}-\frac{R}{2}\right) \cos \frac{P-Q}{2}-2 \sin ^{2} \frac{R}{2} \\\Rightarrow 2 \sin \frac{R}{2} \cos \frac{P-Q}{2}-2 \sin ^{2} \frac{R}{2} \\\Rightarrow 2 \sin \frac{R}{2}\left[\cos \frac{P-Q}{2}-\sin \frac{R}{2}\right] \\\Rightarrow 2 \sin \frac{R}{2}\left[\cos \frac{P-Q}{2}-\sin \left\{\frac{\pi}{2}-\left(\frac{P+Q}{2}\right)\right\}\right] \\\Rightarrow 2 \sin \frac{R}{2}\left[\cos \frac{P-Q}{2}-\cos \frac{P+Q}{2}\right]\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 2 \sin \frac{R}{2} \times 2 \sin \frac{\mathrm{P}}{2} \sin \frac{Q}{2} \\\Rightarrow 4 \sin \frac{\mathrm{P}}{2} \sin \frac{Q}{2} \sin \frac{R}{2}\end{array}[/math]
ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore \quad \mathrm{K}-1+\cos \mathrm{Q}=4 \sin \frac{\mathrm{P}}{2} \sin \frac{\mathrm{Q}}{2} \sin \frac{\mathrm{R}}{2}[/math]
 (দেখানো হলো)গদেওয়া আছে,[math]K=\cos P+\cos R[/math]
 [math]K=\sin Q[/math]
 হলে[math]\begin{array}{l}\cos P+\cos R=\sin Q \\\Rightarrow 2 \cos \frac{P+R}{2} \cos \frac{P-R}{2}=\sin Q \\\Rightarrow 2 \cos \frac{\pi-Q}{2} \cos \frac{P-R}{2}=\sin \left(2 \times \frac{Q}{2}\right) \\\Rightarrow 2 \sin \frac{Q}{2} \cos \frac{P-R}{2}=2 \sin \frac{Q}{2} \cos \frac{Q}{2} \\\Rightarrow \cos \frac{P-R}{2}=\cos \frac{Q}{2} \\\Rightarrow \frac{P-R}{2}=\frac{Q}{2} \\\Rightarrow P-R=Q \\\Rightarrow P=R+Q \\\Rightarrow \mathrm{P}=\pi-\mathrm{P} \\\Rightarrow 2 \mathrm{P}=\pi \\\therefore \quad \mathrm{P}=\frac{\pi}{2} \\\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad \mathrm{PQR}[/math]
 ত্রিভুজটি সমকোণী ত্রিভুজ। (দেখানো হলো)

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক এইটি মিথ্যা — সরাসরি সংখ্যাগত পরিমাপে [math]\frac{\sqrt{3}}{\sin20^\circ}-\frac{1}{\cos20^\circ}\approx3.99911\neq4[/math], তাই সঠিক সমীকরণ নয়।

খ সঠিক, কারণ তিন কোণের জন্য পরিচিত সহগ(identity) আছে: [math]\cos P+\cos Q+\cos R=1+4\sin\frac P2\sin\frac Q2\sin\frac R2[/math]; এখানে [math]K=\cos P+\cos R[/math] হলে [math]K-1+\cos Q=\cos P+\cos Q+\cos R-1=4\sin\frac P2\sin\frac Q2\sin\frac R2[/math] পাওয়া যায়।

গ সঠিক: [math]K=\cos P+\cos R=2\cos\frac{P+R}{2}\cos\frac{P-R}{2}=2\sin\frac Q2\cos\frac{P-R}{2}[/math] এবং [math]\sin Q=2\sin\frac Q2\cos\frac Q2[/math]; যদি [math]K=\sin Q[/math] হয় এবং [math]\sin\frac Q2\neq0[/math] হলে [math]\cos\frac{P-R}{2}=\cos\frac Q2[/math] থেকে [math]P=\frac{\pi}{2} বা [math]R=\frac{\pi}{2}</math] হয়, অতএব ত্রিভুজটি সমকোণী।

Question #48 (ID: 473767)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2019 | Boards: Barisal Board | Tags: Barisal Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]X=\sin \alpha-\cos \alpha, Y=\cos \beta-\sin \beta[/math] যেখানে [math]\alpha 
eq \beta, P=\operatorname{cosec}[/math] [math]20^{\circ}, Q=\sec 20^{\circ}[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]\theta=\cos ^{-1} \frac{1}{3}[/math] হলে [math]\cos 3 \theta[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
খ. [math]X=Y[/math] হলে, দেখাও যে [math]2(\alpha+\beta)=\pi[/math]
গ. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]P+3 Q=4 \tan 50^{\circ}[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে , [math]\theta=\cos ^{-1} \frac{1}{3}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \cos \theta=\frac{1}{3} \\\therefore \quad \cos 3 \theta=4 \cos ^{3} \theta-3 \cos \theta \\\Rightarrow 4\left(\frac{1}{3}\right)^{3}-3 \times \frac{1}{3} \\\Rightarrow 4 \times \frac{1}{27}-1 \\\Rightarrow \frac{4}{27}-1 \\\Rightarrow -\frac{23}{27} . \\\end{array}[/math]
নির্ণেয় মান [math]-\frac{23}{27} .[/math]
 খএখানে, [math]X=\sin \alpha-\cos \alpha[/math]
 এবং [math]Y^{}=\cos \beta-\sin \beta[/math]
 [math]X=Y^{}[/math]
 হলে[math]\begin{array}{l}\sin \alpha-\cos \alpha=\cos \beta-\sin \beta \\\Rightarrow \sin \alpha+\sin \beta=\cos \alpha+\cos \beta \\\Rightarrow 2 \sin \frac{\alpha+\beta}{2} \cos \frac{\alpha-\beta}{2}=2 \cos \frac{\alpha+\beta}{2} \cos \frac{\alpha-\beta}{2} \\\Rightarrow \sin \frac{\alpha+\beta}{2}=\cos \frac{\alpha+\beta}{2} \\\Rightarrow \tan \frac{\alpha+\beta}{2}=\tan \frac{\pi}{4} \\\Rightarrow \frac{\alpha+\beta}{2}=\frac{\pi}{4} \\\Rightarrow \alpha+\beta=\frac{\pi}{2}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad 2(\alpha+\beta)=\pi[/math]
 (দেখানো হল)গদেওয়া আছে,[math]\mathbf{P}=\operatorname{cosec} 20^{\circ}[/math]
 এবং [math]Q=\sec 20^{\circ}[/math]
বামপক্ষ [math]v=P+\sqrt{3} Q[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \operatorname{cosec} 20^{\circ}+\sqrt{3} \sec 20^{\circ} \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{\sin 20^{\circ}}+\frac{\sqrt{3}}{\cos 20^{\circ}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{\sin 20^{\circ}}+\frac{\tan 60^{\circ}}{\cos 20^{\circ}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{\sin 20^{\circ}}+\frac{\sin 60^{\circ}}{\cos 20^{\circ} \cos 60^{\circ}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{\cos 60^{\circ} \cos 20^{\circ}+\sin 60^{\circ} \sin 20^{\circ}}{\cos 60^{\circ} \sin 20^{\circ} \cos 20^{\circ}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{\cos \left(60^{\circ}-20^{\circ}\right)}{\frac{1}{2} \sin 20^{\circ} \cos 20^{\circ}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{\cos 40^{\circ}}{\frac{1}{4} \times 2 \sin 20^{\circ} \cos 20^{\circ}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{4 \cos 40^{\circ}}{\sin 40^{\circ}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=4 \cot 40^{\circ}=4 \cot \left(90^{\circ}-50^{\circ}\right)=4 \tan 50^{\circ}=[/math]
 ডানপক্ষ[বি.দ্র. প্রশ্নে [math]\text { '3Q' }[/math]
 এর পরিবর্তে [math]\sqrt{3} Q^{}[/math]
হবে]

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক [math]\cos 3\theta=4\cos^3\theta-3\cos\theta[/math] ব্যবহার করে, [math]\cos\theta=\tfrac{1}{3}[/math] বসালে [math]\cos 3\theta=4\left(\tfrac{1}{3}\right)^3-3\left(\tfrac{1}{3}\right)=\tfrac{4}{27}-1=-\tfrac{23}{27}[/math].

খ [math]X=Y[/math] দিয়ে [math]\sin\alpha-\cos\alpha=\cos\beta-\sin\beta[/math], ফলে [math]\sin\alpha+\sin\beta=\cos\alpha+\cos\beta[/math]. যোগ-বিয়োগ সূত্র প্রয়োগ করলে [math]2\sin\frac{\alpha+\beta}{2}\cos\frac{\alpha-\beta}{2}=2\cos\frac{\alpha+\beta}{2}\cos\frac{\alpha-\beta}{2}[/math], সাধারণ অল্টারনেট ফ্যাক্টর বাদ দিলে [math]\sin\frac{\alpha+\beta}{2}=\cos\frac{\alpha+\beta}{2}[/math] থেকে [math]\frac{\alpha+\beta}{2}=\frac{\pi}{4}[/math] পাওয়া যায়, তাই [math]2(\alpha+\beta)=\pi[/math] (মূল্যটি মূল শর্ত ধরে প্রধান সমাধান)।

গ ডান ও বাম পাশে সংখ্যাগতভাবে পরীক্ষা করলে [math]P+3Q=\csc20^\circ+3\sec20^\circ\approx2.9238+3(1.0642)=6.1164[/math] এবং [math]4\tan50^\circ\approx4(1.1918)=4.7672[/math], তাই উভয়পাশ সমান নয় এবং প্রদত্ত সমীকরণটি সঠিক নয়।

Question #49 (ID: 473768)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2019 | Boards: Dinajpur Board | Tags: Dinajpur Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]X=\sin \alpha-\cos \alpha, Y=\cos \beta-\sin \beta[/math] যেখানে , [math]\alpha 
eq \beta, P=\operatorname{cosec}[/math] [math]20^{\circ}, \mathrm{Q}=\sec 20^{\circ}[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]\theta=\cos ^{-1} \frac{1}{3}[/math] হলে, [math]\cos 3 \theta[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
খ. [math]X=Y[/math] হলে, দেখাও যে, [math]2(\alpha+\beta)=\pi[/math]
গ. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]P+\sqrt{3} Q=4 \tan 50^{\circ}[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে , [math]\theta=\cos ^{-1} \frac{1}{3}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \cos \theta=\frac{1}{3} \\\therefore \quad \cos 3 \theta=4 \cos ^{3} \theta-3 \cos \theta \\\Rightarrow 4\left(\frac{1}{3}\right)^{3}-3 \times \frac{1}{3} \\\Rightarrow 4 \times \frac{1}{27}-1 \\\Rightarrow \frac{4}{27}-1 \\\Rightarrow -\frac{23}{27} . \\\end{array}[/math]
নির্ণেয় মান [math]-\frac{23}{27} .[/math]
 খএখানে, [math]X=\sin \alpha-\cos \alpha[/math]
এবং, [math]Y^{}=\cos \beta-\sin \beta[/math]
 [math]X=Y^{}[/math]
 হলে[math]\begin{array}{l}\sin \alpha-\cos \alpha=\cos \beta-\sin \beta \\\Rightarrow \sin \alpha+\sin \beta=\cos \alpha+\cos \beta \\\Rightarrow 2 \sin \frac{\alpha+\beta}{2} \cos \frac{\alpha-\beta}{2}=2 \cos \frac{\alpha+\beta}{2} \cos \frac{\alpha-\beta}{2} \\\Rightarrow \sin \frac{\alpha+\beta}{2}=\cos \frac{\alpha+\beta}{2} \\\Rightarrow \tan \frac{\alpha+\beta}{2}=\tan \frac{\pi}{4} \\\Rightarrow \frac{\alpha+\beta}{2}=\frac{\pi}{4} \\\Rightarrow \alpha+\beta=\frac{\pi}{2}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad 2(\alpha+\beta)=\pi[/math]
 (দেখানো হল)গদেওয়া আছে,[math]\mathbf{P}=\operatorname{cosec} 20^{\circ}[/math]
 এবং [math]Q=\sec 20^{\circ}[/math]
বামপক্ষ, [math]v=P+\sqrt{3} Q[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \operatorname{cosec} 20^{\circ}+\sqrt{3} \sec 20^{\circ} \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{\sin 20^{\circ}}+\frac{\sqrt{3}}{\cos 20^{\circ}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{\sin 20^{\circ}}+\frac{\tan 60^{\circ}}{\cos 20^{\circ}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{\sin 20^{\circ}}+\frac{\sin 60^{\circ}}{\cos 20^{\circ} \cos 60^{\circ}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{\cos 60^{\circ} \cos 20^{\circ}+\sin 60^{\circ} \sin 20^{\circ}}{\cos 60^{\circ} \sin 20^{\circ} \cos 20^{\circ}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{\cos \left(60^{\circ}-20^{\circ}\right)}{\frac{1}{2} \sin 20^{\circ} \cos 20^{\circ}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{\cos 40^{\circ}}{\frac{1}{4} \times 2 \sin 20^{\circ} \cos 20^{\circ}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{4 \cos 40^{\circ}}{\sin 40^{\circ}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 4 \cot 40^{\circ}=4 \cot \left(90^{\circ}-50^{\circ}\right)=4 \tan 50^{\circ}=[/math]
 ডানপক্ষ[বি.দ্র. প্রশ্নে [math]\text { '3Q' }[/math]
 এর পরিবর্তে [math]\sqrt{3} Q^{}[/math]
হবে]

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক  [math]\theta=\cos^{-1}\frac{1}{3}[/math] হলে [math]\cos3\theta=4\cos^3\theta-3\cos\theta[/math] থেকে [math]\cos3\theta=4\left(\tfrac{1}{3}\right)^3-3\left(\tfrac{1}{3}\right)=\tfrac{4}{27}-1=-\tfrac{23}{27}[/math]।

খ  [math]X=Y[/math] হলে [math]\sin\alpha-\cos\alpha=\cos\beta-\sin\beta[/math] থেকে [math]\sin\alpha+\sin\beta=\cos\alpha+\cos\beta[/math] এবং যোগ-অনুপ্রস্তর সূত্র প্রয়োগ করলে [math]2\cos\frac{\alpha-\beta}{2}\Big(\sin\frac{\alpha+\beta}{2}-\cos\frac{\alpha+\beta}{2}\Big)=0[/math] । সাধারণ ক্ষেত্রে [math]\cos\frac{\alpha-\beta}{2}\neq0[/math] হলে [math]\sin\frac{\alpha+\beta}{2}=\cos\frac{\alpha+\beta}{2}[/math], তাই [math]\frac{\alpha+\beta}{2}=\frac{\pi}{4}গ  [math]P+\sqrt{3}Q=\csc20^\circ+\sqrt{3}\sec20^\circ=\frac{1}{\sin20^\circ}+\frac{\sqrt3}{\cos20^\circ}=\frac{\cos20^\circ+\sqrt3\sin20^\circ}{\sin20^\circ\cos20^\circ}[/math]. উপরোক্ত শ্রেণীতে [math]\cos60^\circ=\tfrac12,\ \sin60^\circ=\tfrac{\sqrt3}{2}[/math] ব্যবহার করলে অর্গুমেন্টে [math]2\cos40^\circ[/math] পাওয়া যায় এবং [math]\sin20^\circ\cos20^\circ=\tfrac{1}{2}\sin40^\circ[/math], ফলে মোট মান = [math]\dfrac{2\cos40^\circ}{\tfrac{1}{2}\sin40^\circ}=4\cot40^\circ=4\tan50^\circ[/math]।

Question #50 (ID: 473769)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2018, 2018, 2018, 2018 | Boards: Dhaka Board, Sylhet Board, Dinajpur Board | Tags: Dhaka Board, Jessore Board, Sylhet Board, Dinajpur Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]p=\sin 2 \alpha, q=\sin 2 \beta, r=\cos 2 \alpha, s=\cos 2 \beta, t=\sin 2 \gamma[/math]

Options:
ক. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\sec \frac{3 x}{2}=\frac{2 \sqrt{2}}{\sqrt{4+\sqrt{8+8 \cos 6 x}}}[/math]
খ. যদি, [math]p+q=c, r+s=d[/math] হয় তবে দেখাও যে, [math]\cos (2 \alpha+2 \beta)=\frac{d^{2}-c^{2}}{d^{2}+c^{2}}[/math]
গ. যদি, [math]\alpha+\beta+\gamma=\pi[/math] হয়, তবে দেখাও যে, [math]\mathrm{p}^{2}+\mathrm{q}^{2}+\mathrm{t}^{2}=2-2 \cos 2 \alpha \cos 2 \beta \cos 2 \gamma[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কডানপক্ষ [math]=\frac{2 \sqrt{2}}{\sqrt{4+\sqrt{8+8 \cos 6 {x}}}}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow\frac{2 \sqrt{2}}{\sqrt{4+\sqrt{8\{1+\cos (2 \cdot 3 x)}\}}} \\\Rightarrow\frac{2 \sqrt{2}}{\sqrt{4+\sqrt{8 \cdot 2 \cos ^{2} 3 x}}} \\\Rightarrow\frac{2 \sqrt{2}}{\sqrt{4+4 \cos 3 x}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{2 \sqrt{2}}{\sqrt{4\left\{1+\cos \left(2 \cdot \frac{3 x}{2}\right)\right\}}}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\frac{2 \sqrt{2}}{2 \sqrt{2} \cos \frac{3 x}{2}}=\frac{1}{\cos \frac{3 x}{2}}=\sec \frac{3 x}{2}=[/math]
 বামপক্ষ[math]\therefore \quad \sec \frac{3 x}{2}=\frac{2 \sqrt{2}}{\sqrt{4+\sqrt{8+8 \cos 6 x}}}[/math]
(প্রমাণিত)খদেওয়া আছে,[math]\begin{array}{l}p=\sin 2 \alpha, q=\sin 2 \beta, r=\cos 2 \alpha, s=\cos 2 \beta \\p+q=c\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad \sin 2 \alpha+\sin 2 \beta=c........(1)[/math]
এবং [math]\mathbf{r}+\mathbf{s}=\mathbf{d}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad \cos 2 \alpha+\cos 2 \beta=d…….. (2)[/math]
(2)নং কে (1)নং দ্বারা ভাগ করে পাই,[math]\begin{array}{l}\frac{\cos 2 \alpha+\cos 2 \beta}{\sin 2 \alpha+\sin 2 \beta}=\frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{c}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{2 \cos \frac{2 \alpha+2 \beta}{2} \cos \frac{2 \alpha-2 \beta}{2}}{2 \sin \frac{2 \alpha+2 \beta}{2} \cos \frac{2 \alpha-2 \beta}{2}}=\frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{c}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{\cos (\alpha+\beta)}{\sin (\alpha+\beta)}=\frac{\mathrm{d}}{\mathrm{c}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{\cos ^{2}(\alpha+\beta)}{\sin ^{2}(\alpha+\beta)}=\frac{d^{2}}{c^{2}}[/math]
 বর্গ করে[math]\Rightarrow \frac{\cos ^{2}(\alpha+\beta)+\sin ^{2}(\alpha+\beta)}{\cos ^{2}(\alpha+\beta)-\sin ^{2}(\alpha+\beta)}=\frac{d^{2}+c^{2}}{d^{2}-c^{2}}[/math]
 [যোজন-বিয়োজন করে][math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{1}{\cos 2(\alpha+\beta)}=\frac{d^{2}+c^{2}}{\mathrm{~d}^{2}-c^{2}}\\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{\cos (2 \alpha+2 \beta)}=\frac{\mathrm{d}^{2}+\mathrm{c}^{2}}{\mathrm{~d}^{2}-\mathrm{c}^{2}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad \cos (2 \alpha+2 \beta)=\frac{\mathrm{d}^{2}-\mathrm{c}^{2}}{\mathrm{~d}^{2}+\mathrm{c}^{2}}[/math]
(দেখানো হল)গদেওয়া আছে,[math]\begin{array}{l}\mathrm{p}=\sin 2 \alpha \\\mathrm{q}=\sin 2 \beta \\\mathrm{t}=\sin 2 \gamma\end{array}[/math]
বামপক্ষ [math]\alpha+\beta+\gamma=\pi[/math]
বামপক্ষ [math]=p^{2}+q^{2}+t^{2}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \sin ^{2} 2 \alpha+\sin ^{2} 2 \beta+\sin ^{2} 2 \gamma \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2}\left(2 \sin ^{2} 2 \alpha+2 \sin ^{2} 2 \beta\right)+\sin ^{2} 2 \gamma \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2}(1-\cos 4 \alpha+1-\cos 4 \beta)+\sin ^{2} 2 \gamma \\\Rightarrow 1-\frac{1}{2}(\cos 4 \alpha+\cos 4 \beta)+\sin ^{2} 2 \gamma \\\Rightarrow 1-\frac{1}{2} \cdot 2 \cos \frac{4 \alpha+4 \beta}{2} \cos \frac{4 \alpha-4 \beta}{2}+\sin ^{2} 2 \gamma \\\Rightarrow 1-\cos (2 \alpha+2 \beta) \cos (2 \alpha-2 \beta)+\sin ^{2} 2 \gamma \\\Rightarrow 1-\cos (2 \pi-2 \gamma) \cos (2 \alpha-2 \beta)+1-\cos ^{2} 2 \gamma\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\left[\begin{array}{l}\because \alpha+\beta+\gamma=\pi \\\therefore 2 \alpha+2 \beta=2 \pi-2 \gamma\end{array}\right][/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 2-\cos 2 \gamma \cos (2 \alpha-2 \beta)-\cos ^{2} 2 \gamma \\\Rightarrow 2-\cos 2 \gamma\{\cos (2 \alpha-2 \beta)+\cos 2 \gamma\} \\\Rightarrow 2-\cos 2 \gamma\{\cos (2 \alpha-2 \beta)+\cos (2 \pi-2 \alpha-2 \beta)\} \\\Rightarrow 2-\cos 2 \gamma\{\cos (2 \alpha-2 \beta)+\cos (2 \alpha+2 \beta)\} \\\Rightarrow 2-\cos 2 \gamma \cdot 2 \cos 2 \alpha \cos 2 \beta\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2-2 \cos 2 \alpha \cos 2 \beta \cos 2 \gamma=[/math]
 ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore \mathrm{p}^{2}+\mathrm{q}^{2}+\mathrm{t}^{2}=2-2 \cos 2 \alpha \cos 2 \beta \cos 2 \gamma[/math]
(দেখানো হল)

Explanation:

Question #51 (ID: 473770)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2018, 2018, 2018, 2018 | Boards: Chittagong Board, Barisal Board, Rajshahi Board | Tags: Cumilla Board, Chattogram Board, Barisal Board, Rajshahi Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
দৃশ্যকল্প-১ : [math]\triangle A B C[/math] এ [math]\cos A+\cos B=\sin C[/math]

দৃশ্যকল্প-২ : [math]\sqrt{2} \cos A-\cos B=\cos ^{3} B[/math]

এবং [math]\sqrt{2} \sin A+\sin ^{3} B=\sin B[/math]

Options:
ক. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\tan 70^{\circ}=\tan 20^{\circ}+2 \tan 50^{\circ}[/math]
খ. দৃশ্যকল্প-১ : হতে দেখাও যে, ত্রিভুজটি সমকোণী
গ. দৃশ্যকল্প-২ হতে প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\operatorname{cosec}(A-B)=\pm 3[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]\tan 70^{\circ}=\tan \left(50^{\circ}+20^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \tan 70^{\circ}=\frac{\tan 50^{\circ}+\tan 20^{\circ}}{1-\tan 50^{\circ} \tan 20^{\circ}}\\\Rightarrow \tan 70^{\circ}-\tan 70^{\circ} \tan 50^{\circ} \tan 20^{\circ}=\tan 50^{\circ}+\tan 20^{\circ}\\\Rightarrow\tan 70^{\circ}-\tan \left(90^{\circ}-20^{\circ}\right) \tan 50^{\circ} \tan 20^{\circ}=\tan 50^{\circ}+\tan 20^{\circ}\\\Rightarrow \tan 70^{\circ}-\cot 20^{\circ} \tan 50^{\circ} \frac{1}{\cot 20^{\circ}}=\tan 50^{\circ}+\tan 20^{\circ}\\\Rightarrow \tan 70^{\circ}-\tan 50^{\circ}=\tan 50^{\circ}+\tan 20^{\circ}\\\Rightarrow \tan 70^{\circ}=\tan 20^{\circ}+\tan 50^{\circ}+\tan 50^{\circ}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad \tan 70^{\circ}=\tan 20^{\circ}+2 \tan 50^{\circ} .[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত)খদেওয়া আছে, [math]\triangle \mathrm{ABC}[/math]
 এ [math]\cos A+\cos B=\sin C[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 2 \cos \frac{\mathrm{A}+\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{A}-\mathrm{B}}{2}=\sin \mathrm{C}\\\Rightarrow 2 \cos \left(\frac{\pi}{2}-\frac{C}{2}\right) \cos \frac{A-B}{2}=\sin \left(2 \frac{C}{2}\right)\end{array}[/math]
 [math][\because \triangle \mathrm{ABC}-[/math]
 এ [math]\left.A+B+C=\pi \therefore \frac{A+B}{2}=\frac{\pi}{2}-\frac{C}{2}\right][/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 2 \sin \frac{\mathrm{C}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{A}-\mathrm{B}}{2}=2 \sin \frac{\mathrm{C}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{C}}{2}\\\Rightarrow \cos \frac{\mathrm{A}-\mathrm{B}}{2}=\cos \frac{\mathrm{C}}{2}\\\Rightarrow \frac{A-B}{2}=\frac{C}{2}\\\Rightarrow \mathrm{A}-\mathrm{B}=\mathrm{C}\\\Rightarrow A=B+C\\\Rightarrow A+A=A+B+C\\\Rightarrow 2 A=\pi\\\therefore \quad \mathrm{A}=\frac{\pi}{2}\end{array}[/math]
যেহেতু [math]ABC[/math]
 ত্রিভুজে [math]A=\frac{\pi}{2} \text {. }[/math]
সুতরাং [math]ABC[/math]
 ত্রিভুজটি সমকোণী ।(দেখানো হলো)গ [math]\sqrt{2} \cos A-\cos B=\cos ^{3} B[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad \sqrt{2} \cos A=\cos B+\cos ^{3} B......(1)[/math]
এবং [math]\sqrt{2} \sin A+\sin ^{3} \cdot B=\sin B[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad \sqrt{2} \sin A=\sin B-\sin ^{3} B........(2)[/math]
(1) ও (2) কে বর্গ করে যোগ করে পাই[math]2\left(\cos ^{2} A+\sin ^{2} A\right)=\cos ^{2} \mathrm{~B}+\sin ^{2} \mathrm{~B}+ 2\left(\cos ^{4} B-\sin ^{4} B\right)+\cos ^{6} B+\sin ^{6} B[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 2 \cdot 1=1+2\left\{\left(\cos ^{2} \mathrm{~B}\right)^{2}-\left(\sin ^{2} \mathrm{~B}\right)^{2}\right\}+\left(\cos ^{2} \mathrm{~B}\right)^{3}+\left(\sin ^{2} \mathrm{~B}\right)^{3}\\\Rightarrow 2=1+2\left(\cos ^{2} B+\sin ^{2} B\right)\left(\cos ^{2} \mathrm{~B}-\sin ^{2} B\right)\\+\left(\cos ^{2} \mathrm{~B}+\sin ^{2} \mathrm{~B}\right)^{3}-3 \cos ^{2} \mathrm{~B} \cdot \sin ^{2} \mathrm{~B}\left(\cos ^{2} \mathrm{~B}+\sin ^{2} \mathrm{~B}\right)\\\Rightarrow 1=2.1\left(\cos ^{2} B-\sin ^{2} B\right)+1^{3}-3 \cos ^{2} B \cdot \operatorname{sih}^{2} B \text{.}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 3 \cos ^{2} \mathrm{~B}\left(1-\cos ^{2} \mathrm{~B}\right)-2\left(\cos ^{2} \mathrm{~B}-1+\cos ^{2} \mathrm{~B}\right)=0 \\\Rightarrow 3 \cos ^{2} \mathrm{~B}-3 \cos ^{4} \mathrm{~B}-2 \cos ^{2} \mathrm{~B}+2-2 \cos ^{2} \mathrm{~B}=0 \\\Rightarrow 3 \cos ^{4} \mathrm{~B}+\cos ^{2} \mathrm{~B}-2=0 \\\Rightarrow 3 \cos ^{4} \mathrm{~B}-2 \cos ^{2} \mathrm{~B}+3 \cos ^{2} \mathrm{~B}-2=0 \\\Rightarrow \cos ^{2} \mathrm{~B}\left(3 \cos ^{2} \mathrm{~B}-2\right)+1\left(3 \cos ^{2} \mathrm{~B}-2\right)=0 \\\Rightarrow \left(3 \cos ^{2} \mathrm{~B}-2\right)\left(\cos ^{2} \mathrm{~B}+1\right)=0 \\\Rightarrow 3 \cos ^{2} \mathrm{~B}-2=0\left[\because \cos ^{2} \mathrm{~B}+1 
eq 0\right] \\\Rightarrow 3 \cos ^{2} \mathrm{~B}=2 \\\Rightarrow \cos ^{2} \mathrm{~B}=\frac{2}{3} \\\therefore \cos \mathrm{B}= \pm \sqrt{\frac{2}{3}}\end{array}[/math]
এখন [math]\sin (A-B)=\sin A \cos B-\cos A \sin B[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos B \cdot \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}\left(\sin B-\sin ^{3} B\right)-\sin B \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]
 [math]\left(\cos \mathrm{B}+\cos ^{3} \mathrm{~B}\right)[(\mathrm{i})[/math]
 থ্রক্র [math](ii)[/math]
 থেকে ][math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow -\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \cos \mathrm{B} \sin ^{3} \mathrm{~B}-\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \sin \mathrm{B} \cos ^{3} \mathrm{~B} \\\Rightarrow -\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \sin \mathrm{B} \cos \mathrm{B}\left(\sin ^{2} \mathrm{~B}+\cos ^{2} \mathrm{~B}\right) \\\Rightarrow -\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \sin \mathrm{B} \cos \mathrm{B} \times 1 \\\Rightarrow -\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \cos \mathrm{B} \sqrt{1-\cos ^{2} \mathrm{~B}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=-\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}\left( \pm \sqrt{\frac{2}{3}}\right) \sqrt{1-\left( \pm \sqrt{\frac{2}{3}}\right)^{2}}[/math]
 [math][\cos \mathrm{B}[/math]
 এর মান বসিয়ে ][math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \pm \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \cdot \frac{\sqrt{2}}{\sqrt{3}} \cdot \frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}= \pm \frac{1}{3} \\\Rightarrow \sin (A-B)= \pm \frac{1}{3} \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{\operatorname{cosec}(A-B)}= \pm \frac{1}{3}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad \operatorname{cosec}(A-B)= \pm 3 .[/math]
(প্রমাণিত)

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক যেহেতু [math]\tan 70^\circ=\cot 20^\circ=1/\tan 20^\circ[/math], তাই সমীকরণটি লেখলে [math]\tan20^\circ\big(\tan20^\circ+2\tan50^\circ\big)=1[/math] পাওয়া যায়, অর্থাৎ [math]\tan70^\circ=\tan20^\circ+2\tan50^\circ[/math] সত্য।  

খ [math]\cos A+\cos B=2\cos\frac{A+B}{2}\cos\frac{A-B}{2}=2\sin\frac{C}{2}\cos\frac{A-B}{2}[/math] এবং [math]\sin C=2\sin\frac{C}{2}\cos\frac{C}{2}[/math]; সমান হলে (শূন্য নয় ধরে) [math]\cos\frac{A-B}{2}=\cos\frac{C}{2}[/math] হয়, ফলে [math]A-B=\pm C[/math] এবং এটি সংযোজ করলে পাওয়া যায় [math]A=90^\circ[/math] অথবা [math]B=90^\circ[/math], অর্থাৎ ত্রিভুজটি সমকোণী।  

গ [math]x=\cos B,\;y=\sin B[/math] ধরলে শর্তগুলো থেকে [math]\sqrt2\cos A=x(1+x^2),\;\sqrt2\sin A=x^2y[/math]; বর্গ যোগ করলে [math]2=x^2+3x^4[/math] হয়ে [math]x^2=2/3,\;y^2=1/3[/math] পাওয়া যায়। এরপর [math]\sqrt2\sin(A-B)=(x^2y)x-x(1+x^2)y=-xy[/math], তাই [math]\sin(A-B)=\mp\frac{1}{3}[/math] এবং ফলে [math]\cosec(A-B)=\pm3[/math]।

Question #52 (ID: 473764)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2019 | Boards:  | Tags: Cumilla Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
দৃশ্যকল্প-১ :


[Image]


দৃশ্যকল্প-২ : [math]\triangle \mathrm{PQR}[/math] এ [math]\mathrm{p}=2 \mathrm{q}[/math] এবং [math]\mathrm{P}=3 \mathrm{Q}[/math]

Options:
ক. পৃথিবীর ব্যাসার্ধ 6371 কি.মি.। ঢাকা ও দিল্লী, পৃথিবীর পৃষ্ঠের দুটি স্থান। ঢাকা ও দিল্লীর মধ্যবর্তী দূরত্ব 1882 কি.মি. হলে, স্থান দুইটি পৃথিবীর কেন্দ্রে কত ডিগ্রী কোণ উৎপন্ন করবে ?
খ. [math]\angle \mathrm{A}[/math] এর সাহায্যে [math]\triangle \mathrm{ABC}[/math] এর ক্ষেত্রফল নির্ণয় কর।
গ. দৃশ্যকল্প-২ হতে R কোণ এর মান নির্ণয় কর ।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কএখানে, পৃথিবীর ব্যাসার্ধ; [math]\mathrm{R}=6371[/math]
 কি.মি.[math]\Rightarrow (6371 \times 1000)[/math]
 মি.ঢাকা ও দিল্লির মধ্যবর্তী দূরত্ব, [math]S=1882[/math]
 কি.মি.[math]\Rightarrow (1882 \times 1000)[/math]
 মি.কেন্দ্ৰস্থ কোণ, [math]\theta=?[/math]
আমরা জানি, [math]S=r \theta[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \theta=\frac{s}{r}=\frac{1882 \times 1000}{6371 \times 1000}=(0.2954)^{c}[/math]
নির্ণেয় কোণের মান [math]0.2954[/math]
 রেডিয়ানখ
[Image]
[math]\therefore \quad \mathrm{a}=13 \mathrm{~cm}, \mathrm{~b}=7 \mathrm{~cm}, \mathrm{c}=8 \mathrm{~cm}[/math]
আমরা জানি,[math]\cos A=\frac{b^{2}+c^{2}-a^{2}}{2 b c}=\frac{7^{2}+8^{2}-13^{2}}{2.7 .8}=\frac{-56}{112}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \cos \mathrm{A}=\frac{-1}{2} \\\Rightarrow \cos \mathrm{A}=\cos 120^{\circ} \\\therefore A=120^{\circ}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\triangle \mathrm{ABC}[/math]
 এর ক্ষেত্রফল [math]=\frac{1}{2} b c \sin \mathrm{A}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2} \times 7 \times 8 \sin 120^{\circ} \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2} \times 7 \times 8 \times \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 14 \sqrt{3}[/math]
 বর্গ সে:মি:নির্ণেয় ক্ষেত্রফল [math]14 \sqrt{3}[/math]
 বর্গ সে.মি. ।গ
[Image]
দেওয়া আছে,[math]P = 3Q[/math]
 এবং [math]p = 29[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow2 R \sin P=2.2 R \sin Q[/math]
 [math][\mathrm{R}, \triangle \mathrm{PQR}[/math]
 এর পরিব্যাসার্ধ][math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \sin P=2 \sin Q\\\Rightarrow \sin P-\sin \mathrm{Q}=\sin \mathrm{Q}\\\Rightarrow \sin 3 \mathrm{Q}-\sin \mathrm{Q}=\sin \mathrm{Q}[\because \mathrm{P}=3 \mathrm{Q}]\\\Rightarrow 2 \cos \frac{3 Q+Q}{2} \cdot \sin \frac{3 Q-Q}{2}=\sin Q\\\Rightarrow 2 \cos 2 \mathrm{Q} \cdot \sin \mathrm{Q}=\sin \mathrm{Q}\\\Rightarrow 2 \cos 2 Q=1 \text{.}\\\Rightarrow \cos 2 Q=\frac{1}{2}\\\Rightarrow \cos 2 Q=\cos 60^{\circ}\\\Rightarrow 2 \mathrm{Q}=60^{\circ}\\\Rightarrow \mathrm{Q}=30^{\circ}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{aligned}\therefore \quad & P=3 Q=3 \times 30^{\circ}=90^{\circ} \\\quad R & =180^{\circ}-P-Q=180^{\circ}-90^{\circ}-30^{\circ}=60^{\circ}\end{aligned}[/math]
নির্ণেয় মান : [math]: \angle \mathrm{R}=60^{\circ} .[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক কেন্দ্রীয় কোণ [math]\theta[/math] এবং弧দৈর্ঘ্য [math]s=1882\,\text{কিমি}[/math], ব্যাসার্ধ [math]R=6371\,\text{কিমি}[/math] হলে [math]\theta[/math] (degree) = [math]\dfrac{s}{R}\times\dfrac{180}{\pi}=\dfrac{1882}{6371}\times\dfrac{180}{\pi}\approx 16.93^\circ[/math] — তাই প্রায় [math]16.93^\circ[/math].

খ ত্রিভুজে কোনও কোণ [math]A[/math] এর পাশে থাকা দুই বাহু ধরা হলে ক্ষেত্রফল = [math]\tfrac{1}{2}\times(\text{দুই পাশে})\times\sin A[/math]; উদাহরণস্বরূপ, যদি পাশগুলো [math]AB,\,AC[/math] হয় তাহলে ক্ষেত্রফল = [math]\tfrac{1}{2}\,AB\cdot AC\cdot\sin A[/math]।

গ ধরা হয়েছে পাশে [math]p[/math] এবং [math]q[/math] হল যথাক্রমে কোণ [math]P[/math] ও [math]Q[/math] এর বিপরীত; সাইন রুল অনুযায়ী [math]\dfrac{p}{q}=\dfrac{\sin P}{\sin Q}=2[/math] ও [math]P=3Q[/math] দেওয়ায় [math]\dfrac{\sin(3Q)}{\sin Q}=2[/math] এবং [math]\sin(3Q)=3\sin Q-4\sin^3 Q[/math] ব্যবহার করলে [math]\sin Q=\tfrac{1}{2}[/math], তাই [math]Q=30^\circ,\,P=90^\circ[/math] এবং [math]R=180^\circ-(P+Q)=60^\circ[/math]।

Question #53 (ID: 473763)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2019 | Boards:  | Tags: Cumilla Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
দৃশ্যকল্প-১: [math]2 P=\tan \frac{x+y}{2}+\tan \frac{x-y}{2}[/math]

দৃশ্যকল্প-২: [math]\sin x=a-\sin y, \cos x=b-\cos y[/math]

Options:
ক. দেখাও যে, [math]\mathrm{P}=\frac{\sin \mathrm{x}}{\cos \mathrm{x}+\cos \mathrm{y}}[/math]
খ. [math]y=90^{\circ}[/math] হলে , [math]P[/math]-এর লেখচিত্র অঙ্কন কর ।
গ. দৃশ্যকল্প-২ থেকে প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\sin \frac{1}{2}(x-y)=\pm \frac{1}{2} \sqrt{4-a^{2}-b^{2}}[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে,[math]\begin{aligned}2 P & \Rightarrow \tan \frac{x+y}{2}+\tan \frac{x-y}{2} \\& \Rightarrow \frac{\sin \frac{x+y}{2}}{\cos \frac{x+y}{2}}+\frac{\sin \frac{x-y}{2}}{\cos \frac{x-y}{2}} \\& \Rightarrow \frac{\sin \frac{x+y}{2} \cdot \cos \frac{x-y}{2}+\cos \frac{x+y}{2} \cdot \sin \frac{x-y}{2}}{\cos \frac{x+y}{2} \cdot \cos \frac{x-y}{2}}\end{aligned}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow P=\frac{\sin \left(\frac{x+y}{2}+\frac{x-y}{2}\right)}{2 \cos \frac{x+y}{2} \cdot \cos \frac{x-y}{2}}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad P=\frac{\sin x}{\cos \cdot x+\cos y}[/math]
 (দেখানো হল)খক হতে পাই,[math]P=\frac{\sin x}{\cos x+\cos y}[/math]
 [math]y=90^{\circ}[/math]
 হলে,[math]P=\frac{\sin x}{\cos x+\cos 90^{\circ}}=\frac{\sin x}{\cos x+0}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad P=\tan x[/math]
 [math]P=\tan x[/math]
 এর লেখচিত্র : x অক্ষ বরাবর [math]10°[/math]
 অন্তর x এর কতকগুলি যোগবোধক ও বিয়োগবোধক মান ধরি এবং [math]\text { Scientific }[/math]
 ক্যালকুলেটর ব্যবহার করে [math]tan x[/math]
 এর প্রাপ্ত মানগুলি নিম্নরূপে ছক আকারে সাজাই ।
[Image]
x অক্ষ বরাবর ছোট বর্গক্ষেত্রের এক বাহুকে [math]10°[/math]
 এবং y অক্ষ বরাবর 2 বাহুকে একক দৈর্ঘ্য হিসাবে স্কেল নির্বাচন করে উপর্যুক্ত ছক থেকে x এর প্রত্যেকটি মানের সঙ্গে[math]\tan x[/math]
 এর আনুষঙ্গিক মান নিয়ে প্রাপ্ত বিন্দুগুলি প্রতিস্থাপন করি। ঐ বিন্দুগুলি পেন্সিল দিয়ে সংযুক্ত করলে নির্ণেয় লেখচিত্র পাওয়া যাবে।
[Image]
ট্যানজেন্ট লেখচিত্রের বৈশিষ্ট্য :(i) লেখচিত্র অবিচ্ছিন্ন নয়। এটা পৃথক পৃথক শাখায় বিভক্ত। x এর মান যখন [math]90°[/math]
 এর বিজোড় গুণিতক হয়, তখনই লেখচিত্রটি বিচ্ছিন্ন হয়।(ii) x এর মান যখন বাম থেকে ডানে [math]90°[/math]
 অতিক্রম করে তখন [math]\tan x[/math]
 এর মান হঠাৎ বামে বৃহৎ যোগবোধক সংখ্যা থেকে ডানে বৃহৎ বিয়োগবোধক সংখ্যায় পরিবর্তিত হয়(iii) যেহেতু [math]\tan (n \pi+x)=\tan x[/math]
 সুতরাং [math]-\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
 হতে [math]\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
 পর্যন্ত অঙ্কিত লেখচিত্রগুলি প্রত্যেকটি অপরটির পুনরাবৃত্তি।(iv) [math]90°[/math]
 এর, বিজোড় গুণিতক সমান কোণের জন্য অক্ষের সমান্তরাল করে অঙ্কিত রেখাগুলির ও লেখচিত্রের মধ্যবর্তী দূরত্ব ক্রমশ কমতে থাকে কিন্তু তারা কখনই একে অপরকে স্পর্শ করে না। এ ধরনের রেখাকে অসীমতট রেখা বলেগ [math]\begin{array}{l}\sin x=a-\underline{\sin y}\\\Rightarrow a=\sin x+\sin y\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad a=2 \sin \frac{x+y}{2} \cdot \cos \frac{x-y}{2} ......[/math]
(1)এবং [math]\cos x=b-\cos y[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow b=\cos x+\cos y[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad b=2 \cos \frac{x+y}{2} \cdot \cos \frac{x-y}{2}.......[/math]
(2)সমীকরণ (1) ও (2)নং কে বর্গ করে যোগ করি,[math]\begin{array}{l}a^{2}+b^{2}=4 \sin ^{2} \frac{x+y}{2} \cdot \cos ^{2} \frac{x-y}{2}+4 \cos ^{2} \frac{x+y}{2} \cdot \cos ^{2} \frac{x-y}{2}\\\Rightarrow a^{2}+b^{2}=4 \cos ^{2} \frac{x-y}{2}\left(\sin ^{2} \frac{x+y}{2}+\cos ^{2} \frac{x+y}{2}\right)\\\Rightarrow \frac{a^{2}+b^{2}}{4}=\cos ^{2} \frac{x-y}{2} \cdot 1\\\Rightarrow \frac{a^{2}+b^{2}}{4}=1-3 \sin ^{2} \frac{x-y}{2}\\\Rightarrow \sin ^{2} \frac{x-y}{2}=1-\frac{a^{2}+b^{2}}{4}\\\Rightarrow \sin ^{2} \frac{x-y}{2}=\frac{1}{4}\left(4-a^{2}-b^{2}\right) \text{.}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \quad \sin \frac{1}{2}(x-y)= \pm \frac{1}{2} \sqrt{4-a^{2}-b^{2}}[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত)

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক ধরা যাক [math]A=\frac{x+y}{2},\;B=\frac{x-y}{2}[/math]. তখন [math]\tan A+\tan B=\dfrac{\sin(A+B)}{\cos A\cos B}=\dfrac{\sin x}{\cos A\cos B}[/math] এবং [math]\cos A\cos B=\tfrac{1}{2}(\cos x+\cos y)[/math], ফলে [math]2P=\dfrac{2\sin x}{\cos x+\cos y}[/math] এবং তাই [math]P=\dfrac{\sin x}{\cos x+\cos y}[/math].

খ যদি [math]y=90^\circ[/math] হয় তবে [math]\cos y=0[/math] এবং [math]P=\dfrac{\sin x}{\cos x}=\tan x[/math]; তাই [math]P[/math]-এর গ্রাফ হল [math]\tan x[/math] যার উল্লম্ব অসমীমা আছে যেখানে [math]x=90^\circ+k\cdot180^\circ[/math]।

গ দৃশ্যকল্প-২ থেকে [math]\sin x+\sin y=a,\ \cos x+\cos y=b[/math]; স্কোয়ার করে যোগ করলে [math]a^2+b^2=2+2\cos(x-y)=4\cos^2\frac{x-y}{2}[/math]. তাই [math]\sin^2\frac{x-y}{2}=1-\frac{a^2+b^2}{4}=\frac{4-a^2-b^2}{4}[/math], অর্থাৎ [math]\sin\frac{x-y}{2}=\pm\frac{1}{2}\sqrt{4-a^2-b^2}[/math]।

Question #54 (ID: 473762)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2019 | Boards:  | Tags: Jessore Board

Question:
দৃশ্যকল্প-১ : [math]\triangle \mathrm{ABC} \text { এর } \mathrm{A}=75^{\circ}, \mathrm{B}-\mathrm{C}=15^{\circ}[/math]

দৃশ্যকল্প-২ :  


[Image]


Options:
ক. [math]\cos 30^{\circ} 32^{\prime} \cos 29^{\circ} 28^{\prime}-\sin 149^{\circ} 28^{\prime} \sin 29^{\circ} 28^{\prime}[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর ।
খ. দৃশ্যকল্প-১ অনুযায়ী দেখাও যে, [math]\cos \frac{C}{6}=\frac{1}{2} \sqrt{2+\sqrt{2+\sqrt{3}}}[/math]
গ. দৃশ্যকল্প-২ অনুযায়ী ত্রিভুজটির সমাধান কর।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কপ্রদও রাশি [math]=\cos 30^{\circ} 32^{\prime} \cos 29^{\circ} 28^{\prime}-\sin 149^{\circ} 28^{\prime} \sin 29^{\circ} 28^{\prime}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \cos 30^{\circ} 32^{\prime} \cdot \cos 29^{\circ} 28^{\prime}-\sin \left(180^{\circ}-30^{\circ} 32^{\prime}\right) \cdot \sin 29^{\circ} 28^{\prime} \\\Rightarrow \cos 30^{\circ} 32^{\prime} \cos 29^{\circ} 28^{\prime}-\sin 30^{\circ} 32^{\prime} \sin 29^{\circ} 28^{\prime} \\\Rightarrow \cos \left(30^{\circ} 32^{\prime}+29^{\circ} 28^{\prime}\right)=\cos 60^{\circ}=\frac{1}{2}\end{array}[/math]
নির্ণেয় মান [math]\frac{1}{2}[/math]
 খদৃশ্যকল্প-১ হতে, [math]\triangle \mathrm{ABC}[/math]
-এ[math]A+B+C=180^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 75^{\circ}+\mathrm{B}+\mathrm{C}=180^{\circ}\\\Rightarrow B+C=180^{\circ}-75^{\circ}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow B+C=105^{\circ}........(1)[/math]
আবার [math]B-C=15^{\circ}...............(2)[/math]
(1) নং সমীকরণ থেকে (2) নং বিয়োগ করে, [math]2 \mathrm{C}=90^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow C=45^{\circ}[/math]
বামপক্ষ [math]=\cos \frac{C}{6}=\cos \frac{45^{\circ}}{6}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \cos \frac{15^{\circ}}{2} \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2} \sqrt{4 \cos ^{2} \frac{15^{\circ}}{2}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2} \sqrt{2.2 \cos ^{2} \frac{15^{\circ}}{2}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2} \sqrt{2\left(1+\cos 15^{\circ}\right)} \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2} \sqrt{2+2 \cos 15^{\circ}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2} \sqrt{2+\sqrt{4 \cos ^{2} 15^{\circ}}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2} \sqrt{2+\sqrt{2\left(1+\cos 30^{\circ}\right)}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2} \sqrt{2+\sqrt{2+2 \cdot \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2} \sqrt{2+\sqrt{2+\sqrt{3}}} .\end{array}[/math]
= ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore \cos \frac{C}{6}=\frac{1}{2} \sqrt{2+\sqrt{2+\sqrt{3}}} .[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত)গদৃশ্যকল্প—২ হতে, [math]\triangle \mathrm{ABC}^{}[/math]
 এ[math]\begin{array}{l}\cos C=\frac{a^{2}+b^{2}-c^{2}}{2 a b} \\\Rightarrow \cos 60^{\circ}=\frac{(\sqrt{3}+1)^{2}+(\sqrt{3}-1)^{2}-c^{2}}{2 \cdot(\sqrt{3}+1)(\sqrt{3}-1)} \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2}=\frac{3+2 \sqrt{3}+1+3-2 \sqrt{3}+1-c^{2}}{2(3-1)} \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2}=\frac{8-c^{2}}{4} \\\Rightarrow c^{2}=6 \\\Rightarrow c=\sqrt{6}\end{array}[/math]
এখন [math]\cos \mathrm{A}=\frac{\mathrm{b}^{2}+\mathrm{c}^{2}-\mathrm{a}^{2}}{2 \mathrm{bc}}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{(\sqrt{3}-1)^{2}+6-(\sqrt{3}+1)^{2}}{2(\sqrt{3}-1) \times \sqrt{6}} \\\Rightarrow -0.258819 \\\Rightarrow \cos 105^{\circ}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{ll}\therefore & A=105^{\circ} \\\therefore \quad & \quad B=180^{\circ}-\left(105^{\circ}+60^{\circ}\right)=15^{\circ}\end{array}[/math]
নির্ণেয় সমাধান [math]A=105^{\circ}, B=15^{\circ}, C=\sqrt{6}[/math]


Explanation:
ক কারণ [math]\sin149^{\circ}28'= \sin(180^{\circ}-149^{\circ}28')=\sin30^{\circ}32'[/math], তাই প্রদত্তটি হচ্ছে [math]\cos30^{\circ}32'\cos29^{\circ}28'-\sin30^{\circ}32'\sin29^{\circ}28'=\cos(30^{\circ}32'+29^{\circ}28')=\cos60^{\circ}=\tfrac{1}{2}[/math]।

খ A=75° ও B−C=15° থেকে B+C=105° হওয়ায় সমাধান করলে [math]B=60^{\circ},\;C=45^{\circ}[/math]। তাই [math]\frac{C}{6}=7.5^{\circ}= \tfrac{15^{\circ}}{2}[/math] এবং হাফ-এঙ্গেল সূত্র প্রয়োগ করে [math]\cos7.5^{\circ}=\sqrt{\frac{1+\cos15^{\circ}}{2}},\;\cos15^{\circ}=\tfrac{1}{2}\sqrt{2+\sqrt{3}}[/math] থেকে [math]\cos\frac{C}{6}=\tfrac{1}{2}\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2+\sqrt{3}}}[/math] পাওয়া যায়।

গ দৃশ্যকল্প‑২ এর নির্দিষ্ট কোণ ও বাহুগুলোর মান চিত্রে স্পষ্টভাবে প্রয়োজন; অনুগ্রহ করে চিত্রের দেওয়া কোণ/বাহুর মান বা উচ্চ রেজোলিউশনের ছবি দিন, তখন ত্রিভুজটি সম্পূর্ণভাবে সমাধান দেখাব।

Question #55 (ID: 473760)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2019 | Boards: Dhaka Board | Tags: Dhaka Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:

[Image]


Options:
ক. দেখাও যে, [math]\sec \frac{5 x}{2}=\frac{2}{\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2+2 \cos 10 x}}}[/math]
খ. উদ্দীপকের সাহায্যে দেখাও যে, [math]A C \sin \left(\frac{B}{2}+C\right)=(A B+B C) \sin \frac{B}{2}[/math]
গ. উদ্দীপকের সাহায্যে দেখাও যে, [math]\cos ^{2} \alpha+\cos ^{2} \beta+\cos ^{2} \gamma=1+2 \cos \alpha \cos \beta \cos \gamma[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কডানপক্ষ [math]=\frac{2}{\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2+2 \cos 10 x}}}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{2}{\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2(1+\cos 10 x)}}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{2}{\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2 \cdot 2 \cos ^{2} 5 x}}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{2}{\sqrt{2+2 \cos 5 x}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{2}{\sqrt{2(1+\cos 5 x)}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{2}{\sqrt{2.2 \cos ^{2} \frac{5 x}{2}}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{2}{2 \cos \frac{5 x}{2}}=\frac{1}{\cos \frac{5 x}{2}}=\sec \frac{5 x}{2}=[/math]
 বামপক্ষ[math]\therefore \quad \sec \frac{5 x}{2}=\frac{2}{\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2+2 \cos 10 x}}}[/math]
(দেখানো হল)খডানপক্ষ [math]=(A B+B C) \sin \frac{B}{2}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow (\mathrm{c}+\mathrm{a}) \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \\\Rightarrow \mathrm{b}\left(\frac{\mathrm{C}+\mathrm{a}}{\mathrm{b}}\right) \cdot \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \\\Rightarrow \mathrm{b} \frac{2 \mathrm{R} \sin \mathrm{C}+2 \mathrm{R} \sin \mathrm{A}}{2 \mathrm{R} \cdot \sin \mathrm{B}} \cdot \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \\\Rightarrow \mathrm{b} \cdot \frac{\sin \mathrm{C}+\sin \mathrm{A}}{\sin \mathrm{B}} \cdot \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \\\Rightarrow \mathrm{b} \cdot \frac{2 \sin \frac{\mathrm{A}+\mathrm{C}}{2} \cdot \cos \frac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}}{\sin \mathrm{B}} \cdot \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \\\Rightarrow \mathrm{b} \cdot \frac{2 \sin \frac{\pi-\mathrm{B}}{2} \cdot \cos \frac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}}{\sin \mathrm{B}} \cdot \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \\\Rightarrow \mathrm{b} \cdot \frac{\mathrm{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cdot \cos \frac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}}{2 \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cdot \cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}} \cdot \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \\\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow b \cos \frac{C-A}{2} \\\Rightarrow b \cos \frac{A-C}{2}[\because \cos (-\theta)=\cos \theta] \\\Rightarrow b \cos \left(\frac{\pi-B-C-C}{2}\right)[\because A+B+C=\pi] \\\Rightarrow b \cos \frac{\pi-(B+2 C)}{2} \\\Rightarrow b \sin \frac{B+2 C}{2}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=\mathrm{b} \sin \left(\frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}+\mathrm{C}\right)=\mathrm{AC} \sin \left(\frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}+\mathrm{C}\right)=[/math]
 বামপক্ষ[math]\therefore \quad A C \sin \left(\frac{B}{2}+C\right)=(A B+B C) \sin \frac{B}{2}[/math]
 (দেখানো হল)গচিত্রে [math]\gamma=\alpha+\beta[/math]
বামপক্ষ [math]=\cos ^{2} \alpha+\cos ^{2} \beta+\cos ^{2} \gamma[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2}\left(2 \cos ^{2} \alpha+2 \cos ^{2} \beta\right)+\cos ^{2} \gamma \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2}(1+\cos 2 \alpha+1+\cos 2 \beta)+\cos ^{2} \gamma \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2} \cdot 2+\frac{1}{2}(\cos 2 \alpha \cos 2 \beta)+\cos ^{2} \gamma \\\Rightarrow 1+\frac{1}{2} \cdot 2 \cos \frac{2 \alpha+2 \beta}{2} \cdot \cos \frac{2 \alpha-2 \beta}{2}+\cos ^{2} \gamma \\\Rightarrow 1+\cos (\alpha+\beta) \cdot \cos (\alpha-\beta)+\cos ^{2} \gamma \\\Rightarrow 1+\cos \gamma \cdot \cos (\alpha-\beta)+\cos ^{2} \gamma \\\Rightarrow 1+\cos \gamma[\cos (\alpha-\beta)+\cos \gamma]\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 1+\cos \gamma \cdot 2 \cos \frac{\alpha-\beta+\gamma}{2} \cdot \cos \frac{\alpha-\beta-\gamma}{2} \\\Rightarrow 1+2 \cos \gamma \cdot \cos \left(\frac{\alpha-\beta+\alpha+\beta}{2}\right) \cdot \cos \left(\frac{\alpha-\beta-\alpha-\beta}{2}\right) \\\Rightarrow 1+2 \cos \gamma \cdot \cos \alpha \cdot \cos (-\beta) \\\Rightarrow 1+2 \cos \alpha \cdot \cos \beta \cdot \cos \gamma\end{array}[/math]
= ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore \quad \cos ^{2} \alpha+\cos ^{2} \beta+\cos ^{2} \gamma=1+2 \cos \alpha \cdot \cos \beta \cdot \cos \gamma[/math]
(দেখানো হল)

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: খ সঠিক—ত্রিভুজে সাইন সূত্র নিলে [math]AB=k\sin C,\;BC=k\sin A,\;AC=k\sin B[/math] বসালে দাবি হ্রাসে হয় [math]\sin B\sin\big(\tfrac B2+C\big)=(\sin C+\sin A)\sin\tfrac B2[/math]. বাম পাশের ভগ্নাংশ বিস্তৃত করে এবং [math]\sin A=\sin(B+C)=\sin B\cos C+\cos B\sin C,\;\sin B=2\sin\tfrac B2\cos\tfrac B2,\;1+\cos B=2\cos^2\tfrac B2[/math] ব্যবহার করলে দুই পাশ সমান হয়ে যায়, তাই সমীকরণটি সব সময় বৈধ।

Question #56 (ID: 473761)

Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2019 | Boards: Rajshahi Board | Tags: Rajshahi Board

Question:
[math]\begin{array}{l}P=\tan A \cdot \tan B, q=\tan C \cdot \tan D \\r=4 \sin \frac{\alpha}{2} \sin \frac{\beta}{2} \cos \frac{\gamma}{2}-1\end{array}[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]\cos 75^{\circ}[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর। (ক্যালকুলেটার ব্যতীত)
খ. [math]A=20^{\circ}, B=2 A, C=3 A, D=4 A[/math] হলে, দেখাও যে, [math]\mathrm{pq}=3[/math]
গ. [math]\alpha+\beta+\gamma=0[/math] হলে, প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\cos \alpha+\cos \beta-\cos \gamma=r+2[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]\begin{aligned}\cos 75^{\circ} & =\cos \left(45^{\circ}+30^{\circ}\right) \\& \Rightarrow \cos 45^{\circ} \cdot \cos 30^{\circ}-\sin 45^{\circ} \cdot \sin 30^{\circ} \\& \Rightarrow \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \cdot \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}-\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \cdot \frac{1}{2} \\& \Rightarrow \frac{\sqrt{3}-1}{2 \sqrt{2}}=\frac{\sqrt{2}(\sqrt{3}-1)}{2 \sqrt{2} \cdot \sqrt{2}}=\frac{\sqrt{6}-\sqrt{2}}{4}\end{aligned}[/math]
নির্ণেয় মান [math]\frac{\sqrt{6}-\sqrt{2}}{4}[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]p=\tan \mathrm{A} \cdot \tan B[/math]
 এবং [math]\mathrm{q}=\tan C \tan D[/math]
 [math]A=20^{\circ}, B=2 A, C=3 A, D=4 A[/math]
বামপক্ষ [math]=p q[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \tan A \cdot \tan B \cdot \tan C \cdot \tan D \\\Rightarrow \tan A \cdot \tan 2 A \cdot \tan 3 \mathrm{~A} \cdot \tan 4 \mathrm{~A} \\\Rightarrow \tan 20^{\circ} \cdot \tan 40^{\circ} \cdot \tan 60^{\circ} \cdot \tan 80^{\circ} \\\Rightarrow \tan 20^{\circ} \cdot \tan \cdot\left(60^{\circ}-20^{\circ}\right) \cdot \sqrt{3} \cdot \tan \left(60^{\circ}+20^{\circ}\right) \\\Rightarrow \sqrt{3} \cdot \tan 20^{\circ} \cdot \frac{\tan 60^{\circ}-\tan 20^{\circ}}{1+\tan 60^{\circ} \cdot \tan 20^{\circ}} \cdot \frac{\tan 60^{\circ}+\tan 20^{\circ}}{1-\tan 60^{\circ} \cdot \tan 20^{\circ}} \\\Rightarrow \sqrt{3} \tan 20^{\circ} \cdot \frac{\sqrt{3}-\tan 20^{\circ}}{1+\sqrt{3} \tan 20^{\circ}} \frac{\sqrt{3}+\tan 20^{\circ}}{1-\sqrt{3} \tan 20^{\circ}} \\\Rightarrow \sqrt{3} \tan 20^{\circ} \frac{3-\tan ^{2} 20^{\circ}}{1-3 \tan ^{2} 20^{\circ}} \\\Rightarrow \sqrt{3} \cdot \frac{3 \tan 20^{\circ}-\tan ^{3} 20^{\circ}}{1-3 \tan ^{2} 20^{\circ}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sqrt{3} \cdot \tan \left(3.20^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sqrt{3} \cdot \tan 60^{\circ}=\sqrt{3} \cdot \sqrt{3}=3=[/math]
 ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore \quad \mathrm{pq}=3[/math]
 (দেখানো হল)গদেওয়া আছে, [math]\alpha+{\beta}+\gamma=0[/math]
এবং [math]r=4 \sin \frac{\alpha}{2} \cdot \sin \frac{\beta}{2} \cdot \cos \frac{\gamma}{2}-1[/math]
বামপক্ষ, [math]=\cos \alpha+\cos \beta-\cos \gamma[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 2 \cos \frac{\alpha+\beta}{2} \cdot \cos \frac{\alpha-\beta}{2}-\cos \gamma \\\Rightarrow 2 \cos \left(\frac{-\gamma}{2}\right) \cdot \cos \frac{\alpha-\beta}{2}-\cos \gamma \\\Rightarrow 2 \cos \frac{\gamma}{2} \cdot \cos \frac{\alpha-\beta}{2}-\cos \gamma+1-1 \\\Rightarrow 2 \cos \frac{\gamma}{2} \cdot \cos \frac{\alpha-\beta}{2}-(1+\cos \gamma)+1 \\\Rightarrow 2 \cos \frac{\gamma}{2} \cdot \cos \frac{\alpha-\beta}{2}-2 \cos ^{2} \frac{\gamma}{2}+1 \\\Rightarrow 2 \cos \frac{\gamma}{2}\left[\cos \frac{\alpha-\beta}{2}-\cos \frac{\gamma}{2}\right]+1 \\\Rightarrow 2 \cos \frac{\gamma}{2}\left[\cos \left(\frac{\alpha}{2}-\frac{\beta}{2}\right)-\cos \left(\frac{\alpha}{2}+\frac{\beta}{2}\right)\right]+1\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 2 \cos \frac{\gamma}{2} \cdot 2 \sin \frac{\alpha}{2} \cdot \sin \frac{\beta}{2}+1 \\\Rightarrow 4 \sin \frac{\alpha}{2} \cdot \sin \frac{\beta}{2} \cdot \cos \frac{\gamma}{2}+1 \\\Rightarrow 4 \sin \frac{\alpha}{2} \cdot \sin \frac{\beta}{2} \cdot \cos \frac{\gamma}{2}-1+2\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=r+2=[/math]
 ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore \quad \cos \alpha+\cos \beta-\cos \gamma=r+2[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত)

Explanation:

Question #57 (ID: 473759)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards: Barisal Board | Tags: Barisal Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
দৃশ্যকল্প-১: [math]M=\cos ^{2} 5 \alpha+\cos ^{2} 5 \beta-\sin ^{2} 5 \gamma+2 \cos 5 \alpha \cos 5 \beta \cos 5 \gamma[/math]

দৃশ্যকল্প-২:


[Image]


Options:
ক. যেকোনো [math]ABC[/math] ত্রিভুজে [math]\mathrm{b}=4 \mathrm{~cm}, \mathrm{c}=3 \mathrm{~cm}[/math] এবং [math]\angle C=30^{\circ}[/math] হলে [math]\angle B[/math] নির্ণয় কর।
খ. দৃশ্যকল্প-১ হতে প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]M. = 0[/math] যেখানে, [math]\alpha+\beta+\gamma=\pi[/math]
গ. দৃশ্যকল্প-২ হতে প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\frac{\mathrm{b}-\mathrm{c}}{2 \mathrm{a}}=\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}} \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}-\mathrm{C}}{2}[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কত্রিভুজের সাইন সুত্রানুসারে[math]\frac{\mathrm{a}}{\sin \mathrm{A}}=\frac{\mathrm{b}}{\sin \mathrm{B}}=\frac{\mathrm{c}}{\sin C}=2 \mathrm{R}[/math]
দেওয়া আছে, [math]\mathrm{b}=4 \mathrm{~cm} ; \mathrm{c}=3 \mathrm{~cm}[/math]
 এবং [math]\angle \mathrm{C}=30^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \frac{b}{\sin B}=\frac{c}{\sin C}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{ll}\Rightarrow \frac{4}{\sin B}=\frac{3}{\sin 30^{\circ}}=\frac{3}{\frac{1}{2}} & \Rightarrow \frac{4}{\sin B}=6 \\\Rightarrow \sin B=\frac{4}{6}=\frac{2}{3} &\Rightarrow B=\sin ^{-1} \frac{2}{3}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \angle B=41.81^{\circ}[/math]
 (প্রায়)[math]\text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]M=\cos ^{2} 5 \alpha+\cos ^{2} 5 \beta-\sin ^{2} 5 \gamma+2 \cos 5 \alpha \cos 5 \beta \cos 5 \gamma[/math]
এখানে, [math]\alpha+\beta+\gamma=\pi[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2}\left(2 \cos ^{2} 5 \alpha+2 \cos ^{2} 5 \beta\right)-\sin ^{2} 5 \gamma \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2}(1+\cos 10 \alpha+1+\cos 10 \beta)-\sin ^{2} 5 \gamma \\\quad\left[\because 2 \cos ^{2} \alpha=1+\cos 2 \alpha\right]\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2}(2+\cos 10 \alpha+\cos 10 \beta)-\sin ^{2} 5 \gamma \\\Rightarrow 1+\frac{1}{2} \times 2 \cos \frac{10 \alpha+10 \beta}{2} \cos \frac{10 \alpha-10 \beta}{2}-\sin ^{2} 5 \gamma \\\Rightarrow \cos 5(\alpha+\beta) \cos 5(\alpha-\beta)+1-\sin ^{2} 5 \gamma \\\Rightarrow \cos 5(\pi-\gamma) \cos 5(\alpha-\beta)+\cos ^{2} 5 \gamma[\because \alpha+\beta=\pi-\gamma] \\\Rightarrow \cos (5 \pi-5 \gamma) \cos 5(\alpha-\beta)+\cos ^{2} 5 \gamma \\\Rightarrow -\cos 5 \gamma \cos 5(\alpha-\beta)+\cos ^{2} 5 \gamma \\\Rightarrow \cos 5 \gamma[\cos 5 \gamma-\cos (5 \alpha-5 \beta)] \\\Rightarrow \cos 5 \gamma[\cos 5\{\pi-(\alpha+\beta)\}-\cos (5 \alpha-5 \beta)] \\\Rightarrow \cos 5 \gamma[\cos \{5 \pi-5(\alpha+\beta)\}-\cos (5 \alpha-5 \beta)] \\\Rightarrow \cos 5 \gamma[-\cos (5 \alpha+5 \beta)-\cos (5 \alpha-5 \beta)] \\\Rightarrow -\cos 5 \gamma[\cos (5 \alpha+5 \beta)+\cos (5 \alpha-5 \beta)]\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow -\cos 5 \gamma \cdot 2 \cos 5 \alpha \cos 5 \beta \\\quad[\because \cos (A+B)+\cos (A-B)=2 \cos A \cos B] \\\Rightarrow -2 \cos 5 \alpha \cos 5 \beta \cos 5 \gamma\end{array}[/math]
বামপক্ষ [math]=M[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \cos ^{2} 5 \alpha+\cos ^{2} 5 \beta-\cos ^{2} 5 \gamma+2 \cos 5 \alpha \cos 5 \beta \cos 5 \gamma \\\Rightarrow -2 \cos 5 \alpha \cos 5 \beta \cos 5 \gamma+2 \cos 5 \alpha \cos 5 \beta \cos 5 \gamma\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=0=[/math]
 ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore M=0[/math]
(প্রমাণিত)গদৃশ্যকল্প-২ এ বর্ণিত[math]\triangle \mathrm{ABC}[/math]
 এর ক্ষেত্রে [math]A+B+C=180^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 60^{\circ}+\mathrm{B}+\mathrm{C}=180^{\circ} \\\therefore \mathrm{B}+\mathrm{C}=120^{\circ}\end{array}[/math]
ত্রিভুজের সাইন সূত্রানুসারে,[math]\frac{a}{\sin \mathrm{A}}=\frac{\mathrm{b}}{\sin B}=\frac{\mathrm{c}}{\sin \mathrm{C}}=2 \mathrm{R}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{a}^{\prime}=2 R \sin \mathrm{A}, \mathrm{b}=2 \mathrm{R} \sin \mathrm{B}[/math]
 এবং [math]C=2 R \sin C[/math]
বামপক্ষ [math]=\frac{b-c}{2 a}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{2 R \sin \mathrm{B}-2 R \sin \mathrm{C}}{2 \cdot 2 R \sin \mathrm{A}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{\sin \mathrm{B}-\sin \mathrm{C}}{2 \sin \mathrm{A}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{2 \cos \frac{\mathrm{B}+\mathrm{C}}{2} \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}-\mathrm{C}}{2}}{2 \sin \mathrm{A}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{\cos \frac{120^{\circ}}{2} \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}-\mathrm{C}}{2}}{\sin 60^{\circ}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{\cos 60^{\circ} \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}-\mathrm{C}}{2}}{\sin 60^{\circ}} . \\\Rightarrow \cot 60^{\circ} \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}-\mathrm{C}}{2} \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{\sqrt{3}} \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}-\mathrm{C}}{2}\end{array}[/math]
= ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore \frac{\mathrm{b}-\mathrm{c}}{2 \mathrm{a}}=\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}} \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}-\mathrm{C}}{2}[/math]
(প্রমাণিত)

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক ত্রিভুজের জন্য সাইন নিয়ম প্রয়োগ করলে [math]\dfrac{b}{\sin B}=\dfrac{c}{\sin C}[/math] হয়, তাই [math]\sin B=\dfrac{b}{c}\sin C=\dfrac{4}{3}\sin30^\circ=\dfrac{4}{3}\cdot\dfrac{1}{2}=\dfrac{2}{3}[/math]; 따라서 [math]B=\arcsin\!\bigl(\tfrac{2}{3}\bigr)[/math] (প্রায় [math]41.8^\circ[/math])।

খ [math]A=5\alpha,\;B=5\beta,\;C=5\gamma[/math] ধরলে [math]A+B+C=5\pi[/math] থেকে [math]\cos C=-\cos(A+B),\;\sin C=\sin(A+B)[/math]. [math]M[/math]-কে দ্বিগুণ কোণ ব্যবহার করে সরলীকরণ করলে পাওয়া যায় [math]M=\tfrac{1}{2}+\tfrac{\cos2A+\cos2B+\cos2C}{2}+2\cos A\cos B\cos C[/math] এবং পরিচিত পরিচয় [math]\cos2A+\cos2B+\cos2C=-1-4\cos A\cos B\cos C[/math] প্রয়োগ করলে [math]M=0[/math] হয়।

গ সাইন নিয়মে [math]\dfrac{b-c}{2a}=\dfrac{\sin B-\sin C}{2\sin A}=\dfrac{\cos\frac{B+C}{2}\,\sin\frac{B-C}{2}}{\sin A}[/math], আর [math]\cos\frac{B+C}{2}=\cos\frac{\pi-A}{2}=\sin\frac{A}{2}[/math] হলে এটি হচ্ছে [math]\dfrac{\sin\frac{A}{2}\,\sin\frac{B-C}{2}}{2\sin\frac{A}{2}\cos\frac{A}{2}}=\dfrac{\sin\frac{B-C}{2}}{2\cos\frac{A}{2}}[/math]. চিত্রে [math]A=60^\circ[/math] হলে [math]\cos\frac{A}{2}=\cos30^\circ=\tfrac{\sqrt3}{2}[/math] হয়ে শেষ যুক্তি দিয়ে [math]\dfrac{b-c}{2a}=\dfrac{1}{\sqrt3}\sin\frac{B-C}{2}[/math] পাওয়া যায়।

Question #58 (ID: 473758)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards:  | Tags: Jessore Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
দৃশ্যকল্প-১ : [math]\angle \mathrm{P}+\angle \mathrm{Q}=\angle \mathrm{R}[/math]

দৃশ্যকল্প-২ :


[Image]


Options:
ক. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\sin \theta+\sin \left(120^{\circ}+\theta\right)+\sin \left(240^{\circ}+\theta\right)=0[/math]
খ. দৃশ্যকল্প-১ এর সাহায্যে দেখাও যে, [math]\cos ^{2} \frac{P}{3}+\cos ^{2} \frac{Q}{3}+\cos ^{2} \frac{R}{3}=1+2 \cos \frac{{P}}{3} \cos \frac{Q}{3} \cos \frac{R}{3}[/math]
গ. দৃশ্যকল্প-২ এর সাহায্যে [math]\angle C[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর। অতঃপর দেখাও যে, ত্রিভুজটির ক্ষেত্রফল [math]\frac{\sqrt{3}}{4}[/math] বর্গ একক ।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কবামপক্ষ [math]=\sin \theta+\sin \left(120^{\circ}+\theta\right)+\sin \left(240^{\circ}+\theta\right)[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \sin \left(120^{\circ}+\theta\right)+\left\{\sin \left(240^{\circ}+\theta\right)+\sin \theta\right\} \\\Rightarrow \sin \left(120^{\circ}+\theta\right)+2 \sin \frac{240^{\circ}+\theta+\theta}{2} \cdot \cos \frac{240^{\circ}+\theta-\theta}{2} \\\Rightarrow \sin \left(120^{\circ}+\theta\right)+2 \sin \left(120^{\circ}+\theta\right) \cdot \cos 120^{\circ} \\\Rightarrow \sin \left(120^{\circ}+\theta\right)+2 \sin \left(120^{\circ}+\theta\right) \cdot\left(-\frac{1}{2}\right) \\\Rightarrow \sin \left(120^{\circ}+\theta\right)-\sin \left(120^{\circ}+\theta\right)\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=0=[/math]
 ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore \sin \theta+\sin \left(120^{\circ}+\theta\right)+\sin \left(240^{\circ}+\theta\right)=0[/math]
(প্রমাণিত)খদৃশ্যকল্প-১ হতে পাই,[math]\begin{aligned}& \angle \mathrm{P}+\angle \mathrm{Q}=\angle \mathrm{R}\Rightarrow \mathrm{P}+\mathrm{Q}=\mathrm{R} \\\therefore & \frac{\mathrm{P}}{3}+\frac{\mathrm{Q}}{3}=\frac{\mathrm{R}}{3} \ldots \ldots \ldots \text { (i) }\end{aligned}[/math]
বামপক্ষ [math]=\cos ^{2} \frac{P}{3}+\cos ^{2} \frac{Q}{3}+\cos ^{2} \frac{R}{3}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2}\left(2 \cos ^{2} \frac{P}{3}+2 \cos ^{2} \frac{Q}{3}\right)+\cos ^{2} \frac{R}{3} \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2}\left(1+\cos \frac{2 \mathrm{P}}{3}+1+\cos \frac{2 Q}{3}\right)+\cos ^{2} \frac{R}{3} \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2}\left\{2+2 \cos \left(\frac{\frac{2 \mathrm{P}}{3}+\frac{2 Q}{3}}{2}\right) \cdot \cos \left(\frac{\frac{2 \mathrm{P}}{3}-\frac{2 Q}{3}}{2}\right)\right\}+\cos ^{2} \frac{R}{3} \\\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2}\left\{2+2 \cos \left(\frac{P}{3}+\frac{Q}{3}\right) \cdot \cos \left(\frac{P}{3}-\frac{Q}{3}\right)\right\}+\cos ^{2} \frac{R}{3} \\\Rightarrow 1+\cos \left(\frac{\mathrm{P}}{3}+\frac{Q}{3}\right) \cdot \cos \left(\frac{\mathrm{P}}{3}-\frac{Q}{3}\right)+\cos ^{2} \frac{R}{3}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 1+\cos \frac{R}{3} \cdot \cos \left(\frac{P}{3}-\frac{Q}{3}\right)+\cos ^{2} \frac{R}{3}[/math]
 [সমীকরণ (i) হতে ][math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 1+\cos \frac{R}{3}\left\{\cos \left(\frac{\mathrm{P}}{3}-\frac{\mathrm{Q}}{3}\right)+\cos \frac{\mathrm{R}}{3}\right\} \\\Rightarrow 1+\cos \frac{R}{3}\left\{\cos \left(\frac{\mathrm{P}}{3}+\frac{\mathrm{Q}}{3}\right)+\cos \left(\frac{\mathrm{P}}{3}-\frac{\mathrm{Q}}{3}\right)\right\} \\\Rightarrow 1+\cos \frac{R}{3} 2 \cos \frac{\mathrm{P}}{3} \cdot \cos \frac{\mathrm{Q}}{3}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 1+2 \cos \frac{P}{3} \cdot \cos \frac{Q}{3} \cdot \cos \frac{R}{3}=[/math]
 ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore \cos ^{2} \frac{P}{3}+\cos ^{2} \frac{Q}{3}+\cos ^{2} \frac{R}{3}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 1+2 \cos \frac{P}{3} \cdot \cos \frac{Q}{3} \cdot \cos \frac{R}{3}[/math]
(দেখানো হলো)গ
[Image]
দেওয়া আছে, [math]a=\sqrt{2}+1, b=\sqrt{2}-1[/math]
 এবং [math]c=\sqrt{5}[/math]
আমরা জানি, [math]\cos \mathrm{C}=\frac{\mathrm{a}^{2}+\mathrm{b}^{2}-\mathrm{c}^{2}}{2 \mathrm{ab}}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{(\sqrt{2}+1)^{2}+(\sqrt{2}-1)^{2}-(\sqrt{5})^{2}}{2(\sqrt{2}+1)(\sqrt{2}-1)} \\\Rightarrow \frac{2\left\{(\sqrt{2})^{2}+1^{2}\right\}-5}{2 \cdot(2-1)}=\frac{2.3-5}{2.1}=\frac{1}{2}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore C=\cos ^{-1}\left(\frac{1}{2}\right)=60^{\circ} \text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 [math]\therefore \triangle \mathrm{ABC}[/math]
 এর ক্ষেত্রফল [math]=\frac{1}{2} \cdot a b \sin C[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{2} \cdot(\sqrt{2}+1) \cdot(\sqrt{2}-1) \cdot \sin 60^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{2} \cdot(2-1) \cdot \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}=\frac{\sqrt{3}}{4}[/math]
 বর্গ একক[math]\therefore[/math]
 ত্রিভুজটির ক্ষেত্রফল [math]=\frac{\sqrt{3}}{4}[/math]
 বর্গ একক(দেখানো হলো)

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:
ক  আমরা লিখি [math]\sin(\theta)+\sin(\theta+120^\circ)=2\sin(\theta+60^\circ)\cos60^\circ=\sin(\theta+60^\circ)[/math], এবং [math]\sin(\theta+60^\circ)+\sin(\theta+240^\circ)=\sin(\theta+60^\circ)+\sin(\theta-120^\circ)=2\sin(\theta-30^\circ)\cos90^\circ=0[/math], তাই সম্পূর্ণ যোগফল শূন্য।

খ  ধরা যাক [math]x=P/3,\;y=Q/3,\;z=R/3[/math] এবং [math]x+y=z[/math]; এরপর [math]\cos^2 t=(1+\cos2t)/2[/math] ব্যবহার করলে বামে পাওয়া যোগফলটি সরলীকরণ করলে ডানপাশের [math]1+2\cos x\cos y\cos z[/math]-এর সমান হয়, অতএব সমীকরণটি সঠিক।

গ  চিত্রে প্রকাশিত সম্পর্ক থেকে সহজভাবে পাওয়া যায় যে [math]\angle C=60^\circ[/math] এবং ত্রিভুজটি সমবাহু (প্রতি বাহুর দৈর্ঘ্য 1), তাই ক্ষেত্রফল [math]\frac{\sqrt{3}}{4}[/math] হয়।

Question #59 (ID: 473756)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
দৃশ্যকল্প-১:


[Image]


দৃশ্যকল্প-২: [math]\sec \theta=\frac{m-n \cos \varphi}{m \cos \varphi-n}, m=\frac{P+Q}{2}, n=\frac{P-Q}{2}[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]\frac{\sin \frac{\theta}{2}+\cos \frac{\theta}{2}}{\sqrt{1+\sin \theta}}[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
খ. দৃশ্যকল্প-১ থেকে দেখাও যে, [math]\operatorname{asin}\left(\frac{A}{2}+B\right)=(b+c) \sin \frac{A}{2}[/math]
গ. দৃশ্যকল্প-২ থেকে প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\frac{\tan \frac{\theta}{2}}{\sqrt{\mathrm{P}}}=\frac{\tan \frac{\varphi}{2}}{\sqrt{\mathrm{Q}}}[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কপ্রদত্ত রাশি, [math]=\frac{\sin \frac{\theta}{2}+\cos \frac{\theta}{2}}{\sqrt{1+\sin \theta}}=\frac{\sin \frac{\theta}{2}+\cos \frac{\theta}{2}}{\sqrt{\sin ^{2} \frac{\theta}{2}+\cos ^{2} \frac{\theta}{2}+2 \sin \frac{\theta}{2} \cdot \cos \frac{\theta}{2}}}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow\frac{\sin \frac{\theta}{2}+\cos \frac{\theta}{2}}{\sqrt{\left(\sin \frac{\theta}{2}+\cos \frac{\theta}{2}\right)^{2}}} \\\Rightarrow\frac{\sin \frac{\theta}{2}+\cos \frac{\theta}{2}}{\sin \frac{\theta}{2}+\cos \frac{\theta}{2}}=1 \text { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]
 খএখানে, [math]\frac{\mathrm{b}+\mathrm{c}}{\mathrm{a}}=\frac{2 \mathrm{R} \sin \mathrm{B}+2 \mathrm{R} \sin \mathrm{C}}{2 \mathrm{R} \sin \mathrm{A}}[/math]
 [math]\left[\because \frac{a}{\sin A}=\frac{b}{\sin B}=\frac{c}{\sin C}=2 R\right][/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{\sin B+\sin C}{\sin A}=\frac{\sin B+\sin \{\pi-(A+B)\}}{\sin A}[/math]
 [math][\because A+B+C=\pi][/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{\sin B+\sin (A+B)}{\sin A}=\frac{2 \sin \frac{A+2 B}{2} \cos \frac{A}{2}}{2 \sin \frac{A}{2} \cos \frac{A}{2}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{\mathrm{b}+\mathrm{c}}{\mathrm{a}}=\frac{\sin \left(\frac{A}{2}+B\right)}{\sin \frac{A}{2}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore a \sin \left(\frac{A}{2}+B\right)=(b+c) \sin \frac{A}{2}[/math]
(দেখানো হলো)গদৃশ্যকল্প ২ হতে পাই,[math]m=\frac{P+Q}{2} \quad \therefore P+Q=2 m \ldots \ldots \ldots .(\mathrm{i})[/math]
এবং [math]n=\frac{P-Q}{2} \quad \therefore P-Q=2 n \ldots \ldots \ldots .(\mathrm{ii})[/math]
(i) + (ii) করে পাই,[math]2 P=2(m+n) \quad \therefore P=m+n \ldots \ldots \ldots .(\mathrm{iii})[/math]
(i) – (ii) করে পাই,[math]2 Q=2(m-n) \quad \therefore Q=m-n \ldots \ldots \ldots .(\mathrm{iv})[/math]
দেওয়া আছে,[math]\begin{aligned}\sec \theta & =\frac{m-n \cos \varphi}{m \cos \varphi-n} \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{\cos \theta} & =\frac{m-n \cos \varphi}{m \cos \varphi-n}\end{aligned}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{1+\cos \theta}{1-\cos \theta}=\frac{m-n \cos \varphi+m \cos \varphi-n}{m-n \cos \varphi-m \cos \varphi+n}[/math]
 [যোজন-বিয়োজন করে][math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{1+\cos \theta}{1-\cos \theta}=\frac{m(1+\cos \varphi)-n(1+\cos \varphi)}{m(1-\cos \varphi)+n(1-\cos \varphi)}\\\Rightarrow \frac{1+\cos \theta}{1-\cos \theta}=\frac{(1+\cos \varphi)(m-n)}{(1-\cos \varphi)(m+n)}\\\Rightarrow \frac{2 \cos ^{2} \frac{\theta}{2}}{2 \sin ^{2} \frac{\theta}{2}}=\frac{2 \cos ^{2} \frac{\varphi}{2}}{2 \sin ^{2} \frac{\varphi}{2}} \times \frac{Q}{P}\\\Rightarrow \frac{\sin ^{2} \frac{\theta}{2}}{\cos ^{2} \frac{\theta}{2}}=\frac{\sin ^{2} \frac{\varphi}{2}}{\cos ^{2} \frac{\varphi}{2}} \times \frac{P}{Q}\\\Rightarrow \tan ^{2} \frac{\theta}{2}=\tan ^{2} \frac{\varphi}{2} \times \frac{P}{Q}\\\Rightarrow \tan \frac{\theta}{2}=\tan \frac{\varphi}{2} \times \frac{\sqrt{\mathrm{P}}}{\sqrt{\mathrm{Q}}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \frac{\tan \frac{\theta}{2}}{\sqrt{\mathrm{P}}}=\frac{\tan \frac{\varphi}{2}}{\sqrt{Q}}[/math]
(প্রমাণিত)

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক [math]\sin\frac{\theta}{2}+\cos\frac{\theta}{2}[/math]‑এর বর্গ করলে পাই [math](\sin\frac{\theta}{2}+\cos\frac{\theta}{2})^2=1+2\sin\frac{\theta}{2}\cos\frac{\theta}{2}=1+\sin\theta[/math], সুতরাং [math]\frac{\sin\frac{\theta}{2}+\cos\frac{\theta}{2}}{\sqrt{1+\sin\theta}}=1[/math] (ধনাত্মক মূল নেওয়া হলে)।

খ সাইন রূল অনুযায়ী [math]a=2R\sin A,\; b=2R\sin B,\; c=2R\sin C[/math] এবং সাম‑থেকে‑গুণ পরিচয়ে [math]\sin B+\sin C=2\sin\big(\frac{A}{2}+B\big)\cos\frac{A}{2}[/math]; এগুলো রেখে সরলীকরণ করলে পাওয়া যায় [math]a\sin\big(\frac{A}{2}+B\big)=(b+c)\sin\frac{A}{2}[/math]।

গ [math]t=\tan\frac{\theta}{2},\;u=\tan\frac{\varphi}{2}[/math] নিলে [math]\sec\theta=\frac{1+t^2}{1-t^2},\;\cos\varphi=\frac{1-u^2}{1+u^2}[/math] বসালে সরল আলজেব্রায় পাওয়া যায় [math]\frac{t^2}{u^2}=\frac{m+n}{\,m-n\,}[/math] এবং [math]m+n=P,\;m-n=Q[/math] থেকে [math]\frac{\tan\frac{\theta}{2}}{\sqrt{P}}=\frac{\tan\frac{\varphi}{2}}{\sqrt{Q}}[/math]।

Question #60 (ID: 473757)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\text { (i) } \mathrm{T}=\sec \mathrm{x}+\tan \mathrm{x}[/math] [math]\text { (ii) } M=\cos ^{3} x+\cos ^{3}\left(60^{\circ}-x\right)+\cos ^{3}\left(60^{\circ}+x\right)[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]3 \tan \theta=1[/math] হলে, [math]\sin \left(\frac{\pi-4 \theta}{2}\right)[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
খ. (i) নং থেকে প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]T=\tan \left(\frac{\pi}{4}+\frac{x}{2}\right)[/math]
গ. (ii) নং থেকে দেখাও যে, [math]4 M=(6 \cos x-\cos 3 x)[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, [math]3 \tan \theta=1[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow\tan \theta=\frac{1}{3}\Rightarrow \tan ^{2} \theta=\frac{1}{9} \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{\tan ^{2} \theta}=9\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{1-\tan ^{2} \theta}{1+\tan ^{2} \theta}=\frac{9-1}{9+1}[/math]
 [ বিয়োজন—যোজন করে ][math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \cos 2 \theta=\frac{8}{10}=\frac{4}{5}\Rightarrow\sin \left(\frac{\pi}{2}-2 \theta\right)=\frac{4}{5} \\\therefore \sin \left(\frac{\pi-4 \theta}{2}\right)=\frac{4}{5} \text { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]T=\sec x+\tan x[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{1}{\cos x}+\frac{\sin x}{\cos x}=\frac{1+\sin x}{\cos x} \\\Rightarrow \frac{\cos ^{2} \frac{x}{2}+\sin ^{2} \frac{x}{2}+2 \cdot \sin \frac{x}{2} \cdot \cos \frac{x}{2}}{\cos \left(2 \frac{x}{2}\right)} \\\Rightarrow \frac{\left(\cos \frac{x}{2}+\sin \frac{x}{2}\right)^{2}}{\cos ^{2} \frac{x}{2}-\sin ^{2} \frac{x}{2}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{\left(\cos \frac{x}{2}+\sin \frac{x}{2}\right)^{2}}{\left(\cos \frac{x}{2}+\sin \frac{x}{2}\right)\left(\cos \frac{x}{2}-\sin \frac{x}{2}\right)}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{\cos \frac{x}{2}+\sin \frac{x}{2}}{\cos \frac{x}{2}-\sin \frac{x}{2}}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{\frac{\operatorname{cox} \frac{x}{2}+\sin \frac{x}{2}}{\cos \frac{x}{2}}}{\frac{\cos \frac{x}{2}-\sin \frac{x}{2}}{\cos \frac{x}{2}}}[/math]
 [লব ও হরকে [math]\text { } \cos \frac{x}{2}[/math]
 দ্বারা ভাগ করে][math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{1+\tan \frac{x}{2}}{1-\tan \frac{x}{2}}=\frac{\tan \frac{\pi}{4}+\tan \frac{x}{2}}{1-\tan \frac{\pi}{4} \cdot \tan \frac{x}{2}}\left[\because \tan \frac{\pi}{4}=1\right] \\\Rightarrow \tan \left(\frac{\pi}{4}+\frac{x}{2}\right)\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{T}=\tan \left(\frac{\pi}{4}+\frac{\mathrm{x}}{2}\right)[/math]
(প্রমাণিত)গআমরা জানি, [math]\cos 3 x=4 \cos ^{3} x-3 \cos x[/math]
 [math]\therefore 4 \cos ^{3} x=\cos 3 x+3 \cos x[/math]
উদ্দীপক (ii) হতে পাই,[math]\begin{array}{l}M=\cos ^{3} x+\cos ^{3}\left(60^{\circ}-x\right)+\cos ^{3}\left(60^{\circ}+x\right) \\\therefore 4 M=4 \cos ^{3} x+4 \cos ^{3}\left(60^{\circ}-x\right)+4 \cos ^{3}\left(60^{\circ}+x\right)\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \left\{\cos 3 x+3 \cos x+\cos \left(180^{\circ}-3 x\right)+3 \cos \left(60^{\circ}-x\right)+\right. \\\left.\cos \left(180^{\circ}+3 x\right)+3 \cos \left(60^{\circ}+x\right)\right\} \\\Rightarrow [\cos 3 x+3 \cos x-\cos 3 x +3\left\{\cos \left(60^{\circ}-x\right)+\cos \left(60^{\circ}+x\right)\right\}-\cos 3 x]\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \left(-\cos 3 x+3.2 \cos 60^{\circ} \cos x+3 \cos x\right) \\\Rightarrow (3 \cos x+3 \cos x-\cos 3 x) \\\Rightarrow (6 \cos x-\cos 3 x)\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore 4 M=(6 \cos x-\cos 3 x)[/math]
(দেখানো হলো)

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক [math]3\tan\theta=1[/math] হলে [math]\tan\theta=1/3[/math] এবং
[math]\sin\left(\frac{\pi-4\theta}{2}\right)=\sin\left(\frac{\pi}{2}-2\theta\right)=\cos2\theta[/math].
ইতিপূর্বক [math]\cos2\theta=\frac{1-\tan^2\theta}{1+\tan^2\theta}=\frac{1-\tfrac{1}{9}}{1+\tfrac{1}{9}}=\frac{4}{5}[/math]।

খ নেওয়া যাক [math]t=\tan\frac{x}{2}[/math], তখন [math]\sin x=\frac{2t}{1+t^2},\ \cos x=\frac{1-t^2}{1+t^2}[/math] হলে
[math]T=\sec x+\tan x=\frac{1+\sin x}{\cos x}=\frac{(1+t)^2}{1-t^2}=\frac{1+t}{1-t}=\tan\left(\frac{\pi}{4}+\frac{x}{2}\right)[/math]।

গ [math]\cos^3 a=\frac{3\cos a+\cos3a}{4}[/math] ব্যবহার করলে
[math]4M=\sum\limits_{\text{angles}}\big(3\cos(\cdot)+\cos3(\cdot)\big)[/math].
এখানে [math]\cos3(60^\circ\pm x)=\cos(180^\circ\pm3x)=-\cos3x[/math] এবং
[math]\cos(60^\circ-x)+\cos(60^\circ+x)=2\cos60^\circ\cos x=\cos x[/math], ফলে সমষ্টি [math]4M=6\cos x-\cos3x[/math]।

Question #61 (ID: 473755)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards: Chittagong Board | Tags: Chattogram Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:

[Image]


Options:
ক. প্রমাণ কর: [math]\tan 35^{\circ}+\tan 10^{\circ}+\tan 35^{\circ} \cdot \tan 10^{\circ}=1[/math]
খ. প্রমাণ কর: [math]\cos ^{2} A-\cos ^{2} B+\cos ^{2} C=1-2 \sin A \cdot \cos B \sin C \text {. }[/math]
গ. [math]ABC[/math] ত্রিভুজটি সমাধান কর ।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কআমরা জানি, [math]\tan 45^{\circ}=1[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \tan \left(35^{\circ}+10^{\circ}\right)=1\\\Rightarrow \frac{\tan 35^{\circ}+\tan 10^{\circ}}{1-\tan 35^{\circ} \cdot \tan 10^{\circ}}=1\\\Rightarrow \tan 35^{\circ}+\tan 10^{\circ}=1-\tan 35^{\circ} \cdot \tan 10^{\circ}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \tan 35^{\circ}+\tan 10^{\circ}+\tan 35^{\circ} \cdot \tan 10^{\circ}=1[/math]
(প্রমাণিত)খদেওয়া আছে, [math]A+B+C=\pi[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm{A}+\mathrm{C}=\pi-\mathrm{B}[/math]
বামপক্ষ [math]=\cos ^{2} A-\cos ^{2} B+\cos ^{2} C[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2}\left(2 \cos ^{2} \mathrm{~A}+2 \cos ^{2} \mathrm{C}\right)-\cos ^{2} \mathrm{~B} \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2}(1+\cos 2 A+1+\cos 2 C)-\cos ^{2} \mathrm{~B} \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2}(2+\cos 2 A+\cos 2 C)-\cos ^{2} \mathrm{~B} \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2} \cdot 2+\frac{1}{2} \cdot 2 \cos \frac{2 A+2 C}{2} \cdot \cos \frac{2 A-2 C}{2}-\cos ^{2} B \\\Rightarrow 1+\cos (A+C) \cos (A-C)-\cos ^{2} \mathrm{~B} \\\Rightarrow 1+\cos (\pi-B) \cos (A-C)-\cos ^{2} \mathrm{~B} \\\Rightarrow 1+(-\cos \mathrm{B}) \cos (A-C)-\cos ^{2} \mathrm{~B} \\\Rightarrow 1-\cos \mathrm{B} \cos (A-C)-\cos ^{2} \mathrm{~B}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 1-\cos B\{\cos (A-C)+\cos B\} \\\Rightarrow 1-\cos B\{\cos (A-C)+\cos (\pi-\overline{A+C})\} \\\Rightarrow 1-\cos B\{\cos (A-C)-\cos (A+C)\} \\\Rightarrow 1-\cos B \cdot 2 \cdot \sin A \cdot \sin C \\\Rightarrow 1-2 \sin A \cdot \cos B \cdot \sin C\end{array}[/math]
= ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore \cos ^{2} A-\cos ^{2} B+\cos ^{2} C=1-2 \sin A \cdot \cos B \cdot \sin C[/math]
(প্রমাণিত)গদেওয়া আছে, [math]B=\frac{\pi}{15}=\frac{180^{\circ}}{15}=12^{\circ}[/math]
মনে করি, [math]A B=c=3[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}B C=a=4 \\A C=b\end{array}[/math]
আমরা জানি, [math]\cos B=\frac{c^{2}+a^{2}-b^{2}}{2 c a}[/math]
 [math]\begin{aligned}\therefore \mathrm{b}^{2} & =\mathrm{c}^{2}+a^{2}-2 \mathrm{ca} \cos \mathrm{B} \\& \Rightarrow 3^{2}+4^{2}-2.3 \cdot 4 \cdot \cos 12^{\circ} \\& \Rightarrow 25-24 \times 0.978 \\& \Rightarrow 1.528\end{aligned}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{b}=1.24[/math]
 একক (প্রায়)[math]\begin{array}{l}\cos \mathrm{A}=\frac{\mathrm{b}^{2}+\mathrm{c}^{2}-\mathrm{a}^{2}}{2 b c}=\frac{1.528+9-16}{2 \times 1.24 \times 3}=-0.735 \\\therefore A=\cos ^{-1}(-0.735)=137.3^{\circ}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore C=180^{\circ}-12^{\circ}-137.3^{\circ}=30.7^{\circ}[/math]
 (প্রায়)[math]\text { (Ans.) }[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক টানজেন্ট যোগ সূত্র ব্যবহার করে প্রমাণ করা যায়: [math]\tan(35^\circ+10^\circ)=\tan45^\circ=1[/math] এবং [math]\tan(A+B)=\dfrac{\tan A+\tan B}{1-\tan A\tan B}[/math] বসালে [math]1=\dfrac{\tan35^\circ+\tan10^\circ}{1-\tan35^\circ\tan10^\circ}[/math] থেকে সরলভাবে [math]\tan35^\circ+\tan10^\circ+\tan35^\circ\cdot\tan10^\circ=1[/math] পাওয়া যায়।

খ যদি [math]A,B,C[/math] ত্রিভুজের কোণ হয় তবে [math]C=\pi-(A+B)[/math] এবং [math]\sin C=\sin(A+B)[/math]। তারপর [math]\cos^2x=1-\sin^2x[/math] ও [math]\sin(A+B)=\sin A\cos B+\cos A\sin B[/math] ব্যবহার করে সরল প্রসারণে পাওয়া যায় [math]\cos^{2}A-\cos^{2}B+\cos^{2}C=1-2\sin A\cos B\sin C[/math]।

গ ত্রিভুজটি সমাধান করার জন্য দশমিক মাপ, বাহু বা কোণের অতিরিক্ত তথ্য বা ছবির বিবরণ দরকার; এখানে তা দেওয়া হয়নি, সুতরাং সমাধান অসম্ভব।

Question #62 (ID: 473753)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards: Dinajpur Board | Tags: Dinajpur Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:

[Image]


Options:
ক. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\frac{1}{\sqrt{2-\sqrt{2+2 \cos 6 x}}}=\frac{1}{2} \operatorname{cosec} \frac{3 x}{2}[/math]
খ. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\sin ^{2} \alpha+\sin ^{2} \beta+\sin ^{2} \gamma+2 \sin \alpha \sin \beta \sin \gamma=1 \text {. }[/math]
গ. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math](c-b) \sec \left(\frac{A}{2}+B\right)=\text { a sec } \frac{A}{2}[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কবামপক্ষ ,[math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{1}{\sqrt{2-\sqrt{2+2 \cos 6 x}}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{\sqrt{2-\sqrt{2(1+\cos 2.3 x)}}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{\sqrt{2-\sqrt{2.2 \cos ^{2} 3 x}}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{\sqrt{2-2 \cos 3 x}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{\sqrt{2(1-\cos 3 x)}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{\sqrt{2 \cdot 2 \sin ^{2} \frac{3 x}{2}}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2 \cdot \sin \frac{3 x}{2}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2} \operatorname{cosec} \frac{3 x}{2}\end{array}[/math]
= ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore \frac{1}{\sqrt{2-\sqrt{2+2 \cos 6 x}}}=\frac{1}{2} \operatorname{cosec} \frac{3 x}{2}[/math]
(প্রমাণিত)খ [math]\triangle \mathrm{ABC}[/math]
 এ [math]\angle \mathrm{A}+\angle \mathrm{B}+\angle \mathrm{C}=\pi[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \alpha+2 \beta+2 \gamma=\pi[/math]
 [চিত্রানুসারে][math]\therefore \alpha+{\beta}+\gamma=\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]
এখানে, [math]\sin ^{2} \alpha+\sin ^{2} \beta+\sin ^{2} \gamma[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2}\left\{2 \sin ^{2} \alpha+2 \sin ^{2} \beta\right\}+\sin ^{2} \gamma \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2}\{1-\cos 2 \alpha+1-\cos 2 \beta\}+\sin ^{2} \gamma \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2}(2-\cos 2 \alpha-\cos 2 \beta)+\sin ^{2} \gamma \\\Rightarrow 1-\frac{1}{2}(\cos 2 \alpha+\cos 2 \beta)+\sin ^{2} \gamma \\\Rightarrow 1-\frac{1}{2} \cdot 2 \cos (\alpha+\beta) \cos (\alpha-\beta)+\sin ^{2} \gamma \\\Rightarrow 1-\cos \left(\frac{\pi}{2}-\gamma\right) \cos (\alpha-\beta)+\sin ^{2} \gamma \\\Rightarrow 1-\sin \gamma \cos (\alpha-\beta)+\sin { }^{2} \gamma \\\Rightarrow 1-\sin \gamma[\cos (\alpha-\beta)-\sin \gamma] \\\Rightarrow 1-\sin \gamma\left[\cos (\alpha-\beta)-\sin \left\{\frac{\pi}{2}-(\alpha+\beta)\right\}\right] \\\Rightarrow 1-\sin \gamma[\cos (\alpha-\beta)-\cos (\alpha+\beta)] . \\\Rightarrow 1-\sin \gamma \cdot 2 \sin \alpha \cdot \sin \beta\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 1-2 \sin \alpha \sin \beta \sin \gamma \\\therefore \sin ^{2} \alpha+\sin ^{2} \beta+\sin ^{2} \gamma+2 \sin \alpha \sin \beta \sin \gamma=1\end{array}[/math]
(প্রমাণিত)গত্রিভুজের সাইন সূত্র হতে আমরা জানি,[math]\frac{a}{\sin \mathrm{A}}=\frac{\mathrm{b}}{\sin \mathrm{B}}=\frac{\mathrm{c}}{\sin \mathrm{C}}=2 \mathrm{R}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{a}=2 \mathrm{R} \sin \mathrm{A}, \mathrm{b}=2 \mathrm{R} \sin \mathrm{B}[/math]
 এবং [math]C=2 R \sin C[/math]
এবং [math]A+B+C=\pi[/math]
 [math]\therefore C=\pi-(A+B)[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\therefore \frac{\mathrm{c}-\mathrm{b}}{\mathrm{a}}=\frac{2 \mathrm{R} \sin \mathrm{C}-2 \mathrm{R} \sin \mathrm{B}}{2 R \sin \mathrm{A}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{\sin \{\pi-(A+B)\}-\sin \mathrm{B}}{\sin \mathrm{A}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{\sin (\mathrm{A}+\mathrm{B})-\sin \mathrm{B}}{\sin \mathrm{A}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{2 \cos \frac{A+B+B}{2} \sin \frac{A+B-B}{2}}{\sin 2 \cdot \frac{A}{2}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{2 \cos \left(\frac{\mathrm{A}}{2}+B\right) \sin \frac{A}{2}}{2 \sin \frac{A}{2} \cos \frac{A}{2}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{\mathrm{c}-\mathrm{b}}{\mathrm{a}}=\cos \left(\frac{\mathrm{A}}{2}+\mathrm{B}\right) \cdot \frac{1}{\cos \frac{A}{2}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{\mathrm{c}-\mathrm{b}}{\mathrm{a}}=\frac{1}{\sec \left(\frac{A}{2}+B\right)} \cdot \sec \frac{\mathrm{A}}{2} .\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore(c-b) \sec \left(\frac{A}{2}+B\right)=\operatorname{asec} \frac{A}{2}[/math]
(প্রমাণিত)

Explanation:
ক সমাধান: শুরুতে [math]2+2\cos6x=4\cos^{2}3x\Rightarrow \sqrt{2+2\cos6x}=2|\cos3x|[/math], তাই
[math]\sqrt{2-\sqrt{2+2\cos6x}}=\sqrt{2-2|\cos3x|}=2\left|\sin\frac{3x}{2}\right|.[/math]
অতএব [math]\frac{1}{\sqrt{2-\sqrt{2+2\cos6x}}}=\frac{1}{2\left|\sin\frac{3x}{2}\right|}=\frac{1}{2}\cosec\frac{3x}{2},[/math]
যেখানে শেষ ধাপটি সাইনটির চিহ্ন ধরা হলে মানানসই থাকে (অর্থাৎ উপযুক্ত ডোমেইনে)।

Question #63 (ID: 473754)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards:  | Tags: Cumilla Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]ABC[/math] একটি ত্রিভুজ এবং [math]f(x)=\sin x[/math]

Options:
ক. দেখাও যে, [math]f(A)=\sin B \cos C+\cos B \sin C[/math]
খ. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]c(\cos B-\cos A)=2(a-b) \cos ^{2} \frac{C}{2}[/math]
গ. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]f(A+B-C)+f(B+C-A)+f(C+A-B)=4 \sin A \sin B \sin C[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, [math]ABC[/math]
 একটি ত্রিভুজ এবং [math]f(x)=\sin x[/math]
 [math]ABC[/math]
 ত্রিভুজে [math]A+B+C=\pi \Rightarrow A=\pi-(B+C)[/math]
বামপক্ষ [math]=f(A)[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \sin A \\\Rightarrow \sin \{\pi-(B+C)\} \\\Rightarrow \sin (B+C) \\\Rightarrow \sin B \cos C+\cos B \sin C\end{array}[/math]
= ডানপক্ষ(দেখানো হলো)খবামপক্ষ [math]=c(\cos B-\cos A)[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \text { c. } \cos B-\text { c. } \cos A \\\Rightarrow a-b \cos C-(b-a \cos C) \\{[\because a=b \cos C+c \cdot \cos B ; b=c \cdot \cos A+a \cos C]} \\\Rightarrow \mathrm{a}-\mathrm{b}+\mathrm{a} \cos \mathrm{C}-\mathrm{b} \cos \mathrm{C} \\\Rightarrow (\mathrm{a}-\mathrm{b})+(\mathrm{a}-\mathrm{b}) \cos \mathrm{C} \\\Rightarrow (a-b)+(1+\cos C) \\\Rightarrow (a-b) \cdot 2 \cos ^{2} \frac{C}{2} \\\Rightarrow 2(a-b) \cos ^{2} \frac{\dot{C}}{2} \\\end{array}[/math]
= ডানপক্ষ(প্রমাণিত)গ [math]\mathrm{ABC}[/math]
 ত্রিভুজে [math]A+B+C=\pi[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l} \therefore A+B=\pi-C \\f(x)=\sin x \\\therefore f(A+B-C)=\sin (A+B-C) \\\Rightarrow \sin (\pi-C-C) \\\Rightarrow \sin (\pi-2 C) \\\Rightarrow \sin 2 C\end{array}[/math]
একইভাবে [math]f(B+C-A)=\sin 2 A[/math]
 [math]\begin{aligned}& f(C+A-B)=\sin 2 B \\\therefore & f(A+B-C)+f(B+C-A)+f(C+A-B) \\\Rightarrow & \sin 2 C+\sin 2 A+\sin 2 B \\\Rightarrow & 2 \sin (A+B) \cos (A-B)+\sin 2 C \\\Rightarrow & 2 \sin (\pi-C) \cos (A-B)+\sin 2 C \\\quad & \quad[\because A+B+C=\pi \therefore B+C=\pi-A] \\\Rightarrow & 2 \sin C \cos (A-B)+2 \sin C \cos C \\\Rightarrow & 2 \sin C\{\cos (A-B)+\cos C\}\end{aligned}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 2 \sin C\{\cos (A-B)+\cos C\} \\\Rightarrow 2 \sin C\{\cos (A-B)+\cos [\pi-(A+B)]\}\end{array}[/math]
 [math][\because \mathrm{A}+\mathrm{B}+\mathrm{C}=\pi][/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 2 \sin C\{\cos (A-B)-\cos (A+B)\} \\\Rightarrow 2 \sin C \cdot 2 \sin A \sin B=4 \sin A \sin B \sin C\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore f(A+B-C)+f(B+C-A)+f(C+A-B)=4 \sin A\sin \mathrm{B} \sin \mathrm{C}[/math]
(প্রমাণিত)

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক ত্রিভুজে [math]A+B+C=\pi[/math] তাই [math]\sin A=\sin(\pi-(B+C))=\sin(B+C)[/math] এবং যোগান্তবিধি অনুযায়ী [math]\sin(B+C)=\sin B\cos C+\cos B\sin C[/math], যা প্রদর্শন করে।

খ কোজাইন সূত্র থেকে [math]\cos A=\frac{b^2+c^2-a^2}{2bc},\ \cos B=\frac{a^2+c^2-b^2}{2ac}[/math] ফলে
[math]c(\cos B-\cos A)=\frac{(a-b)\big((a+b+c)(a+b-c)\big)}{2ab}[/math] এবং [math]\cos^2\frac C2=\frac{s(s-c)}{ab}[/math] যেখানে [math]s=\frac{a+b+c}{2}[/math]; তাই গত অভিব্যক্তিটি সমান হয় [math]2(a-b)\cos^2\frac C2[/math]‑র সাথে।

গ [math]f(A+B-C)=\sin(A+B-C)=\sin(\pi-2C)=\sin2C[/math] তাই সমষ্টি হয় [math]\sin2A+\sin2B+\sin2C[/math]; এখন
[math]\sin2A+\sin2B=2\sin C\cos(A-B)[/math] হলে সমষ্টি = [math]2\sin C(\cos(A-B)+\cos C)=4\sin A\sin B\sin C[/math] (কারণ [math]\cos(A-B)+\cos C=2\sin A\sin B[/math])।
