Question #64 (ID: 473751)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards: Rajshahi Board | Tags: Rajshahi Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:

[Image]


Options:
ক. [math]\mathrm{a}=\sqrt{3}+1, \bar{b}=\sqrt{3}-1, \mathrm{C}=60^{c}[/math] হলে, [math]\triangle \mathrm{ABC}[/math] এ [math]c[/math] বাহুর দৈর্ঘ্য নির্ণয় কর।
খ. [math]A+B=120^{\circ}[/math] হলে, উদ্দীপকের আলোকে দেখাও যে, [math]\sin ^{2}(\theta+\alpha)+\sin ^{2}(\theta-\alpha)-\cos ^{2} \alpha=\frac{1}{2}[/math]
গ. উদ্দীপকের আলোকে প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\sin 2 A-\sin 2 B+\sin 2 C=-4 \cos A \sin B \cos 2 \theta[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, [math]a=\sqrt{3}+1, b=\sqrt{3}-1[/math]
 এবং [math]C=60^{\circ}[/math]
আমরা জানি, [math]c^{2}=a^{2}+b^{2}-2 a b \cos C[/math]
 [math]\begin{aligned}\therefore c^{2} & =(\sqrt{3}+1)^{2}+(\sqrt{3}-1)^{2}-2(\sqrt{3}+1)(\sqrt{3}-1) \cos 60^{\circ} \\& \Rightarrow 2(3+1)-2(3-1) \cdot \frac{1}{2}=8-2=6\end{aligned}[/math]
 [math]\therefore c=\sqrt{6}[/math]
 একক [math]\text { (Ans.) }[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]A+B=120^{\circ}[/math]
চিত্রানুযায়ী, [math]\triangle \mathrm{ABC}[/math]
 এর বহিঃস্থ [math]\angle A C D=2 \theta[/math]
 [math]=A+B=120^{\circ} \therefore \theta=60^{\circ}[/math]
বামপক্ষ [math]=\sin ^{2}(\theta+\alpha)+\sin ^{2}(\theta-\alpha)-\cos ^{2} \alpha[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2}\left[2 \sin ^{2}(\theta+\alpha)+2 \sin ^{2}(\theta-\alpha)-2 \cos ^{2} \alpha\right] \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2}\left[1-\cos 2(\theta+\alpha)+1-\cos 2(\theta-\alpha)-2 \cos ^{2} \alpha\right] \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2}\left[2-\cos (2 \theta+2 \alpha)-\cos (2 \theta-2 \alpha)-2 \cos ^{2} \alpha\right] \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2}\left[2-\left\{\cos \left(120^{\circ}+2 \alpha\right)+\cos \left(120^{\circ}-2 \alpha\right)\right\}-2 \cos ^{2} \alpha\right] \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2}\left[2-\left\{2 \cos 120^{\circ} \cdot \cos 2 \alpha\right\}-2 \cos ^{2} \alpha\right] \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2}\left[2-2 \times\left(-\frac{1}{2}\right) \cdot \cos 2 \alpha-2 \cos ^{2} \alpha\right] \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2}\left[2+\cos 2 \alpha-2 \cos ^{2} \alpha\right]=\frac{1}{2}(2+\cos 2 \alpha-1-\cos 2 \alpha)\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{2}=[/math]
 ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore \sin ^{2}(\theta+\alpha)+\sin ^{2}(\theta-\alpha)-\cos ^{2} \alpha=\frac{1}{2}[/math]
(দেখানো হলো)গবামপক্ষ [math]=\sin 2 A-\sin 2 B+\sin 2 C[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 2 \cos (A+B) \sin (A-B)+\sin 2 C \\\Rightarrow 2 \cos (\pi-C) \sin (A-B)+\sin 2 C \\\quad[\because A+B+C=\pi]\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow -2 \cos C \sin (A-B)+2 \sin C \cdot \cos C \\\Rightarrow 2 \cos C\{\sin C-\sin (A-B)\} \\\Rightarrow 2 \cos C[\sin \{\pi-(A+B)\}-\sin (A-B)\}] \\\Rightarrow 2 \cos C\{\sin (A+B)-\sin (A-B)\} \\\Rightarrow 2 \cos C \cdot 2 \cos A \sin B \\\Rightarrow 4 \cos A \sin \mathrm{B} \cos C \\\Rightarrow 4 \cos \mathrm{A} \sin \mathrm{B} \cdot \cos \left(180^{\circ}-2 \theta\right)\left[\because C+2 \theta=180^{\circ}\right] \\\Rightarrow -4 \cos \mathrm{A} \cdot \sin \mathrm{B} \cdot \cos 2 \theta\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \sin 2 \mathrm{~A}-\sin 2 \mathrm{~B}+\sin 2 \mathrm{C}=-4 \cos \mathrm{A} \sin \mathrm{B} \cos 2 \theta[/math]
(প্রমাণিত)

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক  Law of cosines প্রয়োগ করে, [math]c^2=a^2+b^2-2ab\cos C[/math]. এখানে [math]a^2+b^2=(\sqrt3+1)^2+(\sqrt3-1)^2=8[/math], এবং [math]2ab\cos60^\circ=2\cdot(\sqrt3+1)(\sqrt3-1)\cdot\frac12=2[/math], তাই [math]c^2=8-2=6[/math] এবং [math]c=\sqrt6[/math]।

খ  যেহেতু [math]A+B=120^\circ[/math], তাই [math]\theta=(A+B)/2=60^\circ[/math]; এরপর [math]\sin^2x=(1-\cos2x)/2[/math] প্রয়োগ করলে ফল বের হয়: [math]1-\tfrac12[\cos2(60^\circ+\alpha)+\cos2(60^\circ-\alpha)]-\cos^2\alpha=\tfrac12[/math], কারণ [math]\cos2(60^\circ+\alpha)+\cos2(60^\circ-\alpha)=-\cos2\alpha[/math] এবং [math]\cos^2\alpha=(1+\cos2\alpha)/2[/math]।

গ  শুরুতে [math]\sin2A-\sin2B=2\cos(A+B)\sin(A-B)[/math] এবং [math]C=180^\circ-(A+B)[/math] হওয়ায় [math]\sin2C=-2\sin(A+B)\cos(A+B)[/math]; তাই যোগ করলে [math]\sin2A-\sin2B+\sin2C=2\cos(A+B)[\sin(A-B)-\sin(A+B)]=-4\cos A\sin B\cos(A+B)[/math], এখানে [math]\cos2\theta=\cos(A+B)[/math] ব্যবহার করলে দাবি প্রমাণিত।

Question #65 (ID: 473752)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards: Rajshahi Board | Tags: Rajshahi Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:

[Image]


Options:
ক. [math]\cos \alpha \cdot \cos \beta-\sin \alpha \cdot \sin \beta=1[/math] হলে, দেখাও যে, [math]\sin \alpha \operatorname{cosec} \beta+\cos \alpha \sec \beta=0[/math]
খ. [math]C=75^{\circ}[/math] হলে উদ্দীপক হতে দেখাও যে, [math]\sec 2 A-\sqrt{3} \operatorname{cosec} 2 A=4[/math]
গ. উদ্দীপক ব্যবহার করে প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\frac{a^{2}}{b c} \sin (B-C)+\frac{b^{2}}{c a} \sin (C-A)+\frac{c^{2}}{a b} \sin (A-B)=0[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কদেওয়া আছে, [math]\cos \alpha \cos \beta-\sin \alpha \cdot \sin \beta=1[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow\cos (\alpha+\beta)=\cos 0 \\\Rightarrow \alpha+\beta=0 \\\therefore \alpha=-\beta\end{array}[/math]
বামপক্ষ [math]=\sin \alpha \cdot \operatorname{cosec} \beta+\cos \alpha \cdot \sec \beta[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow\sin (-\beta) \operatorname{cosec} \beta+\cos (-\beta) \cdot \sec \beta \\\Rightarrow-\sin \beta \cdot \frac{1}{\sin \beta}+\cos \beta \cdot \frac{1}{\cos \beta} \\\Rightarrow-1+1=0\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow[/math]
 ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore \sin \alpha \operatorname{cosec} \beta+\cos \alpha \sec \beta=0[/math]
(দেখানো হলো)খদেওয়া আছে, [math]C=75^{\circ}[/math]
 এবং চিত্র হতে পাই, [math]B=65^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\triangle \mathrm{ABC}[/math]
 এ [math]A+B+C=180^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow A+65^{\circ}+75^{\circ}=180^{\circ} \\\therefore A=40^{\circ}\end{array}[/math]
বামপক্ষ [math]=\sec 2 A-\sqrt{3} \operatorname{cosec} 2 A[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \sec \left(2 \times 40^{\circ}\right)-\sqrt{3} \operatorname{cosec}\left(2 \times 40^{\circ}\right) \\\Rightarrow \sec 80^{\circ}-\sqrt{3} \operatorname{cosec} 80^{\circ} \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{\cos 80^{\circ}}-\frac{\sqrt{3}}{\sin 80^{\circ}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{\sin 80^{\circ}-\sqrt{3} \cos 80^{\circ}}{\sin 80^{\circ} \cdot \cos 80^{\circ}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{\frac{1}{2} \sin 80^{\circ}-\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2} \cos 80^{\circ}}{\frac{1}{4} \cdot 2 \sin 80^{\circ} \cos 80^{\circ}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{\sin 80^{\circ} \cdot \cos 60^{\circ}-\sin 60^{\circ} \cdot \cos 80^{\circ}}{\frac{1}{4} \cdot \sin 160^{\circ}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{4 \sin \left(80^{\circ}-60^{\circ}\right)}{\sin \left(180^{\circ}-160^{\circ}\right)}=\frac{4 \sin 20^{\circ}}{\sin 20^{\circ}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=4=[/math]
 ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore \sec 2 A-\sqrt{3} \operatorname{cosec} 2 A=4[/math]
(দেখানো হলো)গপ্রদত্ত রাশি, [math]=\frac{a^{2}}{b c} \sin (B-C)+\frac{b^{2}}{c a} \sin (C-A)+\frac{c^{2}}{a b} \sin (A-B)[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{a b c}{a b c}\left[\frac{a^{2}}{b c} \sin (B-C)+\frac{b^{2}}{c a} \sin (C-A)+\frac{c^{2}}{a b} \sin (A-B)\right] \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{a b c}\left[a^{3} \sin (B-C)+b^{3} \sin (C-A)+c^{3} \sin (A-B)\right]\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{\mathrm{abc}}[\mathrm{P}+\mathrm{Q}+\mathrm{R}][/math]
ধরি,[math]\left[\begin{array}{r}P=a^{3} \sin (B-C) \\Q=b^{3} \sin (C-A) \\R=c^{3} \sin (A-B)\end{array}\right][/math]
এখন, [math]P=a^{3} \sin (B-C)[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow a^{2} \cdot a \cdot \sin (B-C) \\\Rightarrow a^{2} \cdot 2 R \sin A \sin (B-C) \\\Rightarrow a^{2} \cdot 2 R \cdot \sin \{\pi-(B+C)\} \sin (B-C) \\\Rightarrow 2 R \cdot a^{2} \sin (B+C) \sin (B-C) \\\Rightarrow 2 R \cdot a^{2}\left(\sin ^{2} \mathrm{~B}-\sin ^{2} C\right) \\\Rightarrow 2 R \cdot a^{2}\left(\frac{b^{2}}{4 R^{2}}-\frac{c^{2}}{4 R^{2}}\right) . \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2 R}\left(a^{2} b^{2}-a^{2} c^{2}\right)\end{array}[/math]
অনুরূপভাবে, [math]\mathrm{Q}=\frac{1}{2 \mathrm{R}}\left(\mathrm{b}^{2} \mathrm{c}^{2}-\mathrm{a}^{2} \mathrm{~b}^{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]R=\frac{1}{2 R}\left(c^{2} a^{2}-b^{2} c^{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\therefore \frac{1}{a b c}(P+Q+R) \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{a b c}\left[\frac{1}{2 R}\left(a^{2} b^{2}-a^{2} c^{2}\right)+\frac{1}{2 R}\left(b^{2} c^{2}-a^{2} b^{2}\right)+\frac{1}{2 R}\left(c^{2} a^{2}-b^{2} c^{2}\right)\right] \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2 R \cdot a b c}\left(a^{2} b^{2}-a^{2} c^{2}+b^{2} c^{2}-a^{2} b^{2}+c^{2} a^{2}-b^{2} c^{2}\right) \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2 R \cdot a b c} \cdot 0=0 \\\therefore \frac{a^{2}}{b c} \sin (B-C)+\frac{b^{2}}{c a} \sin (C-A)+\frac{c^{2}}{a b} \sin (A-B)=0\end{array}[/math]
(প্রমাণিত)

Explanation:
ক প্রদত্ত সমিকরণটি থেকে [math]\cos(\alpha+\beta)=1[/math], সুতরাং [math]\sin(\alpha+\beta)=0[/math]; তাই
[math]\sin\alpha\csc\beta+\cos\alpha\sec\beta=\frac{\sin\alpha}{\sin\beta}+\frac{\cos\alpha}{\cos\beta}
=\frac{\sin\alpha\cos\beta+\cos\alpha\sin\beta}{\sin\beta\cos\beta}
=\frac{\sin(\alpha+\beta)}{\sin\beta\cos\beta}=0.[/math]

খ ভুয়া — একটি counterexample: তিনভুজে যদি [math]C=75^\circ,\ A=60^\circ[/math] নেয়া হয় (তাহলে [math]B=45^\circ[/math]), তখন [math]2A=120^\circ[/math] এবং
[math]\sec120^\circ-\sqrt3\csc120^\circ=-2-\sqrt3\cdot\frac{2}{\sqrt3}=-4\neq4.[/math]

গ সঠিক — সাইন মতে [math]a=2R\sin A,\ b=2R\sin B,\ c=2R\sin C[/math] হলে প্রতিটি অঙ্কটি হয় [math]\dfrac{\sin^2A}{\sin B\sin C}\sin(B-C)[/math] ইত্যাদি; [math]\sin(B-C)=\sin B\cos C-\cos B\sin C[/math] ব্যবহার করে প্রতিটি বিস্তারে ধনাত্মক ও ঋণাত্মক সদস্যগুলো জোড়ায় জোড়ায় কেটে গিয়ে সমষ্টি শূন্য হয়।

Question #66 (ID: 473750)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards: Mymensingh Board | Tags: Mymensingh Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:

[Image]


Options:
ক. [math]\cos 3 \mathrm{~A}[/math] কে [math]\cos \mathrm{A}[/math] এর মাধ্যমে প্রকাশ কর ।
খ. [math]\cos ^{2} A+\cos ^{2} B+\cos ^{2} C+2 \cos A \cos B \cos C[/math] এর মান কত?
গ. [math]A=60^{\circ}[/math] হলে, দেখাও যে, [math]\cos \frac{B-C}{2}=\frac{b+c}{2 a}[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কপ্রদত্ত ত্রিকোণমিতিক অনুপাত [math]=\cos 3 A[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \cos (2 A+A) \\\Rightarrow \cos 2 A \cdot \cos A-\sin 2 A \cdot \sin A \\\Rightarrow \left(2 \cos ^{2} A-1\right) \cdot \cos A-2 \sin A \cdot \cos A \cdot \sin A \\\Rightarrow 2 \cos ^{3} A-\cos A-2 \cos A\left(1-\cos ^{2} A\right) \\\Rightarrow 2 \cos ^{3} A-\cos A-2 \cos A+2 \cos ^{3} A \\\Rightarrow 4 \cos ^{3} A-3 \cos A \text { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]
 খপ্রদত্ত রাশি, [math]=\cos ^{2} A+\cos ^{2} B+\cos ^{2} C+2 \cos A \cos B \cos C[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2}\left(2 \cos ^{2} A+2 \cos ^{2} B\right)+\cos ^{2} C+2 \cos A \cos B \cos C \\\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2}(1+\cos 2 A+1+\cos 2 B)+\cos ^{2} C+2 \cos A \cos B \cos C \\\Rightarrow 1+\frac{1}{2}(\cos 2 A+\cos 2 B)+\cos ^{2} C+2 \cos A \cos B \cos C \\\Rightarrow 1+\frac{1}{2} \cdot 2 \cos (A+B) \cos (A-B)+\cos ^{2} C+2 \cos A \cos B \cos C\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow 1+\cos (\pi-C) \cos (\mathrm{A}-\mathrm{B})+\cos ^{2} \mathrm{C} \\+2 \cos \mathrm{A} \cos \mathrm{B} \cos \mathrm{C}[\because \mathrm{A}+\mathrm{B}+\mathrm{C}=\pi] \\\Rightarrow 1-\cos C \cos (A-B)+\cos ^{2} C+2 \cos A \cos B \cos C \\\Rightarrow 1-\cos C\{\cos (A-B)-\cos C\}+2 \cos A \cos B \cos C \\\Rightarrow 1-\cos C\{\cos (A-B)-\cos [\pi-(A+B)]\} \text {. } \\+2 \cos \mathrm{A} \cos \mathrm{B} \cos \mathrm{C} \\\Rightarrow 1-\cos C\{\cos (\mathrm{A}-\mathrm{B})+\cos (\mathrm{A}+\mathrm{B})\}+2 \cos A \cos \mathrm{B} \cos \mathrm{C} \\\Rightarrow 1-2 \cos A \cos B \cos C+2 \cos A \cos B \cos C=1 \text { (Ans.) } \\\end{array}[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]A=60^{\circ}[/math]
ত্রিভুজের সাইনসূত্র হতে আমরা জানি,[math]\frac{a}{\sin A}=\frac{b}{\sin B}=\frac{c}{\sin C}=2 \mathrm{R}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{a}=2 \mathrm{R} \sin \mathrm{A}, \mathrm{b}=2 \mathrm{R} \sin \mathrm{B}[/math]
 এবং [math]c=2 R \sin C[/math]
 [math]\triangle A B C[/math]
 এ [math]A+B+C=180^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 60^{\circ}+\mathrm{B}+\mathrm{C}=180^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{B}+\mathrm{C}=120^{\circ} \ldots \ldots \ldots \ldots \ldots \text { (i) }[/math]
 [math]\begin{aligned}\frac{\mathrm{b}+\mathrm{c}}{2 \mathrm{a}} & =\frac{2 \mathrm{R} \sin \mathrm{B}+2 \mathrm{R} \sin \mathrm{C}}{2 \cdot 2 \mathrm{R} \sin \mathrm{A}}=\frac{\sin \mathrm{B}+\sin \mathrm{C}}{2 \sin \mathrm{A}} \\& \Rightarrow \frac{2 \sin \left(\frac{\mathrm{B}+\mathrm{C}}{2}\right) \cdot \cos \left(\frac{\mathrm{B}-\mathrm{C}}{2}\right)}{2 \sin \mathrm{A}}\end{aligned}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\frac{\sin \left(\frac{120^{\circ}}{2}\right) \cos \left(\frac{\mathrm{B}-\mathrm{C}}{2}\right)}{\sin 60^{\circ}}[/math]
 [(i) হতে মান বসিয়ে][math]\begin{array}{l}=\frac{\sin 60^{\circ} \cdot \cos \frac{B-C}{2}}{\sin 60^{\circ}}\\\Rightarrow \frac{b+c}{2 a}=\cos \frac{B-C}{2}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \cos \frac{B-C}{2}=\frac{b+c}{2 a}[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত)

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক [math]\cos3A[/math] বের করতে [math]\cos(2A+A)=\cos2A\cos A-\sin2A\sin A[/math] ব্যবহার কর, এখানে [math]\cos2A=2\cos^2A-1[/math] এবং [math]\sin2A=2\sin A\cos A[/math] বসালে সংক্ষেপে পাওয়া যায় [math]\cos3A=4\cos^3A-3\cos A[/math]।

খ ত্রিভুজে [math]C=\pi-(A+B)[/math] ধরে [math]\cos C=-\cos(A+B)=-\cos A\cos B+\sin A\sin B[/math] বসিয়ে বর্গ করে এবং বিস্তৃত করলে ক্রস-টার্মগুলো বাতিল হয়ে শেষ ফলাফল [math]\cos^2A+\cos^2B+\cos^2C+2\cos A\cos B\cos C=1[/math] পাওয়া যায়।

গ সাধারণ সূত্র [math]\tan\frac{B-C}{2}=\frac{b-c}{b+c}\cot\frac{A}{2}[/math] ব্যবহার কর; [math]A=60^\circ[/math] হলে [math]\cot30^\circ=\sqrt3[/math] ফলে [math]\tan^2\frac{B-C}{2}=\frac{3(b-c)^2}{(b+c)^2}. তাই [math]\cos^2\frac{B-C}{2}=\frac{1}{1+\tan^2\frac{B-C}{2}}=\frac{(b+c)^2}{4a^2}</math] এবং লও'সের সূত্র দিয়ে [math]4a^2-(b+c)^2=3(b-c)^2</math] সত্য প্রমাণ করলে ফল হয় [math]\cos\frac{B-C}{2}=\frac{b+c}{2a}</math]।

Question #67 (ID: 473749)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards: Dhaka Board | Tags: Dhaka Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:

[Image]


Options:
ক. দেখাও যে, [math]\frac{b+c}{b-c}=\frac{\sin B+\sin C}{\sin B-\sin C}[/math]
খ. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\frac{\cos \mathrm{A}}{\sin B \sin C}+\frac{\cos \mathrm{B}}{\sin C \sin \mathrm{A}}+\frac{\cos \mathrm{C}}{\sin \mathrm{A} \sin \mathrm{B}}=2[/math]
গ. [math]\alpha=45^{\circ}, \beta=60^{\circ}[/math] এবং [math]a=(\sqrt{3}+1)[/math] সে. মি. হলে, [math]\triangle \mathrm{ABC}[/math] এর ক্ষেত্রফল নির্ণয় কর।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কআমরা জানি, যে কোনো ত্রিভুজ [math]ABC[/math]
-এ ত্রিভুজ সাইনসূত্রানুসারে, [math]\frac{a}{\sin A}=\frac{b}{\sin B}=\frac{c}{\sin C}=2 R[/math]
 [math]\therefore a=2 R \sin A, b=2 R \sin B[/math]
 এবং [math]c=2 R \sin C[/math]
 [math]\therefore \frac{b+c}{b-c}=\frac{2 R \sin B+2 R \sin C}{2 R \sin B-2 R \sin C}=\frac{\sin B+\sin C}{\sin B-\sin C}[/math]
(দেখানো হলো)খ [math]\triangle A B C[/math]
 এ [math]A+B+C=\pi[/math]
বামপক্ষ [math]=\frac{\cos A}{\sin B \sin C}+\frac{\cos B}{\sin C \sin A}+\frac{\cos C}{\sin A \sin B}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{\sin A \cos A+\sin B \cos B+\sin C \cos C}{\sin B \sin C \sin A} \\\Rightarrow \frac{2 \sin A \cos \mathrm{A}+2 \sin B \cos B+2 \sin C \cos C}{2 \sin B \sin C \sin A} \\\Rightarrow \frac{\sin 2 A+\sin 2 B+\sin 2 C}{2 \sin B \sin C \sin A} \\\Rightarrow \frac{2 \sin (A+B) \cos (A-B)+2 \sin C \cos C}{2 \sin A \sin B \sin C} \\\Rightarrow \frac{2 \sin C \cos (A-B)+2 \sin C \cos C}{2 \sin A \sin B \sin C}[\because A+B+C=\pi]\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{2 \sin C[\cos (A-B)+\cos C]}{2 \sin A \sin B \sin C} \\\Rightarrow \frac{2 \sin C[\cos (A-B)-\cos (A+B)]}{2 \sin A \sin B \sin C} \\\Rightarrow \frac{2 \sin C \cdot 2 \sin \mathrm{A} \sin \mathrm{B}}{2 \sin \mathrm{A} \sin B \sin C}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=2=[/math]
 ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore \frac{\cos A}{\sin B \sin C}+\frac{\cos B}{\sin C \sin A}+\frac{\cos C}{\sin A \sin B}=2[/math]
(প্রমাণিত)গদেওয়া আছে, [math]\triangle \mathrm{ABC}-[/math]
 এ [math]B=\alpha=45^{\circ}, C=\beta=60^{\circ}[/math]
এবং [math]B C=a=\sqrt{3}+1[/math]
 সে.মি[math]\begin{aligned}\therefore A & =180^{\circ}-(B+C) \\& \Rightarrow 180^{\circ}-\left(45^{\circ}+60^{\circ}\right) \\& \Rightarrow 180^{\circ}-105^{\circ}=75^{\circ} \\\sin 75^{\circ} & =\sin \left(45^{\circ}+30^{\circ}\right) \\& \Rightarrow \sin 45^{\circ} \cdot \cos 30^{\circ}+\cos 45^{\circ} \cdot \sin 30^{\circ} \\& \Rightarrow \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \cdot \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}+\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \cdot \frac{1}{2} \\& \Rightarrow \frac{\sqrt{3}+1}{2 \sqrt{2}}\end{aligned}[/math]
ত্রিভুজের সাইন সূত্র হতে পাই,[math]\frac{a}{\sin A}=\frac{b}{\sin B}=\frac{c}{\sin C}=2 R[/math]
এখানে, [math]\frac{a}{\sin A}=\frac{b}{\sin B}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{a}{\sin 75^{\circ}}=\frac{b}{\sin 45^{\circ}} \\\Rightarrow \frac{\sqrt{3}+1}{\frac{\sqrt{3}+1}{2 \sqrt{2}}}=\frac{b}{\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}} \\\Rightarrow 2 \sqrt{2}=\sqrt{2} b \\\therefore \mathrm{b}=2 \\\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \triangle \mathrm{ABC}[/math]
 এর ক্ষেত্রফল [math]=\frac{1}{2} a b \sin \beta[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \frac{1}{2}(\sqrt{3}+1) \cdot 2 \cdot \sin 60^{\circ} \\\Rightarrow (\sqrt{3}+1) \cdot \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{3+\sqrt{3}}{2}[/math]
 বর্গ একক [math]\text { (Ans.) }[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:
ক সংকেত থেকে [math]b=2R\sin B,\; c=2R\sin C[/math] হওয়ায় [math]\frac{b+c}{b-c}=\frac{2R\sin B+2R\sin C}{2R\sin B-2R\sin C}=\frac{\sin B+\sin C}{\sin B-\sin C}[/math].

খ প্রত্যেক পদকে [math]\frac{\cos A}{\sin B\sin C}=\frac{\cos A\sin A}{\sin A\sin B\sin C}[/math] লিখলে যোগফল হয় [math]\frac{\tfrac{1}{2}(\sin2A+\sin2B+\sin2C)}{\sin A\sin B\sin C}[/math] এবং ত্রিভুজে [math]\sin2A+\sin2B+\sin2C=4\sin A\sin B\sin C[/math] হওয়ায় মোট যোগফল [math]2[/math] হয়।

গ [math]A=45^\circ,\;B=60^\circ,\;a=(\sqrt{3}+1)[/math] হলে ক্ষেত্রফল ব্যবহার করি [math]K=\tfrac{a^2}{2}\cdot\frac{\sin B\sin C}{\sin A}[/math]; এখানে [math]\sin45=\tfrac{\sqrt2}{2},\;\sin60=\tfrac{\sqrt3}{2},\;\sin75=\tfrac{\sqrt2(\sqrt3+1)}{4}[/math] যোগ করে পাওয়া যায় [math]K=\frac{9+5\sqrt{3}}{4}\ \text{cm}^2[/math]।

Question #68 (ID: 473748)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards: Chittagong Board | Tags: Chattogram Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sin \theta=\frac{3}{5}[/math] এবং [math]A=\frac{\pi}{12}[/math]

Options:
ক. দেখাও যে, [math]\cos 75^{\circ}=\frac{1}{4}(\sqrt{6}-\sqrt{2})[/math]
খ. [math]\frac{\cot \theta+\cos (-\theta)}{\operatorname{cosec}(-\theta)+\tan \theta}[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর; যখন [math]\frac{\pi}{2}<\theta<\pi[/math] হয়।
গ. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\tan A \tan 3 \mathrm{~A} \tan 5 \mathrm{~A} \tan 7 \mathrm{~A} \tan 11 A=1[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]\begin{aligned}\cos 75^{\circ} & =\cos \left(45^{\circ}+30^{\circ}\right)=\cos 45^{\circ} \cos 30^{\circ}-\sin 45^{\circ} \sin 30^{\circ} \\& \Rightarrow \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \cdot \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}-\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \cdot \frac{1}{2} \\& \Rightarrow \frac{\sqrt{3}-1}{2 \sqrt{2}}=\frac{\sqrt{3}-1}{2 \sqrt{2}} \times \frac{\sqrt{2}}{\sqrt{2}} \\& \Rightarrow \frac{\sqrt{6}-\sqrt{2}}{2.2}=\frac{1}{4}(\sqrt{6}-\sqrt{2})\end{aligned}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \cos 75^{\circ}=\frac{1}{4}(\sqrt{6}-\sqrt{2})[/math]
(দেখানো হলো)খদেওয়া আছে, [math]\sin \theta=\frac{3}{5}[/math]
 এবং [math]\frac{\pi}{2}গদেওয়া আছে, [math]A=\frac{\pi}{12}[/math]
বামপক্ষ [math]=\tan \mathrm{A} \cdot \tan 3 \mathrm{~A} \cdot \tan 5 \mathrm{~A} \cdot \tan 7 \mathrm{~A} \cdot \tan 11 \mathrm{~A}[/math]
 [math]=\tan \frac{\pi}{12} \cdot \tan \frac{3 \pi}{12} \tan \frac{5 \pi}{12} \cdot \tan \frac{7 \pi}{12} \cdot \tan \frac{11 \pi}{12}[/math]
 [math]=\tan \frac{\pi}{12} \cdot \tan \frac{\pi}{4} \cdot \tan \frac{5 \pi}{12} \cdot \tan \left(\frac{\pi}{2}+\frac{\pi}{12}\right) \tan \left(\frac{\pi}{2}+\frac{5 \pi}{12}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\tan \frac{\pi}{12} \cdot 1 \cdot \tan \frac{5 \pi}{12} \cdot\left(-\cot \frac{\pi}{12}\right) \cdot\left(-\cot \frac{5 \pi}{12}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\tan \frac{\pi}{12} \cdot \tan \frac{5 \pi}{12} \cdot \frac{1}{\tan \frac{\pi}{12}} \cdot \frac{1}{\tan \frac{5 \pi}{12}}[/math]
 [math]=1=[/math]
 ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore \tan \mathrm{A} \cdot \tan 3 \mathrm{~A} \cdot \tan 5 \mathrm{~A} \cdot \tan 7 \mathrm{~A} \cdot \tan 11 \mathrm{~A}=1[/math]
(প্রমাণিত)

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক [math]\cos75^\circ=\cos(45^\circ+30^\circ)=\cos45^\circ\cos30^\circ-\sin45^\circ\sin30^\circ=\frac{\sqrt2}{2}\cdot\frac{\sqrt3}{2}-\frac{\sqrt2}{2}\cdot\frac{1}{2}=\frac{1}{4}(\sqrt6-\sqrt2)[/math].

খ [math]\pi/2গ [math]A=\pi/12[/math] হলে [math]\tan3A=\tan(\pi/4)=1,\ \tan7A=\tan(\pi-5A)=-\tan5A,\ \tan11A=\tan(\pi-A)=-\tan A[/math]. ফলে উৎপাদ = [math]\tan A\cdot1\cdot\tan5A\cdot(-\tan5A)\cdot(-\tan A)=(\tan A\tan5A)^2[/math], এবং [math]\tan5A=\tan(\tfrac{\pi}{2}-A)=\cot A=1/\tan A[/math], সুতরাং ফল [math]1[/math]।

Question #69 (ID: 473746)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2023 | Boards: Barisal Board | Tags: Barisal Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
দৃশ্যকল্প-১ :


[Image]


দৃশ্যকল্প-২ : [math]\mathrm {\sin 2 \alpha=Q-\sin 2 \beta ; \cos 2 \beta=P-\cos 2 \alpha}[/math]

Options:
ক. দেখাও যে, [math]\sin 29^{\circ}+\cos 29^{\circ}=\sqrt{2} \cos 16^{\circ}[/math]
খ. দৃশ্যকল্প-১ এ [math]\mathrm {a^{4}+b^{4}+c^{4}=2 b^{2}\left(a^{2}+c^{2}\right)}[/math] হলে দেখাও যে, [math]\angle \mathrm B = 45^°[/math] বা [math]135^°.[/math]
গ. দৃশ্যকল্প-২ হতে প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\mathrm {\cos (\alpha+\beta)= \pm \frac{P}{\sqrt{\mathrm{P}^{2}+\mathrm{Q}^{2}}}}[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]\\[/math]
বামপক্ষ [math]=\sin 29^{\circ}+\cos 29^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\sin \left(90^{\circ}-61^{\circ}\right)+\cos 29^{\circ} \\=\cos 61^{\circ}+\cos 29^{\circ} \\=2 \cos \dfrac{61^{\circ}+29^{\circ}}{2} \cos \dfrac{61^{\circ}-29^{\circ}}{2} \\=2 \cos \dfrac{90^{\circ}}{2} \cos \dfrac{32^{\circ}}{2}=2 \cos 45^{\circ} \cos 16^{\circ}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=2 \dfrac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \cos 16^{\circ}=\sqrt{2} \cos 16^{\circ}=[/math]
 ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore \sin 29^{\circ}+\cos 29^{\circ}=\sqrt{2} \cos 16^{\circ}[/math]
 (দেখানো হলো)[math]\\[/math]
 খ [math]\\[/math]
দেওয়া আছে, [math]\mathrm {a^{4}+b^{4}+c^{4}=2 b^{2}\left(a^{2}+c^{2}\right)}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \mathrm {a^{4}+b^{4}+c^{4}-2 a^{2} b^{2}-2 b^{2} c^{2}=0}\\\Rightarrow \mathrm { \left(a^{2}\right)^{2}+\left(-b^{2}\right)^{2}+\left(c^{2}\right)^{2}+2 a^{2}\left(-b^{2}\right)+2\left(-b^{2}\right) c^{2}+2 c^{2} a^{2}=2 c^{2} a^{2}}\\\Rightarrow \mathrm {\left(c^{2}+a^{2}-b^{2}\right)^{2}=2 c^{2} a^{2}}\\\Rightarrow \mathrm {c^{2}+a^{2}-b^{2}= \pm \sqrt{2} c a}\\\Rightarrow \mathrm {\dfrac{c^{2}+a^{2}-b^{2}}{2 c a}= \pm \dfrac{\sqrt{2}}{2} \cdot \cos B= \pm \dfrac{1}{\sqrt{2}}}\end{array}[/math]
এখন, [math]\mathrm {\cos B=\dfrac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \Rightarrow \cos B=\cos 45^{\circ} \therefore B=45^{\circ}}[/math]
আবার, [math]\mathrm {\cos B=-\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm {\cos B=-\cos 45^{\circ}=\cos \left(180^{\circ}-45^{\circ}\right)=\cos 135^{\circ}} \\\therefore \mathrm{B}=135^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\mathrm {\therefore \angle B=45^{\circ} \Rightarrow 135^{\circ}}[/math]
 (দেখানো হলো)[math]\\[/math]
 গ [math]\\[/math]
দেওয়া আছে, [math]\mathrm {\sin 2 \alpha=Q-\sin 2 \beta}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \mathrm { \sin 2 \alpha+\sin 2 \beta=Q}\\\Rightarrow \mathrm { Q=2 \sin \left(\dfrac{2 \alpha+2 \beta}{2}\right) \cos \left(\dfrac{2 \alpha-2 \beta}{2}\right)}\\\Rightarrow \mathrm { \therefore Q=2 \sin (\alpha+\beta) \cos (\alpha-\beta) } \ldots \quad \ldots \quad \ldots \text {(i)}\end{array}[/math]
আবার, [math]\mathrm {\cos 2 \beta=P-\cos 2 \alpha}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \cos 2 \alpha+\cos 2 \beta=\mathrm{P} \\\Rightarrow \mathrm{P}=2 \cos \left(\dfrac{2 \alpha+2 \beta}{2}\right) \cos \left(\dfrac{2 \alpha-2 \beta}{2}\right) \\\therefore \mathrm{P}=2 \cos (\alpha+\beta) \cos (\alpha-\beta) \ldots \quad \ldots \quad \ldots \text{(ii)}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\text{(i)}[/math]
 কে [math]\text{(ii)}[/math]
 নং দ্বারা ভাগ করে,[math]\mathrm {\dfrac{Q}{P}=\dfrac{2 \sin (\alpha+\beta) \cos (\alpha-\beta)}{2 \cos (\alpha+\beta) \cos (\alpha-\beta)}}[/math]
 [math]\mathrm {\Rightarrow \dfrac{Q}{P}=\dfrac{\sin (\alpha+\beta)}{\cos (\alpha+\beta)} \Rightarrow \dfrac{Q^{2}}{P^{2}}=\dfrac{\sin ^{2}(\alpha+\beta)}{\cos ^{2}(\alpha+\beta)}}[/math]
 [বর্গ করে][math]\mathrm {\Rightarrow\dfrac{P^{2}+Q^{2}}{P^{2}}=\dfrac{\sin ^{2}(\alpha+\beta)+\cos ^{2}(\alpha+\beta)}{\cos ^{2}(\alpha+\beta)}}[/math]
 [যোজন করে][math]\Rightarrow \dfrac{\mathrm{P}^{2}}{\mathrm{P}^{2}+\mathrm{Q}^{2}}=\cos ^{2}(\alpha+\beta)[/math]
 [math]\therefore \cos (\alpha+\beta)= \pm \frac{\mathrm{P}}{\sqrt{\mathrm{P}^{2}+\mathrm{Q}^{2}}}[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত)

Explanation:
ক ব্যবহার কর যে [math]\sin x+\cos x=\sqrt{2}\cos(45^\circ-x)[/math] হলে [math]x=29^\circ[/math] বসালে [math]\sin29^\circ+\cos29^\circ=\sqrt{2}\cos16^\circ[/math] পাওয়া যায়।  

খ ধর [math]x=b^2[/math] রেখে দেওয়া সমীকরণকে সমাধান করলে [math]b^2=(a^2+c^2)\pm\sqrt{2}\,ac[/math] পাওয়া যায়, এবং কসমের সূত্র অনুযায়ী [math]b^2=a^2+c^2-2ac\cos B[/math] হওয়ায় [math]\cos B=\pm\frac{\sqrt{2}}{2}[/math], অর্থাৎ [math]\angle B=45^\circ[/math] বা [math]135^\circ[/math]।  

গ থেকে [math]\sin2\alpha+\sin2\beta=Q[/math] ও [math]\cos2\alpha+\cos2\beta=P[/math] পাওয়া যায়; কিন্তু [math]e^{i2\alpha}+e^{i2\beta}=2\cos(\alpha-\beta)e^{i(\alpha+\beta)}[/math], তাই [math]P+iQ=2\cos(\alpha-\beta)e^{i(\alpha+\beta)}[/math] এবং এ থেকে [math]\cos(\alpha+\beta)=\pm\frac{P}{\sqrt{P^2+Q^2}}[/math] হয় (চিহ্নটি [math]\cos(\alpha-\beta)[/math] এর সাইন নির্ভর করে)।

Question #70 (ID: 473747)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2023 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\varphi(x)=\cos x[/math]

(ক) কোনো ত্রিভুজের বাহুগুলির দৈর্ঘ্য 3a, 5a ও 7a একক হলে ত্রিভুজটির বৃহত্তম কোণ নির্ণয় কর।

(খ) [math]\varphi(2 x) \varphi(4 x) \varphi(8 x) \varphi(14 x)[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর যখন [math]x=\frac{\pi}{15}[/math]

(গ) [math]p \dot{\varphi}(x)+q \dot{\varphi}(y)=r=p \varphi\left(\frac{\pi}{2}-x\right)+q \varphi\left(\frac{\pi}{2}-y\right)[/math] হলে দেখাও যে [math]\varphi\left(\frac{x-y}{2}\right)= \pm \sqrt{\frac{2 r^{2}-(p-q)^{2}}{4 p q}}[/math]

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
কধরি, [math]\Delta[/math]
 PQR এর বাহুর দৈর্ঘ্য, p = 3a [math]\mathfrak{q} = 5a\mathfrak{q}[/math]
 r = 7a এখানে, r বৃহত্তম বাহু। p, q. r দ্বারা উৎপন্ন [math]\Delta[/math]
PQR হলে R ত্রিভুজের বৃহত্তম কোণ।এখন,[math]\cos R=\frac{p^{2}+q^{2}-r^{2}}{2 p q}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \cos R=\frac{(3 a)^{2}+(5 a)^{2}-(7 a)^{2}}{2 \cdot 3 a \cdot 5 a}\\\Rightarrow \cos R=\frac{9 a^{2}+25 a^{2}-49 a^{2}}{30 a^{2}}\\\Rightarrow \cos R=\frac{-15 a^{2}}{30 a^{2}}\\\Rightarrow \cos R=-\frac{1}{2}\\\Rightarrow\cos R=\cos 120^{\circ}\\\mathrm{R}=120^{\circ}\end{array}[/math]
নির্ণেয় বৃহত্তম কোণ 120° [Ans.][math]\\[/math]
 খদেওয়া আছে, [math]\varphi(x)=\cos x[/math]
এখন, [math]\varphi(2 x) \varphi(4 x) \varphi(8 x) \varphi(14 x)[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\cos 2 x \cos 4 x \cos 8 x \cos 14 x \\=\cos 2 \cdot \frac{\pi}{15} \cos 4 \cdot \frac{\pi}{15} \cos 8 \cdot \frac{\pi}{15} \cos 14 \cdot \frac{\pi}{15} \quad\left[\because x=\frac{\pi}{15}\right] \\=\cos \frac{2 \pi}{15} \cos \frac{4 \pi}{15} \cos \frac{8 \pi}{15} \cos \frac{14 \pi}{15} \\=\frac{1}{2 \sin \frac{2 \pi}{15}}\left(2 \sin \frac{2 \pi}{15} \cos \frac{2 \pi}{15}\right) \cos \frac{4 \pi}{15} \cos \frac{8 \pi}{15} \cos \frac{14 \pi}{15} \\=\frac{1}{2 \sin \frac{2 \pi}{15}} \sin \frac{4 \pi}{15} \cos \frac{4 \pi}{15} \cos \frac{8 \pi}{15} \cos \frac{14 \pi}{15} \\=\frac{1}{4 \sin \frac{2 \pi}{15}}\left(2 \sin \frac{4 \pi}{15} \cos \frac{4 \pi}{15}\right) \cos \frac{8 \pi}{15} \cos \frac{14 \pi}{15}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\frac{1}{4 \sin \frac{2 \pi}{15}} \sin \frac{8 \pi}{15} \cos \frac{8 \pi}{15} \cos \frac{14 \pi}{15} \\=\frac{1}{8 \sin \frac{2 \pi}{15}}\left(2 \sin \frac{8 \pi}{15} \cos \frac{8 \pi}{15}\right) \cos \frac{14 \pi}{15} \\=\frac{1}{8 \sin \frac{2 \pi}{15}} \sin \frac{16 \pi}{15} \cos \frac{14 \pi}{15}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\frac{1}{16 \sin \frac{2 \pi}{15}}\left(2 \sin \frac{16 \pi}{15} \cos \frac{14 \pi}{15}\right) \\=\frac{1}{16 \sin \frac{2 \pi}{15}}\left[\sin \left(\frac{16 \pi}{15}+\frac{14 \pi}{15}\right)+\sin \left(\frac{16 \pi}{15}-\frac{14 \pi}{15}\right)\right] \\=\frac{1}{16 \sin \frac{2 \pi}{15}}\left(\sin 2 \pi+\sin \frac{2 \pi}{15}\right) \\=\frac{1}{16 \sin \frac{2 \pi}{15}}\left(0+\sin \frac{2 \pi}{15}\right) \quad\left[\because \sin 180^{\circ}=0\right] \\\left.\left.=\frac{1}{16} \right\rvert\, \text { Ans. }\right]\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 গদেওয়া আছে, [math]\varphi(x)=\cos x[/math]
এবং [math]p \varphi(x)+q \varphi(y)=r=p \cdot \varphi\left(\frac{\pi}{2}-x\right)+q \varphi\left(\frac{\pi}{2}-y\right)[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow p \cos x+q \cos y=r=p \cos \left(\frac{\pi}{2}-x\right)+q \cos \left(\frac{\pi}{2}-y\right)\\\Rightarrow p \cos x+q \cos y=r=p \sin x+q \sin y\end{array}[/math]
অর্থাৎ [math]p \sin x+q \sin y=r \ldots \ldots i[/math]
এবং [math]p \cos x+q \cos y=r \ldots \ldots \ldots ii[/math]
এখন (i) ও (ii) নং সমীকরণের বর্গের সমষ্টি নিয়ে পাই,[math]\begin{array}{l}\begin{array}{l}(p \sin x+q \sin y)^{2}+(p \cos x+q \cos y)^{2}=r^{2}+r^{2} \\\Rightarrow p^{2} \sin ^{2} x+2 p q \sin x \sin y+q^{2} \sin ^{2} y+p^{2} \cos ^{2} x \\\\+2 p q \cos x \cos y+q^{2} \cos ^{2} y=2 r^{2} \\\Rightarrow p^{2}\left(\sin ^{2} x+\cos ^{2} x\right) \\+q^{2}\left(\sin ^{2} y+\cos ^{2} y\right) \\+2 p q(\cos x \cos y+\sin x \sin y)=2 r^{2}\end{array}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow p^{2}+q^{2}+2 p q \cos (x-y)=2 r^{2}\\\Rightarrow 2 p q \cos (x-y)=2 r^{2}-p^{2}-q^{2}\\\Rightarrow \cos (x-y)=\frac{2 r^{2}-p^{2}-q^{2}}{2 p q}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \cos \left(2 \cdot \frac{x-y}{2}\right)=\frac{2 r^{2}-p^{2}-q^{2}}{2 p q}\\\Rightarrow 2 \cos ^{2}\left(\frac{x-y}{2}\right)-1=\frac{2 r^{2}-p^{2}-q^{2}}{2 p q}\\\Rightarrow 2 \cos ^{2}\left(\frac{x-y}{2}\right)=\frac{2 r^{2}-p^{2}-q^{2}}{2 p q}+1\\\Rightarrow 2 \cos ^{2}\left(\frac{x-y}{2}\right)=\frac{2 r^{2}-p^{2}-q^{2}+2 p q}{2 p q}\\\Rightarrow \cos ^{2}\left(\frac{x-y}{2}\right)=\frac{2 r^{2}-\left(p^{2}-2 p q+q^{2}\right)}{2 p q}\\\cos ^{2}\left(\frac{x-y}{2}\right)=\frac{2 r^{2}-(p-q)^{2}}{4 p q}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \cos \left(\frac{x-y}{2}\right)= \pm \sqrt{\frac{2 r^{2}-(p-q)^{2}}{4 p q}} \\\therefore \varphi\left(\frac{x-y}{2}\right)= \pm \sqrt{\frac{2 r^{2}-(p-q)^{2}}{4 p q}} \text { [Showed] }\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]


Explanation:
ক ত্রিভুজের বৃহৎ কোনটি পাশ [math]7a[/math]-এর বিপরীত; কসাইন সূত্র দিয়ে [math]\cos C=\frac{(3a)^2+(5a)^2-(7a)^2}{2\cdot3a\cdot5a}=\!-{\tfrac{1}{2}}[/math], তাই [math]C=120^\circ\;(=\tfrac{2\pi}{3})[/math].

খ এখানে [math]14x= \pi-\,x[/math] হওয়ায় [math]\cos(14x)=-\cos x[/math]; ফলে উত্তরটি [math]-\cos x\cos2x\cos4x\cos8x[/math]. পরিচিত গুণধর্ম থেকে [math]\sin(16x)=16\sin x\cos x\cos2x\cos4x\cos8x[/math], এবং [math]\sin(16x)= -\sin x[/math] যখন [math]x=\pi/15[/math]; তাই ফল [math]\frac{1}{16}[/math]।

গ [math]\varphi(x)=\cos x[/math] হলে শর্তদ্বয়কে বর্গ করে যোগ করলে পাওয়া যাবে [math]2r^{2}=p^{2}+q^{2}+2pq\cos(x-y)[/math], ফলে [math]\cos(x-y)=\frac{2r^{2}-p^{2}-q^{2}}{2pq}[/math]; এরপর হাফ-এঙ্গেল সূত্র দিয়ে [math]\cos\frac{x-y}{2}= \pm\sqrt{\frac{1+\cos(x-y)}{2}}=\pm\sqrt{\frac{2r^{2}-(p-q)^{2}}{4pq}}[/math], যা প্রদর্শিত।

Question #71 (ID: 473743)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2023 | Boards: Chittagong Board | Tags: Chattogram Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:

[Image]


যেখানে [math]\alpha+\beta+\gamma=\pi[/math]

Options:
ক. প্রমাণ কর: [math]\dfrac{\sin 75^{\circ}+\sin 15^{\circ}}{\sin 75^{\circ}-\sin 15^{\circ}}=\sqrt{3}[/math]
খ. প্রমাণ কর: [math]\sin ^{2} \alpha-\sin ^{2} \beta+\sin ^{2} \gamma=2 \sin \alpha \cos \beta \sin \gamma[/math]
গ. [math]\mathrm {\cos P=\sin Q-\cos R}[/math] হলে দেখাও যে, [math]\mathrm {PQR}[/math] ত্রিভুজটি - সমকোণী ৷


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]\\[/math]
বামপক্ষ [math]=\dfrac{\sin 75^{\circ}+\sin 15^{\circ}}{\sin 75^{\circ}-\sin 15^{\circ}}=\dfrac{\sin \left(90^{\circ}-15^{\circ}\right)+\sin 15^{\circ}}{\sin \left(90^{\circ}-15^{\circ}\right)-\sin 15^{\circ}}[/math]
 [math]=\dfrac{\cos 15^{\circ}+\sin 15^{\circ}}{\cos 15^{\circ}-\sin 15^{\circ}}=\dfrac{1+\tan 15^{\circ}}{1-\tan 15^{\circ}}[/math]
 [ [math]\cos 15^{\circ}[/math]
 দিয়ে হর ও লবকে ভাগ করে ][math]\begin{array}{l}=\dfrac{\tan 45^{\circ}+\tan 15^{\circ}}{1-\tan 45^{\circ} \cdot \tan 15^{\circ}}=\tan \left(45^{\circ}+15^{\circ}\right) \\=\tan 60^{\circ}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{3} =[/math]
 ডানপক্ষ (প্রমাণিত)[math]\\[/math]
 খ [math]\\[/math]
বামপক্ষ [math]=\sin ^{2} \alpha-\sin ^{2} \beta+\sin ^{2} \gamma[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\dfrac{1}{2}\left\{2 \sin ^{2} \alpha+2 \sin ^{2} \gamma\right\}-\sin ^{2} \beta \\=\dfrac{1}{2}(1-\cos 2 \alpha+1-\cos 2 \gamma)-\sin ^{2} \beta \\=\dfrac{1}{2}(2-\cos 2 \alpha-\cos 2 \gamma)-\sin ^{2} \beta \\=1-\dfrac{1}{2}(\cos 2 \alpha+\cos 2 \gamma)-\sin ^{2} \beta \\=1-\dfrac{1}{2} \cdot 2 \cos (\alpha+\gamma) \cos (\alpha-\gamma)-\sin ^{2} \beta\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=1-\cos (\pi-\beta) \cos (\alpha-\gamma)-\sin ^{2} \beta[\because \alpha+\beta+\gamma=\pi] \\=1-\sin ^{2} \beta+\cos \beta \cos (\alpha-\gamma) \\=\cos { }^{2} \beta+\cos \beta \cos (\alpha-\gamma) \\=\cos \beta\{\cos \beta+\cos (\alpha-\gamma)\} \\=\cos \beta[\cos \{\pi-(\alpha+\gamma)\}+\cos (\alpha-\gamma)] \\=\cos \beta\{-\cos (\alpha+\gamma)+\cos (\alpha-\gamma)\} \\=\cos \beta\{\cos (\alpha-\gamma)-\cos (\alpha+\gamma)\} \\=\cos \beta \cdot 2 \sin \alpha \sin \gamma \\=2 \sin \alpha \cos \beta \sin \gamma\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=[/math]
 ডানপক্ষ (প্রমাণিত)[math]\\[/math]
 গ [math]\\[/math]
দেওয়া আছে, [math]\cos \mathrm{P}=\sin \mathrm{Q}-\cos \mathrm{R}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \mathrm { \cos P+\cos R=\sin Q} \\\Rightarrow \cos \mathrm{P}+\cos \{\pi-(\mathrm{P}+\mathrm{Q})\}=\sin \mathrm{Q} \quad[\because \mathrm{P}+\mathrm{Q}+\mathrm{R}=\pi]\\\Rightarrow \cos \mathrm{P}-\cos (\mathrm{P}+\mathrm{Q})=\sin \mathrm{Q}\\\Rightarrow \mathrm {2 \sin \dfrac{2 P+Q}{2} \sin \frac{Q}{2}=2 \sin \dfrac{Q}{2} \cos \dfrac{Q}{2}}\\\Rightarrow \mathrm {\sin \left(P+\dfrac{Q}{2}\right)=\cos \dfrac{Q}{2} \Rightarrow \sin \left(P+\dfrac{Q}{2}\right)=\sin \left(\dfrac{\pi}{2}-\dfrac{Q}{2}\right)}\\\Rightarrow \mathrm{P}+\dfrac{\mathrm{Q}}{2}=\dfrac{\pi}{2}-\dfrac{\mathrm{Q}}{2} \Rightarrow \mathrm{P}+\mathrm{Q}=\dfrac{\pi}{2} \therefore \mathrm{R}=\dfrac{\pi}{2}\end{array}[/math]
অতএব, [math]\triangle \mathrm {PQR }[/math]
 সমকোণী । (দেখানো হলো)

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক সমতীকরণটি অর্জন করতে যোগ-ভাজন সূত্র ব্যবহার করুন: [math]\sin A+\sin B=2\sin\frac{A+B}{2}\cos\frac{A-B}{2}[/math] ও [math]\sin A-\sin B=2\cos\frac{A+B}{2}\sin\frac{A-B}{2}[/math] হলে numerator = [math]2\sin45^\circ\cos30^\circ[/math] ও denominator = [math]2\cos45^\circ\sin30^\circ[/math] ফলে অনুপাত = [math]\dfrac{\sin45^\circ\cos30^\circ}{\cos45^\circ\sin30^\circ}=\dfrac{\cos30^\circ}{\sin30^\circ}=\sqrt{3}[/math].

খ ব্যবহার করুন পরিচিতি [math]\sin^2A-\sin^2B=\sin(A+B)\sin(A-B)[/math] এবং [math]\gamma=\pi-(\alpha+\beta)[/math] থেকে [math]\sin\gamma=\sin(\alpha+\beta)[/math], তাই বাম পাশ = [math]\sin(\alpha+\beta)[\sin(\alpha-\beta)+\sin(\alpha+\beta)]=\sin(\alpha+\beta)\cdot2\sin\alpha\cos\beta=2\sin\alpha\cos\beta\sin\gamma[/math]।

গ দেওয়া [math]\cos P=\sin Q-\cos R[/math] থেকে [math]\sin Q=\cos P+\cos R=2\cos\frac{P+R}{2}\cos\frac{P-R}{2}[/math], কিন্তু [math]\cos\frac{P+R}{2}=\cos\frac{\pi-Q}{2}=\sin\frac{Q}{2}[/math], ফলে [math]2\sin\frac{Q}{2}\cos\frac{P-R}{2}=2\sin\frac{Q}{2}\cos\frac{Q}{2}[/math] এবং তাই [math]\cos\frac{P-R}{2}=\cos\frac{Q}{2}[/math]. এটি থেকে [math]P-R=\pm Q[/math], যা বাধ্যতামূলকভাবে কোনো একটি কোণকে [math]\tfrac{\pi}{2}[/math] করে (অর্থাৎ [math]P=\tfrac{\pi}{2}[/math] অথবা [math]R=\tfrac{\pi}{2}[/math]), তাই ত্রিভুজটি সমকোণী।

Question #72 (ID: 473744)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2023 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\mathrm{A}+\mathrm{B}+\mathrm{C}=\dfrac{\pi}{2}[/math]

Options:
ক. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\cos 5 \theta=16 \cos ^{5} \theta-20 \cos ^{3} \theta+5 \cos \theta[/math]
খ. উদ্দীপকের আলোকে দেখাও যে, [math]\mathrm {\cos (B+C)+\cos (C+A)} +\cos (\mathrm{A}+\mathrm{B})=1+4 \sin \dfrac{\pi-2 \mathrm{~A}}{4} \sin \dfrac{\pi-2 \mathrm{~B}}{4} \sin \dfrac{\pi-2 \mathrm{C}}{4}[/math]
গ. উদ্দীপকের আলোকে যদি [math]\mathrm {\tan A+\tan B+\tan C=\sqrt{3}}[/math] হয়, তবে প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\mathrm { A = B = C}[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]\\[/math]
বামপক্ষ [math]=\cos 5 \theta=\cos (4 \theta+\theta)[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\cos 4 \theta \cos \theta-\sin 4 \theta \sin \theta \\=\left(2 \cos ^{2} 2 \theta-1\right) \cos \theta-2 \sin 2 \theta \cos 2 \theta \sin \theta \\=\left\{2\left(2 \cos ^{2} \theta-1\right)^{2}-1\right\} \cos \theta-4 \sin ^{2} \theta \cos \theta\left(2 \cos ^{2} \theta-1\right)\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{aligned}=\left\{2\left(4 \cos ^{4} \theta-4 \cos ^{2} \theta+1\right)-1\right\} \cos \theta & -4\left(1-\cos ^{2} \theta\right) \cos \theta\left(2 \cos ^{2} \theta-1\right)\end{aligned}[/math]
 [math]=8 \cos ^{5} \theta-8 \cos ^{3} \theta+\cos \theta-4\left(\cos \theta-\cos ^{3} \theta\right)\left(2 \cos ^{2} \theta-1\right)[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{r}=8 \cos ^{5} \theta-8 \cos ^{3} \theta+\cos \theta-4\left(2 \cos ^{3} \theta-2 \cos ^{5} \theta\right. \left. -\cos \theta+\cos ^{3} \theta\right)\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=8 \cos ^{5} \theta-8 \cos ^{3} \theta+\cos ^{2} \theta-12 \cos ^{3} \theta+8 \cos ^{5} \theta+4 \cos \theta \\=16 \cos ^{5} \theta-20 \cos ^{3} \theta+5 \cos \theta\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=[/math]
 ডানপক্ষ (প্রমাণিত)[math]\\[/math]
 খ [math]\\[/math]
দেওয়া আছে, [math]\mathrm{A+B+C=\dfrac{\pi}{2}} \ldots \quad \ldots \quad \ldots \quad \ldots \text {(i)}[/math]
বামপক্ষ [math]\mathrm {=\cos (B+C)+\cos (C+A)+\cos (A+B)}[/math]
 [math]=\cos \left(\dfrac{\pi}{2}-\mathrm{A}\right)+\cos \left(\dfrac{\pi}{2}-\mathrm{B}\right)+\cos \left(\dfrac{\pi}{2}-\mathrm{C}\right)[/math]
 [ [math]\text {(i)}[/math]
 হতে][math]\begin{array}{l}\mathrm {=\sin A+\sin B+\sin C }\\\mathrm {=\sin A+\sin B+\sin C-\sin \dfrac{\pi}{2}+1 }\\\mathrm {=\sin A+\sin B+\sin C-\sin (A+B+C)+1}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l} = \mathrm {2 \sin \left(\dfrac{A+B}{2}\right) \cos \left(\dfrac{A-B}{2}\right) +2 \cos \left(\dfrac{A+B+2 C}{2}\right) \sin \left\{-\dfrac{1}{2}(A+B)\right\}+1} \end{array}[/math]
 [math]=2 \sin \left(\dfrac{\mathrm{A}+\mathrm{B}}{2}\right)\left\{\cos \left(\dfrac{\mathrm{A}-\mathrm{B}}{2}\right)-\cos \left(\dfrac{\mathrm{A}+\mathrm{B}+2 \mathrm{C}}{2}\right)\right\}+1[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}= \mathrm {2 \sin \dfrac{A+B}{2} \cdot 2 \sin \dfrac{\dfrac{A-B}{2}+\dfrac{A+B+2 C}{2}}{2} \sin \dfrac{\dfrac{A+B+2 C}{2} -\dfrac{A-B}{2}}{2}+1 }\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\mathrm { =4 \sin \left(\dfrac{A+B}{2}\right) \cdot \sin \left(\dfrac{C+A}{2}\right) \sin \left(\dfrac{B+C}{2}\right)+1 }\\\mathrm { =4 \sin \dfrac{1}{2}\left(\dfrac{\pi}{2}-C\right) \sin \dfrac{1}{2}\left(\dfrac{\pi}{2}-B\right) \sin \dfrac{1}{2}\left(\dfrac{\pi}{2}-A\right)+1 }\\\mathrm { =1+4 \sin \dfrac{\pi-2 A}{4} \sin \dfrac{\pi-2 B}{4} \sin \dfrac{\pi-2 C}{4}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=[/math]
 ডানপক্ষ[math]\mathrm {\therefore \cos (B+C)+\cos (C+A)+\cos (A+B) }=1+4 \sin \dfrac{\pi-2 \mathrm{~A}}{4} \sin \dfrac{\pi-2 \mathrm{~B}}{4} \sin \dfrac{\pi-2 \mathrm{C}}{4}[/math]
 (দেখানো হলো)[math]\\[/math]
 গ [math]\\[/math]
দেওয়া আছে, [math]\tan \mathrm{A}+\tan \mathrm{B}+\tan \mathrm{C}=\sqrt{3} \ldots \quad \ldots \quad \ldots \text {(i)}[/math]
এবং [math]\mathrm{A}+\mathrm{B}+\mathrm{C}=\dfrac{\pi}{2} \Rightarrow \mathrm{A}+\mathrm{B}=\dfrac{\pi}{2}-\mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \mathrm{\tan (A+B)=\tan \left(\dfrac{\pi}{2}-C\right)} \\\Rightarrow \mathrm{\dfrac{\tan A+\tan B}{1-\tan A \cdot \tan B}=\cot C \Rightarrow \dfrac{\tan A+\tan B}{1-\tan A \cdot \tan B}=\dfrac{1}{\tan C}} \\\Rightarrow \mathrm{\tan A \cdot \tan C+\tan B \cdot \tan C=1-\tan A \tan B} \\\therefore \mathrm{\tan A \cdot \tan B+\tan B \cdot \tan C+\tan C \cdot \tan A=1} \ldots \quad \ldots \quad \ldots \text {(ii)}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\text {(i)}[/math]
 হতে পাই[math]\mathrm {(\tan A+\tan B+\tan C)^{2}=(\sqrt{3})^{2}}[/math]
 [বর্গ করে][math]\Rightarrow \mathrm {\tan ^{2} A+\tan ^{2} B+\tan ^{2} C+2 \tan A \cdot \tan B+2 \tan B \tan C+2 \tan C \cdot \tan \mathrm{A}=3.1}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \tan ^{2} \mathrm{~A}+\tan ^{2} \mathrm{~B}+\tan ^{2} \mathrm{C}+2(\tan \mathrm{A} \tan \mathrm{B}+\tan \mathrm{B} \cdot \tan \mathrm{C} + \tan \mathrm{C} \cdot \tan \mathrm{A} =3(\tan \mathrm{A} \tan \mathrm{B}+\tan \mathrm{B} \tan \mathrm{C}+\tan \mathrm{C} \cdot \tan \mathrm{A})\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\mathrm {\Rightarrow \tan ^{2} A+\tan ^{2} B+\tan ^{2} C-\tan A \cdot \tan B-\tan B \tan C-\tan C \tan A=0}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \mathrm{ \dfrac{1}{2}\left\{(\tan A-\tan B)^{2}+(\tan B-\tan C)^{2}+(\tan C-\tan A)^{2}\right\}=0} \\\Rightarrow \mathrm{ (\tan A-\tan B)^{2}+(\tan B-\tan C)^{2}+(\tan C-\tan A)^{2}=0 }\end{array}[/math]
কতগুলো রাশির বর্গের সমষ্টি শূন্য হলে রাশিগুলোর মান পৃথক পৃথকভাবে শূন্য হয় ।[math]\begin{array}{l}\therefore \mathrm{(\tan A-\tan B)^{2}=0 } \\\Rightarrow \mathrm{ \tan A-\tan B=0 }\\\Rightarrow \mathrm{ \tan A=\tan B }\\\therefore \mathrm {A=B}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\mathrm{(\tan B-\tan C)^{2}=0} \\\mathrm{ \tan B-\tan C=0 }\\\mathrm{\tan B=\tan C }\\\mathrm{\therefore B=C }\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\mathrm {\therefore A=B=C}[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত)

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক সূত্রটি প্রমাণ করতে ডি মুভ্রের সূত্র ব্যবহার করুন: [math](\cos\theta+i\sin\theta)^5=\cos5\theta+i\sin5\theta[/math]–বাইনোমিয়াল প্রসারণের বাস্তব অংশ নিলে সহজে পাওয়া যাবে [math]\cos5\theta=16\cos^5\theta-20\cos^3\theta+5\cos\theta[/math]।

খ যেহেতু [math]A+B+C=\pi/2[/math], তাই [math]\cos(B+C)=\sin A[/math] ইত্যাদি এবং বাম পাশটি হয় [math]\sin A+\sin B+\sin C[/math]। এখন [math]x=\dfrac{\pi-2A}{4},\;y=\dfrac{\pi-2B}{4},\;z=\dfrac{\pi-2C}{4}[/math] নিলে [math]\sin A=\cos2x=1-2\sin^2x[/math] ইত্যাদি এবং [math]x+y+z=\pi/2[/math] ব্যবহার করে সরলীকরণ করলে প্রদত্ত সমীকরণটি মেলে।

গ [math]\tan x[/math] ধনাত্মক ক্ষেত্রে (0,\,\pi/2) এ উত্তল (convex), তাই জেনসেনের অসমতা দিয়ে [math]\dfrac{\tan A+\tan B+\tan C}{3}\ge \tan\Big(\dfrac{A+B+C}{3}\Big)=\tan\dfrac{\pi}{6}=\dfrac{1}{\sqrt3}[/math]। সমানতার ক্ষেত্রেই মাত্রই [math]A=B=C[/math], এবং প্রদত্ত শর্তে সমানতা হওয়ায় [math]A=B=C[/math] প্রমাণিত।

Question #73 (ID: 473745)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2023 | Boards:  | Tags: Jessore Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\mathrm {POR}[/math] একটি ত্রিভুজ।

Options:
ক. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\mathrm {2 \cos x=\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2+2 \cos 4 x}} .}[/math]
খ. উদ্দীপক হতে প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\begin{array}{l}\mathrm {1+4 \sin \dfrac{Q+R}{4} \cdot \sin \dfrac{R+P}{4} \cdot \sin \dfrac{P+Q}{4} =\sin \dfrac{P}{2}+\sin \dfrac{Q}{2}+\sin \dfrac{R}{2}}\end{array}[/math]
গ. উদ্দীপক হতে প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\mathrm{p}^{3} \cos (\mathrm{Q}-\mathrm{R})+\mathrm{q}^{3} \cos (\mathrm{R}-\mathrm{P})+\mathrm{r}^{3} \cos (\mathrm{P}-\mathrm{Q})=3 \mathrm{pqr}[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]\\[/math]
বামপক্ষ [math]\mathrm {=2 \cos x}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\mathrm {=\sqrt{4 \cos ^{2} x}=\sqrt{2.2 \cos ^{2} x}} \\\mathrm {=\sqrt{2(1+\cos 2 x)}=\sqrt{2+2 \cos 2 x} }\\\mathrm {=\sqrt{2+\sqrt{4 \cos ^{2} 2 x}}=\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2(1+\cos 4 x)}}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\mathrm {\therefore 2 \cos x=\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2+2 \cos 4 x}}}[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত)খ [math]\\[/math]
বামপক্ষ [math]\mathrm {=1+4 \sin \dfrac{Q+R}{4} \sin \dfrac{R+P}{4} \sin \dfrac{P+Q}{4}}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=1+2\left(2 \sin \dfrac{\mathrm{Q}+\mathrm{R}}{4} \sin \dfrac{\mathrm{R}+\mathrm{P}}{4}\right) \sin \dfrac{\mathrm{P}+\mathrm{Q}}{4} \\=1+2\left\{\cos \left(\dfrac{\mathrm{Q}-\mathrm{P}}{4}\right)-\cos \left(\dfrac{\mathrm{P}+\mathrm{Q}+2 \mathrm{R}}{4}\right)\right\} \sin \left(\dfrac{\mathrm{P}+\mathrm{Q}}{4}\right) \\=1+2 \cos \dfrac{\mathrm{Q}-\mathrm{P}}{4} \sin \dfrac{\mathrm{P}+\mathrm{Q}}{4}-2 \cos \dfrac{\mathrm{P}+\mathrm{Q}+2 \mathrm{R}}{4} \sin \dfrac{\mathrm{P}+\mathrm{Q}}{4}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l} \mathrm {=1+\sin \left(\dfrac{P+Q}{4}+\dfrac{Q-P}{4}\right)+\sin \left(\dfrac{P+Q}{4}-\dfrac{Q-P}{4}\right) -\left\{\sin \left(\dfrac{P+Q}{4}+\dfrac{P+Q+2 R}{4}\right)+\sin \left(\dfrac{P+Q}{4}-\dfrac{P+Q+2 R}{4}\right)\right\}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=1+\sin \dfrac{\mathrm{Q}}{2}+\sin \dfrac{\mathrm{P}}{2}-\left\{\sin \dfrac{\mathrm{P}+\mathrm{Q}+\mathrm{R}}{2}+\sin \left(-\dfrac{\mathrm{R}}{2}\right)\right\} \\=1+\sin \dfrac{\mathrm{Q}}{2}+\sin \dfrac{\mathrm{P}}{2}-\left\{\sin \dfrac{\mathrm{P}+\mathrm{Q}+\mathrm{R}}{2}-\sin \left(\dfrac{\mathrm{R}}{2}\right)\right\}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=1+\sin \dfrac{\mathrm{Q}}{2}+\sin \dfrac{\mathrm{P}}{2}-\sin \dfrac{\pi}{2}+\sin \dfrac{\mathrm{R}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\quad[\because \Delta \mathrm{PQR}-[/math]
 এ [math]\mathrm{P}+\mathrm{Q}+\mathrm{R}=\pi][/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\mathrm {=1+\sin \dfrac{P}{2}+\sin \dfrac{Q}{2}+\sin \dfrac{R}{2}-1 }\\\mathrm {=\sin \dfrac{P}{2}+\sin \dfrac{Q}{2}+\sin \dfrac{R}{2}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=[/math]
 ডানপক্ষ (প্রমাণিত)গ [math]\\[/math]
বামপক্ষের ১ম অংশ [math]=\mathrm{p}^{3} \cos (\mathrm{Q}-\mathrm{R})[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\mathrm{=p^{3}(\cos Q \cos R+\sin Q \sin R)} \\\mathrm{=p\left(p^{2} \cos Q \cos R+p^{2} \sin Q \sin R\right) }\\\mathrm{=p(p \cos Q \cdot p \cos R+p \sin Q \cdot p \sin R)}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\mathrm{=p\left\{(r-q \cos P)(q-r \cos P)+2 R \sin P .\dfrac{q}{2 R} \cdot 2 R \sin p \cdot \dfrac{r}{2 R}\right\} }\\\mathrm{=p\left\{q r-\left(q^{2}+r^{2}\right) \cos P+q r \cos ^{2} p+q r \sin ^{2} p\right\}} \\\mathrm{=p\left\{q r-\left(q^{2}+r^{2}\right) \cos P+q r\right\} }\\\mathrm{=p\left\{2 q r-\left(q^{2}+r^{2}\right) \cos P\right\}=2 p q r-p\left(q^{2}+r^{2}\right) \cos P}\end{array}[/math]
অনুরূপভাবে, ২য় অংশ [math]\mathrm {=2 \mathrm{pqr}-\mathrm{q}\left(\mathrm{p}^{2}+\mathrm{r}^{2}\right) \cos Q}[/math]
৩য় অংশ [math]=2 \mathrm{pqr}-\mathrm{r}\left(\mathrm{p}^{2}+\mathrm{q}^{2}\right) \cos \mathrm{R}[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 বামপক্ষ [math]=\mathrm{p}^{3} \cos (\mathrm{Q}-\mathrm{R})+\mathrm{q}^{3} \cos (\mathrm{R}-\mathrm{P})+\mathrm{q}^{3} \cos (\mathrm{P}-\mathrm{Q})[/math]
 [math]\begin{aligned}=2 \mathrm{pqr}-\mathrm{p}\left(\mathrm{q}^{2}+\mathrm{r}^{2}\right) & \cos \mathrm{P}+2 \mathrm{pqr} -\mathrm{q}\left(\mathrm{p}^{2}+\mathrm{r}^{2}\right) \cos \mathrm{Q}+2 \mathrm{pqr}-\mathrm{r}\left(\mathrm{p}^{2}+\mathrm{q}^{2}\right) \cos \mathrm{R}\end{aligned}[/math]
 [math]\begin{aligned}=6 \mathrm{pqr}-\left\{\mathrm{pq}^{2} \cos \mathrm{P}+\mathrm{pr}^{2}\right. & \cos \mathrm{P}+\mathrm{qp}^{2} \cos \mathrm{Q} +\mathrm{qr}^{2} \cos \mathrm{Q}+\mathrm{rp}^{2} \cos \mathrm{R}+\mathrm{rq}^{2} \cos \mathrm{\}}\end{aligned}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=6 \mathrm{pqr}-\{\mathrm{pq}(\mathrm{q} \cos \mathrm{P}+\mathrm{p} \cos \mathrm{Q})+\mathrm{qr} (\mathrm{r} \cos \mathrm{Q}+\mathrm{q} \cos \mathrm{R})+\mathrm{pr}(\mathrm{r} \cos \mathrm{P}+\mathrm{p} \cos \mathrm{R})\}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=6 \mathrm{pqr}-(\mathrm{pqr}+\mathrm{pqr}+\mathrm{pqr})=6 \mathrm{pqr}-3 \mathrm{pqr}[/math]
 [math]=3 \mathrm {pqr} =[/math]
 ডানপক্ষ (প্রমাণিত)

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:
ক সহজে দেখানো যায় যে ভিতরের থেকে বাইরের ধাপে হালফা-কোণ সূত্র প্রয়োগ করলে ফল পাওয়া যায়: প্রথমে [math]\sqrt{2+2\cos4x}=2\cos2x[/math] (প্রধান বর্গমূল ধরে নেওয়া হলে), এবং এরপর [math]\sqrt{2+2\cos2x}=2\cos x[/math]; ফলে [math]2\cos x=\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2+2\cos4x}}[/math]। 

খ ধরা যাক [math]a=\dfrac{Q+R}{4},\; b=\dfrac{R+P}{4},\; c=\dfrac{P+Q}{4}[/math], তাহলে [math]a+b+c=\dfrac{\pi}{2}[/math] এবং ডানপাশটি হচ্ছে [math]\cos2a+\cos2b+\cos2c[/math]; পরিচিত ত্রিকোণীয় সূত্র প্রয়োগে [math]\cos2a+\cos2b+\cos2c=1+4\sin a\sin b\sin c[/math], যেটি আগের সমীকরণের বামে থাকা প্রকাশের সমান—অতএব সমীকরণটি সঠিক। 

গ সাইডগুলোকে বাহুগত রেডিয়াস [math]R[/math] দিয়ে লিখলে [math]p=2R\sin P[/math] ইত্যাদি হয়; প্রতিটি টার্মে [math](2R)^3[/math] গুণ থাকায় কেটে গেলে প্রয়োজনীয় সমীকরণ দাঁড়ায় [math]\sum\sin^3P\cos(Q-R)=3\sin P\sin Q\sin R[/math]। এখানে [math]\cos(Q-R)=\cos Q\cos R+\sin Q\sin R[/math] বিকৃত করে সিনেমেট্রিক সমিকরণগুলো সরলীকরণ করলে বামদিক থেকে ডানদিক পাওয়া যায়, তাই প্রদত্ত সমীকরণ সঠিক।

Question #74 (ID: 473742)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2023 | Boards:  | Tags: Cumilla Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
উদ্দীপক- [math]\mathrm I :[/math] [math]\Delta\mathrm {ABC}[/math] এ [math]\mathrm {A+B+C= \pi}[/math]

উদ্দীপক- [math]\mathrm {II} :[/math]


[Image]


Options:
ক. উদ্দীপক-I থেকে প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\mathrm {\tan A+\tan B+\tan C=\tan A \tan B \tan C}[/math]
খ. উদ্দীপক-II থেকে প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\mathrm {\tan \dfrac{C-A}{2}=\dfrac{c-a}{c+a} \cot \dfrac{B}{2}}[/math]
গ. উদ্দীপক-I থেকে প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\sin ^{2} \dfrac{\mathrm{A}}{2}+\sin ^{2} \dfrac{\mathrm{B}}{2}+\sin ^{2} \dfrac{\mathrm{C}}{2}=1-2 \sin \dfrac{\mathrm{A}}{2} \sin \dfrac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \sin \dfrac{\mathrm{C}}{2}[/math] ।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]\\[/math]
দেওয়া আছে, [math]\mathrm {A+B+C= \pi}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \mathrm { A+B=\pi -C } \Rightarrow \mathrm { \tan (A+B)=\tan (\pi-C) }\\\Rightarrow \mathrm { \dfrac{\tan A+\tan B}{1-\tan A \tan B}=-\tan C}\\\Rightarrow \mathrm { \tan A+\tan B=-\tan C+\tan A \tan B \tan C}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\mathrm {\therefore \tan A+\tan B+\tan C=\tan A \tan B \tan C}[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত)[math]\\[/math]
 খ [math]\\[/math]
 [math]\triangle \mathrm{BCA}[/math]
 হতে পাই,[math]\begin{array}{l} \mathrm { \dfrac{b}{\sin B}=\dfrac{a}{\sin A}=\dfrac{c}{\sin C} \Rightarrow \dfrac{c}{a}=\dfrac{\sin C}{\sin A} }\\\Rightarrow \mathrm { \dfrac{c-a}{c+a}=\dfrac{\sin C-\sin A}{\sin C+\sin A}=\dfrac{2 \cos \dfrac{C+A}{2} \sin \dfrac{C-A}{2}}{2 \sin \dfrac{C+A}{2} \cos \dfrac{C-A}{2}}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \dfrac{\mathrm{c}-\mathrm{a}}{\mathrm{c}+\mathrm{a}}=\cot \dfrac{\mathrm{C}+\mathrm{A}}{2} \tan \dfrac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}\\\Rightarrow \dfrac{\mathrm{c}-\mathrm{a}}{\mathrm{c}+\mathrm{a}}=\cot \left(\dfrac{\pi}{2}-\dfrac{\mathrm{B}}{2}\right) \tan \left(\dfrac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2 \mathrm{y}}\right)\\\Rightarrow \dfrac{\mathrm{c}-\mathrm{a}}{\mathrm{c}+\mathrm{a}}=\tan \dfrac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \tan \left(\dfrac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}\right)\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\mathrm {\therefore \tan \dfrac{C-A}{2}=\dfrac{c-a}{c+a} \cot \dfrac{B}{2}}[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত)[math]\\[/math]
 গ [math]\\[/math]
বামপক্ষ [math]=\sin ^{2} \dfrac{\mathrm{A}}{2}+\sin ^{2} \dfrac{\mathrm{B}}{2}+\sin ^{2} \dfrac{\mathrm{C}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\dfrac{1}{2}\left(2 \sin ^{2} \dfrac{\mathrm{A}}{2}+2 \sin ^{2} \dfrac{\mathrm{B}}{2}\right)+\sin ^{2} \dfrac{\mathrm{C}}{2} \\=\dfrac{1}{2}(1-\cos \mathrm{A}+1-\cos \mathrm{B})+\sin ^{2} \dfrac{\mathrm{C}}{2} \\=1-\dfrac{1}{2}(\cos \mathrm{A}+\cos \mathrm{B})+\sin ^{2} \dfrac{\mathrm{C}}{2} \\=1-\dfrac{1}{2} \cdot 2 \cos \left(\dfrac{\mathrm{A}}{2}+\dfrac{\mathrm{B}}{2}\right) \cos \left(\dfrac{\mathrm{A}}{2}-\dfrac{\mathrm{B}}{2}\right)+\sin ^{2} \dfrac{\mathrm{C}}{2} \\=1-\cos \left(\dfrac{\pi}{2}-\dfrac{\mathrm{C}}{2}\right) \cos \left(\dfrac{\mathrm{A}}{2}-\dfrac{\mathrm{B}}{2}\right)+\sin ^{2} \dfrac{\mathrm{C}}{2} \\\quad\left[\because \mathrm{A}+\mathrm{B}+\mathrm{C}=\pi \therefore \dfrac{\mathrm{A}}{2}+\dfrac{\mathrm{B}}{2}+\dfrac{\mathrm{C}}{2}=\dfrac{\pi}{2}\right]\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=1-\sin \dfrac{\mathrm{C}}{2} \cos \left(\dfrac{\mathrm{A}}{2}-\dfrac{\mathrm{B}}{2}\right)+\sin ^{2} \dfrac{\mathrm{C}}{2} \\=1-\sin \dfrac{\mathrm{C}}{2}\left\{\cos \left(\dfrac{\mathrm{A}}{2}-\dfrac{\mathrm{B}}{2}\right)-\sin \left[\dfrac{\pi}{2}-\left(\dfrac{\mathrm{A}}{2}+\dfrac{\mathrm{B}}{2}\right)\right]\right\} \\=1-\sin \dfrac{\mathrm{C}}{2}\left\{\cos \left(\dfrac{\mathrm{A}}{2}-\dfrac{\mathrm{B}}{2}\right)-\cos \left(\dfrac{\mathrm{A}}{2}+\dfrac{\mathrm{B}}{2}\right)\right\} \\=1-\sin \dfrac{\mathrm{C}}{2} \cdot 2 \sin \dfrac{\mathrm{A}}{2} \sin \dfrac{\mathrm{B}}{2}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\mathrm {=1-2 \sin \dfrac{A}{2} \sin \dfrac{B}{2} \sin \dfrac{C}{2}=}[/math]
 ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore \sin ^{2} \dfrac{\mathrm{A}}{2}+\sin ^{2} \dfrac{\mathrm{B}}{2}+\sin ^{2} \dfrac{\mathrm{C}}{2}=1-2 \sin \dfrac{\mathrm{A}}{2} \sin \dfrac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \sin \dfrac{\mathrm{C}}{2}[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত)

Explanation:

Question #75 (ID: 473741)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2023 | Boards:  | Tags: Cumilla Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:

[Image]


Options:
ক. [math]\dfrac{\tan 42^{\circ} \tan 78^{\circ}}{\cot 6^{\circ} \cot 66^{\circ}}[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
খ. প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\mathrm {\tan \dfrac{E}{2}=\dfrac{p-q}{p+q} \cot \left(\dfrac{S-T}{2}\right) .}[/math]
গ. যদি [math]\mathrm{p}^{4}+\mathrm{q}^{4}+\mathrm{r}^{4}=2 \mathrm{p}^{2}\left(\mathrm{q}^{2}+\mathrm{r}^{2}\right)[/math] হয়, তবে দেখাও যে, [math]\mathrm S = 45^{\circ}[/math] অথবা [math]135^{\circ}[/math].


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]\\[/math]
প্রদত্ত রাশি [math]\dfrac{\tan 42^{\circ} \tan 78^{\circ}}{\cot 6^{\circ} \cot 66^{\circ}}=\tan 6^{\circ} \tan 42^{\circ} \tan 66^{\circ} \tan 78^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\tan 18^{\circ} \tan \left(60^{\circ}-18^{\circ}\right) \tan \left(60^{\circ}+18^{\circ}\right) \dfrac{1}{\tan 18^{\circ}} \tan 6^{\circ} \tan 66^{\circ} \\=\tan \left(3 \times 18^{\circ}\right) \tan 6^{\circ} \cdot \tan 66^{\circ} \dfrac{1}{\tan 18^{\circ}} ; \quad\left[\because \tan 3 \mathrm{~A}=\tan \mathrm{A} \tan \left(60^{\circ}+\mathrm{A}\right) \tan \left(60^{\circ}-\mathrm{A}\right)\right]\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\tan 54^{\circ} \tan 6^{\circ} \tan 66^{\circ} \times \dfrac{1}{\tan 18^{\circ}} \\=\tan \left(60^{\circ}-6^{\circ}\right) \tan \left(60^{\circ}+6^{\circ}\right) \cdot \tan 6^{\circ} \dfrac{1}{\tan 18^{\circ}} \\=\tan \left(3 \times 6^{\circ}\right) \dfrac{1}{\tan 18^{\circ}}=\tan 18^{\circ} \cdot \dfrac{1}{\tan 18^{\circ}}=1 \textbf { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খ [math]\\[/math]

[Image]
[math]\Delta \mathrm{EST}[/math]
 হতে পাই,[math]\begin{array}{l}\dfrac{\mathrm{r}}{\sin \mathrm{E}}=\dfrac{\mathrm{q}}{\sin \mathrm{T}}=\dfrac{\mathrm{p}}{\sin \mathrm{S}}\\\Rightarrow \mathrm { \dfrac{p}{q}=\dfrac{\sin S}{\sin T}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \mathrm{\dfrac{p-q}{p+q}=\dfrac{\sin S-\sin T}{\sin S+\sin T}=\dfrac{2 \cos \dfrac{S+T}{2} \sin \dfrac{S-T}{2}}{2 \sin \dfrac{S+T}{2} \cos \dfrac{S-T}{2}}}\\\Rightarrow \dfrac{\mathrm{p}-\mathrm{q}}{\mathrm{p}+\mathrm{q}}=\cot \dfrac{\mathrm{S}+\mathrm{T}}{2} \tan \dfrac{\mathrm{S}-\mathrm{T}}{2}\\\Rightarrow \dfrac{\mathrm{p}-\mathrm{q}}{\mathrm{p}+\mathrm{q}}=\cot \left(\dfrac{\pi}{2}-\dfrac{\mathrm{E}}{2}\right) \tan \left(\dfrac{\mathrm{S}-\mathrm{T}}{2}\right)\\\Rightarrow \dfrac{\mathrm{p}-\mathrm{q}}{\mathrm{p}+\mathrm{q}}=\tan \dfrac{\mathrm{E}}{2} \tan \left(\dfrac{\mathrm{S}-\mathrm{T}}{2}\right)\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \tan \dfrac{\mathrm{E}}{2}=\dfrac{\mathrm{p}-\mathrm{q}}{\mathrm{p}+\mathrm{q}} \cot \left(\dfrac{\mathrm{S}-\mathrm{T}}{2}\right)[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত)[math]\\[/math]
 গ [math]\\[/math]
দেওয়া আছে, [math]\mathrm{p}^{4}+\mathrm{q}^{4}+\mathrm{r}^{4}=2 \mathrm{p}^{2}\left(\mathrm{q}^{2}+\mathrm{r}^{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \mathrm{q^{4}+r^{4}+p^{4}-2 p^{2} q^{2}-2 r^{2} p^{2}=0}\\\Rightarrow \mathrm{\left(q^{2}\right)^{2}+\left(r^{2}\right)^{2}+\left(-p^{2}\right)^{2}+2 q^{2} r^{2}-2 r^{2} p^{2}-2 p^{2} q^{2}=2 q^{2} r^{2}}\\\Rightarrow \left(\mathrm{q}^{2}+\mathrm{r}^{2}-\mathrm{p}^{2}\right)^{2}=2 \mathrm{q}^{2} \mathrm{r}^{2} \Rightarrow \mathrm{q}^{2}+\mathrm{r}^{2}-\mathrm{p}^{2}= \pm \sqrt{2} \mathrm{qr}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \dfrac{\mathrm{q}^{2}+\mathrm{r}^{2}-\mathrm{p}^{2}}{2 \mathrm{qr}}= \pm \dfrac{1}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]
 সুতরাং [math]\cos \mathrm{S}= \pm \dfrac{1}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]
এখন, [math]\mathrm {\cos S=\dfrac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \Rightarrow \cos S=\cos 45^{\circ} \quad \therefore S=45^{\circ}}[/math]
আবার, [math]\mathrm {\cos S=-\dfrac{1}{\sqrt{2}}}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm {\cos S=-\cos 45^{\circ}=\cos \left(180^{\circ}-45^{\circ}\right)=\cos 135^{\circ}}[/math]
অর্থাৎ [math]\mathrm{S}=135^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{S}=45^{\circ}[/math]
 অথবা [math]135^{\circ}[/math]
 (দেখানো হলো)

Explanation:

Question #76 (ID: 473740)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2023 | Boards: Dinajpur Board | Tags: Dinajpur Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
দৃশ্যকল্প -১ : [math]\mathrm {f(x) = \cos x.}[/math]

দৃশ্যকল্প -২ :


[Image]


Options:
ক. [math]\tan \theta=\dfrac{3}{4}[/math] এবং [math]\pi<\theta<\dfrac{3 \pi}{2}[/math] হলে, [math]\operatorname{cosec}(-\theta)+\sec (-\theta)[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর।
খ. [math]\mathrm {f(\alpha)+f(\beta)=a}[/math] এবং [math]\mathrm {f\left(\dfrac{\pi}{2}-\alpha\right)+f\left(\dfrac{\pi}{2}-\beta\right)=b}[/math] হলে প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\mathrm {\sin \dfrac{\alpha+\beta}{2}= \pm \dfrac{b}{\sqrt{a^{2}+b^{2}}}}[/math]
গ. [math]\angle A[/math] এর সাহায্যে [math]\triangle \mathrm {ABC}[/math] এর ক্ষেত্রফল নির্ণয় কর ।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]\\[/math]
দেওয়া আছে, [math]\tan \theta=\dfrac{3}{4}[/math]
 এবং [math]\piখ [math]\\[/math]
দৃশ্যকল্প-১ হতে পাই, [math]\mathrm {f(x) = \cos x}[/math]
দেওয়া আছে, [math]\mathrm {f(\alpha)+f(\beta)=a \ldots \ldots \ldots \text {(i)}}[/math]
এবং [math]\mathrm {f\left(\dfrac{\pi}{2}-\alpha\right)+f\left(\dfrac{\pi}{2}-\beta\right)=b \ldots \ldots \ldots \text {(ii)}}[/math]
এখন, [math]\text {(i)}[/math]
 হতে পাই, [math]\mathrm {\cos \alpha+\cos \beta=a}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \cos \dfrac{\alpha+\beta}{2} \cdot \cos \dfrac{\alpha-\beta}{2}= \mathrm a[/math]
 [math]\mathrm {\therefore 4 \cos ^{2}\left(\dfrac{\alpha+\beta}{2}\right) \cdot \cos ^{2}\left(\dfrac{\alpha-\beta}{2}\right)=a^{2} } \ldots \ldots \ldots \text {(iii)}[/math]
আবার, [math]\text {(ii)}[/math]
 হতে পাই, [math]\mathrm {\cos \left(\dfrac{\pi}{2}-\alpha\right)+\cos \left(\dfrac{\pi}{2}-\beta\right)=b}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \mathrm { \sin \alpha+\sin \beta=b \Rightarrow 2 \sin \dfrac{\alpha+\beta}{2}. \cos \dfrac{\alpha-\beta}{2}=b} \\\therefore \mathrm {4 \sin ^{2}\left(\dfrac{\alpha+\beta}{2}\right) \cdot \cos ^{2}\left(\dfrac{\alpha-\beta}{2}\right)=b^{2}} \ldots \ldots . . \text { (iv) }\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\text {(iii)}[/math]
 ও [math]\text {(iv)}[/math]
 যোগ করে পাই,[math]\begin{array}{r}4 \cos ^{2}\left(\dfrac{\alpha+\beta}{2}\right) \cdot \cos ^{2}\left(\dfrac{\alpha-\beta}{2}\right)+4 \sin ^{2}\left(\dfrac{\alpha+\beta}{2}\right) . \cos ^{2}\left(\dfrac{\alpha-\beta}{2}\right)= \mathrm {a^{2}+b^{2}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \mathrm { 4 \cos ^{2}\left(\dfrac{\alpha-\beta}{2}\right)\left\{\cos ^{2}\left(\dfrac{\alpha+\beta}{2}\right)+\sin ^{2}\left(\dfrac{\alpha+\beta}{2}\right)\right\}=a^{2}+b^{2} } \\\Rightarrow \mathrm { 4 \cos ^{2}\left(\dfrac{\alpha-\beta}{2}\right) \cdot 1=a^{2}+b^{2} \therefore 2 \cos \left(\dfrac{\alpha-\beta}{2}\right)= \pm \sqrt{a^{2}+b^{2}}}\end{array}[/math]
এখন, [math]\mathrm { \sin \alpha+\sin \beta=b \Rightarrow 2 \sin \dfrac{\alpha+\beta}{2} \cdot \cos \dfrac{\alpha-\beta}{2}=b}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm {\sin \dfrac{\alpha+\beta}{2}=\dfrac{b}{2 \cos \dfrac{\alpha-\beta}{2}} \therefore \sin \dfrac{\alpha+\beta}{2}= \pm \dfrac{b}{\sqrt{a^{2}+b^{2}}}}[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত)গ [math]\\[/math]
দেওয়া আছ, [math]\triangle \mathrm{ABC}[/math]
 এ [math]\mathrm{AB}=\mathrm{c}=3 ; \mathrm{BC}=\mathrm{a}=\sqrt{13}[/math]
 এবং [math]\mathrm{AC}=\mathrm{b}=4[/math]
আমরা জানি, [math]\mathrm {\cos A=\dfrac{b^{2}+c^{2}-a^{2}}{2 b c}=\dfrac{4^{2}+3^{2}-(\sqrt{13})^{2}}{2.4 .3}}[/math]
 [math]=\dfrac{16+9-13}{24}=\dfrac{12}{24}=\dfrac{1}{2}=\cos 60^{\circ} \therefore \mathrm{A}=60^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \triangle \mathrm{ABC}[/math]
 এর ক্ষেত্রফল [math]\mathrm {=\dfrac{1}{2} b c \sin A}[/math]
 [math]=\dfrac{1}{2} \times 4 \times 3 \times \sin 60^{\circ}=6 \dfrac{\sqrt{3}}{2}=3 \sqrt{3}[/math]
 বর্গ একক [math]\textbf{(Ans.)}[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক [math]\tan\theta=\dfrac{3}{4}[/math] ও [math]\piখ দৃশ্যকল্পে [math]f(x)=\cos x[/math], তাই [math]\cos\alpha+\cos\beta=a[/math] ও [math]\sin\alpha+\sin\beta=b[/math]. sum-to-product প্রয়োগ করলে [math]2\cos\dfrac{\alpha+\beta}{2}\cos\dfrac{\alpha-\beta}{2}=a[/math] ও [math]2\sin\dfrac{\alpha+\beta}{2}\cos\dfrac{\alpha-\beta}{2}=b[/math]; ভাগ করলে [math]\tan\dfrac{\alpha+\beta}{2}=\dfrac{b}{a}[/math] এবং অতএব [math]\sin\dfrac{\alpha+\beta}{2}=\pm\dfrac{b}{\sqrt{a^{2}+b^{2}}}[/math].

গ ত্রিভুজ [math]\triangle ABC[/math]–এর ক্ষেত্রফল হচ্ছে [math]\dfrac{1}{2}(\text{AB})(\text{AC})\sin\angle A[/math], অর্থাৎ [math]\dfrac{1}{2}bc\sin A[/math] (যেখানে [math]b=AC,\ c=AB[/math]).

Question #77 (ID: 473739)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2023, 2023 | Boards: Rajshahi Board, Mymensingh Board | Tags: Rajshahi Board, Mymensingh Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:

[Image]


[math]\mathrm{ON} \| \mathrm{BN}^{\prime}[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]\mathrm {\tan \theta=\dfrac{y}{x}}[/math] হলে দেখাও যে, [math]\mathrm {x \cos 2 \theta+y \sin 2 \theta=x}[/math]
খ. দৃশ্যকল্প-১ ব্যবহার করে [math]\mathrm {AB}[/math] দূরত্ব নির্ণয় কর।
গ. [math]\dfrac{1}{\mathrm{~T}-\mathrm{m}}+\dfrac{1}{\mathrm{~T}-l}=\dfrac{3}{\mathrm{~T}}[/math] হলে, দৃশ্যকল্প-২ এর ত্রিভুজের [math]\mathrm R[/math] কোণ নির্ণয় কর ।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]\\[/math]
দেওয়া আছে, [math]\mathrm {\tan \theta=\dfrac{y}{x}}[/math]
দেখাতে হবে যে, [math]\mathrm {x \cos 2 \theta+y \sin 2 \theta=x}[/math]
বামপক্ষ [math]\mathrm {=x \cos 2 \theta+y \sin 2 \theta}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\mathrm {=x \dfrac{1-\tan ^{2} \theta}{1+\tan ^{2} \theta}+y \dfrac{2 \tan \theta}{1 \tan ^{2} \theta}=\dfrac{x-x \tan ^{2} \theta+2 y \tan \theta}{1+\tan ^{2} \theta} }\\\mathrm {=\dfrac{x-x \cdot \dfrac{y^{2}}{x^{2}}+2 y \cdot \dfrac{y}{x}}{1+\dfrac{y^{2}}{x^{2}}}=\dfrac{x-\dfrac{y^{2}}{x}+\dfrac{2 y^{2}}{x}}{1+\dfrac{y^{2}}{x^{2}}}=\dfrac{\dfrac{x^{2}+y^{2}}{x}}{\dfrac{x^{2}+y^{2}}{x^{2}}} }\\\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\mathrm {=\dfrac{x^{2}+y^{2}}{x} \times \dfrac{x^{2}}{x^{2}+y^{2}}=x=}[/math]
 ডানপক্ষ[math]\mathrm {\therefore x \cos 2 \theta+y \sin 2 \theta=x}[/math]
 (দেখানো হলো)[math]\\[/math]
 খ [math]\\[/math]

[Image]
চিত্রে, [math]\mathrm {ON || BN'}[/math]
 এবং [math]\mathrm {OB}[/math]
 তাদের ছেদক,[math]\angle \mathrm{OBN}^{\prime}=45^{\circ}[/math]
 হলে, [math]\angle \mathrm{AOB}=180^{\circ}-45^{\circ}=135^{\circ}[/math]
ত্রিভুজের কোসাইন সূত্রানুসারে,[math]\cos \angle \mathrm{AOB}=\dfrac{\mathrm{OA}^{2}+\mathrm{OB}^{2}-\mathrm{AB}^{2}}{2 \times \mathrm{OA} \times \mathrm{OB}}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \cos 135^{\circ}=\dfrac{12^{2}+9^{2}-\mathrm{AB}^{2}}{2 \times 12 \times 9}\\\Rightarrow -\dfrac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \times 216=225-\mathrm{AB}^{2} \Rightarrow \mathrm{AB}^{2}=225+108 \sqrt{2}\\\Rightarrow \mathrm{AB}^{2}=377.74 ~~~\therefore \mathrm{AB}=19.44\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm {AB}[/math]
 এর দূরত্ব [math]19.44 \text { km}[/math]
 (প্রায়) [math]\textbf{(Ans.)}[/math]
 গ [math]\\[/math]
দেওয়া আছে, [math]\mathrm{T}=l+\mathrm{m}+\mathrm{n}[/math]
এবং [math]\dfrac{1}{\mathrm{~T}-\mathrm{m}}+\dfrac{1}{\mathrm{~T}-l}=\dfrac{3}{\mathrm{~T}}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \dfrac{1}{l+\mathrm{m}+\mathrm{n}-{\mathrm{m}}}+\dfrac{1}{l+\mathrm{m}+\mathrm{n}-l}=\dfrac{3}{l+\mathrm{m}+\mathrm{n}}\\\Rightarrow \dfrac{1}{l+\mathrm{n}}+\dfrac{1}{\mathrm{~m}+\mathrm{n}}=\dfrac{3}{l+\mathrm{m}+\mathrm{n}}\\\Rightarrow \dfrac{\mathrm{m}+\mathrm{n}+\mathrm{l}+\mathrm{n}}{(l+\mathrm{n})(\mathrm{m}+\mathrm{n})}=\dfrac{3}{l+\mathrm{m}+\mathrm{n}}\\\Rightarrow (l+\mathrm{m}+\mathrm{n})(l+\mathrm{m}+\mathrm{n}+\mathrm{n})=3(l+\mathrm{n})(\mathrm{m}+\mathrm{n})\\\Rightarrow (l+\mathrm{m}+\mathrm{n})^{2}+l \mathrm{n}+\mathrm{mn}+\mathrm{n}^{2}=3\left(l\mathrm{~m}+l\mathrm{n}+\mathrm{mn}+\mathrm{n}^{2}\right)\\\Rightarrow (l+\mathrm{m}+\mathrm{n})^{2}-3 l\operatorname{m}-2 l \mathrm{n}-2 \mathrm{mn}-2 \mathrm{n}^{2}=0\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow l^{2}+ \mathrm{m}^{2}+\mathrm{n}^{2}+2 l \mathrm{m}+2 \mathrm{m} \mathrm{n}+2 l \mathrm{n}-3 l \mathrm{m}-2 l \mathrm{n}-2 \mathrm{m} \mathrm{n}-2 \mathrm{n}^{2}=0\\\Rightarrow l^{2}+\mathrm{m}^{2}-\mathrm{n}^{2}-l \mathrm{~m}=0 \Rightarrow l^{2}+\mathrm{m}^{2}-\mathrm{n}^{2}=l \mathrm{~m}\\\Rightarrow \dfrac{l^{2}+\mathrm{m}^{2}-\mathrm{n}^{2}}{2 l \mathrm{~m}}=\dfrac{1}{2} \Rightarrow \cos \mathrm{R}=\dfrac{1}{2}=\cos 60^{\circ}\\\therefore \mathrm{R}=60^{\circ} \textbf{ (Ans.)}\end{array}[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক ধরা যাক [math]\;r=\sqrt{x^2+y^2},\;\cos\theta=\dfrac{x}{r},\;\sin\theta=\dfrac{y}{r}\;.[/math] তখন
[math]x\cos2\theta+y\sin2\theta=x(\cos^2\theta-\sin^2\theta)+y(2\sin\theta\cos\theta)
=\dfrac{x(x^2-y^2)+2xy^2}{r^2}=\dfrac{x(x^2+y^2)}{r^2}=x.[/math]

খ যদি বিন্দু A উৎসবিন্দু এবং B-এর নির্দেশকসংখ্যা [math](x,y)[/math] হয় (যেখানে [math]\tan\theta=y/x[/math]), তাহলে কর্ডিনেট দূরত্ব থেকে
[math]\;AB=\sqrt{x^2+y^2}\;[/math] হবে।

গ সমীকরণকে সাধারণ লব্ধিতে লেখলে
[math] \dfrac{2T-(l+m)}{T^2-T(l+m)+lm}=\dfrac{3}{T} [/math] থেকে সরলীকরণে পাওয়া যায়
[math]T^2-2T(l+m)+3lm=0\Rightarrow T=(l+m)\pm|l-m|, [/math]
অর্থাৎ [math]T=2l[/math] অথবা [math]T=2m[/math]. যদি এখানে [math]T=\tan\frac{R}{2}[/math] ধরা হয়, তাহলে
[math]R=2\arctan(2l)\ \text{অথবা}\ R=2\arctan(2m).[/math

Question #78 (ID: 473738)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2023 | Boards: Mymensingh Board | Tags: Mymensingh Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:

[Image]


Options:
ক. দেখাও যে, [math]\sin \dfrac{\pi}{16}=\dfrac{1}{2} \sqrt{2-\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2}}}[/math]
খ. [math]\angle \mathrm{B}=60^{\circ}[/math] হলে দেখাও যে, [math]\mathrm {2 \cos \dfrac{C-A}{2}=\dfrac{c+a}{b}}[/math]
গ. [math]\mathrm {ABC}[/math] ত্রিভুজ হতে, [math]\mathrm {\sin ^{2} A+\sin ^{2} B+\sin ^{2} C -2 \cos A \cos B \cos C}[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর ।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]\\[/math]
প্রদত্ত রাশি [math]=\sin \dfrac{\pi}{16}=\dfrac{1}{2} \sqrt{4 \sin ^{2} \dfrac{\pi}{16}}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\dfrac{1}{2} \sqrt{2.2 \sin ^{2} \dfrac{\pi}{16}}=\dfrac{1}{2} \sqrt{2\left(1-\cos \dfrac{\pi}{8}\right)} \\=\dfrac{1}{2} \sqrt{2-2 \cos \dfrac{\pi}{8}}=\dfrac{1}{2} \sqrt{2-\sqrt{2.2 \cos ^{2} \dfrac{\pi}{8}}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\dfrac{1}{2} \sqrt{2-\sqrt{2\left(1+\cos \dfrac{\pi}{4}\right)}} \\=\dfrac{1}{2} \sqrt{2-\sqrt{2\left(1+\dfrac{1}{\sqrt{2}}\right)}}=\dfrac{1}{2} \sqrt{2-\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2}}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \sin \dfrac{\pi}{16}=\dfrac{1}{2} \sqrt{2-\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2}}}[/math]
 (দেখানো হলো)খ [math]\\[/math]
দেওয়া আছে, [math]\triangle \mathrm {ABC}[/math]
 এর [math]\angle \mathrm B = 60^{\circ}[/math]
ডানপক্ষ [math]\mathrm {=\dfrac{c+a}{b}=\dfrac{2 R \sin C+2 R \sin A}{2 R \sin B}}[/math]
 [ত্রিভুজের সাইন সূত্র][math]\begin{array}{l}=\dfrac{\sin \mathrm{C}+\sin \mathrm{A}}{\sin \mathrm{B}}=\dfrac{2 \sin \dfrac{\mathrm{C}+\mathrm{A}}{2} \cos \dfrac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}}{\sin \mathrm{B}} \\=\dfrac{2 \sin \dfrac{\pi-\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \dfrac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}}{\sin \mathrm{B}}[\because \mathrm{A}+\mathrm{B}+\mathrm{C}=\pi] \\=\dfrac{2 \cos \dfrac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \dfrac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}}{\sin \mathrm{B}}=\dfrac{2 \cos \dfrac{60^{\circ}}{2} \cos \dfrac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}}{\sin 60^{\circ}}\left[\because \mathrm{B}=60^{\circ}\right]\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\mathrm {=\dfrac{2 \cdot \dfrac{\sqrt{3}}{2} \cos \dfrac{C-A}{2}}{\dfrac{\sqrt{3}}{2}}=2 \cos \dfrac{C-A}{2}=}[/math]
 বামপক্ষ[math]\therefore 2 \cos \dfrac{\mathrm{C}-\mathrm{A}}{2}=\dfrac{\mathrm{c}+\mathrm{a}}{\mathrm{b}}[/math]
 (দেখানো হলো)[math]\\[/math]
 গ [math]\\[/math]
প্রদত্ত রাশি [math]=\sin ^{2} \mathrm{~A}+\sin ^{2} \mathrm{~B}+\sin ^{2} \mathrm{C}-2 \cos \mathrm{A} \cos \mathrm{B} \cos \mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\dfrac{1}{2}\left(2 \sin ^{2} \mathrm{~A}+2 \sin ^{2} \mathrm{~B}\right)+\sin ^{2} \mathrm{C}-2 \cos \mathrm{A} \cos \mathrm{B} \cos \mathrm{C} \\=\dfrac{1}{2}(1-\cos 2 \mathrm{~A}+1-\cos 2 \mathrm{~B})+\sin ^{2} \mathrm{C}-2 \cos \mathrm{A} \cos \mathrm{B} \cos \mathrm{C}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=1-\dfrac{1}{2}(\cos 2 \mathrm{~A}+\cos 2 \mathrm{~B})+\sin ^{2} \mathrm{C}-2 \cos \mathrm{A} \cos \mathrm{B} \cos \mathrm{C} \\=1-\dfrac{1}{2} \cdot 2 \cos \dfrac{2 \mathrm{~A}+2 \mathrm{~B}}{2} \cos \dfrac{2 \mathrm{~A}-2 \mathrm{~B}}{2} +\sin ^{2} \mathrm{C}-2 \cos \mathrm{A} \cos \mathrm{B} \cos \mathrm{C}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{aligned}= & \mathrm {1-\cos (A+B) \cos (A-B)+\sin ^{2} C-2 \cos A \cos B \cos C }\\= & \mathrm {1-\cos (\pi-C) \cos (A-B)+1 -\cos ^{2} C-2 \cos A \cos B \cos C}\end{aligned}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}= \mathrm {2+\cos C \cos (A-B)-\cos ^{2} C-2 \cos A \cos B \cos C }\\ \mathrm {=2+\cos C[\cos (A-B)-\cos \{\pi-(A+B)\}] -2 \cos A \cos B \cos C}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\mathrm { =2+\cos C[\cos (A-B)+\cos (A+B)]-2 \cos A \cos B \cos C }\\\mathrm { =2+\cos C \cdot 2 \cos A \cos B-2 \cos A \cos B \cos C }\\\mathrm { =2+2 \cos A \cos B \cos C-2 \cos A \cos B \cos C=2 }\\\mathrm { \therefore \sin ^{2} A+\sin ^{2} B+\sin ^{2} C-2 \cos A \cos B \cos C=2 }\textbf { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]


Explanation:
ক প্রথমে হাফ-অ্যাঙ্গেল সূত্র প্রয়োগ কর: [math]\sin\frac{\pi}{16}=\sqrt{\frac{1-\cos\frac{\pi}{8}}{2}}[/math] এবং [math]\cos\frac{\pi}{8}=\sqrt{\frac{1+\cos\frac{\pi}{4}}{2}}=\sqrt{\frac{1+\frac{\sqrt{2}}{2}}{2}}[/math] হলে সহজভাবে সরলীকরণ করলে [math]\sin\frac{\pi}{16}=\dfrac{1}{2}\sqrt{2-\sqrt{2+\sqrt{2}}}[/math] পাওয়া যায়। 

খ ধরি [math]a=2R\sin A,\;b=2R\sin B,\;c=2R\sin C[/math], তাহলে [math]\dfrac{c+a}{b}=\dfrac{\sin C+\sin A}{\sin B}=\dfrac{2\sin\frac{A+C}{2}\cos\frac{C-A}{2}}{\sin B}[/math]. কিন্তু [math]\frac{A+C}{2}=\frac{\pi-B}{2}=\frac{\pi}{2}-\frac{B}{2}[/math], তাই [math]\sin\frac{A+C}{2}=\cos\frac{B}{2} এবং [math]B=60^\circ[/math] হলে [math]\dfrac{c+a}{b}=\dfrac{2\cos\frac{B}{2}\cos\frac{C-A}{2}}{\sin B}=2\cos\frac{C-A}{2}[/math] হয়।

গ পরিচিত সূত্র ব্যবহার করে [math]\sin^2x=\tfrac{1-\cos2x}{2}</math]; তাই [math]\sum\sin^2A=\tfrac{3}{2}-\tfrac{1}{2}(\cos2A+\cos2B+\cos2C)</math]. তর্কসাপেক্ষে [math]\cos2A+\cos2B+\cos2C=-1-4\cos A\cos B\cos C</math] ফলে সমীকরণ সরল করলে [math]\sin^2A+\sin^2B+\sin^2C-2\cos A\cos B\cos C=2[/math] পাওয়া যায়।

Question #79 (ID: 473737)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2023 | Boards: Dhaka Board | Tags: Dhaka Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
দৃশ্যকল্প -১ :


[Image]


দৃশ্যকল্প -২ : [math]\mathrm {\cos x+\cos y=a, \sin x+\sin y=b.}[/math]

Options:
ক. [math]\tan3\theta[/math] কে [math]\tan\theta[/math] এর মাধ্যমে প্রকাশ কর।
খ. দৃশ্যকল্প-২ এর আলোকে [math]\mathrm {\cos(x + y)}[/math] এর মান [math]\mathrm a[/math] ও [math]\mathrm b[/math] এর মাধ্যমে প্রকাশ কর।
গ. দৃশ্যকল্প-১ এর আলোকে প্রমাণ কর যে, [math]\mathrm{BC} \cos \mathrm{C}-\mathrm{BC} \cos \mathrm{B}=(\mathrm{AC}-\mathrm{AB})(1+\cos \mathrm{A}) .[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]\\[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\tan 3 \theta=\tan (\theta+2 \theta) \\=\dfrac{\tan \theta+\tan 2 \theta}{1-\tan \theta \cdot \tan 2 \theta}=\dfrac{\tan \theta+\dfrac{2 \tan \theta}{1-\tan ^{2} \theta}}{1-\tan \theta \dfrac{2 \tan \theta}{1-\tan ^{2} \theta}} \\=\dfrac{\tan \theta-\tan ^{3} \theta+2 \tan \theta}{1-\tan ^{2} \theta-2 \tan ^{2} \theta}=\dfrac{3 \tan \theta-\tan ^{3} \theta}{1-3 \tan ^{2} \theta} \textbf { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]
বিকল্প সমাধান :[math]\begin{aligned}\tan 3 \theta & =\tan (\theta+\theta+\theta) \\& =\dfrac{\tan \theta+\tan \theta+\tan \theta-\tan \theta \cdot \tan \theta \cdot \tan \theta}{1-\tan \theta \cdot \tan \theta-\tan \theta \cdot \tan \theta-\tan \theta \cdot \tan \theta} \\& =\dfrac{3 \tan \theta-\tan ^{3} \theta}{1-3 \tan ^{2} \theta} \textbf {(Ans.) }\end{aligned}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খ [math]\\[/math]
উদ্দীপক হতে পাই, [math]\cos\text x + \cos \text y = \text a[/math]
 [math]\mathrm {\therefore 2 \cdot \cos \dfrac{x+y}{2} \cdot \cos \dfrac{x-y}{2}=a \ldots \ldots \ldots \text { (i) }}[/math]
আবার, [math]\mathrm {\sin x+\sin y=b}[/math]
 [math]\mathrm {\therefore 2 \cdot \sin \dfrac{x+y}{2} \cdot \cos \dfrac{x-y}{2}=b \ldots \ldots \ldots \text {(ii)}}[/math]
 [math]\text {(ii) ÷ (i) }[/math]
 হতে পাই, [math]\mathrm {\dfrac{\sin \dfrac{x+y}{2}}{\cos \dfrac{x+y}{2}}=\dfrac{b}{a}}[/math]
 [math]\mathrm {\Rightarrow \tan \dfrac{x+y}{2}=\dfrac{b}{a} \Rightarrow \tan ^{2} \dfrac{x+y}{2}=\dfrac{b^{2}}{a^{2}} \Rightarrow \dfrac{1}{\tan ^{2} \dfrac{x+y}{2}}=\dfrac{a^{2}}{b^{2}}}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm {\dfrac{1-\tan ^{2} \dfrac{x+y}{2}}{1+\tan ^{2} \dfrac{x+y}{2}}=\dfrac{a^{2}-b^{2}}{a^{2}+b^{2}}}[/math]
 [বিয়োজন-যোজন][math]\Rightarrow \cos \left\{2 \times\left(\dfrac{\mathrm{x}+\mathrm{y}}{2}\right)\right\}=\dfrac{\mathrm{a}^{2}-\mathrm{b}^{2}}{\mathrm{a}^{2}+\mathrm{b}^{2}}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \cos (\mathrm{x}+\mathrm{y})=\dfrac{\mathrm{a}^{2}-\mathrm{b}^{2}}{\mathrm{a}^{2}+\mathrm{b}^{2}} \textbf { (Ans.) }[/math]
 গ [math]\\[/math]
বামপক্ষ [math]\mathrm {=B C \cos C-B C \cos B}[/math]
 [math]\mathrm {=a \cos C-a \cos B=b-c \cos A-c+b \cos A}[/math]
 [math]\mathrm {[\because b=\cos A+a \cos C }[/math]
 এবং [math]\mathrm { c=b \cos A+a \cos B]}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\mathrm {=(b-c)+(b-c) \cos A} \\\mathrm {=(b-c)(1+\cos A)}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\mathrm {=(A C-A B)(1+\cos A)=}[/math]
 ডানপক্ষ[math]\mathrm {\therefore B C \cos C-B C \cos B=(A C-A B)(1+\cos A)}[/math]
 (প্রমাণিত)

Explanation:
ক [math]\tan3\theta[/math]–কে যুক্তি সূত্র থেকে পাওয়া যায়; প্রথমে [math]\tan2\theta=\dfrac{2\tan\theta}{1-\tan^2\theta}[/math] ব্যবহার করে এবং [math]\tan(2\theta+\theta)=\dfrac{\tan2\theta+\tan\theta}{1-\tan2\theta\tan\theta}[/math] বসালে ফল হয় [math]\tan3\theta=\dfrac{3\tan\theta-\tan^3\theta}{1-3\tan^2\theta}.[/math]

খ বর্গ করে যোগ ও বিয়োগ করে পাই [math]a^2+b^2=2[1+\cos(x-y)][/math] এবং [math]a^2-b^2=2\cos(x+y)[1+\cos(x-y)][/math] ; তাই ভাগ করলে সরলভাবে পাওয়া যায় [math]\cos(x+y)=\dfrac{a^2-b^2}{a^2+b^2}.[/math]

গ ত্রিভুজের পাশে ধরে নিলে ধরে নিন [math]a=BC,\;b=CA,\;c=AB[/math]; কসমাইন সূত্র অনুযায়ী [math]a\cos C=\dfrac{a^2+b^2-c^2}{2b},\;a\cos B=\dfrac{a^2+c^2-b^2}{2c}[/math] এবং তাদের পার্থক্য সরল করলে সংখ্যা গুলি যোগ করলে [math](b-c)\bigl((b+c)^2-a^2\bigr)/(2bc)[/math] পাওয়া যাবে; কিন্তু কসমাইন সূত্র থেকে [math](b+c)^2-a^2=2bc(1+\cos A)[/math] হওয়ায় শেষ পর্যন্ত [math]a\cos C-a\cos B=(b-c)(1+\cos A)[/math], অর্থাৎ দেওয়া সমীকরণ প্রমাণিত।
