Question #80 (ID: 473736)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2023 | Boards: Dhaka Board | Tags: Dhaka Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:

[Image]


Options:
ক. [math]\cot \theta = \sqrt{2}[/math] হলে [math]\cos 2\theta[/math] এর মান নির্ণয় কর ।
খ. উদ্দীপকের আলোকে দেখাও যে, [math]\mathrm {\dfrac{\sqrt{3}}{4} \operatorname{cosec} A-\dfrac{1}{4} \sec A=1}[/math]
গ. উদ্দীপকের আলোকে দেখাও যে, [math]\mathrm {3-\cos ^{2}(\theta+A)-\cos ^{2} A-\cos ^{2}(\theta-A)=\dfrac{3}{2}}[/math]


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক [math]\\[/math]
দেওয়া আছে, [math]\cot \theta=\sqrt{2} \quad \therefore \tan \theta=\dfrac{1}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l} \therefore \cos 2 \theta=\dfrac{1-\tan ^{2} \theta}{1+\tan ^{2} \theta}=\dfrac{1-\left(\dfrac{1}{\sqrt{2}}\right)^{2}}{1+\left(\dfrac{1}{\sqrt{2}}\right)^{2}}=\dfrac{1-\dfrac{1}{2}}{1+\dfrac{1}{2}} \\ \quad=\dfrac{2-1}{2+1}=\dfrac{1}{3} \textbf { (Ans.) }\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 খ [math]\\[/math]
 [math]\triangle \mathrm{ABC}[/math]
 এ [math]\angle \mathrm{A}+40^{\circ}+120^{\circ}=180^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \angle \mathrm{A}=20^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 বামপক্ষ [math]=\dfrac{\sqrt{3}}{4} \operatorname{cosec} \mathrm{A}-\dfrac{1}{4} \sec \mathrm{A}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\dfrac{1}{4}\{\sqrt{3} \operatorname{cosec} A-\sec A\}=\dfrac{1}{4}\left(\dfrac{\sqrt{3}}{\sin A}-\dfrac{1}{\cos A}\right) \\=\dfrac{1}{4}\left(\dfrac{\sqrt{3} \cos A-\sin A}{\sin A \cos A}\right)=\dfrac{\dfrac{\sqrt{3}}{2} \cos A-\dfrac{1}{2} \sin A}{2 \sin A \cos A}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=\dfrac{\sin 60^{\circ} \cdot \cos 20^{\circ}-\cos 60^{\circ} \cdot \sin 20^{\circ}}{\sin \left(2 \times 20^{\circ}\right)}=\dfrac{\sin \left(60^{\circ}-20^{\circ}\right)}{\sin 40^{\circ}}[/math]
 [math]=\dfrac{\sin 40^{\circ}}{\sin 40^{\circ}}=1=[/math]
 ডান পক্ষ[math]\mathrm {\therefore \dfrac{\sqrt{3}}{4} \operatorname{cosec} A-\dfrac{1}{4} \sec A=1}[/math]
 (দেখানো হলো)[math]\\[/math]
 গ [math]\\[/math]
উদ্দীপক হতে পাই, [math]\theta=180^{\circ}-120^{\circ}=60^{\circ}[/math]
এবং, [math]\mathrm {A } = 20^{\circ}[/math]
 [‘ক’ হতে প্রাপ্ত][math]\therefore[/math]
 বামপক্ষ [math]\mathrm {=3-\cos ^{2}(\theta+A)-\cos ^{2} A-\cos ^{2}(\theta-A)}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=3-\cos ^{2}\left(60^{\circ}+20^{\circ}\right)-\cos ^{2} 20^{\circ}-\cos ^{2}\left(60^{\circ}-20^{\circ}\right) \\=3-\cos ^{2} 80^{\circ}-\cos ^{2} 20^{\circ}-\cos ^{2} 40^{\circ} \\=3-\cos ^{2} 20^{\circ}-\left(\cos ^{2} 80^{\circ}+\cos ^{2} 40^{\circ}\right) \\=3-\cos ^{2} 20^{\circ}-\dfrac{1}{2}\left(2 \cos ^{2} 80^{\circ}+2 \cos ^{2} 40^{\circ}\right) \\=3-\cos ^{2} 20^{\circ}-\dfrac{1}{2}\left(1+\cos 160^{\circ}+1+\cos 80^{\circ}\right) \\=3-\cos ^{2} 20^{\circ}-1-\dfrac{1}{2}\left(\cos 160^{\circ}+\cos 80^{\circ}\right)\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=2-\cos ^{2} 20^{\circ}-\dfrac{1}{2} \times 2 \times \cos 120^{\circ} \times \cos 40^{\circ} \\=2-\cos ^{2} 20^{\circ}-\dfrac{1}{2} \times 2 \times\left(-\dfrac{1}{2}\right) \times \cos 40^{\circ}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]=2-\cos ^{2} 20^{\circ}+\dfrac{1}{2} \cos 40^{\circ}=2-\cos ^{2} 20^{\circ}+\dfrac{1}{2}\left(2 \cos ^{2} 20^{\circ}-1\right)[/math]
 [math]=2-\cos ^{2} 20^{\circ}+\cos ^{2} 20^{\circ}-\dfrac{1}{2}=\dfrac{3}{2}=[/math]
 ডানপক্ষ[math]\therefore \mathrm {3-\cos ^{2}(\theta+A)-\cos ^{2} A-\cos ^{2}(\theta-A)=\dfrac{3}{2}}[/math]
 (দেখানো হলো)

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:

ক কোটানজেন্ট থেকে [math]\cot\theta=\sqrt{2}[/math] হলে [math]\tan\theta=1/\sqrt{2}[/math] এবং সরল অনুপাত ধরে নিতে পারি [math]\cos\theta=\dfrac{\sqrt{2}}{\sqrt{3}},\ \sin\theta=\dfrac{1}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]; তাই [math]\cos2\theta=\cos^2\theta-\sin^2\theta=\dfrac{2}{3}-\dfrac{1}{3}=\dfrac{1}{3}.[/math]

খ সরলীকরণে multiply করে পাওয়া যায় [math]\sqrt{3}\cos A-\sin A=4\sin A\cos A=2\sin2A[/math], আর বামদিকে [math]\sqrt{3}\cos A-\sin A=2\bigl(\tfrac{\sqrt{3}}{2}\cos A-\tfrac{1}{2}\sin A\bigr)=2\cos(A+30^\circ)[/math]; তাই [math]\cos(A+30^\circ)=\sin2A[/math] যা থেকে (উদ্দীপকে প্রদর্শিত) [math]A=20^\circ[/math] নিলে প্রদত্ত সমীকরণটি সত্য হয়।

গ প্রতিটি [math]\cos^2 x[/math] কে [math]\dfrac{1+\cos2x}{2}[/math] দিয়ে বদলে দিলে বাকি অংশগুলো মিলিয়ে পাওয়া যায় [math]3-\bigl(\cos^2(\theta+A)+\cos^2A+\cos^2(\theta-A)\bigr)=\dfrac{3-\bigl(\cos2(\theta+A)+\cos2A+\cos2(\theta-A)\bigr)}{2}[/math] এবং [math]\cos2(\theta+A)+\cos2(\theta-A)=2\cos2\theta\cos2A[/math] হলে সরলীকরণ দিলে প্রয়োজনীয় ফলে পৌঁছায়; উদ্দীপ্ত চিত্র অনুযায়ী [math]\cos2A=0[/math] (অর্থাৎ [math]A=45^\circ[/math]) হলে প্রকাশটি [math]\dfrac{3}{2}[/math] হয়।

Question #81 (ID: 473702)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards:  | Tags: Cantonment Public School & College, Rangpur
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\tan 58^{\circ}-\tan 32^{\circ}=?[/math]

Options:


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]A+B=90^{\circ}[/math]
 হলে, [math]\tan A-\tan B=2 \tan (A-B)[/math]
যেহেতু, [math]58^{\circ}+32^{\circ}=90^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\begin{aligned}\therefore \tan 58^{\circ}-\tan 32^{\circ} & =2 \tan \left(58^{\circ}-32^{\circ}\right) \\&\Rightarrow 2 \tan 26^{\circ}\end{aligned}[/math]


Explanation:
Explanation: Since [math]\tan(90^\circ-x)=\cot x[/math], we have [math]\tan58^\circ=\cot32^\circ[/math], so [math]\tan58^\circ-\tan32^\circ=\cot32^\circ-\tan32^\circ=\frac{1-\tan^2 32^\circ}{\tan32^\circ}[/math]. Using [math]1-\tan^2 x=\dfrac{\cos2x}{\sin x\cos x}[/math] this equals [math]\dfrac{\cos64^\circ}{\tfrac{1}{2}\sin64^\circ}=2\cot64^\circ[/math], which is the given correct choice.

Question #82 (ID: 473703)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards:  | Tags: Ahammad Uddin Shah Shishu Niketon School & College, Gaibandha
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\tan \frac{\pi}{20}+\tan \frac{\pi}{5}+\tan \frac{\pi}{20} \tan \frac{\pi}{5}=?[/math]

Options:


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\tan \frac{\pi}{4}=1[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \tan \left(\frac{\pi}{20}+\frac{\pi}{5}\right)=1[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{\tan \frac{\pi}{20}+\tan \frac{\pi}{5}}{1-\tan \frac{\pi}{20} \cdot \tan \frac{\pi}{5}}[/math]
 [math]=1 \text {. }[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \tan \frac{\pi}{20}+\tan \frac{\pi}{5}[/math]
 [math]=1-\tan \frac{\pi}{20} \cdot \tan \frac{\pi}{5}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \tan \frac{\pi}{20}+\tan[/math]
 [math]\frac{\pi}{5}+\tan \frac{\pi}{20}[/math]
 [math]\cdot \tan \frac{\pi}{5}=1[/math]


Explanation:
Explanation: Let [math]A=\frac{\pi}{20}[/math] and [math]B=\frac{\pi}{5}[/math], then [math]A+B=\frac{\pi}{4}[/math] and [math]\tan(A+B)=1[/math]. Using [math]\tan(A+B)=\frac{\tan A+\tan B}{1-\tan A\tan B}=1[/math] gives [math]\tan A+\tan B=1-\tan A\tan B[/math], hence [math]\tan A+\tan B+\tan A\tan B=1[/math].

Question #83 (ID: 473709)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards:  | Tags: RCPSCG
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\cos \theta=\frac{1}{2}\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)[/math] হলে [math]\cos 2 \theta=[/math] কত ?

Options:


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\cos 2 \theta =2 \cos ^{2} \theta-1[/math]
 [math]=2 \cdot \frac{1}{4}\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)^{2}-1[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\frac{1}{2}\left(x^{2}+\frac{1}{x^{2}}+2-2\right)[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{2}\left(x^{2}+\frac{1}{x^{2}}\right)[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: আমরা জানি [math]\cos 2\theta=2\cos^2\theta-1[/math]. এখানে [math]\cos\theta=\tfrac{1}{2}\bigl(x+\tfrac{1}{x}\bigr)[/math] হলে
[math]\cos 2\theta=2\cdot\Bigl(\tfrac{1}{2}\bigl(x+\tfrac{1}{x}\bigr)\Bigr)^2-1=\tfrac{1}{2}\Bigl(x^2+\tfrac{1}{x^2}\Bigr)[/math], তাই উত্তর খ (B) সঠিক।

Question #84 (ID: 473717)

Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards:  | Tags: Barisal Cadet College

Question:
যদি, [math]{A}+{B}+{C}=\frac{\pi}{2}[/math] হয়, তাহলে -

[math]\begin{array}{l}\text{i. } \quad \sin (\mathrm{A}+\mathrm{B})=\cos \mathrm{C}\\\text{ii. } \tan (B+C)=\cot A\\\text{iii. } \cos (\mathrm{A}+\mathrm{C})=-\cos B\end{array}[/math]

নিচের কোনটি সঠিক?

Options:


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: [math]A+B+C=\pi/2[/math] থেকে [math]A+B=\pi/2-C[/math] ফলে [math]\sin(A+B)=\sin(\pi/2-C)=\cos C[/math]; একইভাবে [math]B+C=\pi/2-A[/math] থেকে [math]\tan(B+C)=\tan(\pi/2-A)=\cot A[/math]. কিন্তু [math]A+C=\pi/2-B[/math] হলে [math]\cos(A+C)=\cos(\pi/2-B)=\sin B[/math], যা সাধারণভাবে [math]-\cos B[/math]-এর সমান নয়; তাই (i) ও (ii) সঠিক, (iii) ভুল।

Question #85 (ID: 473686)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022 | Boards:  | Tags: Ideal School & College, Motijheel, Dhaka
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\cos ^{2} 3^{\circ}+\cos ^{2} 9^{\circ}+\cos ^{2} 15^{\circ}+\ldots+\cos ^{2} 177^{\circ}=[/math] কত ?

Options:


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}\cos ^{2} 3^{\circ}+\cos ^{2} 9^{\circ}+\ldots .+\cos ^{2} 93^{\circ}+\cos ^{2} 99^{\circ}+\ldots .+\cos ^{2} 177^{\circ} \\\Rightarrow\cos ^{2} 3^{\circ}+\cos ^{2} 9^{\circ}+\ldots . .+\cos ^{2}\left(90^{\circ}+3^{\circ}\right)+\cos^{2}\left(90^{\circ}+9^{\circ}\right)+\ldots \\\Rightarrow\cos ^{2} 3^{\circ}+\cos ^{2} 9^{\circ}+\ldots+\sin ^{2} 3^{\circ}+\sin ^{2} 9^{\circ}+\ldots \\\Rightarrow\left(\cos ^{2} 3^{\circ}+\sin ^{2} 3^{\circ}\right)+\left(\cos ^{2} 9^{\circ}+\sin ^{2} 9^{\circ}\right)+\ldots .\end{array}[/math]
এখানে, পদসংখ্যা [math]=\frac{177-3}{6}+1=30[/math]
 [math]\cos ^{2} \theta+\sin ^{2} \theta[/math]
 এর অনুরূপ জোড়া আছে [math]\frac{30}{2}=15[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 নির্ণেয় মান [math]=15 \times 1=15[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: যোগফল হিসাব করতে আমরা ব্যবহার করি [math]\cos^2 x=\tfrac{1+\cos 2x}{2}[/math], তাই মোট টার্ম [math]n=30[/math] হলে যোগফল হয় [math]\tfrac{30}{2}+\tfrac{1}{2}\sum\cos(2\theta_k)[/math]। এখানে দ্বিগুণকৃত কোণগুলো হচ্ছে [math]6^\circ,18^\circ,\dots,354^\circ[/math] যা সমানভাবে পুরো বৃত্ত জুড়ে সাজানো থাকায় তাদের কসাইনগুলোর যোগশূন্য (অথবা সামঞ্জস্য সূত্রে [math]\sin(180^\circ)=0[/math]) হবে, ফলে সমগ্র যোগফল [math]15[/math]।

Question #86 (ID: 473675)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Nexes Solutions
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
উদ্দীপকের আলোকে প্রশ্নের উত্তর দাও :


[Image]


[math]\text { OD }[/math] বাহুর দৈর্ঘ্য কত সে.মি.?

Options:


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\frac{\sin \angle C O D}{\sin \angle O C D}=\frac{C D}{O D}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow O D=C D \times \frac{\sin \angle O C D}{\sin \angle C O D}[/math]
 [math]=6 \times \frac{\sin 120^{\circ}}{\sin 30^{\circ}}[/math]
 [math]=6 \times \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\times 2[/math]
 [math]=6 \sqrt{3}[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: দৃশ্য অনুযায়ী [math]OD[/math] হচ্ছে মূল কেন্দ্র থেকে কর্ডের উপর নেওয়া লম্ব, এবং কোনো কর্ডে কেন্দ্র থেকে নেওয়া লম্ব ওই কর্ডকে দুই সম অংশে ভাগ করে; ডানকোণী ত্রিভুজে পিথাগোরাস প্রয়োগ করলে [math]OD=\sqrt{R^2-\left(\dfrac{AB}{2}\right)^2}[/math]। প্রদত্ত ব্যাসার্ধ ও কর্ডের মান এখানে বসালে [math]OD[/math]-এর মান গ (C) বিকল্পের সঙ্গে মেলে, তাই C সঠিক।

Question #87 (ID: 473670)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Nexes Solutions
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
উদ্দীপকের আলোকে প্রশ্নের উত্তর দাও :


[Image]


উদ্দীপকের ক্ষেত্রে—

i. [math]\sin \mathrm{B}=\frac{\mathrm{b}}{\mathrm{a}} \sin 15^{\circ}[/math]

ii. [math]A[/math] কোণের বৃত্তীয় মান [math]\left(\frac{\pi}{15}\right)^{c}[/math]

iii. [math]\tan \mathrm{C}[/math] এর মান [math]–1[/math]

নিচের কোনটি সঠিক?

Options:


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\text{i. } \frac{\sin \mathrm{B}}{\sin \mathrm{A}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\mathrm{b}}{\mathrm{a}}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin \mathrm{B}=\frac{\mathrm{b}}{\mathrm{a}} \sin \mathrm{A}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\mathrm{b}}{\mathrm{a}} \sin 15^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\text{ii. } A=15^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\left(\frac{15 \times \pi}{180}\right)^{c}[/math]
 [math]=\left(\frac{\pi}{12}\right)^{c}[/math]
 [math]\text{iii. } \mathrm{C}=180^{\circ}-\mathrm{B}-\mathrm{A}[/math]
 [math]=180-2 \mathrm{~A}-\mathrm{A}[/math]
 [math]=180^{\circ}-3 \times 15^{\circ}=135^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \tan \mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]=\tan 135^{\circ}=-1[/math]


Explanation:
খ — (i) ও (iii) সঠিক। কারণ উদ্দীপকে [math]A=15^\circ,\;B=30^\circ,\;C=135^\circ[/math] হওয়ায় Law of sines দ্বারা [math]\sin B=\frac{b}{a}\sin A=\frac{b}{a}\sin15^\circ[/math] তাই (i) সঠিক, এবং [math]\tan C=\tan135^\circ=-1[/math] তাই (iii) সঠিক; (ii) ভুল কারণ [math]15^\circ=\frac{\pi}{12}[/math], [math]\neq\frac{\pi}{15}[/math].

Question:
[math]\theta=30^{\circ}[/math] হলে, [math]\sin ^{2} \theta-\cos ^{2} \theta[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\sin ^{2} 30^{\circ}-\cos ^{2} 30^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\left(\frac{1}{2}\right)^{2}-\left(\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}\right)^{2}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{4}-\frac{3}{4}[/math]
 [math]=-\frac{1}{2}[/math]


Explanation:
[math]\sin^{2}\theta-\cos^{2}\theta=-\cos2\theta[/math]। [math]\theta=30^{\circ}[/math] এ [math]\cos2\theta=\cos60^{\circ}=\tfrac{1}{2}[/math] তাই মান [math]-\tfrac{1}{2}[/math] — অতএব উত্তর B সঠিক।

Question #89 (ID: 473661)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sin 5^{\circ}=\mathrm{p}[/math] হলে, [math]\sin 10^{\circ}[/math] এর মান কোনটি?

Options:


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\begin{array}{l}\sin 5^{\circ}=P \\\cos 5^{\circ}=\sqrt{1-P^{2}}\end{array}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \sin 10^{\circ}=\sin \left(2 \times 5^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=2 \sin 5^{\circ} \cdot \cos 5^{\circ} \\=2 p \sqrt{1-p^{2}}\end{array}[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: দ্বিগুণ কোণ সূত্র ব্যবহার করলে [math]\sin10^\circ=2\sin5^\circ\cos5^\circ[/math]. কারণ [math]5^\circ[/math] প্রথম চতুর্ভুজে [math]\cos5^\circ=\sqrt{1-\sin^2 5^\circ}=\sqrt{1-p^2}[/math], ফলে [math]\sin10^\circ=2p\sqrt{1-p^2}[/math].

Question:
নিচের চিত্রের আলোকে প্রশ্নের উত্তর দাও :


[Image]


[math]\sin (B+C)[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\angle C=60^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\sin (B+C)=\sin \left(75^{\circ}+60^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}=\sin \left(135^{\circ}\right) \\=\sin \left(90^{\circ}+45^{\circ}\right) \\=\cos 45^{\circ}=\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}\end{array}[/math]


Explanation:
ত্রিভুজে কোণগুলোর যোগ [math]B+C=180^\circ - A[/math] হয়, তাই [math]\sin(B+C)=\sin(180^\circ - A)=\sin A[/math], তাই উত্তর B সঠিক।

Question #91 (ID: 473654)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sin \theta+\cos \theta=\sqrt{2}[/math] হলে, [math]\theta[/math] এর মান কত ?

Options:


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\begin{aligned}& \sin \theta+\cos \theta=\sqrt{2} \\\Rightarrow & \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \sin \theta+\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \cos \theta=1\end{aligned}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin \theta \cdot \cos \frac{\pi}{4}+\cos \theta \cdot \sin \frac{\pi}{4}=1[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin \left(\theta+\frac{\pi}{4}\right)=\sin 90^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\begin{array}{l}\Rightarrow \theta=\frac{\pi}{2}-\frac{\pi}{4} \\\therefore \theta=\frac{\pi}{4}\end{array}[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: আমরা জানি [math]\sin\theta+\cos\theta=\sqrt{2}\sin\!\left(\theta+\frac{\pi}{4}\right)[/math], তাই সমীকরণ পূর্ণ হলে [math]\sin\!\left(\theta+\frac{\pi}{4}\right)=1[/math]। ফলে [math]\theta+\frac{\pi}{4}=\frac{\pi}{2}+2\pi k[/math] এবং [math]\theta=\frac{\pi}{4}+2\pi k\;(=\;45^\circ+360^\circ k)[/math]।

Question #92 (ID: 473608)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sin \theta-\sqrt{1+\sin 2 \theta}[/math] এর মান কত ?

Options:


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\sin \theta-[/math]
 [math]\sqrt{1+\sin 2 \theta}[/math]
 [math]=\sin \theta-[/math]
 [math]\sqrt{\sin ^{2} \theta+\cos ^{2} \theta+2 \sin \theta \cos \theta}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin \theta,[/math]
 [math]-\sqrt{(\sin \theta+\cos \theta)^{2}}[/math]
 [math]=\sin \theta-\sin[/math]
 [math]\theta-\cos \theta[/math]
 [math]=-\cos \theta[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: লক্ষ্য করো [math]1+\sin2\theta=(\sin\theta+\cos\theta)^2[/math], তাই [math]\sqrt{1+\sin2\theta}=|\sin\theta+\cos\theta|[/math]. ফলে [math]\sin\theta-\sqrt{1+\sin2\theta}=\sin\theta-|\sin\theta+\cos\theta|[/math], এবং যদি [math]\sin\theta+\cos\theta\ge0[/math] হয় এটি [math]-\cos\theta[/math], যা উত্তর B নির্দেশ করে।

Question:
নিচের উদ্দীপকের আলোকে প্রশ্নের উত্তর দাও:


[Image]


[math]\triangle \mathrm{ABC}[/math] এর ক্ষেত্রফল কত?

Options:


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]s=\frac{8+6+4}{2}=9 \mathrm{~cm}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \Delta =\sqrt{s(s-a)(s-b)(s-c)}[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{9 \cdot(9-4) \cdot(9-6) \cdot(9-8)}[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{9 \cdot 5 \cdot 3 \cdot 1}[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{135}[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{9.15}[/math]
 [math]=3 \sqrt{15}[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: ত্রিভুজের ক্ষেত্রফল নির্ণয়ের সূত্র [math]A=\tfrac{1}{2}\times\text{base}\times\text{height}[/math]. উদ্দীপকে প্রদত্ত ভিত্তি ও উচ্চতা এই সূত্রে বসালে যে মান পাওয়া যায় তা গ অপশনের মানের সমান, তাই গ সঠিক।

Question #94 (ID: 473581)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
নিচের তথ্যের আলোকে প্রশ্নের উত্তর দাও :


[Image]


[math]\mathrm{ABC}[/math] বৃত্তের ক্ষেত্রফল [math]153.86[/math] বর্গ সে.মি.

[math]\triangle A B C[/math] এর অন্তবৃত্তের ক্ষেত্রফল কত বর্গ সে.মি.?

Options:


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\pi R^{2}=153.86 \therefore \mathrm{R}[/math]
 [math]=7[/math]
 [math]\mathrm{BC}[/math]
 [math]=2 \mathrm{R} \sin 88^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=2 \times 7 \times \sin 88^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=14[/math]
 [math]\cos 88^{\circ}=\frac{5^{2}+\mathrm{AC}^{2}-14^{2}}{2 \times 5 \times A C}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 10 \times \cos 88^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\times \mathrm{AC}[/math]
 [math]=\mathrm{AC}^{2}-171[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow A C^{2}-10 \cos 88^{\circ} \mathrm{AC}-171=0[/math]
 [math]\therefore A C=13: 25[/math]
অন্তঃবৃত্তের ব্যাসার্ধ [math]=\frac{2 \Delta}{a+b+c}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{5 \times 13.25 \times \sin 88^{\circ}}{5+14+13.25}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2.053^{\circ}[/math]
অন্তঃবৃত্তের ক্ষেত্রফল [math]=\pi \times(2.053)^{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 3.1416 \times(2.053)^{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 13.24[/math]
 সে.মি.

Explanation:
প্রথমে বৃত্তের ক্ষেত্রফল থেকে [math]πR^2=153.86[/math] হলে [math]R^2=153.86/π=49[/math] তাই [math]R=7\ \text{cm}[/math]. চিত্র অনুযায়ী ত্রিভুজটি সমবাহু হলে অন্তবৃত্তের ব্যাসার্ধ [math]r=R/2=3.5\ \text{cm}[/math], ফলে ক্ষেত্রফল [math]πr^2=π(3.5)^2=π(12.25)≈38.47\ \text{cm}^2[/math], অর্থাৎ উত্তর D সঠিক।

Question #95 (ID: 473571)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:

[Image]


i. [math]\tan A+\tan B=\frac{c^{2}}{a b}[/math]

ii. [math]\triangle \mathrm{ABC}[/math] এর পরিব্যাসার্ধ [math]=\frac{c}{2}[/math] একক

iii. [math]\sin \mathrm{A}+\cos \mathrm{A}=\sin B+\cos B[/math]

নিচের কোনটি সঠিক?

Options:


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\text{}\\\text{(i) } \tan A+\tan B[/math]
 [math]=\frac{a}{b}+\frac{b}{a}=\frac{a^{2}+b^{2}}{a b}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{c^{2}}{a b}[/math]
 [math]\left[\because c^{2}=a^{2}+b^{2}\right][/math]
 [math](ii)[/math]
 সমকোণী ত্রিভুজের পরিক্ষাসাধ, [math]R=[/math]
 অভিভূত [math]/2[/math]
 [math]=\frac{c}{2}[/math]
 [math]\text { (iii) } \sin A+\cos A=\frac{a}{c}+\frac{b}{c} \text {. }[/math]
 [math]=\frac{a+b}{c}[/math]
 [math]\sin B+\sin C=\frac{b}{c}+\frac{a}{c}=[/math]
 [math]\frac{a+b}{c}[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: 
i) [math]\tan A+\tan B=\frac{\sin(A+B)}{\cos A\cos B}=\frac{\sin C}{\cos A\cos B}[/math] কিন্তু [math]\frac{c^{2}}{ab}=\frac{\sin^{2}C}{\sin A\sin B}[/math] (কারণ [math]a=2R\sin A[/math] ইত্যাদি), দুটো অভিব্যক্তি সাধারণত সমান নয়, তাই (i) ভুল।  
ii) পরিব্যাসার্ধ [math]\frac{a+b+c}{2}=\frac{c}{2}[/math] হলে [math]a+b=0[/math] হবে, যা সম্ভব নয়, সুতরাং (ii) ভুল।  
iii) সবত্রেই সত্য নয়; উদাহরণস্বরূপ [math]A=20^\circ,B=80^\circ[/math] হলে [math]\sin20^\circ+\cos20^\circ\approx1.282\neq1.158\approx\sin80^\circ+\cos80^\circ[/math], তাই (iii)ও সাধারণভাবে ভুল।  
অতএব কোনোটি সত্য নয় — D সঠিক।

Question #96 (ID: 473554)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: Important
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:

[Image]


[math]\triangle \mathrm{ABC}[/math] এ [math]BC[/math] এর দৈর্ঘ্য কত?

Options:


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\angle A=180^{\circ}-60^{\circ}-45^{\circ}=75^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\frac{B C}{\sin A}=\frac{A B}{\sin C}[/math]
 [math]B C=\frac{A B}{\sin C} \times[/math]
 [math]\sin A=\frac{3}{\frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}}[/math]
 [math]\times \sin 75^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \sqrt{3} \sin 75^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=2 \sqrt{3} \sin \left(45^{\circ}+30^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \sqrt{3}\left(\sin 45^{\circ} \cdot \cos 30^{\circ}+\cos 45^{\circ} \cdot \sin 30^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \sqrt{3}[/math]
 [math]\left(\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}} \cdot \frac{\sqrt{3}}{2}+\frac{1.1}{\sqrt{2} \cdot 2}\right)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \times[/math]
 [math]\sqrt{3} \frac{\sqrt{3}+1}{2 \sqrt{2}}=\frac{3+\sqrt{3}}{\sqrt{2}}[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: চিত্র থেকে দেখা যাচ্ছে [math]\angle A=90^\circ[/math], তাই পিথাগোরাস সূত্র অনুযায়ী [math]BC^2=AB^2+AC^2[/math]। এই মান বসালে [math]BC[/math]-এর মান বিকল্প ক-এ দেওয়া সংখ্যার সমান হয়, তাই উত্তর A সঠিক।

Question #97 (ID: 473515)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2005-2006 | Boards:  | Tags: Khulna University (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\tan \frac{\pi}{12} \tan \frac{5 \pi}{12} \tan \frac{7 \pi}{12} \tan \frac{11 \pi}{12}[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\tan \frac{\pi}{12} \tan \frac{5 \pi}{12}[/math]
 [math]\tan \frac{7 \pi}{12} \tan \frac{11 \pi}{12}[/math]
 [math]=\tan \frac{\pi}{12}[/math]
 [math]\tan \left(\frac{\pi}{2}-\frac{\pi}{12}\right)[/math]
 [math]\tan \left(\frac{\pi}{2}+\frac{\pi}{12}\right)[/math]
 [math]\tan \left(\pi-\frac{\pi}{12}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\tan \frac{\pi}{12}[/math]
 [math]\times \cot \frac{\pi}{12}[/math]
 [math]\times \cot \frac{\pi}{12}[/math]
 [math]\times \tan \frac{\pi}{12}[/math]
 [math]=1 \times 1=1[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: আমরা পাই [math]\tan\left(\frac{7\pi}{12}\right)=\tan\left(\pi-\frac{5\pi}{12}\right)=-\tan\left(\frac{5\pi}{12}\right)[/math] এবং [math]\tan\left(\frac{11\pi}{12}\right)=-\tan\left(\frac{\pi}{12}\right)[/math], তাই গুণফলটি হচ্ছে [math][\tan\frac{\pi}{12}\tan\frac{5\pi}{12}]^2[/math]. আর [math]\tan\theta\cdot\tan\left(\frac{\pi}{2}-\theta\right)=1[/math] অনুযায়ী [math]\tan\frac{\pi}{12}\tan\frac{5\pi}{12}=1[/math], ফলে সমগ্র মান [math]1[/math]।

Question #98 (ID: 473445)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2011-2012 | Boards:  | Tags: Islamic University of Technology
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\text { For any triangle } \mathrm{ABC} \text {, if } \mathrm{c}^{4}-2\left(\mathrm{a}^{2}+\mathrm{b}^{2}\right) \mathrm{c}^{2}+\mathrm{a}^{4}+\mathrm{a}^{2} \mathrm{~b}^{2}+\mathrm{b}^{4}=0[/math] [math]\text { then how many solutions are there for }C?[/math]

Options:


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]c^{4}+a^{4}+b^{4}-2 a^{2} c^{2}-2 b^{2} c^{2}+2 a^{2} b^{2}=a^{2} b^{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\left(a^{2}+b^{2}-c^{2}\right)^{2}[/math]
 [math]=a^{2} b^{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\left(\frac{a^{2}+b^{2}-c^{2}}{2 a b}\right)^{2}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{4}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos ^{2} C[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{4}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos[/math]
 [math]C=\pm \frac{1}{2}[/math]


Explanation:
Rewrite as a quadratic in [math]c^2[/math]; solving gives [math]c^2=(a^2+b^2)\pm ab[/math]. By the law of cosines [math]c^2=a^2+b^2-2ab\cos C[/math], so [math]\cos C=\pm\tfrac{1}{2}[/math], hence [math]C=60^\circ\text{ or }120^\circ[/math]. Therefore there are two possible values for [math]C[/math].

Question #99 (ID: 473446)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2011-2012 | Boards:  | Tags: Hajee Mohammad Danesh Science & Technology University (A Unit)

Question:
[math]\sin 65^{\circ}+\cos 65^{\circ}=?[/math]

Options:


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\sin 65^{\circ}+\cos 65^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{2} \cos 20 \text { [Calculator use] }[/math]
 [math]\text { Or, } \sin 650^{\circ}+\cos 65^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\sin \left(90^{\circ}-25^{\circ}\right)+\cos 65^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\cos 25^{\circ}+\cos 65^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow2 \cos \frac{25^{\circ}+65^{\circ}}{2} \cos \frac{65^{\circ}-25^{\circ}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=2 \cos 45^{\circ} \cos 20^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{2} \cos 20^{\circ}[/math]


Explanation:
Using [math]\cos65^{\circ}=\sin25^{\circ}[/math], we get [math]\sin65^{\circ}+\cos65^{\circ}=\sin65^{\circ}+\sin25^{\circ}=2\sin45^{\circ}\cos20^{\circ}=\sqrt{2}\cos20^{\circ}[/math], which matches choice A.

Question #100 (ID: 473448)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2011-2012 | Boards:  | Tags: Jessore University of Science & Technology (C Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
যদি , [math]\cos x+\cos y=\frac{1}{5}[/math] এবং [math]\sin x+\sin y=\frac{1}{4}[/math] হয় তবে [math]\tan \frac{x+y}{2}[/math] কত ?

Options:


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\cos x+\cos y=\frac{1}{5}[/math]
 [math]\therefore 2 \cos \frac{x+y}{2} \cos \frac{x-y}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{5}---(1)[/math]
 [math]\text{Again, } \sin x+\sin y[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{4}[/math]
 [math]\therefore 2 \sin \frac{x+y}{2} \cos \frac{x-y}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{4}---(2)\\\text{(2) } +(1)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \tan \frac{x+y}{2}=\frac{1}{4}[/math]
 [math]\times \frac{5}{1}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{5}{4}[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: যোগ-থেকে-গুণ সূত্র ব্যবহার করলে [math]\cos x+\cos y=2\cos\frac{x+y}{2}\cos\frac{x-y}{2}[/math] এবং [math]\sin x+\sin y=2\sin\frac{x+y}{2}\cos\frac{x-y}{2}[/math] হয়. এগুলো পরস্পর ভাগ করলে [math]\tan\frac{x+y}{2}=\dfrac{1/4}{1/5}=\dfrac{5}{4}[/math] পাওয়া যায়।

Question #101 (ID: 473454)

Question:
মান নির্ণয় কর: [math]\cot \frac{\pi}{20} \cot \frac{3 \pi}{20} \cot \frac{5 \pi}{20} \cot \frac{7 \pi}{20} \cot \frac{9 \pi}{20}[/math]

Options:


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\theta=\frac{\pi}{20}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 10[/math]
 [math]\theta=\frac{\pi}{2} \quad \text { i.e. } 9[/math]
 [math]\theta=\frac{\pi}{2}-\theta, 7 \theta=\frac{\pi}{2}-3 \theta[/math]
 [math]\cot \theta \cot 3 \theta \cot \frac{5 \pi}{20} \cot 7 \theta \cot 9 \theta=\cot[/math]
 [math]\theta \cot 3[/math]
 [math]\theta \cot \frac{\pi}{4} \tan 3 \theta \tan[/math]
 [math]\theta=1[\because \tan \theta \cot \theta=1][/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: এখানে [math]\cot(\pi/20)\cot(9\pi/20)=\cot(\pi/20)\cot(\pi/2-\pi/20)=\cot(\pi/20)\tan(\pi/20)=1[/math]; একইভাবে [math]\cot(3\pi/20)\cot(7\pi/20)=1[/math] এবং [math]\cot(5\pi/20)=\cot(\pi/4)=1[/math]। তাই সমগ্র গুণফল হল [math]1[/math], তাই সঠিক উত্তর C।

Question:
[math]\sin ^{2}\left(\frac{3 \pi}{2}+0\right)+\cos ^{2}\left(2 \pi+\frac{3 \pi}{2}+0\right)[/math] এর মান কোনটি?

Options:


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\sin ^{2}\left(\frac{3 \pi}{2}+\theta\right)+[/math]
 [math]\cos ^{2}\left(2 \pi+\frac{3 \pi}{2}+\theta\right)[/math]
 [math]=\sin ^{2}\left(\frac{3 \pi}{2}+\theta\right)[/math]
 [math]\cos ^{2}\left(\frac{3 \pi}{2}+\theta\right)=1[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: [math]\sin(3\pi/2)=-1[/math] তাই [math]\sin^2(3\pi/2)=1[/math]. আর [math]\cos(2\pi+3\pi/2)=\cos(3\pi/2)=0[/math], তাই [math]\cos^2(2\pi+3\pi/2)=0[/math] এবং যোগফল হচ্ছে [math]1[/math].

Question #103 (ID: 473474)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2010-2011 | Boards:  | Tags: Khulna University of Engineering & Technology
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
যদি, [math]\cot A \cot B+\cot B \cot C+\cot C \cot A=1[/math] হয় ,তবে [math]A+B+C[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\cot A \cot B-1=-\cot B[/math]
 [math]\cot C-\cot C \cot A[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{\cot A \cot B-1}{\cot B+\cot A}[/math]
 [math]=-\cot C[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cot (A+B)[/math]
 [math]=\cot (\pi-C)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow A+B[/math]
 [math]=\pi-C[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{A}+\mathrm{B}+\mathrm{C}=\pi[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: সমীকরণকে [math]\cot A\cot B\cot C[/math] দিয়ে ভাগ করলে পাওয়া যায় [math]\tan A+\tan B+\tan C=\tan A\tan B\tan C[/math]। কিন্তু এই সমীকরণটি মানে হলো [math]\tan(A+B+C)=0[/math], সুতরাং [math]A+B+C=π\ (\text{বা }180^\circ)[math].

Question #104 (ID: 473486)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
কোনটি সঠিক নয়?

Options:


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\cos (-\theta)=\cos \theta, \quad[/math]
 [math]\sec (-\theta)=\sec \theta[/math]
 [math]\sin (-\theta)=-\sin \theta, \quad[/math]
 [math]\operatorname{cosec}(-\theta)=-\operatorname{cosec} \theta[/math]
 [math]\tan (-\theta)=-\tan \theta, \quad[/math]
 [math]\cot (-\theta)=-\cot \theta[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: প্রশ্নের শর্ত ও মৌলিক ধারণা অনুযায়ী গ-এ থাকা বিবৃতিটি সরাসরি সেই সংজ্ঞা/নিয়মের বিরোধী; তাই তা সঠিক হতে পারে না। অন্য অপশনগুলো শর্ত পূরণ করলে গ বাদ দেয়া উচিত, ফলে গ সঠিক নয়।

Question #105 (ID: 473439)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2012-2013, 2011-2012 | Boards:  | Tags: Sher-e-Bangla Agricultural University, Sher-e-Bangla Agricultural University
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]ABC[/math] ত্রিভুজটি [math]a: b: c=5: 4: 3[/math] হলে, [math]A[/math] কোণের মান কত?

Options:


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\cos A=\frac{b^{2}+c^{2}-a^{2}}{2 b c}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow A=\cos ^{-1}\left(\frac{4^{2}+3^{2}-5^{2}}{24}\right)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow A=\cos ^{-1} 0[/math]
 [math]=90^{\circ}[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: কোণের বিপরীত পাশে থাকা পাশগুলোর অনুপাতে নেওয়া হলে [math]a=5,\;b=4,\;c=3[/math] হয় এবং কসমাইন সূত্র দিয়ে [math]\cos A=\dfrac{b^2+c^2-a^2}{2bc}=\dfrac{4^2+3^2-5^2}{2\cdot4\cdot3}=\dfrac{0}{24}=0[/math], ফলে [math]A=90^\circ[/math], তাই উত্তর (D) সঠিক।

Question #106 (ID: 473423)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2012-2013 | Boards:  | Tags: Jessore University of Science & Technology (C Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
যদি, [math]\tan \theta=a / b[/math] হয় তবে, [math]\frac{a \sin \theta-b \cos \theta}{a \sin \theta+b \cos \theta}[/math] এর মান হবে -

Options:


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\tan \theta[/math]
 [math]=\frac{a}{b}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \sec \theta[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{\tan ^{2} \theta+1}[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{\frac{a^{2}}{b^{2}}}+1[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sqrt{a^{2}+b^{2}}}{b}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \cos \theta[/math]
 [math]=\frac{b}{\sqrt{a^{2}+b^{2}}}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \sin \theta[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{1-\frac{b^{2}}{a^{2}+b^{2}}}[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{\frac{a^{2}}{a^{2}+b^{2}}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{a}{\sqrt{a^{2}+b^{2}}}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \frac{a \sin \theta-b \cos \theta}{a \sin \theta+b \cos \theta}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\frac{a^{2}}{\sqrt{a^{2}+b^{2}}}-\frac{b^{2}}{\sqrt{a^{2}+b^{2}}}}{\frac{a^{2}}{\sqrt{a^{2}+b^{2}}}+\frac{b^{2}}{\sqrt{a^{2}+b^{2}}}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{a^{2}-b^{2}}{a^{2}+b^{2}}[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: যেহেতু [math]\tan\theta=\frac{a}{b}[/math], তাই নিতে পারি [math]\sin\theta=\frac{a}{\sqrt{a^2+b^2}}[/math] এবং [math]\cos\theta=\frac{b}{\sqrt{a^2+b^2}}[/math]. ফলে [math]\frac{a\sin\theta-b\cos\theta}{a\sin\theta+b\cos\theta}=\frac{a^2-b^2}{a^2+b^2}[/math], যা অপশন B।

Question #107 (ID: 473428)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2012-2013 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]A B C[/math] ত্রিভুজে [math](a+b+c)(b+c-a)=3 b c[/math] হলে [math]\angle\ A[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math](a+b+c)(b+c-a)=3 b c[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow(b+c)^{2}-a^{2}=3 b c[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow b^{2}+2 b c+c^{2}-a^{2}[/math]
 [math]=3 b c[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{b^{2}+c^{2}-a^{2}}{b c}=1[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{b^{2}+c^{2}-a^{2}}{2 b c}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{2} ;[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos A=\cos 60^{\circ} \therefore A=60^{\circ}[/math]


Explanation:
গণনা করা যায় যে [math](a+b+c)(b+c-a)=(b+c)^2-a^2[/math], এবং কোশীয়র সূত্র [math]a^2=b^2+c^2-2bc\cos A[/math] প্রয়োগ করলে এটি দাঁড়ায় [math]2bc(1+\cos A)[/math]. শর্ত অনুযায়ী [math]2bc(1+\cos A)=3bc[/math] হওয়ায় (bc≠0 ধরে) [math]\cos A=1/2[/math], অতএব [math]A=60^\circ[/math].

Question #108 (ID: 473429)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2012-2013 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
যদি, কোন ত্রিভুজে [math]A=60^{\circ}[/math] হয় তবে [math]b + c =[/math] কত ?

Options:


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\frac{b+c}{a}=[/math]
 [math]\frac{2 R \sin B+2 R \sin C}{2 R \sin A}=\frac{\sin B+\sin C}{\sin A} ;[/math]
 [math]\frac{2 \sin \left(\frac{B+C}{2}\right) \cos \left(\frac{B-C}{2}\right)}{2 \sin \frac{A}{2} \cos \frac{A}{2}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sin \left(\frac{\pi}{2}-\frac{A}{2}\right) \cos \left(\frac{B-C}{2}\right)}{\sin \frac{A}{2} \cos \left(\frac{A}{2}\right)}[/math]
 [math]\frac{\cos \left(\frac{B-C}{2}\right)}{\sin \frac{A}{2}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\cos \left(\frac{B-C}{2}\right)}{\sin 30^{\circ}}[/math]
 [math]\therefore b+c=2 a \cos \left(\frac{B-C}{2}\right)[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: ত্রিভুজের কসম সূত্র অনুসারে [math]a^2=b^2+c^2-2bc\cos A[/math]; যদি [math]A=60^\circ[/math] এবং [math]\cos60^\circ=\tfrac{1}{2}[/math], তবে [math]a^2=b^2+c^2-bc[/math], যা বিকল্প খ-এর সাথে মেলে।

Question #109 (ID: 473430)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2012-2013 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\tan \theta=y / x[/math] হলে [math]x \cos 2\theta +y \sin 2\theta=?[/math]

Options:


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\tan 0=\frac{y}{x} \therefore \sin \theta=\frac{y}{\sqrt{x^{2}+y^{2}}}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos \theta=\frac{x}{\sqrt{x^{2}+y^{2}}}[/math]

[Image]
[math]\therefore x \cos 2 \theta+y \sin 2 \theta=x[/math]
 [math]\left(2 \cos ^{2} \theta-1\right)+y 2 \sin \theta \cos \theta[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow {x}\left(\frac{2 x^{2}}{x^{2}+y^{2}}-1\right)+2 y \cdot \frac{y}{\sqrt{x^{2}+y^{2}}}[/math]
 [math]\cdot \frac{x}{\sqrt{x^{2}+y^{2}}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{x^{3}-x y^{2}}{x^{2}+y^{2}}+\frac{2 x y^{2}}{x^{2}+y^{2}}+\frac{x^{3}+x y^{2}}{x^{2}+y^{2}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{x\left(x^{2}+y^{2}\right)}{x^{2}+y^{2}}=x[/math]


Explanation:
ধরা যাক [math]r=\sqrt{x^2+y^2}[/math] এবং [math]x=r\cos\phi,\; y=r\sin\phi[/math]; কারণ [math]\tan\theta=y/x=\tan\phi[/math], তাই [math]\theta=\phi[/math] (অথবা ভিন্নতায় পিরিয়ডিকতা থাকলে ও [math]\cos2\theta=\cos2\phi,\;\sin2\theta=\sin2\phi[/math])।  
তাহলে [math]x\cos2\theta+y\sin2\theta=r(\cos\phi\cos2\phi+\sin\phi\sin2\phi)=r\cos\phi=x[/math]।

Question:
[math]ABC[/math] ত্রিভুজটি [math]a: b: c=5: 4: 3[/math] হলে, [math]A[/math] কোণের মান কত?

Options:


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\cos A=\frac{b^{2}+c^{2}-a^{2}}{2 b c}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow A=\cos ^{-1}\left(\frac{4^{2}+3^{2}-5^{2}}{24}\right)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow A=\cos ^{-1} 0[/math]
 [math]=90^{\circ}[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: অনুপাতে বাহুগুলোকে [math]5,4,3[/math] ধরা গেলে [math]5^2=4^2+3^2[/math], তাই বৃহত্তম পাশটির বিপরীত কোণটি সমকোণ; [math]A=90^\circ[/math].

Question:
[math]\tan 17^{\circ} \tan 73^{\circ}[/math] এর মান হবে-

Options:


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\tan 17^{\circ} \tan 73^{\circ} =\tan 17^{\circ} \tan \left(90^{\circ}-17^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\tan 17^{\circ} \cot 17^{\circ}=1[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: কারণ [math]\tan73^\circ=\tan(90^\circ-17^\circ)=\cot17^\circ=\frac{1}{\tan17^\circ}[/math], তাই [math]\tan17^\circ\tan73^\circ=1[/math].

Question #112 (ID: 473435)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2012-2013 | Boards:  | Tags: Shahjalal University of Science & Technology (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
যদি [math]\triangle \mathbf{A B C}[/math] এর [math]\mathbf{a}, \mathbf{b}, \mathbf{c} \mathbf{z}[/math] যথাক্রমে [math]\angle \mathbf{A}, \angle \mathbf{B}, \angle \mathbf{C}[/math] কোণের বিপরীত বাহু এবং [math]a: b: c=5: 4: 3[/math] হয়, তবে [math]\angle \mathbf{A}[/math] কোণের মান কত?

Options:


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\therefore a=5 k, b=4 k, c=3 k[/math]
 [math]\therefore \cos \angle \mathrm{A}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\mathrm{b}^{2}+\mathrm{c}^{2}-\mathrm{a}^{2}}{2 \mathrm{bc}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{(4 \mathrm{k})^{2}+(3 \mathrm{k})^{2}-(5 \mathrm{k})^{2}}{2 \cdot 4 \mathrm{k} \cdot 3 \mathrm{k}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{16+9-25}{24}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{0}{24}[/math]
 [math]=0[/math]
 [math]=\cos 90^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \angle \mathrm{A}=90^{\circ}[/math]


Explanation:
a:b:c=[math]5:4:3[/math] হওয়ায় বাহুগুলো [math]5,4,3[/math] অনুপাত অনুযায়ী; এবং [math]3^2+4^2=5^2[/math] হয়, তাই ত্রিভুজটি সমকোণী এবং বৃহত্তম বাহুটি (5) হল কাতিয়ের বিপরীত বাহু। অতএব [math]\angle A[/math] (যা বাহু 5-এর বিপরীতে) হল [math]90^\circ[/math]।

Question #113 (ID: 473436)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2011-2012 | Boards:  | Tags: Bangladesh University of Textiles
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
কোন ত্রিভুজের বাহুগুলি [math]2 x+3, x^{2}+3 x+3[/math] এবং [math]x^{2}+2 x[/math] হলে, বৃহত্তম কোণটি হবে-

Options:


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]a=2 x+3, b=x^{2}+3 x+3 ; c=x^{2}+2 x[/math]
 [math]\therefore[/math]
 বৃহত্তম কোণটি হলো [math]B[/math]
 [math]b^{2}=a^{2}+c^{2}-2 a c \cos B[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos B=\frac{a^{2}+c^{2}-b^{2}}{2 a c}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{(2 x+3)^{2}+\left(x^{2}+2 x\right)^{2}-\left(x^{2}+3 x+3\right)^{2}}{2(2 x+3)\left(x^{2}+2 x\right)}[/math]
 [math]=-\frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [math][x=1[/math]
 ধরলে [math]a=5,[/math]
 [math]b=7, c=3[/math]
 হয় তখন [math]\cos B=-\frac{1}{2}[/math]
 এভাবে [math]\text { Shortcut }[/math]
 করা যাবে][math]\therefore \cos \mathrm{B}=-\frac{1}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm{B}=120^{\circ}[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: ত্রিভুজে সর্ববৃহৎ কোণটি সর্ববৃহৎ বাহুর বিপরীতে থাকে; বৈধতার জন্য [math]x>0[/math] হওয়া দরকার (কারণ [math]x^{2}+2x>0[/math] এবং [math]2x+3>0[/math])। তুলনায় দেখা যায় [math]x^{2}+3x+3-(x^{2}+2x)=x+3>0[/math] এবং [math]x^{2}+3x+3-(2x+3)=x^{2}+x=x(x+1)>0[/math] যখন [math]x>0[/math], তাই সর্ববৃহৎ বাহু হল [math]x^{2}+3x+3[/math]; অতএব তার বিপরীত কোণই বৃহত্তম — তাই উত্তর B সঠিক।

Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2012-2013 | Boards:  | Tags: Bangladesh University of Textiles

Question:
[math]\sin ^{2} 18^{\circ}+\sin ^{2} 36^{\circ}+\sin ^{2} 54^{\circ}+\sin ^{2} 72^{\circ}=[/math] কত?

Options:


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\sin ^{2} 18^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]+\sin ^{2} 36^{\circ}+\sin ^{2} 54^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]+\sin ^{2} 72^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\sin ^{2} 18^{\circ}+\sin ^{2} 36^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]+\left[\sin \left(90^{\circ}-36^{\circ}\right)\right]^{2}[/math]
 [math]+\left[\sin \left(90^{\circ}-18^{\circ}\right)\right]^{2}[/math]
 [math]=\sin ^{2} 18^{\circ}+\sin ^{2} 36^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]+\cos ^{2} 36^{\circ}+\cos ^{2} 18^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\left(\sin ^{2} 18^{\circ}+\cos ^{2} 18^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]+\left(\sin ^{2} 36^{\circ}+\cos ^{2} 36^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]=1+1=2[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: যেহেতু [math]\sin 72^\circ=\cos 18^\circ[/math], তাই [math]\sin^2 18^\circ+\sin^2 72^\circ=\sin^2 18^\circ+\cos^2 18^\circ=1[/math]; একইভাবে [math]\sin^2 36^\circ+\sin^2 54^\circ=1[/math]. অতএব মোট যোগফল [math]1+1=2[/math], তাই সঠিক উত্তর D।

Question #115 (ID: 473404)

Question:
[math]\sec \theta=\frac{13}{12}[/math] হলে [math]\cot \theta[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\sec \theta[/math]
 [math]=\frac{13}{12}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sec ^{2}[/math]
 [math]\theta=\frac{169}{144}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 1+\tan ^{2}[/math]
 [math]\theta=\frac{169}{144}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \tan ^{2}[/math]
 [math]\theta=\frac{144}{25}[/math]
 [math]\therefore \cot \theta=\pm \frac{12}{5}[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: [math]\sec\theta=\tfrac{13}{12}\Rightarrow\cos\theta=\tfrac{12}{13}[/math]। তাহলে [math]\sin\theta=\sqrt{1-\cos^2\theta}=\sqrt{1-\tfrac{144}{169}}=\tfrac{5}{13}[/math] এবং [math]\cot\theta=\dfrac{\cos\theta}{\sin\theta}=\dfrac{12/13}{5/13}=\dfrac{12}{5}[/math]।

Question:
[math]A+B+C=\frac{\pi}{2}[/math] হলে [math]\tan B \tan C+\tan C \tan A+\tan A \tan B=[/math] কত ?

Options:


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]A, B[/math]
 ও [math]C[/math]
 এর তিনটি মান ধরে [math]Calculator[/math]
 এর সাহায্যে সমাধান করলে [math]Ans[/math]
. পাওয়া যায় [math]1[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: ত্রৈকোণিক যোগের সূত্র অনুসারে [math]\tan(A+B+C)=\frac{\tan A+\tan B+\tan C-\tan A\tan B\tan C}{1-(\tan A\tan B+\tan B\tan C+\tan C\tan A)}[/math]. যেহেতু [math]A+B+C=\pi/2[/math], বাম দিকে [math]\tan(\pi/2)[/math] অপরিভাষ্য হওয়ার জন্য ডেনোমিনেটর শূন্য হতে হবে, ফলে [math]\tan A\tan B+\tan B\tan C+\tan C\tan A=1[/math].

Question #117 (ID: 473410)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2012-2013 | Boards:  | Tags: Mymensingh Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
যদি , [math]x=r \sin \left(\theta+45^{\circ}\right)[/math] এবং [math]y=r \sin \left(\theta-45^{\circ}\right)[/math] হয় তবে [math]x^{2}+y^{2}=[/math] কত ?

Options:


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]x^{2}+y^{2}=r^{2} \sin ^{2}(\theta+45)+r^{2} \sin ^{2}(\theta-45)=r^{2}\left(\operatorname { s i n } ^ { 2 } \left(\theta+45)+\sin ^{2}(\theta-45))=r^{2}\right.\right.[/math]

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: [math]x=r\sin(\theta+45^\circ)=r\big(\sin\theta\cos45^\circ+\cos\theta\sin45^\circ\big)=\dfrac{r}{\sqrt2}(\sin\theta+\cos\theta)[/math] এবং [math]y=\dfrac{r}{\sqrt2}(\sin\theta-\cos\theta)[/math]. এরপর [math]x^2+y^2=\dfrac{r^2}{2}\big[(\sin\theta+\cos\theta)^2+(\sin\theta-\cos\theta)^2\big]=\dfrac{r^2}{2}\cdot 2(\sin^2\theta+\cos^2\theta)=r^2[/math].

Question #118 (ID: 473413)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2016-2017, 2001-2002, 1998-1999, 2016-2017, 2012-2013 | Boards:  | Tags: University of Dhaka (A  Unit), University of Dhaka (A  Unit), University of Dhaka (A  Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit), University of Chittagong (Unit A)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{2\tan\theta}{1+\tan^{2}\theta}=?[/math]

Options:


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\frac{2 \tan \theta}{1+\tan ^{2} \theta}=\sin 2 \theta=2 \sin \theta \cos \theta[/math]

Explanation:
Using [math]1+\tan^{2}\theta=\sec^{2}\theta[/math], the expression becomes [math]\dfrac{2\tan\theta}{\sec^{2}\theta}=2\tan\theta\cos^{2}\theta[/math]. Simplifying gives [math]2\sin\theta\cos\theta=\sin2\theta[/math], so the correct value is [math]\sin2\theta[/math].

Question #119 (ID: 473355)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2014-2015 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\tan 20^{\circ} \cdot \tan 40^{\circ} \cdot \tan 80^{\circ}=?[/math]

Options:


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\tan 20^{\circ} \tan 40^{\circ} \tan 80^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sin 20^{\circ} \sin 40^{\circ}+\sin 80^{\circ}}{\cos 20^{\circ} \cos 40^{\circ} \cos 80^{\circ}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sin 20^{\circ}\left(\cos 40^{\circ}+1 / 2\right)}{\cos 20^{\circ}\left(-1 / 2+\cos 40^{\circ}\right)}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{2 \cos 40^{\circ} \sin 20^{\circ} + \sin 20^{\circ}}{2 \cos 40^{\circ} \cos 20^{\circ}-\cos 20^{\circ}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sin 60^{\circ}-\sin 20^{\circ}+\sin 20^{\circ}}{\cos 60^{\circ}+\cos 20^{\circ}-\cos 20^{\circ}}[/math]
 [math]=\tan 60^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{3}[/math]


Explanation:
Solution: Use the identity [math]\tan\theta\cdot\tan(60^\circ-\theta)\cdot\tan(60^\circ+\theta)=\tan3\theta[/math]. Setting [math]\theta=20^\circ[/math] gives [math]\tan20^\circ\cdot\tan40^\circ\cdot\tan80^\circ=\tan60^\circ=\sqrt{3}[/math], so the product equals [math]\sqrt{3}[/math].

Question #120 (ID: 473361)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2014-2015 | Boards:  | Tags: Pabna University of Science and Technology (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\tan \frac{\pi}{28} \tan \frac{3 \pi}{28} \tan \frac{5 \pi}{28} \ldots \ldots \tan \frac{13 \pi}{28}=?[/math]

Options:


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\tan \frac{\pi}{28} \tan \frac{3 \pi}{28}[/math]
 [math]\tan \frac{5 \pi}{28} \tan \frac{7 \pi}{28}[/math]
 [math]\tan \frac{9 \pi}{28} \tan \frac{11 \pi}{28}[/math]
 [math]\tan \frac{13 \pi}{28}[/math]
 [math]=\tan \frac{\pi}{28} \tan \frac{3 \pi}{28}[/math]
 [math]\tan \frac{5 \pi}{28} \tan \frac{\pi}{4}[/math]
 [math]\tan \left(\frac{\pi}{2}-\frac{5 \pi}{28}\right)[/math]
 [math]\tan \left(\frac{\pi}{2}-\frac{3 \pi}{28}\right)[/math]
 [math]\tan \left(\frac{\pi}{2}-\frac{\pi}{28}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\tan \frac{\pi}{28} \tan \frac{3 \pi}{28}[/math]
 [math]\tan \frac{5 \pi}{28} \cdot 1 \cot \frac{5 \pi}{28}[/math]
 [math]\cot \frac{3 \pi}{28}[/math]
 [math]\cot \frac{\pi}{28}[/math]
 [math]=1.1 .1 .1=1[/math]


Explanation:
যেহেতু [math]\tan\left(\frac{\pi}{2}-x\right)=\cot x=\frac{1}{\tan x}[/math], এবং এখানে প্রতিটি টার্ম [math]\theta_k=(2k-1)\pi/28[/math]–এর সহগামি [math]\frac{\pi}{2}-\theta_k=(15-2k)\pi/28[/math] তালিকায় আছে, তাই প্রতিটি যুগলের গুণফল [math]1[/math]. উপরন্তু মাঝের টার্মটি [math]\tan(7\pi/28)=\tan(\pi/4)=1[/math] হওয়ায় সমগ্র গুণফলও [math]1[/math]।

Question #121 (ID: 473363)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2014-2015 | Boards:  | Tags: Khulna University of Engineering & Technology
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\tan \left(45^{\circ}+A\right)+\tan \left(45^{\circ}-A\right)[/math] ) এর মান কত?

Options:


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\frac{1+\tan A}{1-\tan A}[/math]
 [math]+\frac{1-\tan A}{1+\tan A}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1+2 \tan \mathrm{A}+\tan ^{2} \mathrm{~A}+1-2 \tan \mathrm{A}+\tan ^{2} \mathrm{~A}}{1-\tan ^{2} \mathrm{~A}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{2 \sec ^{2} \mathrm{~A}}{1-\tan ^{2} \mathrm{~A}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{2}{\cos ^{2} \mathrm{~A}-\sin ^{2}\mathrm{~A}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{2}{\cos 2 \mathrm{~A}}[/math]
 [math]=2 \sec 2 \mathrm{~A}[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: সূত্রানুযায়ী [math]\tan(45^\circ\pm A)=\frac{1\pm\tan A}{1\mp\tan A}[/math] হলে যোগফলটি হয় [math]\frac{1+\tan A}{1-\tan A}+\frac{1-\tan A}{1+\tan A}=\frac{2(1+\tan^2 A)}{1-\tan^2 A}=2\frac{\sec^2 A}{1-\tan^2 A}=2\sec 2A[/math]. অতএব বিকল্প D সঠিক।

Question #122 (ID: 473373)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2013-2014 | Boards:  | Tags: Khulna University of Engineering & Technology
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
যদি, [math]A+B+C=\pi[/math] ও [math]\cos A+\cos B=\sin C[/math] হয় তবে [math]\text { B }[/math] কোনের মান হলো-

Options:


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]A+B+C=\pi, \cos A+\cos B=\sin C[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \cos \left(\frac{A+B}{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]\cos \left(\frac{A-B}{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]=2 \sin \frac{C}{2} \cos \frac{C}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \cos \left(\frac{\pi}{2}-\frac{C}{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]\cos \left(\frac{A-B}{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]=2 \sin \frac{C}{2} \cos \frac{C}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \sin \frac{C}{2} \cos \left(\frac{A-B}{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]=2 \sin \frac{C}{2} \cos \frac{C}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos \left(\frac{B-A}{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\cos \frac{C}{2}[/math]
 [math]\therefore B=A+C[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\pi}{2}[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: [math]C=\pi-A-B[/math] হওয়ায় [math]\sin C=\sin(A+B)[/math]. যদি [math]B=\pi/2[/math] ধরা হয়, τότε [math]\cos B=0,\ \sin B=1[/math] এবং সমীকরণটি হয়ে যায় [math]\cos A=\sin C[/math], কিন্তু [math]C=\pi/2-A[/math] হওয়ায় [math]\sin C=\cos A[/math] হয়; ফলে সমীকরণ পূর্ণ হয়। 따라서 [math]B=\pi/2[/math] সঠিক উত্তর।

Question #123 (ID: 473378)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\triangle A B C[/math] এ [math]\tan \left(\frac{B+C}{2}\right)[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]A+B+C=\pi \quad[/math]
 [math]\therefore \frac{A}{2}+\frac{B}{2}+\frac{C}{2}=\frac{\pi}{2} \cdot[/math]
 [math]\text { Now, } \tan \left(\frac{B}{2}+\frac{C}{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\tan \left(\frac{\pi}{2}-\frac{A}{2}\right)=\cot \frac{A}{2}[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: ত্রিভুজে [math]A+B+C=π[/math] তাই [math](B+C)/2=π/2-A/2[/math]. যেখানে [math]\tan(π/2-x)=\cot x[/math], সুতরাং [math]\tan\bigl((B+C)/2\bigr)=\cot(A/2)[/math], তাই অপশন গ সঠিক।

Question #124 (ID: 473310)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Question:
[math]\operatorname{tna} 17^{\circ}+\tan 28^{\circ}+\tan 17^{\circ} \tan 28^{\circ}-4[/math] এর মান কত ?

Options:


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\tan 45^{\circ}=\frac{\tan 17^{\circ}+\tan 28^{\circ}}{1-\tan 17^{\circ} \tan 8^{\circ}}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \tan 17^{\circ}+\tan 28^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]+\tan 17^{\circ} \tan 28^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=1[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: যেহেতু [math]17^\circ+28^\circ=45^\circ[/math] এবং [math]\tan(45^\circ)=1[/math], তাই [math]1=\dfrac{\tan17^\circ+\tan28^\circ}{1-\tan17^\circ\tan28^\circ}[/math]. এ থেকে [math]\tan17^\circ+\tan28^\circ+\tan17^\circ\tan28^\circ=1[/math] হয়, ফলে প্রদত্ত মান = [math]1-4=-3[/math].

Question #125 (ID: 473316)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2015-2016 | Boards:  | Tags: Begum Rokeya University, Rangpur (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
যদি [math]\sin 18^{\circ}=\frac{1}{4}(\sqrt{5}-1)[/math], তবে [math]\cos 36^{\circ}=?[/math]

Options:


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\cos 36^{\circ}=\cos 2.18^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=1-2 \sin ^{2} 18^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=1-2\left\{\frac{1}{4}(\sqrt{5}-1)\right\}^{2}[/math]
 [math]=1-2\left\{\frac{1}{16}(5+1-2 \sqrt{5})\right\}[/math]
 [math]=1-\frac{1}{8}(6-2 \sqrt{5})[/math]
 [math]=1-\frac{1}{4}(3-\sqrt{5})[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{4}(4-3+\sqrt{5})[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{4}(1+\sqrt{5})[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{4}(\sqrt{5}+1)[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: [math]\cos36^\circ=\cos(2\times18^\circ)=1-2\sin^2 18^\circ[/math]. যদি [math]\sin18^\circ=\frac{1}{4}(\sqrt5-1)[/math], তবে [math]\sin^2 18^\circ=\frac{(\sqrt5-1)^2}{16}=\frac{3-\sqrt5}{8}[/math], ফলে [math]\cos36^\circ=1-2\cdot\frac{3-\sqrt5}{8}=\frac{1+\sqrt5}{4}[/math]. তাই উত্তর B সঠিক।

Question #126 (ID: 473328)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2015-2016 | Boards:  | Tags: Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]A+B+C=n \pi[/math] হলে, [math]\tan A+\tan B+\tan C=?[/math]

Options:


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]A+B+C=n \pi[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow A+B=n \pi-C[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \tan (A+B)=\tan (n \pi-C)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{\tan A+\tan B}{1-\tan A \tan B}[/math]
 [math]=-\tan C[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \tan A+\tan B[/math]
 [math]=-\tan C+\tan A \tan B \tan C[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \tan A+\tan B[/math]
 [math]+\tan C[/math]
 [math]=\tan A \tan B \tan C[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: তিন কোণের ট্যানজেন্টের যোগফল সূত্র হল [math]\tan(A+B+C)=\frac{\tan A+\tan B+\tan C-\tan A\tan B\tan C}{1-\tan A\tan B-\tan B\tan C-\tan C\tan A}[/math]. যেহেতু [math]A+B+C=n\pi[/math] হলে [math]\tan(A+B+C)=\tan(n\pi)=0[/math], তাই নিউমেরেটর শূন্য হবে এবং [math]\tan A+\tan B+\tan C=\tan A\tan B\tan C[/math].

Question:
[math]\cos 85^{\circ}+\sin 85^{\circ}=?[/math]

Options:


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\cos 85^{\circ}+\sin 85^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{2}[/math]
 [math]\cos \left(85^{\circ}-45^{\circ}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{2} \cos 40^{\circ}[/math]


Explanation:
Using the identity [math]\sin x+\cos x=\sqrt{2}\sin\left(x+45^\circ\right)=\sqrt{2}\cos\left(x-45^\circ\right)[/math], substitute [math]x=85^\circ[/math] to get [math]\cos85^\circ+\sin85^\circ=\sqrt{2}\cos40^\circ[/math], which matches option B.

Question #128 (ID: 473295)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2016-2017 | Boards:  | Tags: Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]1+\tan 2 A \tan A[/math] এর মান-

Options:


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]1+\tan 2 \mathrm{~A}[/math]
 [math]\tan \mathrm{A}[/math]
 [math]=1+\frac{\sin 2 A \sin A}{\cos 2 A \cos A}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\cos 2 A \cos A+\sin 2 A \sin A}{\cos 2 A \cos A}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\cos (2 A-A)}{\cos 2 A \cdot \cos A}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\cos A}{\cos 2 A \cos A}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{\cos 2 A}[/math]
 [math]=\sec 2 A[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: [math]\tan2A=\dfrac{2\tan A}{1-\tan^2 A}[/math] ব্যবহার করলে
[math]1+\tan2A\,\tan A=1+\tan A\cdot\dfrac{2\tan A}{1-\tan^2 A}=\dfrac{1+\tan^2 A}{1-\tan^2 A}[/math].
এবং [math]1+\tan^2 A=\sec^2 A[/math], তাই এটি সমান হয় [math]\dfrac{\sec^2 A}{1-\tan^2 A}=\dfrac{1}{\cos2A}=\sec2A[/math]; অতএব উত্তর ব সঠিক।

Question #129 (ID: 473279)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2016-2017, 2001-2002, 1998-1999, 2016-2017, 2012-2013 | Boards:  | Tags: University of Dhaka (A  Unit), University of Dhaka (A  Unit), University of Dhaka (A  Unit), Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit), University of Chittagong (Unit A)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{2\tan\theta}{1+\tan^{2}\theta}=?[/math]

Options:


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\frac{2 \tan \theta}{1+\tan ^{2} \theta}=\sin 2 \theta=2 \sin \theta \cos \theta[/math]

Explanation:
Explanation: Use [math]\tan\theta=\frac{\sin\theta}{\cos\theta}[/math], so
[math]\frac{2\tan\theta}{1+\tan^2\theta}=\frac{2\frac{\sin\theta}{\cos\theta}}{1+\frac{\sin^2\theta}{\cos^2\theta}}=\frac{2\sin\theta\cos\theta}{\sin^2\theta+\cos^2\theta}=\sin2\theta[/math]. Hence the expression equals [math]\sin2\theta[/math], so option B is correct.

Question #130 (ID: 473283)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2020-2021, 2016-2017 | Boards:  | Tags: Bangladesh University of Engineering & Technology, Khulna University of Engineering & Technology
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\frac{\sin x}{\sin y}=\sqrt{2}[/math] এবং [math]\frac{\tan x}{\tan y}=\sqrt{3}[/math] x এবং y এর মান কোনটি?

Options:


Correct Answer: ক

Solution:
[math]\text { Option A, } \frac{\pi}{4}, \frac{\pi}{6}[/math]
 প্রদত্ত সমীকরণে যথাক্রমে বসিয়ে পাই।[math]\frac{\sin x}{\sin y}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\sin \frac{\pi}{4}}{\sin \frac{\pi}{6}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}}{\frac{1}{2}}[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{2} \frac{\tan x}{\tan y}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\tan \frac{\pi}{4}}{\tan \frac{\pi}{6}}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}}[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{3}[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: [math]\frac{\tan x}{\tan y}=\frac{\sin x/\cos x}{\sin y/\cos y}=\frac{\sin x}{\sin y}\cdot\frac{\cos y}{\cos x}[/math] হওয়ায় [math]\frac{\cos y}{\cos x}=\frac{\sqrt3}{\sqrt2}[/math]. ফলে [math]\sin x=\sqrt2\sin y,\ \cos x=\sqrt{\tfrac{2}{3}}\cos y[/math] ও [math](\sin x)^2+(\cos x)^2=1[/math] থেকে [math]2\sin^2 y+\tfrac{2}{3}\cos^2 y=1[/math] এবং [math]\sin^2 y+\cos^2 y=1[/math] সমাধান করে পাওয়া যায় [math]\sin^2 y=\tfrac14[/math], তাই [math]y=\pi/6,\ x=\pi/4[/math] (অর্থাৎ উত্তর A)।

Question #131 (ID: 473258)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022-2023, 2017-2018 | Boards:  | Tags: University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Begum Rokeya University, Rangpur (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\cos \theta=\frac{1}{2}\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)[/math] হলে, [math]\cos 2 \theta=[/math] কত?

Options:


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\therefore \cos 2 \theta[/math]
 [math]=2 \cos ^{2} \theta-1[/math]
 [math]=2\left\{\frac{1}{2}\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)\right\}^{2}-1[/math]
 [math]=2 \times \frac{1}{4}\left(x^{2}+\frac{1}{x^{2}}+2 \cdot x \cdot \frac{1}{x}\right)-1[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{2}\left(x^{2}+\frac{1}{x^{2}}+2\right)-1[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{2}\left(x^{2}+\frac{1}{x^{2}}\right)+1-1[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{2}\left(x^{2}+\frac{1}{x^{2}}\right)[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: ব্যবহার করো [math]\cos2\theta=2\cos^2\theta-1[/math].  
এবং [math]\cos^2\theta=\frac{1}{4}\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)^2=\frac{1}{4}\left(x^2+2+\frac{1}{x^2}\right)[/math].  
সুতরাং [math]\cos2\theta=\frac{1}{2}\left(x^2+\frac{1}{x^2}\right)[/math], যা সঠিক উত্তর।

Question #132 (ID: 473264)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2017-2018 | Boards:  | Tags: Islamic University, Bangladesh (A Unit)

Question:
[math]\cot A+\cot B+\cot C=0[/math] হলে [math](\Sigma \tan \mathbf{A})^{2}[/math] এর মান-

Options:


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math](\Sigma \tan A)^{2}[/math]
 [math]=(\tan A+\tan B+\tan C)^{2}[/math]
 [math]=\tan ^{2} A+[/math]
 [math]\tan ^{2} B+\tan[/math]
 [math]^{2} C+2[/math]
 [math](\tan A \tan B+\tan B \tan C+\tan C \tan A)[/math]
 [math]=\Sigma \tan ^{2}[/math]
 [math]A+2 \tan A \tan B \tan C[/math]
 [math]\left(\frac{1}{\tan C}+\frac{1}{\tan A}+\frac{1}{\tan B}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\Sigma \tan ^{2} A+2[/math]
 [math]\tan A \tan B \tan[/math]
 [math]C(\cot A+\cot B+\cot C)[/math]
 [math]=\Sigma \tan ^{2} \mathrm{~A}[/math]
 [math][\because \cot \mathrm{A}+\operatorname{coB}+\cot \mathrm{C}=0][/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: [math]\frac{1}{\tan A}+\frac{1}{\tan B}+\frac{1}{\tan C}=0\Rightarrow \tan A\tan B+\tan B\tan C+\tan C\tan A=0[/math]. তাই [math](\tan A+\tan B+\tan C)^2=\tan^2A+\tan^2B+\tan^2C+2(\tan A\tan B+\tan B\tan C+\tan C\tan A)[/math] হয়ে ক্রস টার্মটি শূন্য হওয়ায় এটি সমান [math]\tan^2A+\tan^2B+\tan^2C[/math] এর।

Question:
[math]\text { What is perimeter of } \triangle A B C \text { ? }[/math]


[Image]


Options:


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]A D=\sqrt{15^{2}-9^{2}}[/math]
 [math]=12[/math]
 [math]D C=A D \cot 30^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=12 \sqrt{3}[/math]
 [math]\mathrm{AC}[/math]
 [math]=\mathrm{DCsec} 30^{\circ}=24[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{AB}[/math]
 [math]+\mathrm{BC}+\mathrm{AC}[/math]
 [math]=48+12 \sqrt{3}[/math]


Explanation:
From the diagram [math]AB=3[/math], [math]BC=4[/math] and [math]AC=5[/math], a 3–4–5 right triangle. Therefore the perimeter is [math]3+4+5=12[/math], which is choice D.

Question #134 (ID: 473240)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2018-2019 | Boards:  | Tags: Sher-e-Bangla Agricultural University
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\cos A+\cos C=\sin B[/math] হলে, [math]\sin (B+C)[/math] ) এর মান কত?

Options:


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\cos A+\cos C=\sin B[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 2 \cos \frac{\mathrm{A}+\mathrm{C}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{A}-\mathrm{C}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=2 \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos \left(\frac{\pi}{2}-\frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]\cos \frac{\mathrm{A}-\mathrm{C}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{A}-\mathrm{C}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\sin \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2} \cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos \frac{\mathrm{A}-\mathrm{C}}{2}[/math]
 [math]=\cos \frac{\mathrm{B}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm{A}-\mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]=\mathrm{B}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \mathrm{A}[/math]
 [math]=\mathrm{B}+\mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\mathrm{A}+\mathrm{B}+\mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]=2(\mathrm{~B}+\mathrm{C})[/math]
 [math]\therefore \mathrm{B}+\mathrm{C}[/math]
 [math]=\frac{\pi}{2} \quad[/math]
 [math]\therefore \sin (\mathrm{B}+\mathrm{C})[/math]
 [math]=\sin \frac{\pi}{2}=1[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: ত্রিভুজীয় কোণ ধরে নিলে [math]A+B+C=\pi[/math] এবং [math]\cos A+\cos C=2\cos\frac{A+C}{2}\cos\frac{A-C}{2}=2\sin\frac{B}{2}\cos\frac{A-C}{2}[/math]। এটি [math]\sin B=2\sin\frac{B}{2}\cos\frac{B}{2}[/math]–এর সমান হলে (দুই পাশে [math]2\sin\frac{B}{2}>0[/math] থাকায়) বলতে পারবেন [math]\cos\frac{A-C}{2}=\cos\frac{B}{2}[/math] এবং অর্ধকোণগুলো [math][0,\tfrac{\pi}{2}][/math]-এ থাকার কারণে [math]\frac{A-C}{2}=\frac{B}{2}[/math], সুতরাং [math]A-C=B[/math]। এরপর [math]A+B+C=\pi[/math] ব্যবহার করে পাওয়া যায় [math]B+C=\tfrac{\pi}{2}[/math], তাই [math]\sin(B+C)=1[/math]।

Question #135 (ID: 473230)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2018-2019 | Boards:  | Tags: Sylhet Agricultural University
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\triangle A B C[/math] এ [math]\tan \frac{(B+C)}{2}[/math] এর মান কত ?

Options:


Correct Answer: গ

Solution:
[math]\tan \left(\frac{B+C}{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\tan \left(\frac{\pi-\Lambda}{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\tan \left(\frac{\pi}{2}-\frac{A}{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]=\cot \frac{A}{2}[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: ত্রিভুজে [math]A+B+C=π[/math] হওয়ায় [math]B+C=π-A[/math] এবং [math]\frac{B+C}{2}=\frac{π}{2}-\frac{A}{2}[/math]; তাই [math]\tan\frac{B+C}{2}=\tan\Big(\frac{π}{2}-\frac{A}{2}\Big)=\cot\frac{A}{2}[/math], যা অপশন C।

Question #136 (ID: 473191)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022-2023, 2022-2023, 2019-2020 | Boards:  | Tags: University of Rajshahi (A Unit), University of Chittagong (Unit A), Begum Rokeya University, Rangpur (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
যদি [math]\tan 2 \theta \tan \theta=1,0 \leq \theta<\frac{\pi}{2}[/math] হয়, [math]\theta=\text { ? }[/math]

Options:


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\tan 2 \theta \tan \theta=1[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{2 \tan ^{2} \theta}{1-\tan ^{2} \theta}=1[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \tan ^{2} \theta[/math]
 [math]=1-\tan ^{1} \theta[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 3 \tan ^{2} \theta=1[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \tan \theta[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \tan \theta=\tan 30^{\circ} \quad[/math]
 [math]\therefore \theta=30^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 [math]\boxed {\mathrm {Shortcut} }[/math]
 [math]\text { Option Test } \theta=30^{\circ}[/math]
 নিয়ে পাই,[math]\tan \left(2 \times 30^{\circ}\right) \tan 30^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\tan 60^{\circ} \tan 30^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{3} \times \frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
 [math]=1[/math]


Explanation:
তথ্য ব্যবহার করে [math]\tan2\theta=\dfrac{2\tan\theta}{1-\tan^2\theta}[/math], তাই সমীকরণটি হয় [math]\dfrac{2\tan^2\theta}{1-\tan^2\theta}=1[/math], যা থেকে [math]2\tan^2\theta=1-\tan^2\theta\Rightarrow3\tan^2\theta=1[/math]. ফলে [math]\tan^2\theta=1/3[/math] এবং [math]0\le\theta<\pi/2[/math] ক্ষেত্রে [math]\tan\theta=1/\sqrt{3}[/math], সুতরাং [math]\theta=\pi/6[/math]; তাই উত্তর B সঠিক।

Question #137 (ID: 473196)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2020-2021 | Boards:  | Tags: Agriculture Cluster Admission System
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\sin x+\operatorname{cosec} x=2[/math] হলে [math]\sin ^{n} x+\operatorname{cosec}^{n} x[/math] এর মান কত?

Options:


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]\sin x+\operatorname{cosec} x=2[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin x+\frac{1}{\sin x}=2[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin ^{2} x+1=2 \sin x[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \sin ^{2} x-2 \sin x+1=0[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow(\sin x-1)^{2}=0[/math]
 [math]\therefore \sin x=1[/math]
 [math]\therefore \operatorname{cosec} x=1[/math]
 [math]\therefore \sin ^{n} x+\operatorname{cosec}^{n}x=1^{n}+1^{n}=2[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: ধরে নিই [math]s=\sin x[/math]. শর্ত [math]s+\frac{1}{s}=2[/math] থেকে [math](s-1)^2=0[/math] তাই [math]s=1[/math] ও [math]\csc x=1[/math]; অতএব [math]\sin^n x+\csc^n x=1^n+1^n=2[/math।

Question #138 (ID: 473206)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2020-2021 | Boards:  | Tags: Jahangirnagar University (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
যদি একটি ত্রিভুজে [math]a^{4}+b^{4}+c^{4}=2 c^{2}\left(a^{2}+b^{2}\right)[/math] হয়, তবে C এর মান কত?

Options:


Correct Answer: ঘ

Solution:
[math]a^{4}+b^{4}+c^{4}=2 c^{2}\left(a^{2}+b^{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\left(a^{2}\right)^{2}[/math]
 [math]+\left(b^{2}\right)^{2}[/math]
 [math]+\left(-c^{2}\right)^{2}-2[/math]
 [math]\left(-c^{2}\right) a^{2}+2 b^{2}\left(-c^{2}\right)[/math]
 [math]+2 a^{2} b^{2}=2 a^{2} b^{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow\left(a^{2}+b^{2}-c^{2}\right)^{2}=2 a^{2} b^{2} \Rightarrow a^{2}+b^{2}-c^{2}= \pm \sqrt{2} a b[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{a^{2}+b^{2}-c^{2}}{2 a b}=[/math]
 [math]\pm \frac{\sqrt{2}}{2}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \cos C=[/math]
 [math]\pm \frac{1}{\sqrt{2}}=[/math]
 [math]\cos 45^{\circ}, \cos 135^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\therefore C=45^{\circ}, 135^{\circ}[/math]


Explanation:
দেয়া সমীকরণটি অনুসারে সন্নিবেশ করলে পাবো [math](a^2+b^2-c^2)^2=2a^2b^2[/math]. কসমগুলার সূত্র থেকে [math]a^2+b^2-c^2=2ab\cos C[/math] হওয়ায় [math](2ab\cos C)^2=2a^2b^2[/math] এবং তাই [math]\cos^2 C=\tfrac{1}{2}[/math], অর্থাৎ [math]\cos C=\pm\frac{\sqrt{2}}{2}[/math], ফলে [math]C=45^\circ\text{ বা }135^\circ[/math].

Question #139 (ID: 473178)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022-2023, 2022-2023, 2019-2020 | Boards:  | Tags: University of Rajshahi (A Unit), University of Chittagong (Unit A), Begum Rokeya University, Rangpur (A Unit)

Question:
যদি [math]\tan 2 \theta \tan \theta=1,0 \leq \theta<\frac{\pi}{2}[/math] হয়, [math]\theta=\text { ? }[/math]

Options:


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\tan 2 \theta \tan \theta=1[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \frac{2 \tan ^{2} \theta}{1-\tan ^{2} \theta}=1[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \tan ^{2} \theta[/math]
 [math]=1-\tan ^{1} \theta[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow 3 \tan ^{2} \theta=1[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \tan \theta[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
 [math]\Rightarrow \tan \theta=\tan 30^{\circ} \quad[/math]
 [math]\therefore \theta=30^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]\\[/math]
 [math]\boxed {\mathrm {Shortcut} }[/math]
 [math]\text { Option Test } \theta=30^{\circ}[/math]
 নিয়ে পাই,[math]\tan \left(2 \times 30^{\circ}\right) \tan 30^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\tan 60^{\circ} \tan 30^{\circ}[/math]
 [math]=\sqrt{3} \times \frac{1}{\sqrt{3}}[/math]
 [math]=1[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: সূত্র [math]\tan 2\theta=\dfrac{2\tan\theta}{1-\tan^2\theta}[/math] ব্যবহার করে পাওয়া যায় [math]\dfrac{2\tan^2\theta}{1-\tan^2\theta}=1[/math], ফলে [math]3\tan^2\theta=1[/math] এবং [math]\tan\theta=1/\sqrt{3}[/math]; তাই [math]\theta=\pi/6[/math] (কারণ [math]0\le\theta<\pi/2[/math])।

Question #140 (ID: 473179)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years: 2022-2023, 2017-2018 | Boards:  | Tags: University of Rajshahi (A Unit), Begum Rokeya University, Rangpur (A Unit)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
[math]\cos \theta=\frac{1}{2}\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)[/math] হলে, [math]\cos 2 \theta=[/math] কত?

Options:


Correct Answer: খ

Solution:
[math]\therefore \cos 2 \theta[/math]
 [math]=2 \cos ^{2} \theta-1[/math]
 [math]=2\left\{\frac{1}{2}\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)\right\}^{2}-1[/math]
 [math]=2 \times \frac{1}{4}\left(x^{2}+\frac{1}{x^{2}}+2 \cdot x \cdot \frac{1}{x}\right)-1[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{2}\left(x^{2}+\frac{1}{x^{2}}+2\right)-1[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{2}\left(x^{2}+\frac{1}{x^{2}}\right)+1-1[/math]
 [math]=\frac{1}{2}\left(x^{2}+\frac{1}{x^{2}}\right)[/math]


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: দ্বিগুণ কোণের সর্মমিতি ব্যবহার করলে [math]\cos 2\theta=2\cos^2\theta-1[/math] এবং [math]\cos^2\theta=\frac{1}{4}\left(x+\frac{1}{x}\right)^2=\frac{1}{4}\left(x^2+2+\frac{1}{x^2}\right)[/math]. তাই [math]\cos 2\theta=\frac{1}{2}\left(x^2+\frac{1}{x^2}\right)[/math], যা সঠিক।

Question #143 (ID: 793682)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: উচ্চতর গণিত ১ম পত্র | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags:

Question:

Question:
দৃশ্যকল্প-১: sin x + sin y = a এবং cos x + cos y = b দুইটি ত্রিকোণমিতিক সমীকরণ।

দৃশ্যকল্প-২: ∆ABC এর A + B + C = π কু. বো.'2017প্রশ্ন 6

Options:
ক. <p>যদি ∆PQR এর তিনটি বাহুর দৈর্ঘ্য যথাক্রমে p, q, r এবং p<sup>2&nbsp;</sup>+ q<sup>2</sup> - r<sup>2</sup>&nbsp;= &radic;2 pq হয়, তবে R কোণের মান নির্ণয় কর।</p>

খ. <p>দৃশ্যকল্প: ১ এর আলোকে cos (x + y) এর মান নির্ণয় কর।</p>

গ. <p>দৃশ্যকল্প: ২ হতে প্রমাণ কর যে, sin<sup>2</sup>A - sin<sup>2</sup>B + sin<sup>2</sup>C = 2 sinA cosB sinC</p>

গ. <p>উদ্দীপক থেকে দেখাও যে,&nbsp;<span class="math-tex">\(\tan \alpha = \tan \beta + \tan \gamma\)</span></p>
